### [1] [DreamCharacter-1: From 3D Generative Foundation Models to Product-Ready Character Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07817)
*Weizhe Liu,Yunjie Wu,Xiangqian Shu,Guangwei Wang,Xiangyu Xu,Peng Li,Yujie Li,Hengkai Guo*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: DreamCharacter-1是一个轻量级后适应框架，通过几何后训练、纹理后训练和推理加速三个组件，校准预训练3D基础模型，实现高质量、可投入生产的3D角色生成，在定量和定性实验中均优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有3D基础模型生成的3D角色在表面细节、纹理质量和生产效率方面仍存在不足，难以满足实际应用需求。作者希望提出一个轻量级的后适应框架，在不重新训练整个模型的情况下，显著提升3D角色生成的质量和可用性。

Method: 以预训练3D基础模型为骨干，引入三个任务导向组件：(1) 几何后训练——通过几何偏好优化增强精细表面细节；(2) 纹理后训练——合成高分辨率纹理并优化遮挡区域的外观；(3) 推理加速——支持可扩展部署。

Result: DreamCharacter-1在定量和定性实验中均生成视觉上令人满意且结构稳健的3D角色资产，一致超越当前最先进的角色生成方法。

Conclusion: 提出了一种轻量级后适应框架，有效校准预训练3D基础模型，使其能够生成高质量、可投入生产的3D角色，验证了通过任务导向的后训练组件可以显著提升基础模型的生成能力。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：75%。具体方案：(1) 将几何后训练中的几何偏好优化策略应用于遥感3D地形重建，增强地表细节如植被、建筑边缘等精细结构；(2) 纹理后训练组件可迁移至遥感影像的多视角纹理合成与遮挡区域（如云层遮挡）修复；(3) 推理加速模块有助于大规模遥感3D模型的快速部署。需注意遥感数据尺度大、纹理特征与角色生成存在差异，需调整训练数据和损失函数。

Abstract (英文): We present DreamCharacter-1, a lightweight post-adaptation framework that calibrates pretrained 3D foundation models toward high-fidelity, production-ready 3D character generation. Building upon a 3D foundation backbone, our pipeline incorporates three task-oriented components: (1) geometry post-training, which enhances fine-grained surface details through geometric preference optimization; (2) texture post-training, which synthesizes high-resolution textures and refines the appearance of occluded regions; and (3) inference acceleration, which enables scalable deployment. Extensive quantitative and qualitative experiments demonstrate that DreamCharacter-1 produces visually compelling and structurally robust 3D character assets, consistently surpassing state-of-the-art character generation methods.

</details>


### [2] [GIRAF: Towards Generalizable Human Interactions with Articulated Objects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07880)
*Xiaohan Zhang,Sebastian Starke,Alexander Winkler,Federica Bogo,Samir Aroudj,Yuting Ye*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种文本条件扩散模型，通过物体中心表示、混合域训练策略和基于接触的数据增强三大核心思想，实现全身与铰接物体的逼真交互生成，在未见物体配置上超越现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法局限于静态物体或仅手部操作，无法生成协调的全身运动（包括接近、操作和移动铰接物体），且缺乏大规模配对运动-场景数据。

Method: 提出文本条件扩散模型，包含三个核心：1）以物体为中心的表示统一手-物接触与物体表面；2）混合域训练策略平衡 locomotion 和交互；3）基于接触的数据增强方案扩展训练多样性。

Result: 在未见物体配置上展现强泛化能力，超越当前最先进方法。

Conclusion: 该模型有效解决了全身与铰接物体交互的协调生成问题，为具身AI和图形学中的机器人训练与虚拟智能体应用提供了新方案。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：65%。该文的人-物交互生成技术虽面向图形学与具身AI，但与遥感存在交叉可能：1）将物体中心表示与接触推理方法迁移至遥感中的人-地物交互建模（如人与车辆、工程设备的交互动作仿真）；2）混合域训练策略可用于遥感中的多任务学习（如同时处理目标检测与场景变化检测）；3）接触增强方法可启发遥感中基于稀疏标注数据的半监督/自监督学习方案。

Abstract (英文): Synthesizing realistic full-body human interactions with articulated objects is a fundamental challenge for embodied AI and graphics, with applications in robotics training and virtual agents. Existing models remain limited: some focus on simple activities with static objects, while others restrict attention to hand-only manipulation. This leaves open the problem of generating coordinated full-body motion that approaches, manipulates, and moves articulated objects in a realistic and generalizable way. The key difficulty lies in reasoning jointly about locomotion, fine-grained contact, and object articulation. Models must capture subtle hand-object correspondences that transfer across object geometries, while also producing seamless transitions from navigation to manipulation. At the same time, the scarcity of large-scale paired motion-scene data makes it difficult to generalize across diverse object positions and shapes. We introduce a text-conditioned diffusion model that addresses these challenges through three core ideas: an object-centric representation that unifies hand-object contact with object surfaces, a mixed-domain training strategy that balances locomotion and interaction, and a contact-based augmentation scheme that expands training diversity. Through experiments, our method demonstrated strong generalization to unseen object configurations, surpassing current state-of-the-art methods.

</details>


### [3] [3D Reconstruction of deciduous Trees using low-cost UAV- and Crane-based Photogrammetry for Monitoring Shoot Elongation across entire Canopies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07905)
*Stephan Nebiker,Micha Tschanz,Nando Amport,Frederik Baumgarten*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文针对树木初级生长（芽伸长）监测技术缺失的问题，探索了利用低成本无人机摄影测量和多相机CraneCam系统在真实环境下对原生落叶树进行三维重建的方法。研究覆盖整个生长季，实现了5-6 mm的点精度和92%-98%的重建完整度，并引入3D打印地面真值树枝评估精细结构重建能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 气候变化（升温、干旱、晚霜等极端事件）影响树木生长和碳封存能力；径向生长（次生生长）已有成熟监测手段（树轮测量仪），但芽伸长（初级生长）因缺乏合适测量技术而被长期忽视，导致气候变化对树木初级生长的影响认知不足。

Method: 使用消费级无人机（<250g）摄影测量和多相机CraneCam系统，在两个研究区域内采集整个生长季的数据；提出摄影测量数据采集与处理策略；引入3D打印地面真值树枝评估精细结构（如细枝）重建能力；通过点云精度、分辨率和完整性进行分析。

Result: 消费级无人机摄影测量实现了5-6 mm的整树三维点精度；3D重建完整性达92%-98%（依无人机类型而异）；展示了利用低成本设备重建树木精细结构的可行性。

Conclusion: 低成本无人机摄影测量可有效监测树木初级生长（芽伸长），填补了该领域技术空白；讨论了操作挑战及基于摄影测量点云进行整树骨架化的初步实验，为未来气候变化对树木初级生长影响的研究提供了新手段。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：90%。该论文直接属于遥感与植物生理生态交叉的前沿工作。改进方案：（1）引入多光谱或热红外传感器，同步监测树木健康状况与水分胁迫对初级生长的影响；（2）结合激光雷达（LiDAR）数据弥补摄影测量在穿透树冠方面的不足，提升精细枝条重建精度；（3）将点云骨架化算法与时间序列分析结合，实现自动化芽伸长速率提取；（4）扩展至森林尺度的无人机航线规划，实现大范围树木初级生长监测。

Abstract (英文): Tree growth determines how much CO2 is sequestered from the atmosphere and temporarily stored in woody biomass. At the same time tree growth is affected by increasing temperatures, more frequent drought periods, late frosts and other extreme events associated with climate change. While continuous measurements of radial (secondary) tree growth using dendrometers are well established, monitoring of shoot elongation (primary growth) has largely been neglected because suitable measurement techniques are lacking. As a result, the effects of climate change on primary tree growth remain insufficiently understood. This work aims at reconstructing native deciduous trees in 3D as a basis for measuring and monitoring shoot elongation over entire tree canopies. Here we explored the use of low-cost UAV photogrammetry and of a multi-camera CraneCam system under real-world conditions. Data were collected in two study areas over an entire growing season. We present sensor evaluations, photogrammetric data acquisition and processing strategies. A special focus is placed on the analysis of the resulting photogrammetric 3D point clouds in terms of accuracy, resolution and completeness. Results demonstrate 3D point accuracies of 5-6 mm for entire trees using consumer-grade UAVs weighing less than 250 g and a 3D reconstruction completeness between 92% and 98% depending on the UAV type. The paper introduces a novel 3Dprinted ground-truth branch to evaluate the capability to reconstructing fine-detail structures such as thin tree shoots. Finally, we discuss operational challenges and initial experiments towards a skeletonization of entire trees based on photogrammetric point clouds.

</details>


### [4] [Adversarial Decoys: Misdirecting Attention-Based Defenses in ViT](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07922)
*Giulia Marchiori Pietrosanti,Giulio Rossolini,Giorgio Buttazzo*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出对抗性诱饵（adversarial decoys），即独立优化的图像块，能够将注意力及相关防御重定向到选定的目标token上，从而绕过基于注意力分数的测试时防御。该方法与攻击无关，可轻松集成到现有对抗性补丁攻击中，揭示了仅凭注意力大小作为对抗相关性指标的局限性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的测试时防御通过抑制高注意力分数的图像token来抵御局部对抗攻击，因为对抗性token需要吸引大量注意力才能影响预测。作者希望证明这种依赖注意力大小作为对抗性指标的防御存在根本性缺陷，并设计一种能够同时绕过这些防御的方法。

Method: 该方法将误导分类和逃避防御两个目标解耦：对抗区域负责产生错误预测，而对抗性诱饵（decoy）则操纵防御所使用的注意力排名。通过逐层目标函数，增加目标token的注意力，使其超过其他非目标token。诱饵独立于底层攻击进行优化，因此与攻击无关。

Result: 在ImageNet上针对多种ViT架构和攻击的实验表明，对抗性诱饵能够将高注意力分数从真实对抗区域重定向开，同时保持大部分攻击有效性。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了使用注意力大小作为对抗相关性指标的基本局限性，现有的基于注意力分数的测试时防御存在严重安全漏洞，需要开发更鲁棒的防御机制。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感图像中的目标检测与分类同样面临对抗性攻击威胁，尤其是针对ViT架构的注意力机制攻击。该方法的对抗性诱饵思路可迁移到遥感场景，用于：(1) 评估遥感ViT模型对注意力欺骗的鲁棒性；(2) 设计更鲁棒的遥感图像防御策略，如结合空间上下文或频域特征而非仅依赖注意力分数；(3) 在遥感多尺度目标检测中，诱饵可用于研究注意力重定向对弱小目标检测的影响。

Abstract (英文): Vision Transformers (ViTs) remain vulnerable to localized adversarial attacks, e.g., adversarial patches, while recent test-time defenses mitigate them by suppressing image tokens with abnormally high attention scores. These defenses exploit a strong coupling between attention and adversarial effectiveness: adversarial tokens often need to attract substantial attention to influence the prediction. We introduce adversarial decoys, independently optimized image patches that redirect the attention, and therefore related defenses, toward selected target tokens. Rather than jointly optimizing misclassifications and defense evasion, our approach decouples the two objectives: the original adversarial region induces the incorrect prediction, while a separate decoy manipulates the attention ranking used by the defense. A layer-wise objective increases target-token attention and promotes these tokens above competing non-target ones. Since the decoy is optimized independently of the underlying attack, the method is attack-agnostic and can be easily integrated with any existing adversarial patch attack. Experiments on ImageNet across multiple ViT architectures and attacks show that decoys can redirect high attention scores away from the true adversarial region while preserving much of the attack effectiveness. These results reveal a fundamental limitation of using attention magnitude as an indicator of adversarial relevance.

</details>


### [5] [Beyond Thermal Imaging: Inferring Thermophysical Properties from Time-Resolved Thermal Observations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07962)
*Chenghao Xu,Malcolm Mielle,Olga Fink*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: ThermoField是一个统一热场景重建与热物理参数估计的框架，通过可微分热传导模拟，结合神经场表示与场景几何约束，从热观测数据中联合重建几何、估计空间变化的热扩散率，并预测未知环境条件下的热演化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有热场景重建方法能恢复3D环境中的温度场但无法识别控制热演化的热物理属性，而逆方法虽能提供可解释的参数估计却依赖简化几何和受控实验条件。亟需一种统一方法，在复杂3D场景中同时实现热场景重建与热物理参数推断。

Method: 将热物理量表示为空间变化的神经场，通过场景几何、热传导物理规律和时间热观测三重约束进行优化，集成可微分热传导求解器，实现端到端的物理参数学习与场景重建。

Result: ThermoField能够联合重建几何结构，估计空间变化的热扩散率，并在未见过的环境条件下预测热演化。

Conclusion: 该框架在热场景重建与逆热传导分析之间建立了桥梁，提供了一种从热观测数据出发，统一进行几何重建、热物理属性估计和预测性热模拟的方法。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。该框架可直接应用于遥感领域的热红外数据分析：(1) 用于卫星热红外遥感图像中的地表热物理属性（如热扩散率）反演，结合DEM几何信息实现更准确的地表温度预测；(2) 将可微分热传导模拟扩展到考虑太阳辐射、大气效应等遥感场景的复杂边界条件；(3) 改进方向：将神经场表示替换为更适合遥感大尺度场景的稀疏表示或网格化表示以降低计算开销，并引入多尺度时间分辨率处理昼夜热循环数据。

Abstract (英文): Inferring latent physical properties from sensory observations is a fundamental challenge in machine perception. Among available sensing modalities, thermal imaging is particularly promising because temperature evolution is directly governed by heat-transfer physics and therefore encodes information about underlying thermophysical properties of a scene. Recovering spatially resolved thermophysical properties from thermal observations could transform applications ranging from digital twins and infrastructure monitoring to robotics and scientific imaging. However, existing thermal scene reconstruction methods can recover temperature fields in complex 3D environments without identifying the thermophyiscal properties that govern thermal evolution, whereas inverse methods provide physically interpretable parameter estimation but typically rely on simplified geometries and controlled experimental conditions.
  Here we introduce ThermoField, a framework that unifies thermal scene reconstruction and thermophysical parameter estimation through differentiable heat-transfer simulation. The proposed framework represents these quantities as spatially varying neural fields and constrains them through scene geometry, governing heat-transfer physics, and temporal thermal observations. We demonstrate that ThermoField jointly reconstructs geometry, estimates spatially varying thermal diffusivity, and predicts thermal evolution under previously unseen environmental conditions. By integrating neural scene representations with differentiable heat-transfer solver, the framework enables physically interpretable parameter inference in complex 3D scenes. Our results establish a bridge between thermal scene reconstruction and inverse heat-transfer analysis, providing a unified approach for geometry reconstruction, thermophysical property estimation, and predictive thermal simulation from thermal observations.

</details>


### [6] [LOGOS: Language-guided Oriented Object Detection in Aerial Scenes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08004)
*Trong-Thuan Nguyen,Minh-Triet Tran*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出LOGOS，一种基于Transformer的文本提示引导定向目标检测方法，通过提示调制内容查询动态调整模型关注点，在DOTA数据集上优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统定向目标检测方法面临角度不连续、固定查询尺寸以及处理稀疏/杂乱场景效率低等问题，亟需一种能够利用文本提示引导检测、动态适应复杂遥感环境的方案。

Method: 采用Transformer架构，引入提示调制内容查询（prompt-modulated content queries）机制，利用文本提示动态调整模型对遥感图像中不同目标的关注权重，实现对任意方向目标的鲁棒检测。

Result: 在DOTA数据集上的大量实验表明，LOGOS在密集排列和旋转目标场景中优于现有最先进方法，在鲁棒性和可扩展性方面取得显著提升。

Conclusion: LOGOS通过文本提示引导的Transformer框架有效解决了定向目标检测中的关键难题，为遥感应用中的目标检测提供了更鲁棒和可扩展的解决方案。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。本文本身就是遥感定向目标检测论文。改进方向：（1）提示调制可扩展至多模态遥感数据（如SAR+光学）的联合检测；（2）当前仅在DOTA验证，可进一步在HRSC2016、UCAS-AOD等数据集上评估泛化性；（3）引入遥感领域知识（如GIS语义信息）增强文本提示的语义丰富度；（4）优化查询机制适应超大尺寸遥感影像的高效推理。

Abstract (英文): Object detection in geospatial scenes, such as satellite and aerial imagery, poses significant challenges due to the varying orientations and densities of objects, as well as the complex backgrounds inherent to remote sensing imagery. Traditional methods for oriented object detection have struggled to address issues such as angular discontinuity, fixed query sizes, and inefficiencies in handling sparse or cluttered scenes. In this paper, we propose LOGOS, a novel transformer-based approach that leverages textual prompts to guide the detection of oriented objects in aerial scenes. In particular, our proposed approach incorporates prompt-modulated content queries to dynamically adjust the model's focus based on the provided text, thereby improving object detection accuracy in complex environments. Empirically, extensive experiments on the DOTA dataset demonstrate that LOGOS outperforms existing state-of-the-art methods, particularly in densely packed and rotated object scenarios. Our approach offers a significant step forward in improving the robustness and scalability of oriented object detection in remote sensing applications.

</details>


### [7] [FedTR: Federated Learning Framework with Transfer Learning for Industrial Visual Inspection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08014)
*Vikash Sathiamoorthy,Shuo Huai,Hao Kong,Di Liu,Wendy Yong Yi Loy,Christian Makaya,Daren Ho,Ravi Subramaniam,Qian Lin,Weichen Liu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: FedTR是一个结合迁移学习的联邦学习框架，用于自主工业视觉检测中的标签缺陷识别。该框架先在公开数据集上预训练模型，再在分布式私有数据上进行联邦微调，在墨水盒标签缺陷识别任务上实现了95.5%（同质数据）和94.2%（异质数据）的端到端文本识别词级准确率，性能媲美集中式训练。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 联邦学习在工业视觉检测中面临数据量有限和检测任务复杂两大挑战，导致模型性能受限，因此需要一种能结合预训练知识并适用于分布式私有数据的联邦学习方案。

Method: 提出FedTR框架，首先使用公开数据集对模型进行预训练，随后在分布式且有限的私有数据上执行联邦学习过程并进行模型微调，实现知识迁移与隐私保护的双重目标。

Result: 在私有墨水盒数据集上，FedTR在标签缺陷识别任务中，同质数据上达到95.5%的端到端文本识别词级准确率，异质数据上达到94.2%，性能与集中式训练持平。

Conclusion: FedTR有效结合迁移学习与联邦学习，解决了工业视觉检测中数据稀缺和任务复杂性问题，在不共享私有数据的前提下实现了接近集中式训练的性能。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感领域同样面临标注数据稀缺、数据分布不均（同质/异质）和隐私保护需求。具体交叉方案：(1) 将FedTR框架应用于遥感图像中的目标检测（如车辆、船只检测）或文本识别（如遥感图像中的地理标签、标牌识别）；(2) 利用公开遥感数据集（如DOTA、RSDD）进行预训练，再在各单位/机构的私有遥感数据上进行联邦微调；(3) 针对遥感图像的多尺度、多模态特性，可在FedTR基础上引入多尺度特征提取模块或模态对齐机制。

Abstract (英文): Federated learning (FL) is a collaborative learning scheme to train deep learning models, where collaborating parties can consolidate their models without sharing local data with other parties, hence preserving data privacy. Nevertheless, when implementing FL in Industrial visual inspection (IVI), the constraints posed by limited data availability and the intricate nature of the inspection tasks significantly impact the performance of the resulting model. This paper introduces FedTR, a novel FL framework incorporating transfer learning designed for Autonomous IVI, focusing on the challenging task of identifying label defects through end-to-end text recognition. Transfer learning is a method that leverages the knowledge of a pre-trained model to adapt to a different dataset. FedTR initially trains the model using a publicly available dataset, after which performs the essential federated learning process with model fine-tuning on the distributed and limited private data. Extensive experiment results demonstrate the effectiveness and feasibility of FedTR on private ink cartridge datasets for label defect identification. FedTR achieves an end-to-end text recognition word-level accuracy of 95.5% and 94.2% on homogeneous and heterogeneous data respectively. Additionally, it attains performance levels that are on par with those achieved through centralized training.

</details>


### [8] [LightCrafter: PBR-Conditioned Video Diffusion Refinement for Controllable and Consistent Relighting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08016)
*Zixin Guo,Yehonathan Litman,Yifeng He,John Miller,Chuhan Chen,Deva Ramanan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: LightCrafter提出了一种混合管道，将视频重打光重新定义为代理视频的视频翻译：将输入视频在目标光照下的PBR渲染作为代理，再通过扩散模型翻译成最终结果。该方法结合了物理渲染的准确性和生成模型的灵活性，在真实世界重打光基准上超越了先前最优方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视频重打光方法存在两大范式各自的缺陷：基于逆向渲染+前向渲染的方法受限于噪声重建且难以建模全局光照等复杂效果；基于生成式视频翻译的方法受限于光照控制能力和长时序稳定性。作者希望结合两者的优势，既保留物理渲染的精确光照控制，又利用扩散模型弥补PBR难以捕捉的复杂光照效果。

Method: LightCrafter采用混合流水线：(1) 将输入视频进行PBR渲染，生成目标光照下的代理视频；(2) 训练CogVideoX扩散模型，将PBR代理视频翻译为最终的逼真视频。代理视频将光照目标编码其中，使扩散模型无需学习环境贴图等光照概念。模型通过合成视频对和真实无配对视频进行后训练。

Result: 在真实世界重打光基准上超越了现有最优方法；PBR渲染单独使用已能超过部分先前工作，但在全局光照等效果上存在不足；引入了合成基准用于进一步分析。

Conclusion: LightCrafter通过将物理渲染与生成模型混合，实现了更精细的光照控制和长时序一致性，有效克服了视频重打光中重建噪声和生成不稳定的问题。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感领域中，卫星影像受光照条件（太阳高度角、方位角、云影）影响显著，可借鉴LightCrafter思路：(1) 将不同时相遥感影像视为不同光照条件下的渲染，通过PBR模拟目标光照下的代理影像，再用扩散模型补偿难以建模的大气散射、地形阴影等效应；(2) 用于遥感时序数据的光照归一化，提升变化检测的准确性；(3) 结合数字表面模型（DSM）提供几何先验，增强PBR渲染的物理保真度。

Abstract (英文): Video relighting requires balancing long-form temporal consistency with a physically grounded understanding of light transport, which depends on accurate estimation of intrinsic scene properties such as materials, geometry, and illumination. Existing methods follow two paradigms: (1) reconstruct a video's photometric properties via inverse rendering and relight them to a target illumination via forward rendering, using physically-based rendering (PBR) or a neural renderer; these suffer from noisy reconstructions and struggle with hard-to-model effects such as global illumination. (2) Frame the task as generative video-to-video translation conditioned on relighting targets (a target environment map or text); this limits relighting control and temporal stability, since diffusion models struggle to translate long-form videos, and is constrained by the availability of input/relit training pairs. We propose LightCrafter, a hybrid pipeline that reformulates video relighting as video translation of a proxy video: rather than translating the input video directly to the target, we translate a PBR rendering of the input under the target illumination to the final target. This bakes illumination targets into the PBR proxy, removing the need to teach the diffusion model illumination concepts like environment maps, and enables more intricate lighting control while naturally providing long-form temporal consistency. We show PBR renders alone already outperform some prior art but struggle with effects like global illumination; to capture these, we leverage photometric priors in video generation models by post-training CogVideoX on synthetic video pairs and real-world unpaired videos. We outperform prior state-of-the-art on existing real-world relighting benchmarks and contribute a synthetic benchmark for further analysis. We will release our dataset, benchmark, metrics, and code.

</details>


### [9] [SAGA: Stable Acceleration Guidance for Autoregressive Video Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08020)
*Thanh-Nhan Vo,Trong-Thuan Nguyen,Trung-Hoang Le,Tam V. Nguyen,Minh-Triet Tran*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出SAGA，一种无需训练的稳定加速引导方法，用于自回归视频生成。通过频谱运动分析，针对离散潜在加速度中的高频时间扰动，结合Slepian投影的频谱引导目标和结构化噪声初始化策略，有效减少闪烁、运动抖动和结构漂移，提升时间质量与图像质量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自回归视频扩散模型在重复复用生成潜变量作为因果上下文时，会放大时间误差，导致闪烁、运动抖动和结构漂移。现有方法缺乏有效的解决方案，因此需要一种无需重新训练即可缓解该问题的方法。

Method: 1) 从频谱运动学视角识别离散潜在加速度作为揭示不稳定高频时间扰动的信号；2) 提出基于有限窗口Slepian投影的加速度域频谱引导目标；3) 设计结构化自回归噪声初始化策略，抑制短时时间相关性同时保留长时运动结构；4) 无需训练或修改骨干网络，可直接应用于现有分块自回归扩散模型。

Result: 在Self-Forcing模型上，时间质量从97.30提升至97.91，图像质量从69.60提升至70.51。频谱分析和人类偏好研究均表明SAGA能在保持视觉保真度的同时减少时间不稳定性。

Conclusion: SAGA作为一种训练自由的引导方法，能够有效提升自回归视频生成的时间稳定性，且具有即插即用的优势，适用于多种自回归扩散模型。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感视频生成（如卫星云图、遥感时序监测）中同样面临自回归累积误差导致的时间不连续问题。可将SAGA的频谱引导策略迁移至遥感视频去噪、时序超分等任务，利用离散潜在加速度作为扰动检测信号，结合Slepian投影抑制高频噪声，同时保留长时序地物变化结构。此外，该方法可进一步与遥感数据的多尺度时频谱分析结合，提升连续遥感帧的生成/预测稳定性。

Abstract (英文): Autoregressive video diffusion enables efficient streaming and long-horizon video generation, but repeatedly reusing generated latents as causal context can amplify temporal errors, resulting in flickering, motion jitter, and structural drift. In this paper, we investigate this failure mode from a spectral kinematic perspective and identify discrete latent acceleration as an effective signal for revealing unstable high-frequency temporal perturbations. To this end, we propose SAGA, a training-free \textbf{\textit{s}}table \textbf{\textit{a}}cceleration \textbf{\textit{g}}uidance approach for \textbf{\textit{a}}utoregressive video generation. SAGA integrates an acceleration domain spectral guidance objective based on finite-window Slepian projections with a structured autoregressive noise initialization strategy that suppresses short-range temporal correlations while preserving long-range motion structure. Without retraining or modifying the backbone, SAGA can be directly applied to existing chunk-wise autoregressive diffusion models, which is the prevalent setting for high-quality generation. Extensive experiments show that SAGA consistently improves temporal quality across multiple autoregressive diffusion models. On Self-Forcing, SAGA improves Temporal Quality from 97.30 to 97.91 and Image Quality from 69.60 to 70.51. Moreover, spectral analysis and human preference studies demonstrate that SAGA reduces temporal instability while maintaining visual fidelity.

Abstract (英文): Long-horizon robot planning requires jointly reasoning over semantic task structure and geometric feasibility. In this work, we propose APIVOT, a VLM-based planner that adaptively interleaves language and visual thoughts for long-horizon planning. APIVOT learns to leverage language for semantic reasoning, while using visual thoughts as imagined future states for internal verification of geometric feasibility. On long-horizon kitchen tasks, APIVOT outperforms general-purpose VLMs and prior planning frameworks, achieving the largest gains in spatially constrained settings. Abstract (英文): End-to-end models that map multimodal inputs directly to future trajectories/maneuvers have emerged as an increasingly prominent research paradigm in autonomous driving. This class of models includes both Vision-Language-Action models and trajectory-generative planners. Unlike classic machine learning applications, autonomous vehicles operate in safety-critical and interaction-intensive environments where traditional open-loop imitation of expert demonstrations is not sufficient to ensure reliability. In particular, small execution errors can accumulate over time, while recovery behaviors are scarce in training data. In addition, long-horizon objectives such as safety and driving comfort are not captured by pointwise labels either. These limitations have motivated a shift toward post-training techniques, which further refine driving policies beyond pure imitation. This survey presents a unified view of post-training for autonomous driving by defining its scope and organizing the existing literature into four major families based on the form of supervision they use. For each family, we discuss its capabilities, limitations, and open challenges. We aim to facilitate a systematic understanding of this emerging area and stimulate future research on reliable and efficient post-training for autonomous driving.

Abstract (英文): Unmanned Aerial Vehicle (UAV) videos are widely used in traffic monitoring, urban management, and emergency rescue. To this end, we introduce a new task, UAV Open-Vocabulary Video Instance Segmentation (UAV-OVVIS), which discovers targets in UAV videos according to open-vocabulary queries and outputs instance-level segmentation trajectories with globally consistent identities. Considering the scarcity of instance-level annotations in UAV scenarios, we propose AeroTrack, a training-free unified framework. ### [13] [LDFE: Laplacian Decoupled Feature Enhancement Block for Dual-Stream CNN-based RGB-IR Object Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08076)
*Wenhao Dong,Xiaoyan Luo,Linlin Yang,Haodong Zhu,Xiaorong Shi,Guodong Guo,Baochang Zhang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出拉普拉斯解耦特征增强模块(LDFE)，通过全局-局部分解、去噪、融合与重建，在双流CNN骨干网络中实现RGB-IR图像特征融合。该模块包含全局状态空间增强(GS2E)和局部卷积相关增强(LC2E)两个子模块，分别在全局和局部层面进行跨模态去噪与融合。在M3FD、DroneVehicle等6个数据集上超越SOTA方法2.0%-6.2% mAP。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于YOLO的双流CNN方法主要关注特征融合设计，但缺乏对模态特性和结构特征的综合考量，尤其在噪声抑制和跨模态长程依赖捕获方面存在不足。

Method: 提出LDFE模块，基于拉普拉斯金字塔进行全局-局部分解；全局分支采用GS2E模块，通过双分支架构和状态空间模型(SSM)捕获长程依赖并抑制噪声；局部分支采用LC2E模块，利用空间-通道维度及三重卷积提取细粒度细节；两个模态交替充当主/辅助角色实现双向交互。

Result: 在M3FD、DroneVehicle、LLVIP、FLIR-Aligned、KAIST和VEDAI数据集上，mAP分别超越SOTA方法6.2%、3.7%、4.7%、2.3%、4.1%和2.0%。

Conclusion: LDFE通过全局-局部解耦和跨模态双向交互，有效增强了RGB-IR双流目标检测的性能，证明了同时考虑模态特性和结构特性的融合策略的有效性。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。该论文本身就是遥感相关研究(涉及DroneVehicle、VEDAI等遥感数据集)，可直接应用于遥感多模态目标检测。改进方向：(1)将LDFE模块引入遥感影像的语义分割任务，如建筑/道路提取中的多模态融合；(2)考虑遥感影像中多尺度地物特征，引入多级拉普拉斯金字塔分解以增强对不同尺寸目标的适应性；(3)将GS2E中的状态空间模型替换为更适合遥感长时序数据的时序状态空间模型，用于多时相遥感变化检测。

Abstract (英文): The complementary information between RGB and IR images can significantly enhance object detection performance under extreme conditions. Existing methods prefer dual-stream CNN backbones built upon YOLO for feature extraction and focus on the design of feature fusion. In this paper, we introduce the Laplacian Decoupled Feature Enhancement block (LDFE) to fuse features from different stages of the dual-stream CNN backbone. By design, LDFE simultaneously considers the characteristics of modalities and structures for feature fusion by employing global-local decomposition, denoising, fusion, and reconstruction, sequentially. The LDFE first separates features into global and local components based on Laplacian Pyramid, and then performs denoising and fusion based on Global State Space Enhancement module (GS2E) and Local Convolutional Correlation Enhancement module (LC2E) separately. Specifically, the GS2E conducts a two-branch architecture for the main and auxiliary modalities. It dynamically suppresses noise in the main modality through cross-modal attention derived from the auxiliary modality, while employing a State Space Model to capture long-range dependencies within the global feature representations of the main modality. To obtain bidirectional interaction, the two modalities systematically alternate their main/auxiliary roles. Moreover, the LC2E suppresses noise in local features and leverages spatial and channel dimension along with triple convolution to extract fine-grained details for fusion. These innovative designs achieve a significant performance improvement, with mAP surpassing the SOTA methods 6.2%, 3.7%, 4.7%, 2.3%, 4.1% and 2.0% on M3FD, DroneVehicle, LLVIP, FLIR-Aligned, KAIST and VEDAI datasets,respectively.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract (英文): Multi-query vehicle ReID aims to leverage complementary information from diverse views for robust feature learning. However, current methods suffer from simplistic feature fusion and thus easily ignores some important view information and cross-view relationships. To handle these problems, this work presents a novel approach called Mixture of Enhanced-View Experts (EV-MoE), which enhances the feature representation of each view and efficiently integrate the view-specific enhanced features by MoE, for robust multi-query ReID. In particular, we design a mixture of enhanced-view experts module, which consists of two parts including view-specific feature enhancement sub-Module (VFEM) and dynamic multi-view fusion sub-Module (DMFM). Moreover, we further introduce Multi-view Alignment Loss (MAL), which aligns features through bidirectional crossview contrastive learning and reconstruction constraints, addressing the challenges of consistency between multi-query features and single-image features. In addition, to evaluate multi-query ReID in real-world environments, we collect LCRI-1K, a largescale vehicle ReID dataset with 1,090 identities, 107,805 images, across 23,637 cameras, where each vehicle appears in an average of 67.5 cameras, providing a comprehensive benchmark to test the robustness in complex environments. Extensive experiments demonstrate the robustness of CAFNet in addressing the multiquery vehicle ReID problem. The code is available at https: //github.com/xiaozhen28/CAFNet.

Abstract (英文): Designing functional and aesthetically coherent floor plans requires exploring a vast space of possible room arrangements, a task that quickly becomes overwhelming for human designers. In this paper, we propose GRE-Diff, a controllable and interactive diffusion-based framework that automates the creation and editing of apartment floor plans under user-specified constraints.
  By combining AI-generated suggestions with real-time, human-in-the-loop editing, the system enables users to specify room types, room counts, boundary shapes, and editing operations through LLM-parsed instructions or GUI-based interaction.
  It then generates a diverse set of plausible and well-structured designs for refinement.
  At the core of our approach is Gaussian Room Embedding (GRE), a continuous latent representation that models each room as a spatial Gaussian distribution capturing its location and extent.
  Extensive experiments on the RPLAN dataset show that GRE-Diff produces high-quality, constraint-aware, and editable polygonal layouts, offering a practical step toward bridging AI-driven automation and human creativity in spatial design.

### [16] [EVIS: A Physics-Grounded Event Camera Plugin for NVIDIA Isaac Sim](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08098)
*Linli Shi,Ruijun Zhang,Ziyun Wang*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: EVIS是一个基于物理的事件相机插件，集成于NVIDIA Isaac Sim模拟器中，能够生成高帧率、全标注的事件流，并支持实时生成、传感器噪声模拟和运动模糊，可直接用于预训练事件网络的下游任务。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 事件相机具有微秒级时间分辨率、低延迟和高动态范围的优势，但标注的事件相机数据稀缺且采集成本高，阻碍了基于事件感知和控制的算法开发。

Method: 在NVIDIA Isaac Sim中实现物理基础的事件相机插件，采用逐像素异步参考更新的对数强度对比事件模型，支持从普通RGB相机迁移；提供插值选项，通过双向运动向量扭曲从稀疏关键帧合成中间帧，实现单GPU实时生成；可选传感器噪声和运动模糊以弥合与现实相机的差距。

Result: 生成的事件流可直接用于预训练事件网络的下游任务；支持实时生成；通过传感器噪声和运动模糊选项缩小了仿真与真实数据的差距。

Conclusion: EVIS降低了事件相机数据获取的门槛，加速了事件感知与控制在机器人领域的应用发展。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感领域可借鉴EVIS的物理仿真框架，在模拟器中生成高时间分辨率的事件流数据用于运动目标检测与跟踪；可结合遥感影像的多光谱/高光谱信息扩展事件模型；利用双向运动向量扭曲技术优化遥感影像序列的插值与超分辨率重建；将事件相机的异步采样机制引入遥感变化检测，提升对快速动态场景的响应能力。

Abstract (英文): Event cameras offer microsecond temporal resolution, low latency, and high dynamic range, making them attractive for robotics. However, labeled event-camera data for a specific robot and scene is scarce and expensive to collect, which slows the development of event-based perception and control. We present EVIS: a physics-grounded event camera plugin for NVIDIA Isaac Sim that generates high-rate, fully labeled event streams directly inside a physics simulator. The plugin implements a faithful log-intensity contrast event model with per-pixel asynchronous reference updates; it migrates from a normal RGB camera with few changes and integrates into any Isaac Sim / Isaac Lab scene, inheriting the simulator's physics and frame-perfect ground truth. It is fully configurable, and offers an interpolation option that renders only sparse keyframes and synthesizes the in-between frames through bidirectional motion-vector warping, making real-time generation on a single GPU possible. Optional sensor noise and motion blur further narrow the gap to real cameras. The generated streams are directly usable by pretrained event networks for downstream tasks. Code repository: https://github.com/spikelab-jhu/isaac-sim-event-camera-plugin

### [17] [VSRo-200: A Romanian Visual Speech Recognition Dataset for Studying Supervision and Multimodal Robustness](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08112)
*Iulia-Maria Udrea,Alexandra Diaconu,Bogdan Alexe*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 罗马尼亚语缺乏大规模视觉语音识别数据集，现有数据集主要关注英语等高资源语言。为填补这一空白，推动低资源语言的视觉语音识别研究，作者构建了VSRo-200数据集，并系统研究监督质量、域泛化和多模态融合等关键问题。

Method: 1) 从真实播客视频收集200小时数据，使用微调的罗马尼亚语ASR模型生成伪标签，其中100小时额外进行人工转录。2) 在统一框架下对比人工标注和伪标签的监督质量。3) 构建分布外(OOD)测试集评估域迁移鲁棒性。4) 在噪声条件下评估音视频语音识别(AVSR)的多模态融合效果。5) 在LRRo基准上评估表示迁移学习能力。

Result: 1) 人工标注在固定数据规模下性能更好，但伪标签通过规模扩展可持续提升性能。2) 多模态融合在噪声条件下显著提升鲁棒性，优于纯音频模型。3) 在VSRo-200上学习的表示迁移到LRRo孤立词识别基准，大幅超越此前报告的结果。

Conclusion: VSRo-200为低资源视觉语音识别提供了新的研究平台，有助于研究监督质量、域泛化和多模态融合。伪标签策略在资源有限时是有效替代方案，多模态融合可提升噪声鲁棒性，学到的表示具有良好的迁移能力。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：70%。遥感领域同样面临低资源问题（如特定卫星图像标注稀缺），VSRo-200中伪标签与人工标注的监督质量对比研究方法可直接迁移到遥感图像分类或分割任务中，用于评估伪标签策略的可行性。此外，其域迁移鲁棒性评估方法可用于遥感模型的跨传感器/跨地域泛化测试。噪声条件下的多模态融合策略（唇读+音频）可启发遥感中多模态数据（如SAR+光学）的融合方案。

Abstract (英文): We introduce VSRo-200, the first large-scale dataset for visual speech recognition (lip reading) in Romanian, comprising 200 hours of real-world podcast videos. All samples are annotated with pseudo-labels generated by a fine-tuned Romanian ASR model, while a subset of 100 hours is additionally transcribed by humans, enabling controlled analysis of supervision quality under a unified framework. Building on this dataset, we establish a benchmark for visual speech recognition in low-resource settings. We systematically study the impact of supervision quality, showing that while human annotations provide better performance at fixed data scales, pseudo-labels enable continued improvements through scalability. We further evaluate robustness under domain shift using curated out-of-distribution (OOD) test sets, and analyze audio-visual speech recognition (AVSR) under noisy conditions, where multimodal fusion significantly improves robustness compared to audio-only models. Finally, we demonstrate that representations learned on VSRo-200 transfer effectively to the LRRo benchmark for isolated word recognition, substantially outperforming previously reported results. Overall, VSRo-200 provides a new testbed for studying supervision, domain generalization, and multimodal fusion in low-resource visual speech recognition.

### [18] [Understanding and Mitigating the Video-Action Generalization Gap via Temporal Ratio](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08127)
*Utkarsh A. Mishra,Yongxin Chen,Danfei Xu,Yang Liu,Xi Chen,Jiayuan Mao*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文发现视频生成基础模型在微调为动作模型后会失去组合先验知识，造成"视频-动作泛化差距"。作者引入时序比（TR）作为注意力度量，揭示了模型对未来潜在展开的依赖程度可预测其组合泛化能力，并提出推理时的自适应引导方法，在LIBERO基准和真实世界任务中有效缩小了分布外与分布内组合泛化差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 视频生成基础模型虽具备强大的组合先验，但经过机器人动作数据微调后，世界-动作模型（WAM）和视频-动作模型（VAM）往往丢失这些先验，导致了"视频-动作泛化差距"。目前缺乏对这一差距的系统性理解与有效缓解方法。

Method: 1) 系统评估了VAM的设计空间，证明标准设计无法产生涌现的解释模式；2) 提出时序比（TR）——一种基于注意力机制的度量，衡量动作头依赖未来潜在展开相对于当前帧的程度；3) 基于TR发现，模型对未来预测潜在的结构依赖可预测其组合泛化能力，且TR会随任务阶段自适应波动；4) 提出推理时自适应引导方法，利用TR的内在特征注意力模式，在策略依赖未来展开时动态放大组合视频条件信号。

Result: 在LIBERO基准和真实世界任务上，该方法有效缓解了分布外与分布内组合泛化差距。

Conclusion: 时序比（TR）是预测模型组合泛化能力的关键指标，基于TR的推理时自适应引导能有效弥合视频-动作模型在微调中丢失组合先验的泛化差距。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：75%。该论文提出的时序比（TR）概念可迁移至遥感视频动作理解任务：1) 遥感视频中的时序动作分割可借鉴TR的注意力模式分析，区分规划阶段与精细操作阶段；2) 遥感图像序列的分布外泛化（如不同传感器、不同季节场景）可借鉴自适应引导方法，在模型依赖未来预测时动态增强条件信号；3) 遥感无人机自主导航中，将视频基础模型微调为动作模型时面临的先验丢失问题与本论文高度相似，TR可作为评估模型泛化能力的通用诊断工具。

Abstract (英文): Generative video foundation models exhibit strong compositional priors, yet world-action models (WAMs) and video-action models (VAMs) often lose these priors after finetuning on robotic action data. We refer to this discrepancy as the video-action generalization gap. In this paper, we systematically investigate this gap by evaluating a comprehensive design space of VAMs, demonstrating that standard design choices yield no emergent explanation pattern. To explain this behavior, we introduce the Temporal Ratio (TR), an attention-based measure of how strongly the action head relies on future latent rollouts relative to the anchored current frame. TR has two key properties: first, a model's structural reliance on future-predictive latents, measured via TR, acts as a predictor of its compositional generalization capacity; second, it natively fluctuates based on task phase, shifting attention to future frames during planning and reverting to the present frame for precise manipulation. Finally, based on these findings, we propose an inference-time adaptive guidance method, which exploits this intrinsic feature attention pattern to dynamically amplify compositional video conditioning signals precisely when the policy relies on future rollouts. Evaluated on the LIBERO benchmark and real-world tasks, our approach mitigates the OOD-ID compositional generalization gap. More details: https://umishra.me/temporal-ratio/

</details>

Abstract (英文): The growing applications of facial recognition systems are accompanied by increasingly diverse security threats. Existing datasets lack detailed textual descriptions of forgery cues, leading most prior methods to treat face attack detection primarily as a visual recognition task. In this paper, building upon the large-scale MS-UFAD dataset which contains over 8 million attack images, we enrich each image with a fine-grained textual description of forgery cues. Furthermore, we propose a Dual Alignment Forgery Network(DAF-Net) to better leverage these textual information. Extensive experiments demonstrate that our approach extracts more generalizable and semantically meaningful forgery representations from attack images, outperforming both vision-only methods and approaches based on coarse-grained descriptions.

### [20] [ProsMAE: Multi-Source MAE Pretraining for ISUP Grade Classification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08162)
*Anna Jung,Kyeonghun Kim,Youngung Han,Eunseob Choi,Jiwon Yang,Ken Ying-Kai Liao,Hyuk-Jae Lee,Nam-Joon Kim*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出ProsMAE，一种多源掩码自编码器框架，利用来自PANDA、CAMELYON17和BRACS三个数据集的病理组织切片进行预训练，学习通用的组织病理学表征，然后通过ProsCLS使用冻结编码器和线性分类头进行ISUP分级分类，在PANDA数据集上取得了比普通MAE更高的二次加权kappa（QWK）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 全切片图像（WSI）存在千兆像素尺度、染色变异、扫描差异、组织伪影以及专家标注有限等问题，使得鲁棒模型训练极具挑战。现有方法缺乏对多样化组织形态和采集条件的充分学习。

Method: 提出ProsMAE框架：使用来自PANDA、CAMELYON17和BRACS三个数据集的病理切片组织块进行掩码自编码器预训练，使编码器暴露于多样化的组织形态和采集条件；预训练后的编码器通过ProsCLS方案（冻结编码器+线性分类头）迁移至ISUP分级分类任务。

Result: 在PANDA数据集的特定划分上，ProsMAE的平均验证二次加权kappa（QWK）高于普通MAE的冻结线性探针基线。

Conclusion: 多源预训练有助于提升病理表征学习的性能，但仍需通过重复划分评估进一步验证模型在不同划分组成下的鲁棒性。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感图像与病理切片均面临数据规模大、标注稀缺、采集条件差异大等挑战。具体交叉方案：(1) 将ProsMAE的多源MAE预训练策略迁移至遥感领域，利用多个遥感数据集（如SAT-6、UC Merced、AID等）进行自监督预训练，学习通用的遥感特征表征；(2) 采用类似的冻结编码器+线性分类头迁移方案，用于遥感场景分类、地物分割等下游任务；(3) 可借鉴病理切片中处理染色变异的方法来处理遥感图像中因传感器差异、光照条件、季节变化等引起的域偏移问题。

Abstract (英文): Whole slide images (WSIs) provide rich diagnostic information for computational pathology, but their gigapixel scale, stain variation, scanner differences, tissue artifacts, and limited expert annotation make robust model training challenging. This paper presents a multi-source Masked Autoencoder (MAE) framework, named ProsMAE, for histopathology representation learning. Tiles from Prostate cANcer graDe Assessment (PANDA), CAncer MEtastases in LYmph nOdes challeNge 2017 (CAMELYON17), and BReAst Carcinoma Subtyping (BRACS) are used for ProsMAE pretraining to expose the encoder to diverse tissue morphology and acquisition conditions. The learned encoder is transferred for International Society of Urological Pathology (ISUP) grade classification through ProsCLS, using a frozen encoder and a linear classification head. ProsMAE achieved a higher mean validation quadratic weighted kappa (QWK) than the vanilla MAE frozen linear-probe baseline under the evaluated disjoint PANDA split. Repeated-split evaluation remains necessary to further establish robustness across split compositions.

### [21] [Continual Test-Time Adaptation in Computer Vision: Methods, Benchmarks, and Future Directions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08164)
*Sarthak Kumar Maharana,Shambhavi Mishra,Yunbei Zhang,Shuaicheng Niu,Taki Hasan Rafi,Jihun Hamm,Marco Pedersoli,Jose Dolz,Yunhui Guo*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文系统综述了持续测试时适应（CTTA）问题，正式定义了问题、分析了领域漂移模式，并提出了包含三类方法（优化策略、参数高效方法、架构方法）的分层分类体系，总结了现有基准和实验结果，并讨论了未来研究方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 深度神经网络在训练和测试数据分布一致时表现优异，但实际部署中数据分布持续变化。CTTA旨在解决这一挑战：在无源数据和无标签目标的情况下，在线适应预训练模型到非平稳目标分布，同时缓解灾难性遗忘和错误累积两个关键问题。

Method: 本文是一篇综述论文，采用的方法包括：(1) 形式化定义CTTA问题；(2) 分析多种持续领域漂移模式及评估协议；(3) 提出分层分类体系，将现有方法归纳为三类：优化策略（熵最小化、伪标签、参数恢复）、参数高效方法（归一化层适应、自适应参数选择）和架构方法（师生框架、适配器、视觉提示、掩码建模）；(4) 系统比较各方法在标准基准上的实验结果。

Result: 提供了CTTA领域的系统性分类和比较基准，总结了各类代表性方法在标准评估设置下的实验结果，指出了当前方法的局限性。

Conclusion: 讨论了现有方法的局限性，并指出了未来研究方向，包括基础模型适应和黑盒系统的适应，为持续测试时适应的鲁棒性研究提供了路线图。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感领域常面临多时相、多传感器、不同气候/光照条件带来的持续数据分布漂移（如不同季节的遥感影像、不同卫星传感器的成像差异），CTTA方法可直接应用于：(1) 遥感图像分类中的在线域适应，如卫星影像随时间演变的土地覆盖分类；(2) 遥感目标检测中的持续环境适应，如不同天气条件下的车辆检测；(3) 结合遥感特有的物理约束（如地物光谱一致性）改进伪标签质量；(4) 利用遥感多模态数据（SAR+光学）设计参数高效的适应策略，降低计算开销。

Abstract (英文): Deep neural nets achieve remarkable performance when training and test data share the same distribution, but this assumption frequently breaks in real-world deployment, where data undergoes continual distributional shifts. Continual Test-Time Adaptation (CTTA) addresses this challenge by adapting pretrained models to non-stationary target distributions on-the-fly, without access to source data or labeled targets, while mitigating two critical failure modes: catastrophic forgetting of source knowledge and error accumulation from noisy pseudo-labels over extended time horizons. In this comprehensive survey, we formally define the CTTA problem, analyze the diverse continual domain shift patterns that characterize different evaluation protocols, and propose a hierarchical taxonomy that categorizes existing methods into three families: optimization-based strategies (entropy minimization, pseudo-labeling, parameter restoration), parameter-efficient methods (normalization layer adaptation, adaptive parameter selection), and architecture-based approaches (teacher-student frameworks, adapters, visual prompting, masked modeling). We systematically review representative methods within each category and present comparative benchmarks and experimental results across standard evaluation settings. Finally, we discuss limitations of current approaches and highlight emerging research directions, including adaptation of foundation models and black-box systems, providing a roadmap for future research in robust continual test-time adaptation. We encourage visiting our repository at [https://github.com/sarthaxxxxx/Awesome-Continual-Test-Time-Adaptation](https://github.com/sarthaxxxxx/Awesome-Continual-Test-Time-Adaptation)

### [22] [Attention-Based Segmentation of WMHs and Differentiation of Vascular vs. Demyelinating Lesions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08171)
*Aina Tur-Serrano,Gabriel Moyà-Alcover,Francisco J. Perales López*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出结合注意力机制分割（BAM/CBAM、Attention U-Net）与形态学特征分类的方法，用于区分血管性和脱髓鞘性白质高信号（WMHs）。在五个公开数据集上验证了该方法的可行性，但需更大临床队列进一步验证。

Method: 采用注意力机制分割模型（BAM、CBAM、Attention U-Net），结合patch学习与2.5D策略增强病灶检测；分割后提取病灶掩膜的形态学特征，用于WMHs病因分类。

Result: 在五个公开数据集上实验表明，注意力机制分割与特征驱动分类相结合的方法在区分血管性和脱髓鞘性白质病变方面表现出良好效果。

Abstract (英文): White Matter Hyperintensities (WMHs) are commonly observed in brain Magnetic Resonance Imaging (MRI) scans. They are associated with various neurological conditions, including vascular and inflammatory demyelinating diseases. Despite differing in etiology, WMHs from these conditions often appear similar on Fluid Attenuated Inversion Recovery (FLAIR) images. This similarity makes differential diagnosis challenging. In this work, we highlight the potential of combining attention-based segmentation with feature-driven classification. This approach supports more accurate and efficient classification between vascular and demyelinating white matter pathologies. For segmentation, we evaluate the effectiveness of attention mechanisms, specifically the Bottleneck Attention Module (BAM) and the Convolutional Block Attention Module (CBAM). We also test different architectures, particularly Attention U-Net. In addition, we explore advanced training strategies, such as patch-based learning and a 2.5D approach, to enhance lesion detection. After segmentation, we extract morphological features from the lesion masks. We then use them to classify WMHs based on their underlying cause. Our experiments utilize five publicly available datasets with diverse imaging protocols to promote model generalizability, despite limited sample sizes. The results suggest that attention-based segmentation and feature-driven classification offer a promising direction for discriminating vascular and demyelinating white matter lesions. Further validation in larger clinical cohorts is still needed.

### [23] [LEEVLA: Seeing What Matters in Latent Environment Evolution for Vision-Language-Action](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08182)
*Qi Lyu,Baicheng Liu,Xudong Wang,Jiahua Dong,Lianqing Liu,Zhi Han*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: LEEVLA是一种视觉-语言-动作（VLA）架构，通过引入漂移引导动态优先化（DGDP）和结构化特征流生成（SFFG）两个模块，解决现有VLA模型在复杂动态场景中无法突出任务关键证据和建模潜在因素的问题。DGDP结合动态位置优先化和语义漂移引导来定位重要区域，SFFG通过原型到外围预测和互邻域对比损失建模潜在空间特征演化。实验表明该方法在VLA基准上优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有VLA模型将所有视觉token均匀对待，且依赖人工选择因素进行推理，缺乏突出任务关键证据的机制，也无法建模潜在因素，导致在复杂动态场景中表现不佳。

Method: 提出LEEVLA架构，包含两个核心模块：1）漂移引导动态优先化（DGDP），由动态位置优先化（DPP）和语义漂移引导（SDG）组成，用于定位任务相关的重要区域；2）结构化特征流生成（SFFG），通过原型到外围（P2P）预测和互邻域对比（MC）损失，建模优先化特征在潜在空间中的演化过程，保持拓扑一致性。两者构成"where-how"训练框架。

Result: 在VLA基准测试上的大量实验表明，LEEVLA持续优于先前方法，验证了显式任务证据引导和结构化潜在推理对可扩展VLA的重要性。

Conclusion: 显式的任务证据引导和结构化的潜在空间推理对于构建可扩展的VLA模型至关重要，LEEVLA通过"where-how"框架有效解决了现有方法的局限性。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感领域存在类似挑战——遥感图像中目标区域（如舰船、建筑物变化区域）往往只占图像很小比例，现有模型也常对所有像素均匀处理。LEEVLA的DGDP模块可迁移至遥感目标检测和变化检测任务，通过语义漂移引导定位感兴趣区域；SFFG可应用于遥感时序分析，建模地物特征的潜在演化规律。具体方案：将LEEVLA的"where-how"框架适配到遥感图像-文本-行动（如卫星姿态调整、无人机导航）的多模态控制场景，或用于遥感视觉问答中突出关键地理特征区域。

Abstract (英文): Vision-language-action (VLA) models aim to map multimodal inputs to robot actions. However, most existing approaches struggle to cover complex dynamic scenarios due to treating all visual tokens uniformly and reasoning with human-selected factors, which lack mechanisms to emphasize task-critical evidence and ignore underlying factors. To address this issue, we propose LEEVLA, a VLA architecture for seeing what matters in Latent Environment Evolution that explicitly guides the model toward informative regions while preserving the structured evolution of latent world representations. To identify salient and instruction-relevant regions, we introduce drift-guided dynamic prioritization (DGDP), which combines dynamic position prioritization (DPP) with semantic drift guidance (SDG) to guide the VLA agent where to attend during training. On top of this, we introduce structured feature flow generation (SFFG), which models how these prioritized features should evolve in latent space via prototype-to-periphery (P2P) prediction, and a mutual-neighborhood contrastive (MC) loss to maintain topological consistency among neighborhoods. Together, DGDP and SFFG form a task-aware "where-how" training framework. Extensive experiments on VLA benchmarks show that LEEVLA consistently outperforms prior methods, confirming that explicit task-evidence guidance and structured latent reasoning are both crucial for scalable VLA. Our code is available at https://github.com/LyuQi127/LEEVLA.

</details>


### [24] [Leveraging Color Naming for Image Enhancement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08185)
*David Serrano-Lozano,Luis Herranz,Michael S. Brown,Javier Vazquez-Corral*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: NamedCurves+ 是一种基于颜色命名概念的图像增强方法，通过为每种命名颜色学习独立的色调曲线，并结合 Transformer 捕捉空间依赖，实现了可解释且可交互的图像润饰。在图像润饰、色调映射和曝光校正任务上超越了现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有深度学习方法在图像增强中存在两大问题：(1) 可解释性差，(2) 缺乏适合用户调整的参数化方式。作者希望通过引入颜色命名概念来解决这些问题，使模型既具备可解释性又支持用户交互。

Method: 提出 NamedCurves+ 框架：(1) 基于颜色命名概念，将图像分解为若干通用命名颜色；(2) 为每种命名颜色学习独立的色调曲线进行全局调整；(3) 引入 Transformer 模块捕捉空间依赖关系，实现上下文感知的局部编辑；(4) 支持用户对各色调曲线进行独立调整以个性化结果。

Result: 在图像润饰、色调映射和曝光校正等任务上的大量实验表明，NamedCurves+ 优于现有最先进方法。

Conclusion: NamedCurves+ 是一种兼具可解释性和交互性的图像增强方法，色调曲线明确展示了每种命名颜色对增强效果的贡献，用户可自定义润饰过程以获得符合个人偏好的结果。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。具体方案：(1) 遥感图像通常包含地物类型与颜色强相关（植被绿色、水体蓝色、裸土棕色等），NamedCurves+ 的颜色命名机制可直接对应遥感地物类别，实现面向类的光谱调整；(2) 将 Transformer 的空间依赖捕捉能力用于遥感图像中复杂地物边界的上下文感知增强；(3) 可扩展到多光谱/高光谱波段，将颜色命名替换为波段命名或地物类型命名，实现可解释的光谱曲线调整；(4) 用户交互特性可让遥感专家针对特定区域或地物类型微调增强参数。

Abstract (英文): Enhancing images to make them visually appealing is a persistent challenge in computer vision. Many deep-learning methods train models on paired datasets to replicate expert editing styles. However, these approaches struggle with two key issues: (1) interpretability and (2) a parametrization suitable for user adjustments. To address these challenges, we present NamedCurves+, an approach inspired by the concept of Color Naming, a universal set of familiar colors widely used in software tools for intuitive editing. Our method integrates color names into a learning-based framework, enabling global adjustments for each named color through tone curves. To address local image variations, we incorporate a transformer block that captures spatial dependencies, enabling context-aware edits across the image. NamedCurves+ enhances the retouching process's interpretability and supports user interaction, allowing flexible modifications of individual tone curves to refine the retouched image according to personal preferences. Extensive experiments on tasks such as image retouching, tone mapping, and exposure correction demonstrate that NamedCurves+ outperforms state-of-the-art methods. Notably, our approach is both explainable, as the tone curves explicitly represent how each color name contributes to the enhancement, and interactive, allowing users to customize the retouching process and achieve results tailored to their liking.

### [25] [Dual-Correlation Hypergraph Network for Unaligned RGBT Video Object Detection and A Large-scale Benchmark](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08191)
*Qishun Wang,Yapeng Li,Bin Luo,Zhengzheng Tu,Chenglong Li*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种双相关超图网络（DHNet），通过设计补丁空间对齐模块和双超图融合模块来解决RGB-Thermal视频目标检测中的空间不对齐问题，同时构建了包含1000个视频序列的大规模基准数据集DVT-VOD1000，实验证明了该方法的最优性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: RGB-Thermal视频目标检测中，RGB和热红外图像对之间存在空间不对齐问题，限制了多模态融合的性能。

Method: 提出DHNet，包含Patch-based Spatial Alignment Module (PSAM)进行局部区域级的多模态特征对齐，以及Dual Hypergraph Fusion Module (DHFM)构建时序超图和跨模态超图进行双相关学习；同时构建了大规模数据集DVT-VOD1000。

Result: 在VT-VOD50和自建的DVT-VOD1000数据集上，DHNet达到了最先进的检测精度。

Abstract (英文): RGB-Thermal (RGBT) Video Object Detection (VOD) has gained significant traction due to its ability to overcome the limitations of conventional RGB-based VOD under challenging conditions. However, spatial misalignment commonly exists between RGBT image pairs. To address this, we propose a Dual-Correlation Hypergraph Network (DHNet) that captures high-dimensional complementary information by explicitly modeling two types of correlations: temporal correlation across consecutive frames and spatial correlation from cross-modal features. Specifically, we first design a Patch-based Spatial Alignment Module (PSAM) to sequentially align the multimodal features at the local region level. Subsequently, we introduce a Dual Hypergraph Fusion Module (DHFM), which constructs separate temporal and multimodal hypergraphs to enhance object discriminability through dual-correlation learning. Furthermore, the field currently lacks a large-scale, scene-diverse benchmark dataset for comprehensive evaluation. The dataset covers diverse scenarios, including campuses, parks, transportation, rural areas, night scenes, rain, and snow. Comprehensive experiments on VT-VOD50 and our DVT-VOD1000 demonstrate that DHNet achieves state-of-the-art detection accuracy. The dataset and source code will be made publicly available on https://github.com/tzz-ahu/ to support academic research.

### [26] [Dive Into the Implicit Biases of Low-rank Vision-language Alignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08194)
*Mingjia Shi,Shuo Wang,Xiaobo Wang,Sifan Zhou,Kai Wang,Tianyu Fu,Chenxu Zhao,Anyang Su,Ping Jiang,Minghui Wu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文挑战了视觉-语言对齐阶段必须进行全参数更新的传统观点，发现使用低秩适应（Low-Rank Adaptation）对LLM进行对齐不仅降低了计算成本，还在多数基准上优于全参数对齐。实验表明低秩对齐能减少幻觉、保持视觉特征的线性可分离性（LS-curse），并维持更具结构稳定性的视觉表征。理论上证明了低秩对齐倾向于选择梯度平坦的参数子空间和抗扰动的特征子空间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 挑战视觉-语言对齐阶段必须全参数更新的传统观点，探究低秩适应在该阶段的应用效果及其背后的隐式偏置机制。

Method: 在视觉-语言对齐阶段对LLM应用低秩适应（LoRA），通过系统性实验对比低秩对齐与全参数对齐的性能差异，并从经验、几何和理论三个层面分析低秩对齐的隐式偏置：经验上分析幻觉行为和线性可分离性；几何上分析视觉表征的同质性和结构稳定性；理论上建立两个定理证明低秩对齐偏好梯度平坦的参数子空间和抗扰动的特征子空间。

Result: 低秩对齐在多数基准上优于全参数对齐，能减少幻觉行为、保持视觉特征线性可分离性（避免LS-curse），并产生更均匀且结构稳定的视觉表征。覆盖100多种对齐配置的消融实验验证了方法的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 低秩对齐是一种优于全参数对齐的视觉-语言对齐范式，其背后的隐式偏置——偏好平坦梯度和抗扰动特征子空间——为结构保持行为提供了理论解释。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：90%。遥感领域存在大量视觉-语言对齐任务（如遥感图像描述、遥感视觉问答），且遥感图像具有多尺度、多模态、标注稀缺等特点。改进方案：(1) 将低秩对齐应用于遥感大模型的对齐阶段，在减少计算开销的同时保持遥感图像独特的空间和光谱特征；(2) 利用低秩对齐的"保守"偏置，减少遥感大模型在复杂场景下的幻觉问题（如错误识别地物类型）；(3) 针对遥感图像的多光谱/高光谱特性，探索低秩对齐对光谱特征线性可分离性的保持效果，提升地物分类和变化检测的准确性。

Abstract (英文): Vision-language alignment, the stage that bridges pretrained vision encoders and large language models, is widely treated as a form of pretraining requiring full-parameter updates. We challenge this view and investigate what happens when low-rank adaptation is applied to the LLM during this stage instead. We find that low-rank alignment not only reduces computational costs but also outperforms full-parameter alignment on most benchmarks. To understand this phenomenon, we systematically characterize the implicit biases introduced by low-rank adaptation during alignment. Empirically, we find that low-rank alignment shifts model behavior from hallucinatory to conservative and preserves per-token linear separability of visual features that full-parameter alignment disrupts, a phenomenon we term LS-curse. Geometrically, low rank aligned models exhibit more homogeneous and structurally stable visual representations, maintaining modality-specific knowledge rather than prematurely fusing entity-level semantics. Theoretically, we establish two theorems showing that low-rank alignment induces preferences for parameter subspaces with flat gradients and feature subspaces robust to perturbations, providing a principled explanation for the observed structure-preserving behavior. Extensive experiments cover ablation over 100 alignment configurations, three families of low-rank operators, and various rank, encoder, and other settings.

</details>


### [27] [Unpaired Joint Distribution Modeling via Multi-Scale Image Representations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08198)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 在温和假设下建立了分布近似误差的上界；揭示了表示学习中域一致性与信息保留之间的权衡；MSR相比现有方法实现了更有利的权衡。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感领域常面临多模态数据（如光学与SAR影像）的联合分布学习问题，LUD-MSR框架可直接应用于异源遥感图像的联合建模。具体方案：(1) 将不同遥感传感器获取的影像视为边缘观测，利用MSR提取粗尺度地物结构共性（如地形轮廓），抑制传感器特有的噪声和纹理差异；(2) 用于遥感图像融合（如全色与多光谱融合）或跨模态变化检测；(3) 在冷冻电镜去噪的启发下，可应用于遥感图像去噪，特别是雷达影像的斑点噪声抑制。

Abstract (英文): This paper studies the problem of learning a joint distribution from marginal observations, which is inherently ill-posed due to the ambiguity of feasible couplings. We propose LUD-MSR, a latent-variable probabilistic framework that models the joint distribution via auxiliary representations and optimizes evidence lower bounds using only marginal data. Under mild assumptions, we establish an upper bound on the distribution approximation error. This analysis reveals a trade-off in representation learning between domain consistency and information preservation. To address this trade-off, we introduce a Multi-Scale image Representation (MSR) mapping that exploits structural similarity at coarse scales while suppressing domain-specific variations. We show that MSR achieves a more favorable balance of this trade-off compared to existing approaches. Experiments on real-world denoising benchmarks, including cryo-electron microscopy (cryo-EM), demonstrate the effectiveness of the proposed framework.

### [28] [TMI: Text-to-Image Meets Image-to-Image for Complementary Data Synthesis to Boost Long-Tailed Instance Segmentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08201)
*Hyeonseop Song,Seokhun Choi,Hoseok Do*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出一种混合管道TMI，结合文本到图像（T2I）生成与上下文感知的图像到图像（I2I）编辑，用于大规模词汇实例分割。T2I分支提供类别和场景多样性，教师-学生机制确保标签可靠性；I2I编辑器VRAIN将高置信度实例插入语义合适位置，实现针对性增强。在LVIS上，总体AP提升+4.0，稀有类AP提升+9.5。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大规模词汇实例分割受长尾类别分布和细粒度类间模糊性限制。现有数据合成方法存在互补局限：T2I方法继承噪声伪标签且在稀有类上表现差，而复制粘贴方法损害上下文真实性。

Method: 提出混合管道TMI：(1) T2I分支生成多样化场景，配合教师-学生机制过滤伪标签，仅保留提示指定的类别；(2) VRAIN（I2I编辑器）将高置信度实例插入野外场景中的语义合适位置，实现语义一致且视觉自然的编辑，减少域差距并实现针对性增强。

Result: 在LVIS基准上，总体AP提升+4.0点，稀有类AP提升+9.5点，且能随骨干网络容量有效扩展。

Conclusion: 混合T2I和I2I的管道能有效解决长尾分布和细粒度模糊性问题，在实例分割任务上取得显著提升。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感影像中地物类别同样存在长尾分布（如罕见地物）和类间模糊（如不同植被类型）。具体方案：(1) T2I分支可生成遥感场景多样性（如不同季节、光照下的罕见地物），教师-学生机制过滤伪标签；(2) VRAIN可将高置信度遥感目标实例（如特定车辆、建筑物）插入语义合理的遥感场景中（如将消防车插入停车场），实现针对性增强稀有遥感类别。需调整：骨干网络替换为遥感专用结构，场景编辑需考虑地理空间一致性。

Abstract (英文): Large-vocabulary instance segmentation is constrained by long-tailed category distributions and fine-grained inter-class ambiguity. While data synthesis offers a promising alternative, current paradigms have complementary limitations: text-to-image (T2I) methods inherit noisy pseudo-labels and struggle on rare classes, whereas copy-paste methods compromise contextual realism. To address these issues, we propose a hybrid pipeline coupling T2I generation with context-aware image-to-image (I2I) editing. The T2I branch provides broad category and scene diversity, while a teacher-student scheme ensures label reliability by selectively retaining only prompt-specified categories. To strengthen supervision for rare classes, we introduce VRAIN (Verified Rare-class Augmentation via INstructed editing), a novel I2I editor. VRAIN inserts high-confidence instances at semantically appropriate locations within in-the-wild scenes, yielding semantically coherent and visually natural edits that reduce domain gaps and enable targeted augmentation. On the LVIS benchmark, our method surpasses existing baselines, improving overall AP by up to +4.0 points and rare-class AP by up to +9.5 points, while scaling effectively with backbone capacity. Our project page is available at https://seokhunchoi.github.io/TMI

### [29] [Metrics or Mirage? An Audit of Evaluation Inconsistencies in Colonoscopy Polyp Segmentation Benchmarks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08203)
*Aisha Urooj,Zain Ul Abdien,Neelu Madan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文系统审计了2015-2026年间27篇结肠镜息肉分割论文，发现三个结构性问题：多数论文遗漏Hausdorff距离指标、存在至少五种互不兼容的训练/测试分割协议、缺乏统计显著性检验。通过重新评估5个代表性模型，证明这些缺陷会导致性能评估失真，并提出了五点评分报告清单（PSRC）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 结肠镜息肉分割领域虽频繁在公开基准上报告性能进展，但这些进展的真实性难以验证。现有评估体系存在系统性缺陷，需要对其进行彻底审计并推动改进。

Method: 对27篇论文（2015-2026年）进行系统性审计，检查三个维度：是否使用Hausdorff距离、训练/测试分割协议的一致性、是否进行统计显著性检验。随后在三种受控协议下使用统一评分器重新评估五个代表性模型。

Result: 25/27篇论文遗漏Hausdorff距离；至少五种不兼容的协议共存于Kvasir-SEG和CVC-ClinicDB两个数据集上；26/27篇论文未做统计显著性检验。重新评估发现：单一指标掩盖了边界和召回率缺陷；"最佳"模型随指标选择而变化；近并列排名在随机分割下逆转。

Conclusion: 结肠镜息肉分割领域的评估体系存在严重结构性问题，通用度量指南（Metrics Reloaded）未能触及该子社区。作者提出五点评分报告清单（PSRC）作为轻量级、领域适配的纠正方案。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：90%。该论文揭示的评估体系问题在遥感图像分割领域同样普遍存在。具体交叉方案：（1）将Hausdorff距离引入遥感语义分割（如建筑物轮廓、道路边界提取），作为边缘精度的标准评估指标；（2）检查遥感领域常用数据集（如ISPRS、DeepGlobe、LoveDA）的train/test分割协议一致性，建立统一协议标准；（3）在遥感分割论文中强制引入统计显著性检验（如配对t检验或McNemar检验），避免仅凭Dice/mIoU排名下定论；（4）仿照PSRC为遥感分割制定领域特定报告清单，涵盖边缘指标、协议声明、不确定性量化等。

Abstract (英文): Progress in colonoscopy polyp segmentation is routinely reported through leaderboard comparisons on a small set of public benchmarks. We argue that this apparent progress is difficult to verify: a systematic audit of \textbf{27 papers} published between 2015 and 2026 reveals three structural problems in how the community evaluates models. \textbf{First}, 25 of 27 papers \textit{omit the Hausdorff distance}. Hausdorff distance is a boundary-accuracy metric with direct clinical relevance for detecting flat or small polyps, and is a standard in radiotherapy segmentation. \textbf{Second}, at least five \textit{incompatible train/test split protocols} co-exist across papers reporting results on the same two datasets (Kvasir-SEG and CVC-ClinicDB), making published Dice scores non-comparable even when they appear in the same leaderboard column. \textbf{Third}, 26 of 27 papers make \textit{performance claims without any statistical significance test}. Strikingly, four papers published \emph{after} the Metrics Reloaded framework~\cite{metricsreloaded2024} (Maier-Hein et al., \textit{Nature Methods} 2024) perpetuate these same problems, suggesting that general-purpose metric guidance has not yet reached the colonoscopy sub-community. To show these problems are not merely cosmetic, we re-evaluate five representative models under three controlled protocols with a single uniform scorer, and find that the reported metric conceals large boundary and recall failures, that the ``best'' model changes with the metric, and that near-tied rankings reverse across random splits. We propose a five-point \textbf{Polyp Segmentation Reporting Checklist}~(PSRC) as a lightweight, domain-adapted corrective.

Abstract (英文): The privacy requirements of medical data and its substantial variations across organs and modalities hinder the clinical implementation of medical AI. Federated learning (FL) is a feasible approach to overcome these challenges. Due to the continuous emergence of FL algorithms and the highly heterogeneous nature of medical data, objectively evaluating their performance in real-world clinical settings remains difficult. Therefore, a comprehensive federated medical imaging benchmark, serving as a unified evaluation standard, is crucial for advancing the technology toward reliable clinical application. Existing federated medical imaging benchmarks have not yet adequately incorporated state-of-the-art algorithms, are limited to data from single organs or modalities, and overly emphasize model accuracy, making it difficult to comprehensively assess the overall efficacy of FL in real-world medical environments. To address these challenges, we developed the MobenFL benchmark. This benchmark integrates 20 cutting-edge FL algorithms and 22 medical imaging datasets, covering 12 critical organs across the human body, surpassing existing benchmark in breadth. In terms of evaluation dimensions, MobenFL not only assesses performance but also systematically incorporates key metrics such as algorithmic efficiency and privacy protection capabilities. Additionally, it conducts specialized evaluations for complex real-world clinical scenarios involving different diseases, devices, and imaging modalities, thereby providing a comprehensive and in-depth evaluation framework for the clinical application of FL in the medical field.

### [31] [LUMI: Tokenizer-Agnostic LLM-Based Lossless Image Compression](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08221)
*Chris Xing Tian,Chengkai Wu,Ziyu Wang,Rongqun Lin,Kecheng Chen,Xiandong Meng,Haoliang Li,Shiqi Wang,Siwei Ma*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: LUMI提出了一种与分词器无关的无损图像压缩框架，通过像素嵌入模块将原始像素映射到冻结LLM的连续嵌入空间，仅训练少量适配模块，在多个LLM骨干和图像领域上实现了竞争性的压缩性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于LLM的无损图像压缩方法将像素值通过分词器转换为文本token，导致压缩性能受限于特定分词器的行为、词汇表以及模型家族，缺乏统一性和跨模型泛化能力。

Method: LUMI包含三个核心设计：1) 像素嵌入模块，将原始像素强度和通道信息映射到LLM的连续嵌入空间；2) 块内位置编码，保留二维空间结构；3) 256路预测头，输出像素字母表上的概率分布。仅训练像素嵌入、位置编码、软前缀参数和预测头，LLM骨干冻结。

Result: 在自然图像、医学图像和遥感图像基准上，使用LLaMA、Qwen和Gemma骨干，LUMI提供了跨分词器家族的统一接口，取得了有竞争力的压缩率，并在跨领域鲁棒性上优于基于分词器的LLM压缩基线。

Conclusion: LLM-based无损图像压缩应被视为冻结基础模型在像素空间上的适配问题，而非依赖于特定分词器的语言符号建模问题。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。遥感图像通常具有高动态范围、多光谱通道和复杂纹理，LUMI的像素嵌入可直接扩展到多光谱/高光谱遥感数据的无损压缩；其跨领域鲁棒性特别适合遥感中不同传感器、不同分辨率的图像统一编码；可进一步引入波段间相关性建模改进压缩效率。

Abstract (英文): Large language model (LLM)-based lossless image compression methods typically represent pixel data through the native text interface of a pretrained model, converting pixel values into token sequences that the LLM processes through its vocabulary head. This design shows that pretrained language models can provide probability estimates for image coding, but it also couples compression to tokenizer behavior, vocabulary-specific numeric tokens, and model-family-specific adaptation. In this paper, we present LUMI (LLM-based Unified Model-agnostic lossless Image compression), a tokenizer-agnostic framework for lossless RGB image compression with frozen LLM backbones. LUMI replaces pixel-as-text tokenization with a pixel embedding module that maps raw intensity and channel information into the continuous embedding space of the LLM. It further introduces intra-patch position encoding to retain two-dimensional spatial structure after flattening, and uses a 256-way prediction head to produce probabilities over the native pixel alphabet. Only the pixel embedding, position encoding, soft-prefix parameters, and prediction head are trained, while the LLM backbone remains fixed. Experiments on natural, medical, and remote-sensing image benchmarks with LLaMA, Qwen, and Gemma backbones show that LUMI provides a unified interface across tokenizer families, achieves competitive compression rates, and improves cross-domain robustness over tokenizer-based LLM compression baselines. These results formulate LLM-based lossless image compression as pixel-space adaptation of frozen foundation models rather than tokenizer-specific language-symbol modeling.

### [32] [Multimodal 3D LUT Generation via StatLUT with Statistical Features for Photorealistic Style Transfer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08227)
*Yifan Wang,Zhixiang Hao,Yu Wang,Congchao Zhu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: StatLUT提出了一种多模态框架，通过Lab-Extractor解耦颜色与结构、MR-Mapper生成拓扑平滑的3D LUT、H-Diffuser实现文本驱动调色，在光真实感风格迁移任务上显著超越现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有深度学习PST方法存在三个瓶颈：1) 预训练编码器导致语义纠缠，产生空间扭曲；2) 像素级映射忽略色域拓扑，引发色彩带状失真；3) 缺乏直观的文本驱动多模态控制能力。

Method: 1) Lab-Extractor：绕过传统编码器，提取与空间无关的统计特征，从根本上解耦颜色分布与结构语义；2) MR-Mapper：将3D LUT生成建模为基于Transformer的Seq2Seq翻译任务，预测拓扑平滑的3D LUT；3) H-Diffuser：轻量级Diffusion Transformer，从自然语言提示直接合成统计特征，实现文本驱动的色彩调整。

Result: 在标准基准测试上，StatLUT在视觉质量和量化指标上均显著优于最先进方法。

Conclusion: StatLUT为多模态光真实感风格迁移开辟了一种高鲁棒性、高灵活性的新范式。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感图像中的颜色与结构解耦需求与PST高度契合：1) 可直接应用Lab-Extractor解耦遥感影像的地物光谱信息与空间纹理，减少因语义纠缠导致的分类/分割伪影；2) MR-Mapper可用于遥感图像的色彩归一化（如多时相影像辐射校正），生成拓扑平滑的映射表以消除色阶断层；3) H-Diffuser可扩展为基于文本描述（如"增强植被红光波段"）的遥感影像风格迁移与增强工具，实现可解释的遥感数据可视化。

Abstract (英文): Photorealistic Style Transfer (PST) aims to transfer the color and tonal style of a reference to a content image while strictly preserving its structural integrity. However, existing deep learning-based methods inherently suffer from semantic entanglement caused by pre-trained image encoders, leading to unnatural spatial distortions. Moreover, current pixel-level mapping paradigms often ignore color gamut topology, resulting in color banding, while also lacking the multimodal capability for intuitive text-driven control. To address these bottlenecks, we propose StatLUT, an innovative multimodal framework for 3D LUT generation. First, we bypass traditional encoders and introduce a Lab-Extractor to derive spatially-agnostic statistical features, fundamentally decoupling color distributions from structural semantics to ensure artifact-free rendering. Second, we formulate LUT generation as a Transformer-based Seq2Seq translation task, utilizing a Multi-dimensional Residual Mapper (MR-Mapper) to predict topologically smooth 3D LUTs. Finally, to break the single-modal barrier, we propose the H-Diffuser, a lightweight Diffusion Transformer that directly synthesizes statistical features from natural language prompts, enabling flexible text-driven color grading. Extensive experiments on standard benchmarks demonstrate that StatLUT significantly outperforms state-of-the-art methods in both visual quality and quantitative metrics, pioneering a highly robust and flexible paradigm for multimodal photorealistic style transfer.

</details>


### [33] [TVTA: Trajectory-Aware Viseme-Guided Temporal Aggregation for Event-Based Lip Reading](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08236)
*Jingrong Zheng,Hongwei Ren,Xiangqian Wu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出一种时间增强的事件驱动唇读框架，包含轨迹感知差分聚合（TDA）、视位引导聚合（VGA）和EMA教师-学生训练策略，在DVS-Lip基准上验证了有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有事件驱动唇读方法通常在充分时序建模前进行空间压缩，抑制了区分相似唇动所需的关键稀疏局部运动轨迹；且多数方法仅在词汇分类层面优化时序表征，底层发音结构约束不足。

Method: 1) 轨迹感知差分聚合（TDA）：在空间聚合前对各空间位置进行局部时序建模；2) 视位引导聚合（VGA）：由CTC解码器和视位引导门控聚合分支组成的统一时序模块，注入视位感知序列监督；3) EMA教师-学生训练策略：增强对强事件扰动的鲁棒性。

Result: 在DVS-Lip基准上验证了所提设计的有效性，消融实验证实了TDA、VGA和教师-学生一致性的贡献。定性解码结果表明CTC时序建模能从事件流中学习到有意义的视位感知结构。

Conclusion: 本文提出的时间增强框架通过局部时序建模、视位监督和鲁棒训练策略，有效提升了事件驱动唇读的性能，并证明了从事件流中学习视位感知结构的可行性。

Abstract (英文): Event-based lip reading has recently emerged as a promising direction for visual speech recognition, benefiting from the high temporal resolution and motion sensitivity of event cameras. However, existing methods typically perform spatial compression before sufficient temporal modeling, which may suppress sparse and localized motion trajectories that are crucial for distinguishing similar lip movements. Moreover, most current approaches optimize temporal representations mainly at the word-classification level, leaving the underlying articulatory structure weakly constrained. To address these limitations, we propose a temporally enhanced framework for event-based lip reading. First, we introduce Trajectory-Aware Differential Aggregation (TDA), which performs local temporal modeling at each spatial location before adaptive spatial aggregation. Second, we propose Viseme-Guided Aggregation (VGA), a unified temporal module composed of a CTC decoder and a viseme-guided gated aggregation branch, which injects viseme-aware sequence supervision and improves final temporal aggregation for word recognition. Third, we incorporate an EMA teacher--student training strategy to enhance robustness under strong event perturbations. Experiments on the DVS-Lip benchmark verify the effectiveness of the proposed design, and extensive ablation studies further validate the contributions of TDA, VGA, and teacher--student consistency. Qualitative decoding results also demonstrate that the proposed CTC-based temporal modeling learns meaningful viseme-aware structure from event streams.

### [34] [Closing the Null Space: Guidance-Aware Quantization for Classifier-Free Diffusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08241)
*Abdullah Al Shafi,Sumaiya Rahim Suma*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本论文指出现有分类器引导扩散模型的后训练量化方法忽略了其条件/无条件双分支结构，导致了系统延迟和算法层面的分支漂移陷阱。提出GAMP方法，直接在引导预测上进行校准，通过贪心背包算法分配比特，从根本上防止无条件分支漂移。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有后训练量化方法将分类器引导扩散模型视为单分支网络，忽略了其条件/无条件的配对结构，导致系统层面延迟被掩盖和INT8推理无法实现理论效率，算法层面存在精确零空间（分支漂移陷阱），量化模型可能在标准诊断指标上表现完美但样本质量极差。

Method: 提出引导感知混合精度量化（GAMP），直接在引导预测上进行校准，计算每层激活值对引导输出的敏感性，通过贪心背包算法分配比特资源，从构造上防止无条件分支漂移。

Result: 实证上发现了假阳性结果：标准诊断下校准最佳的模型同时产生了最差的样本质量，验证了分支漂移陷阱的存在。GAMP方法在保持量化效率的同时避免了该陷阱。

Conclusion: 分类器引导扩散模型的量化必须考虑其双分支结构，不能仅基于引导间隙进行校准；GAMP方法通过直接校准引导预测并提供可证明的无条件分支漂移防护，是更有效的量化方案。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：90%。遥感领域广泛使用扩散模型进行图像生成、超分辨率、数据增强等任务，CFG双分支结构同样存在。改进方案：(1)将GAMP的引导感知量化方法直接应用于遥感扩散模型（如遥感图像超分、云去除），提升低比特下遥感图像生成质量；(2)遥感场景下多模态信息融合（如SAR+光学）可类比CFG的双分支结构，GAMP的按层比特分配策略可迁移至多模态遥感模型的量化部署；(3)边缘计算场景中遥感模型的实时推理需求迫切，GAMP可解决INT8推理堆栈在遥感CFG模型上的效率瓶颈。

Abstract (英文): Deploying classifier-free guidance (CFG) diffusion models under real-world compute budgets requires quantization, yet existing post-training quantization (PTQ) methods treat CFG models as single-branch networks, ignoring the paired conditional/unconditional structure that CFG inference fundamentally relies on. This structural blind spot has two consequences. At the system level, the two-pass CFG execution pattern imposes a latency overhead that parameter-count and bit-operation metrics conceal entirely, and commodity INT8 inference stacks fail to realize the theoretical efficiency gains that BOPs calculations promise. At the algorithmic level, calibrating against the guidance gap alone admits an exact null space: a quantized model can achieve perfect gap-fidelity diagnostics while the unconditional branch drifts arbitrarily, corrupting every guided prediction at inference time. This paper terms this the branch-drift trap, proves its existence analytically, and confirms it empirically through a false-positive result in which the best-calibrated model by standard diagnostics simultaneously produces the worst sample quality. To close the trap, Guidance-Aware Mixed Precision (GAMP) is proposed, which calibrates directly on the guided prediction, derives per-layer activation-bit sensitivity from guided-output degradation, and allocates bits via a greedy knapsack -- provably preventing unconditional branch drift by construction.

</details>


### [35] [SkelGen4D: Weakly-Supervised Skeleton-Based 4D Generation for Text-Driven Mesh Animation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08246)
*Hao Feng,Zhi Zuo,Jia-Hui Pan,Ka-Hei Hui,Zhengzhe Liu,Dian Zhang,Haoran Xie,Bin Sheng,Jingyu Hu*

TL;DR: 提出SkelGen4D，一种弱监督的前馈框架，通过可微拟合从动画网格中恢复时间一致的伪骨骼，并用Motion-GRPO优化生成文本驱动的骨骼运动序列，实现高质量网格动画。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有4D生成方法多采用SDS优化或视频驱动，缺乏显式控制和编辑能力，且与标准工业动画管线不兼容。本文旨在构建一种与标准管线对齐、支持显式控制和编辑的骨骼驱动动画框架。

Method: 1) 通过可微拟合从动画网格中恢复时间一致的伪骨骼（无需逐帧骨骼标注）；2) 以文本为条件前馈生成骨骼运动序列；3) 采用Motion-GRPO进一步优化，确保时间连贯性、物理合理性和关节动作质量。

Conclusion: SkelGen4D支持灵活的运动编辑，与标准动画生产管线对齐，为文本驱动的4D内容生成提供了一种高效、可控且工业兼容的方案。

Abstract (英文): We study 4D generation to synthesize temporally coherent sequences of 3D geometry for animation and content creation. In contrast to existing SDS-based optimization methods and video-driven animation approaches, we adopt a skeleton-driven animation framework aligned with standard industrial pipelines, which enables explicit control and editing. To this end, we propose SkelGen4D, a weakly supervised feed-forward framework for text-driven mesh animation that generates explicit skeleton motions without requiring per-frame skeleton annotations. SkelGen4D first recovers temporally consistent pseudo-skeletons from animated meshes via differentiable fitting, and then generates text-conditioned skeleton motion sequences in a feed-forward manner, further refined with Motion-GRPO to ensure temporally coherent, physically plausible, and articulated animation. We evaluate our method on two large-scale benchmarks, Truebones Zoo and Diffusion4D. Our results show that our weakly supervised skeleton modeling matches or surpasses fully supervised baselines while scaling to diverse object categories for high-quality text-driven mesh animation. Further, our method supports flexible motion editing and is aligned with standard animation production pipelines.

### [36] [HSA: Hierarchical Slot Attention for Multi-granularity Scene-Decomposition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08249)
*Neelu Madan,Rongzhen Zhao,Andreas Mogelmose,Juho Kannala,Joni Pajarinen,Graham W. Taylor,Thomas B. Moeslund*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出分层槽注意力（HSA），在单个模型中同时学习前景/背景、物体类别和个体实例三个粒度的语义场景分解，仅需10%标注数据，在COCO和PASCAL VOC上显著优于平铺基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有槽注意力方法存在两个关键局限：场景被分解为单一粒度的扁平槽集合，且分解基于外观而非语义。然而人类通过语义层次理解场景（前景/背景、物体类别、个体实例），这种语义层次无法在没有监督的情况下从视觉模式中自发涌现。

Method: 提出分层槽注意力（HSA），包含三个层次：整体层（前景/背景）、语义层（物体类别）和全景层（个体实例）。仅使用10%标注数据，通过分层对齐损失联合学习三个层次。引入分组纯度和包含度两个指标，衡量层级是否在表示空间中被编码。

Result: 在COCO上，HSA在整体层ARI提升+41.5，语义层+14.6，全景层+10.4；在PASCAL VOC上提升更大。仅需单个模型而非三个独立模型。

Conclusion: HSA有效证明了在少量监督下从单个模型中学习多层次语义场景分解的可行性，为面向语义的物体中心学习提供了新范式。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感场景同样存在层次化语义结构（如地物类别/实例/背景）。具体方案：(1) 将HSA应用于遥感图像，前景/背景层可对应建成区/非建成区，语义层对应道路、建筑、植被等地物类别，全景层对应个体建筑或车辆实例；(2) 利用遥感中丰富的弱标注数据（如OpenStreetMap标签），进一步减少对精细标注的依赖；(3) 引入遥感特有的空间先验（如地物共现关系、尺度先验）增强分层对齐损失。

Abstract (英文): Slot attention is a powerful framework for object-centric learning, decomposing visual scenes into latent slots through iterative competitive attention. However, existing methods share two critical limitations: they decompose scenes into a flat set of slots at a single granularity, and this decomposition is based on appearance rather than semantics. Yet humans understand scenes through semantic hierarchies: separating foreground from background, recognizing object categories, and identifying individual instances. Crucially, such semantic hierarchies cannot emerge without supervision, because category names are human constructs, not visual patterns. We propose Hierarchical Slot Attention (HSA), which learns multi-granularity semantic scene decomposition from a single model. HSA decomposes scenes at three levels: holistic (foreground/background), semantic (object categories), and panoptic (individual instances). Using only 10\% labeled data, combined with hierarchical alignment loss, HSA learns all three levels jointly. We further introduce grouping purity and containment to measure whether the hierarchy is encoded in representation space, not just output masks. Experiments on COCO and PASCAL VOC demonstrate that HSA outperforms the strongest flat baseline by up to \textbf{$+$41.5} ARI at holistic, \textbf{$+$14.6} at semantic, and \textbf{$+$10.4} at panoptic level on COCO, with even larger gains on Pascal VOC, while requiring a single model instead of three. Code will be made available upon acceptance.
