### [37] [On the Design of Mixture-of-Experts for Dynamic Gaussian Splatting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08250)
*In-Hwan Jin,Hyeongju Mun,Joonsoo Kim,Kugjin Yun,Kyeongbo Kong*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文针对动态场景重建中单一变形模型鲁棒性不足的问题，提出了两种多变形建模策略：MoDE（将多个变形专家联合优化集成到可变形3D高斯泼溅管线中）和MoE-GS（独立优化各变形专家后通过单独路由阶段组合）。两种方法从混合专家视角出发，探索了不同集成约束下变形专家的交互方式，提升了动态新视角合成的鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有动态3D高斯泼溅方法通常依赖单一的变形模型，难以应对真实世界中异质且空间变化的复杂运动，鲁棒性有限。本文旨在通过多变形建模来解决这一根本性问题。

Method: 从混合专家视角出发，提出两种多变形建模方法：1) MoDE——将多个变形专家直接集成到可变形高斯泼溅管线中，通过联合优化共享的规范高斯表示；2) MoE-GS——变形专家独立优化后，通过单独的路由阶段组合，专家交互发生在非规范高斯表示上。两种方法采用不同的集成约束（何时以及如何让多个变形专家交互）。

Result: 两种方法提供了多变形建模的替代策略，阐明了集成约束如何塑造动态3D高斯表示中变形专家的设计与行为。代码已开源。

Conclusion: 通过MoDE和MoE-GS两种方式，证明了多变形建模能有效提升动态场景重建的鲁棒性，且集成约束的选择对变形专家的行为具有重要影响，为后续动态3D高斯表示的研究提供了新方向。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感领域存在大量动态场景（如车辆运动、植被随风摆动、云层移动、水面波动等），可将本文的MoDE或MoE-GS框架引入遥感动态场景的4D重建中。具体方案：1) 针对遥感视频序列，将不同运动模式（刚性运动如车辆、非刚性运动如植被）分配至不同的变形专家，提升动态重建精度；2) 在卫星或无人机多视角遥感数据中，利用MoE-GS的独立优化加路由机制，处理大尺度场景中不同区域运动模式差异大的问题；3) 将共享规范高斯表示与遥感多时相数据结合，实现时序遥感影像的高质量新视角合成。

Abstract (英文): Dynamic scene reconstruction remains challenging due to the heterogeneous and spatially varying nature of real-world motion. Although recent 3D Gaussian Splatting methods have introduced diverse deformation formulations for dynamic novel view synthesis, each method typically relies on a single deformation model within its representation, which limits robustness across diverse dynamic scenarios. In this work, we study a fundamental problem-multi-deformation modeling for dynamic 3D Gaussian representations-under two distinct integration constraints that differ in when and how multiple deformation experts interact during training. From a Mixture-of-Experts (MoE) perspective, we view multi-deformation modeling as the problem of combining multiple specialized deformation models within a unified 3D representation. We first introduce Mixture of Deformation Experts (MoDE), which integrates multiple deformation experts directly into the deformable Gaussian Splatting pipeline through joint optimization. In MoDE, experts operate on a shared canonical Gaussian representation, enabling multi-deformation modeling without introducing additional training stages or modifying the original optimization schedule. In contrast, we further present Mixture of Experts for Dynamic Gaussian Splatting (MoE-GS) under a different integration constraint, where deformation experts are optimized independently and combined through a separate routing stage. As a result, expert interaction occurs over non-canonical Gaussian representations after individual optimization. Together, these two approaches provide alternative strategies for multi-deformation modeling, clarifying how integration constraints shape the design and behavior of deformation experts in dynamic 3D Gaussian representations. Our code is available at: https://github.com/cvsp-lab/MoE-GS-studio.

### [38] [UniRef-UAV: A Multimodal Benchmark for Universal Referring in UAV Imagery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08267)
*Haibin Tian,Huichao Xie,Xuelin Qian,Ruitao Lu,Junwei Han,Dingwen Zhang*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1）提出Universal Referring任务框架，联合扩展查询模态和输出基数；2）构建UniRef-UAV多模态基准，支持三种查询类型及相应的目标基数（无目标、单目标、多目标），并提供域内和跨域评估协议；3）提出UAV-URNet检测式基线方法，将异构查询映射到共享查询空间，通过集合预测（set prediction）预测可变大小的目标集。

Conclusion: 本文通过统一多模态查询和目标基数，填补了无人机指代任务在实际场景中的空白；UAV-URNet作为稳定可复现的基线，为后续研究提供了基准；多模态查询的有效性表明融合图像信息对无人机视觉定位具有重要意义。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。该工作本身聚焦无人机遥感场景，具有以下改进方向：1）引入多尺度特征融合策略以适应无人机视角下目标尺度剧烈变化的特点；2）结合地理空间先验（如GPS/IMU信息）辅助查询-目标对齐，提升大场景下的定位精度；3）扩展至视频流时序查询，实现连续帧间的目标跟踪与指代；4）探索更轻量的查询融合机制（如交叉注意力）替代当前简单映射，适应无人机边缘设备的计算约束。

Abstract (英文): Unmanned aerial vehicles (UAVs) increasingly rely on visual grounding capabilities to localize task-relevant targets from diverse instructions in complex aerial scenes. Existing referring expression comprehension (REC) benchmarks and methods, however, are largely built around text-only queries and single-object outputs, which limits their applicability to practical UAV scenarios involving reference images, multimodal instructions, absent targets, and multiple valid target instances. To address this gap, we introduce \emph{Universal Referring}, a generalized UAV referring task that jointly expands the query modality and the output cardinality. We construct \emph{UniRef-UAV}, a multimodal benchmark that supports text-only, image-only, and text+image queries with modality-dependent target cardinality, where text-only and text+image queries admit no-target, single-target, and multi-target grounding while image-only queries focus on existence-aware single-instance grounding. It also provides in-domain and cross-domain evaluation protocols for visual-query generalization. We further present \emph{UAV-URNet}, a detection-style baseline that maps heterogeneous queries into a shared query space and predicts variable-size target sets through set prediction. Extensive experiments show that UAV-URNet provides a stable and reproducible baseline with more consistent no-target discrimination and a more lightweight, reproducible implementation than large general-purpose MLLMs. Additional domain analysis, query-representation analysis, and ablation studies demonstrate that multimodal queries help reduce visual-query ambiguity and promote a more unified query--target alignment space. The annotations, visual query crops/images, train/validation/test splits, evaluation scripts, and baseline code will be made publicly available to facilitate reproducible research.

### [39] [Progression as Latent Drift: Generative Forecasting of Slow-Evolving Pathologies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08270)
*Yuxiang Feng,Juncheng Wang,Chao Xu,Wenlong Hou,Huihan Wang,Yijie Qian,Yang Liu,Baigui Sun,Yong Liu,Shujun Wan*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出Latent Drift，一种渐进式生成框架，通过在压缩语义表示中学习变化而非合成全分辨率解剖结构，解决了慢速神经退行性疾病纵向MRI预测中身份崩溃和连续插值陷阱两大难点，在3D脑MRI预测上优于扩散模型和自回归Transformer基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 慢速神经退行性疾病的纵向MRI中真实进展信号微弱（低信号 regime），直接迁移现代生成序列模型不可靠：训练被稳定的基线解剖结构主导，并被密集的样本特异性噪声混淆。现有模型存在身份崩溃（优化倾向于重现当前解剖而无法学习微弱时序变化）和连续插值陷阱（标准平滑网络无法分离局部生物漂移与广泛噪声）两大问题。

Method: 1）在压缩语义表示空间中学习变化，而非合成全分辨率解剖，去除像素级身份预测目标，集中模型容量于进展相关动态；2）应用有限标量量化（Finite Scalar Quantization）到学习到的变化表示，抑制小幅高频噪声波动，保留一致的结构漂移。

Result: 在纵向3D脑MRI实验中，Latent Drift在生成保真度和临床相关评估指标上均优于扩散模型和自回归Transformer基线。

Conclusion: 在低信号场景下，通过语义空间中的离散变化表示建模，可以有效避免身份崩溃和噪声干扰，实现更可靠的神经解剖预测。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感时序变化检测（如地物覆盖变化、城市扩张）同样面临变化微弱、噪声密集的问题。具体方案：1）将Latent Drift的语义压缩表示思想迁移到遥感时序影像，在特征空间而非像素空间建模地物变化；2）利用有限标量量化抑制遥感影像中常见的传感器噪声和光照波动，保留真实的地物漂移信号；3）可应用于森林退化监测、冰川消融预测等慢速变化场景。

Abstract (英文): Forecasting the future anatomy of slow-evolving neurodegenerative diseases could enable earlier, more targeted intervention and improve clinical trial design, but it remains challenging because true progression signals are subtle in longitudinal MRI. In this low-signal regime, transferring modern generative sequence models directly is unreliable: training is dominated by stable baseline anatomy and confounded by dense, sample-specific nuisance variation. We first provide a theoretical analysis that explains these failures through two modes. Identity collapse occurs when optimization is driven toward reproducing the current anatomy, which prevents the model from learning faint temporal change. The continuous interpolation trap arises when standard smooth networks cannot separate localized biological drift from pervasive noise, which leads to spurious changes that diffuse across the volume. To address both issues, we propose Latent Drift, a progressive generative framework that learns change in a compressed semantic representation rather than synthesizing full-resolution anatomy. This design removes pixel-level identity from the prediction target and concentrates model capacity on progression-relevant dynamics. We further apply Finite Scalar Quantization to the learned change representation, which suppresses small, high-frequency nuisance fluctuations while preserving consistent structural drift. Experiments on longitudinal 3D brain MRI show that Latent Drift improves patient-specific neuro-forecasting over diffusion and autoregressive transformer baselines across generative fidelity and clinically relevant evaluation metrics. Project page: \href{https://cutepkq.github.io/latent-drift}{https://cutepkq.github.io/latent-drift}.

</details>


### [40] [Enhancing the KidSat Model: Integrating Geographical Encoding and Data Quality Assessment for Childhood Poverty Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08281)
*Hou Hin Ip,Ka Nam Lam,Joshua Man Yu Ng,Makkunda Sharma,Seth Flaxman,Codie Gerlach-Wood,H Juliette T Unwin*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文在KidSat框架基础上，通过改进数据预处理（DHS重聚合降低标签维度）、两阶段图像质量筛选、以及融合DINOv2视觉嵌入与球谐函数（SH）地理编码，显著提升了卫星影像贫困预测精度，MAE从0.2167降至0.1759（降幅18.83%），并在33个非洲国家取得0.1658的整体MAE。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 卫星影像贫困制图面临三大瓶颈：调查数据稀疏且含噪声、影像质量差（云遮挡/损坏）、纯影像模型缺乏显式空间结构。现有KidSat框架在这些方面仍有改进空间。

Method: (1) 标签优化：将DHS调查目标矩阵从103维降至51维，解决高基数稀疏问题；(2) 两阶段质量筛选：过滤重云层和损坏的观测样本；(3) 特征融合：结合DINOv2视觉嵌入与球谐函数（SH）地理编码特征，并对比SH+SIREN坐标MLP增强；(4) 使用XGBoost/LightGBM梯度提升树作为预测头部，挖掘特征非线性交互。

Result: MAE从0.2167降至0.1759（降幅18.83%）；扩展到33个非洲国家时，最佳配置整体MAE为0.1658；SH特征持续优于纯影像基线；SH+SIREN在缺乏精心设计目标函数时可能表现不佳；梯度提升树头能最有效利用融合特征的非线性交互。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了一套仅使用公开数据即可规模化提升卫星遥感社会经济预测性能的规范化方案，验证了地理编码与视觉特征融合的有效性。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。改进方案：(1) 将两阶段质量筛选范式迁移至其他遥感任务（如作物分类、城市变化检测），用于自动清洗云覆盖样本；(2) 球谐函数地理编码可扩展至遥感时空建模，替代传统经纬度+时间编码，增强模型对全球尺度空间模式的表达能力；(3) DINOv2自监督视觉特征+SH编码的组合可推广至遥感图像检索、土地覆盖分类等任务；(4) 梯度提升树头（XGBoost/LightGBM）可替换遥感回归/分类任务中的全连接层，尤其在样本量有限时提升泛化性能。

Abstract (英文): Accurate poverty mapping using satellite imagery is often hindered by (i) noisy and sparse survey-derived supervision, (ii) image quality issues such as cloud cover and image corruption, and (iii) lack of explicit spatial structure in image-only models. Building on the KidSat framework, we develop an enhanced pipeline that improves predictive accuracy via refined data preprocessing, systematic image quality assessment, and mathematically defined geographic encoding. First, we refine the fine-tuning target matrix by resolving high-cardinality sparsity and reducing one-hot dimensionality from 103 to 51 via DHS re-aggregation. Second, we introduce a simple two-stage quality-screening procedure to filter heavily clouded or corrupted observations. Third, we fuse DINOv2 visual embeddings with Spherical Harmonics (SH) location features. Across extensive experiments, these changes reduce MAE from 0.2167 to 0.1759, corresponding to an 18.83% relative reduction on the cluster-level severe-deprivation proportion scale. When extended from 16 to 33 African countries, the best-performing configuration achieves an overall MAE of 0.1658. We find that SH features consistently improve performance over the image-only backbone, whereas higher-capacity coordinate Multi Layer Perception augmentation (SH+SIREN) can underperform without carefully designed objectives. Finally, gradient-boosted tree heads (XGBoost/LightGBM) most effectively exploit nonlinear interactions in the fused visual-geographic representation. These findings provide a scalable and principled recipe for improving satellite-based socioeconomic predictions using only publicly accessible data.

</details>


### [41] [ARGUS: Accelerated, Robust, General, and Unsupervised Cell Tracking Solutions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08297)
*Noah Jaitner,Kandice Tanner,Ingolf Sack,Hossein S. Aghamiry*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: ARGUS是一个无监督、无需训练数据的细胞追踪框架，结合自适应检测、光流预测和轨迹优化，在Cell Tracking Challenge数据集上实现了0.897-0.964的追踪精度，运行时间在1分钟内。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 时间延迟显微镜中的自动细胞追踪因噪声、形态变化、细胞重叠以及分裂融合等动态事件而极具挑战性，现有方法通常需要大量标注数据或GPU资源，限制了其广泛应用。

Method: ARGUS框架包含四个核心模块：自适应细胞检测、密集Farneback光流预测、帧间线性分配以及序列级别的轨迹片段精炼（重新连接短时间间隔内的轨迹片段）。

Result: 在Cell Tracking Challenge公开数据集上，检测精度达到0.905-0.971，追踪精度达到0.897-0.964，运行时间在1分钟以内（3帧仅需5-6秒）。

Conclusion: ARGUS是一个模块化、可解释的框架，无需训练数据或GPU基础设施，可适应不同成像模态和生物学应用。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感领域中的目标跟踪（如车辆、船只、飞机轨迹追踪）面临与细胞追踪类似的挑战：目标形变、遮挡、背景噪声等。具体交叉方案：(1) 将ARGUS的自适应检测模块用于遥感视频中的运动目标检测，适应不同分辨率和光照条件；(2) Farneback光流可用于遥感图像序列中的运动场估计，辅助运动目标分割；(3) 帧间线性分配与轨迹精炼可直接用于遥感多目标跟踪的帧间关联和断连重接；(4) 该框架的无监督特性特别适用于缺乏标注的遥感视频数据，可结合SAR或光学卫星视频进行目标追踪。

Abstract (英文): Background and Objective: Quantitative analysis of cell dynamics is central to modern biological research, providing critical insights into immune cell interactions, disease progression, and drug mechanisms. Automated cell tracking in time-lapse microscopy remains challenging due to noise, morphological variations, overlapping cells, and dynamic events such as divisions and fusions.
  Methods: We present ARGUS, a framework for Accelerated, Robust, General, and Unsupervised Cell Tracking Solutions. ARGUS combines adaptive cell detection, dense Farneback optical-flow prediction, frame-to-frame linear assignment, and a sequence-level tracklet-refinement step that reconnects trajectory fragments across short temporal gaps.
  Results: On publicly available Cell Tracking Challenge datasets, ARGUS achieved detection accuracy of 0.905-0.971 and tracking accuracy of 0.897-0.964, with runtimes within 1 minute (5-6 seconds for 3 frames).
  Conclusions: ARGUS is a modular, interpretable framework that can be adapted to different imaging modalities and biological applications without training data or GPU infrastructure. The implementation is publicly available at https://github.com/Gitinc/argus

### [42] [Texture Representations in Deep Vision Models: Comparing CNNs, Vision Transformers, and Human Perception](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08321)
*Ludovica de Paolis,Marco Baroni,Alessandro Laio,Eugenio Piasini*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本研究比较了CNN和Vision Transformers（ViTs）在纹理感知上与人类心理物理学数据的一致性，发现ViTs比CNNs更能预测人类纹理识别表现，且纹理表征受网络架构驱动。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在标准物体识别范式之外（即纹理感知任务中），CNN和ViT等计算视觉模型与人类视觉表征的对齐程度，尤其是不同架构模型之间的差异。

Method: 使用三种不同算法从相同源图像生成不同复杂度的纹理刺激；通过基于秩的统计量量化CNN和三种ViT内部表征中的信息；将模型表征与人类心理物理学数据进行比较。

Result: 不同ViT之间纹理表征对齐，但ViT与CNN之间不一致；ViT对不同复杂度的纹理形成相似表征；ViT比CNN能更好地预测人类纹理识别表现。

Conclusion: ViT可能比CNN更忠实地捕捉人类视觉处理纹理的方式，且计算模型中的纹理刺激表征受网络架构驱动。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感图像中纹理信息丰富（如土地覆盖分类、纹理特征提取），该研究的框架可直接迁移：1）使用ViT替代CNN进行遥感图像的纹理分析，有望更贴近人类遥感判读专家的认知模式；2）采用秩统计量评估遥感深度学习模型表征与专家判读结果的对齐程度，作为模型可解释性指标；3）借鉴该研究的多复杂度纹理生成方法构建遥感纹理基准数据集，用于评估模型泛化能力。

Abstract (英文): In computational vision science, Convolutional Neural Networks (CNNs) have emerged as a popular model of biological vision because of the alignment they can exhibit with neural and behavioral data in humans and animals. However, it remains unclear to what extent this alignment persists for visual tasks that extend beyond the canonical object recognition paradigm based on well defined semantic content. In this study, we diverge from the common object-centric view by focusing on another aspect of vision: texture perception. We consider textures of different complexity generated with three different algorithms from the same source images. Using a rank-based statistic, we quantify the information encoded in the internal representations of a CNN and three Vision Transformers (ViTs), and we compare the similarity of these representations to those inferred from human psychophysics data. We find that the representation of textures is aligned in different ViTs, but not between the ViTs and the CNN; that ViTs form similar representations for textures of different complexity; that human performance in recognizing textures can be better predicted from ViTs representations rather than CNN representations. Taken together, these results suggest that ViTs may capture more faithfully than CNNs how texture patterns are visually processed by humans, and that the representations of texture stimuli in computational models may be driven by the network architecture.

### [43] [WCog-VLA: A Dual-Level World-Cognitive Vision-Language-Action Model for End-to-End Autonomous Driving](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08375)
*Xuerun Yan,Zhexi Lian,Nuoheng Zhang,Shiyu Fang,Haoran Wang,Chen Lv,Jia Hu,Binyang Song*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: WCog-VLA提出了一种双层次世界认知VLA框架，通过语义级别的世界认知与推理（3D空间感知、智能体token、Game-CoT推理）和生成级别的世界演化（ADDT扩散模型生成多智能体轨迹），实现从被动驾驶到主动驾驶的转变，在NAVSIM基准上达到92.9 PDMS SOTA成绩。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有VLA模型缺乏全面的世界认知或存在碎片化的世界预见能力，本质上局限于反应式驾驶，无法实现主动式自动驾驶。

Method: 提出双层次WCog-VLA框架：1）语义层：融合3D空间感知与智能体token捕获世界动态，并引入Game-CoT推理；2）生成层：提出ADDT作为生成式世界模型，通过场景表征对齐减少去噪步数加速推理，合成物理合理的多智能体联合轨迹；并构建85k Game-CoT标注数据集。

Result: 在NAVSIM基准上PDMS得分达到92.9，取得SOTA性能。

Conclusion: 通过将语义世界预测与生成世界演化相结合，WCog-VLA成功实现了从反应式到主动式自动驾驶的跨越，验证了双层次世界认知框架的有效性。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感领域中的多智能体路径规划（如无人机编队、卫星轨道协同）可直接借鉴WCog-VLA的双层次框架：1）语义层：用遥感3D空间感知（LiDAR/SAR点云）替代驾驶场景感知，结合遥感时序数据注入智能体token，应用Game-CoT进行多平台博弈推理；2）生成层：ADDT可扩展为遥感多智能体轨迹生成器，通过场景表征对齐（如地理坐标-遥感影像对齐）加速去噪过程，生成物理约束下的无人机/卫星协同路径。此外，85k Game-CoT标注方法可迁移至遥感行为推理数据集构建。

Abstract (英文): Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models have advanced end-to-end autonomous driving. However, existing methods either lack comprehensive world cognition or suffer from fragmented world foresight, inherently confining these models to reactive driving. To address this limitation, we propose WCog-VLA, a novel dual-level World-Cognitive VLA framework that successfully bridges semantic world forecasting with generative world evolution to achieve proactive autonomous driving. At the semantic level, WCog-VLA unifies world cognition and reasoning by incorporating 3D spatial perception and injecting agent tokens to capture the world dynamics, while concurrently enabling Game-theoretic Chain-of-Thought (Game-CoT) reasoning. At the generative level, we introduce the Aligned Decoupled Diffusion Transformer (ADDT) as a powerful generative world model that synthesizes physically-plausible joint multi-agent trajectories. Through scene representation alignment, ADDT reduces the number of denoising steps required and thus significantly accelerates inference. To facilitate strategic reasoning, we further construct a large-scale dataset featuring 85k Game-CoT annotations. Extensive experiments on the NAVSIM benchmark demonstrate that WCog-VLA achieves a State-Of-The-Art (SOTA) PDMS score of 92.9.

### [44] [Classical versus Deep Mirror-Symmetry Scoring: A Benchmark of Thirteen Methods](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08379)
*Maximilian Woehrer*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文首次在统一统计协议下基准测试了13种图像对称性评分方法，发现经典HOG描述符在性能上接近最好的冻结深度特征，但速度快约300倍，表明对于对称性度量任务，冻结深度特征相比调优的经典描述符优势有限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对称性评分方法缺乏统一的统计严谨协议进行比较，无法客观评估各方法的优劣。

Method: 收集9种文献方法并引入4种新方法，在4个单轴和5个多轴数据集上，采用反射精确协议、以机会水平为锚点并进行显著性检验的判别能力评估框架进行基准测试。

Result: 深度骨干网络在单轴和较难的多轴协议上表现最佳；但经典HOG描述符与最佳冻结网络读取头的差距很小（虽显著），且与第二名的CNN滤波器方法在统计上不可区分，运行速度快约300倍；判别信息集中在中等尺度的定向特征上。

Conclusion: 对于对称性度量，冻结深度特征相比调优的经典描述符（如HOG）优势不大；任务训练的深度评分器是否更优仍有待研究。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感图像中的人造目标（如建筑物、道路、农田）常具有对称性，可引入本基准中的最优方法（HOG或冻深层特征）进行快速对称轴检测与评分，用于建筑物对称性分析、道路笔直度评估、农田规整度量化等任务。具体方案：①使用HOG描述符（300x速度优势）对遥感图像进行对称性评分，作为低计算开销的预处理筛选模块；②将冻深层特征作为高精度评分器，用于关键目标的精细对称性分析；③参考本文发现的"中等尺度定向特征"关键性，优化遥感特征提取的网络层选择。

Abstract (英文): Quantifying how mirror-symmetric an image is about a given axis (symmetry scoring) underpins applications from visual aesthetics to medical imaging, yet proposed scoring methods have never been compared on a common, statistically grounded protocol. We benchmark 13 scoring methods (nine collected from literature, four introduced here) spanning from classical features to frozen deep features, across four single-axis and five multi-axis datasets under a reflection-exact protocol with a chance-anchored, significance-tested discrimination skill. Deep backbones perform best on single-axis and harder multi-axis protocols. However, a classical histogram-of-oriented-gradients (HOG) descriptor trails the best frozen-network readout by a small (but significant) margin, is not statistically separable from the runner-up (a CNN-filter measure), and runs ~300x faster on CPU. Our results show that discrimination concentrates in mid-scale oriented features, where deep backbones peak at a low or mid stage, and HOG peaks at a mid cell size. Among existing methods, frozen deep features thus offer little over a tuned classical descriptor for measuring symmetry; whether task-trained deep scorers can do better remains open. We release the scorers and harness in imgsym, an open toolkit for image symmetry detection and measurement.

### [45] [Attribute Retrieving for Open-Vocabulary Endoscopic Compositional Referring Segmentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08397)
*Shun Liu,Nan Xi,Yang Liu,Tianyu Luan,Xuan Gong,David Doermann*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出了ReferEndoscopy——内窥镜领域首个大规模指代图像分割基准数据集，并设计了基于属性检索的AR-ERIS框架，实现开放词汇下的内窥镜组合式指代分割，在模拟和真实内窥镜数据上均达到SOTA性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将指代图像分割(RIS)扩展到内窥镜图像面临三大挑战：(1)高质量标注数据稀缺；(2)内窥镜领域存在复杂的、领域特定的图文关系；(3)现有的视觉-语言模型虽能跨域对齐，但难以捕捉内窥镜场景下细粒度的文本线索，导致性能次优且泛化能力有限。

Method: (1) 构建ReferEndoscopy大规模内窥镜RIS基准数据集；(2) 提出AR-ERIS(Attribute Retrieval-based Endoscopic-RIS)框架，利用属性检索实现开放词汇的内窥镜组合式指代分割；(3) 在ReferEndoscopy数据集上预训练该框架。

Result: 在模拟和真实内窥镜数据上均达到SOTA性能，并展现出强泛化能力。

Conclusion: 基于属性检索的开放词汇组合式分割方案有效解决了内窥镜领域RIS的标注稀缺和细粒度理解难题，数据集和代码将公开发布。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。具体方案：(1) 遥感领域同样面临标注稀缺和领域特定的图文关系问题，可借鉴ReferEndoscopy的数据集构建流程，制作遥感专用RIS基准数据集；(2) 属性检索机制可用于遥感场景中的组合式目标分割，如"红色的屋顶+方形建筑"等细粒度属性组合描述；(3) 开放词汇策略适合遥感中多样化的地物类别，可突破固定类别集的限制；(4) 需注意遥感图像尺度大、目标空间分布稀疏的特点，需对属性检索的空间编码方式进行适配调整。

Abstract (英文): Referring Image Segmentation (RIS) aims to segment image regions specified by natural language, enabling fine-grained and controllable visual understanding. Extending RIS to endoscopic imagery, however, presents unique challenges, including scarce high-quality annotations and complex, domain-specific image-text relationships. Although recent vision-language models demonstrate strong cross-domain alignment, they often fail to capture fine-grained textual cues in endoscopic settings, resulting in suboptimal performance and limited generalization. To address these challenges, we introduce ReferEndoscopy, a large-scale benchmark for RIS in the endoscopy field. Building on this dataset, we propose the Attribute Retrieval-based Endoscopic-RIS (AR-ERIS) framework for open-vocabulary endoscopic compositional referring segmentation. AR-ERIS leverages attribute retrieval for open-vocabulary endoscopic compositional referring segmentation and is pretrained on the curated ReferEndoscopy dataset, achieving state-of-the-art performance with strong generalization across both simulated and real-world endoscopic data. The dataset and code will be publicly released upon completion of the review process.

### [46] [Swapping Faces, Saving Features: A Dual-Purpose Pipeline for Pedestrian Privacy in ITS](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08402)

Method: 提出一个五阶段管线，核心采用人脸替换（face swapping）技术保护行人隐私。具体评估了Roop和Ghost-v2两种人脸替换模型，选择表现更优的Roop模型集成到管线中，在隐藏身份的同时保留关键面部属性。

Abstract (英文): Large-scale and diverse datasets are needed to train AI models to take real-time decisions for autonomous vehicles (AVs), an intelligent transportation system (ITS) application. Pedestrian intention and trajectory prediction are critical models used in AVs, requiring datasets involving diverse pedestrian images. Unrestricted access to these datasets imposes serious security risks, like identity theft and pedestrian tracking. The challenge is to apply privacy preservation procedures while maintaining the image attributes needed to train the models. Existing privacy methods may preserve the pedestrian's privacy, but degrade the image usability, which hinders the models' effectiveness. This work's focus is to implement a five-stage pipeline to protect pedestrians' privacy through face swapping while keeping the essential facial attributes intact. It should be tailored to satisfy the privacy needs of the Egy-DRiVeS dataset. Moreover, Roop and Ghost-v2 face-swapping models are evaluated. Provenly, Roop outperforms Ghost-v2 in various aspects, as will be discussed. Consequently, Roop is the face-swapping model to be used in the pipeline to strike the balance between pedestrian privacy via identity concealment and data usability via facial attribute preservation.

### [47] [Track2Map: Online Deformable SLAM with Motion-Aware Pose Optimization in Robotic Surgery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08408)
*Tianyi Song,Sierra Bonilla,Xinwei Ju,Evangelos Mazomenos,Danail Stoyanov,Adam Schmidt,Omid Mohareri,Sophia Bano,Francisco Vasconcelos*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: Track2Map 是一种面向机器人辅助微创手术的在线三维高斯溅射管道，能够联合优化相机轨迹和三维可变形场景重建，在无相机先验或先验噪声情况下实现鲁棒的三维重建，本质是一种SLAM方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于高斯溅射的密集可变形三维解剖重建大多为离线方法，且严重依赖准确的相机轨迹先验（如机器人运动学），当先验缺失或存在噪声时适用性受限。

Method: 提出在线三维高斯溅射管道 Track2Map，联合优化相机轨迹与可变形场景；引入基于密集二维点轨迹的轨迹锚定形变初始化；利用轨迹统计量检测静态相机周期并减少增量建图中的漂移，以解耦相机运动与场景形变。

Result: 在 StereoMIS 数据集上，Track2Map 在重建质量和相机轨迹精度上均优于对比的 SLAM 方法，以及使用相机轨迹先验的非 SLAM 方法。

Conclusion: Track2Map 有效解决了手术场景中无相机先验或先验噪声条件下的在线三维可变形重建问题，兼具SLAM能力，为RAMIS中的实时解剖重建提供了新方案。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：65%。该方法的在线联合优化相机轨迹与可变形场景的思想可迁移至遥感视频中的动态场景（如云层运动、植被生长）重建。具体交叉方案：1) 将密集2D点轨迹替换为遥感影像中的特征匹配（如SIFT或深度学习特征）进行形变初始化；2) 利用遥感平台的GPS/IMU作为弱先验替代完全无先验场景；3) 针对大尺度场景，引入分块高斯溅射策略以降低内存开销。

Abstract (英文): Gaussian splatting is the current state-of-the-art for dense, deformable 3D anatomy reconstruction in robot-assisted minimally invasive surgery (RAMIS); however, most pipelines are offline and depend on accurate camera trajectory priors (often from robotic kinematics), limiting applicability when priors are missing or noisy. To address these limitations, we propose Track2Map, an online 3D Gaussian Splatting pipeline that jointly optimizes camera trajectory and 3D deformable scene representation directly from surgical video. Track2Map is therefore capable of robust 3D reconstructions when camera trajectory priors are either absent or noisy, and due to its online nature it effectively works as a Simultaneous Localisation and Mapping (SLAM) method. To stabilize optimization in the presence of tissue motion and ambiguous visual cues, we introduce a track-anchored deformation initialization using dense 2D point tracks. Track statistics are further utilized to disentangle camera motion from scene deformation by detecting static camera periods and reducing drift during incremental mapping. Experiments on StereoMIS show improved reconstruction quality and camera trajectory against competing SLAM methods, as well as compared to non-SLAM methods that utilize camera trajectory priors. The code is available at https://track2map.github.io/.

### [48] [DeltaV: Thinking with Visual State Updates in Unified Large Multimodal Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08434)
*Pengjie Wang,Linger Deng,Zujia Zhang,Shaojie Zhang,Zhenbo Luo,Pei Fu,Jian Luan,Xiang Bai,Yuliang Liu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: DeltaV提出了一种视觉更新范式，替代传统ULMMs中生成完整图像的方式，通过增量预测紧凑的更新令牌来捕捉推理步骤间的视觉变化，并结合时序相似性路由（TSIM Router）动态分配令牌预算，以及构建包含105万样本的StructCoT数据集，在减少55.6%视觉令牌的同时提升多模态推理能力3.3%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前统一大型多模态模型（ULMMs）在交错多模态推理中，每个视觉状态都生成为完整图像，导致视觉令牌冗余严重，且对稀疏但关键的推理状态转变的监督被稀释。

Method: 1) 提出视觉更新范式（DeltaV），基于历史视觉状态增量预测紧凑的更新令牌，仅建模视觉变化部分；2) 引入时序相似性路由（TSIM Router），根据边际重建增益阈值动态停止令牌分配；3) 构建StructCoT数据集，包含105万样本、44个任务领域，支持多样化多模态推理。

Result: 1) 新生成的视觉令牌减少55.6%，同时保持重建保真度；2) 多模态推理能力比全图生成提升3.3%；3) DeltaV-2B在领域内评估上超越大幅更大的开源模型8.4%，在外部基准上超越同等规模Qwen3-VL-2B达5.9%。

Conclusion: 视觉更新范式能有效消除冗余令牌生成，提升推理效率与性能，StructCoT数据集有助于模型泛化能力的提升。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感领域存在大量时序数据（如卫星影像序列、变化检测、动态监测），DeltaV的视觉更新范式可直接应用于遥感时序变化建模：1) 将连续时相遥感图像间的变化编码为更新令牌，替代逐帧全图生成，显著降低计算开销；2) TSIM Router可自适应检测遥感场景中剧烈变化区域（如灾害前后、城市扩张）并分配更多令牌，对无变化区域停止分配，提升变化检测与语义分割效率；3) StructCoT的推理链思想可用于遥感多模态任务，如结合文本描述与历史影像进行推理式变化分析。改进方向：需针对遥感图像高分辨率、多光谱特性调整令牌编码方式，并引入地理空间先验知识。

Abstract (英文): Current Unified Large Multimodal Models (ULMMs) support interleaved multimodal reasoning through textual reasoning and intermediate visual states, but typically generate each visual state as a full image. This full-image generation paradigm introduces substantial visual-token redundancy and dilutes supervision on sparse yet reasoning-critical state transitions. We propose DeltaV, a ULMM that replaces full-image generation with visual updates. Conditioned on historical visual states, DeltaV incrementally predicts compact update tokens that capture the visual changes across reasoning steps, avoiding repeated modeling of unchanged content. To align the token budget of each update with the magnitude of visual change, DeltaV introduces a temporal similarity (TSIM) Router, which stops allocating tokens once the marginal reconstruction gain falls below a threshold. To support more diverse and generalizable reasoning, we further construct StructCoT, a large-scale interleaved multimodal reasoning dataset with 1.05M samples spanning 44 task domains. Experiments show that the visual-update paradigm reduces newly generated visual tokens by 55.6\% on average without compromising reconstruction fidelity, and improves multimodal reasoning by 3.3\% over full-image generation. Trained with StructCoT and large-scale multimodal data, DeltaV-2B further outperforms substantially larger open-source models by 8.4\% on in-domain multimodal reasoning evaluations and surpasses the comparable-scale Qwen3-VL-2B by 5.9\% on external multimodal reasoning and understanding benchmarks. Code, models, and StructCoT will be released at https://github.com/Pengjie-W/DeltaV.

</details>

### [50] [VEGAS: Human-Aligned Video Caption Evaluation via Gaze](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08489)
*Shenghui Chen,Po-han Li,Ximeng Sun,Shijia Yang,Emad Barsoum,Zicheng Liu,Sandeep Chinchali,Ufuk Topcu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: VEGAS是一种基于注视分数的训练无关视频描述评估指标，通过测试时的眼动追踪数据采样个性化、符合注意力的文本描述，无需模型重训练即可提升描述与人类关注的匹配度及下游检索性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视觉语言模型生成的视频描述无法捕捉个体观看者的注意力差异，缺乏个性化关注对齐机制。

Method: 提出VEGAS（Video caption Evaluation via GAze Score），一种跨模态信息论指标，利用测试时的眼动（注视）数据通过拒绝采样选择与观看者注意力最匹配的描述，无需模型训练。

Result: 在自我中心活动和教学幻灯片数据集上，VEGAS选择的描述与人类关注点显著对齐，并提升了描述到视频的检索性能。

Abstract (英文): Vision-language models excel at video captioning, yet typically generate descriptions that fail to capture individual viewers' attention. We propose VEGAS (Video caption Evaluation via GAze Score), a training-free metric that leverages test-time gaze to sample personalized, attention-aligned text. It is a cross-modal, information-theoretic metric that quantifies how well a candidate caption matches a viewer's focus. To evaluate VEGAS, we curate a dataset of egocentric activities and instructional slides paired with synchronized gaze and reference annotations. We then select captions based on VEGAS via rejection sampling without model retraining. Experiments show that VEGAS-selected captions align significantly better with human focus and improve downstream caption-to-video retrieval, demonstrating the practical utility of incorporating viewer attention during inference.

### [51] [Cognitive-structured Multimodal Agent for Multimodal Understanding, Generation, and Editing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08497)
*Feng Wang,Canmiao Fu,Zhipeng Huang,Chen Li,Jing Lyu,Ge Li*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出了一种认知结构化的多模态智能体（CMA），通过情景视觉记忆和外化视觉信息，解决了长时多模态对话中的视觉token爆炸和跨轮引用问题。8B参数模型在20轮对话中检索准确率达91.4%，超越32B基线8.2%，推理时间减半。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有统一多模态模型在长时多模态对话中反复将所有历史视觉和文本输入塞入共享上下文窗口，导致视觉token爆炸和跨轮引用不可靠，限制了长时对话能力。

Method: 提出CMA框架，包含三个核心模块：1) 感知抽象引擎（Perceptual Abstraction Engine）进行结构化视觉抽象；2) 认知检索引擎（Cognitive Retrieval Engine）进行跨轮记忆检索；3) 多模态执行控制器（Multimodal Executive Controller）进行自主任务推断和动作规划。同时开发统一场景引擎（Unified Scenario Engine）生成带细粒度检索标注的多轮对话数据，并通过强化学习优化抽象和检索策略。

Result: 8B参数的CMA在20轮对话中检索准确率达91.4%，超越32B基线8.2%；每轮推理时间从23.1秒降至12.7秒；构建了按难度分层的长时视觉对话基准。

Conclusion: 结构化记忆和模块化决策相比 monolithic 参数扩展为长时多模态智能体提供了更可扩展、高效的范式。代码和项目页面已开源。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。该框架可直接应用于遥感领域的多时相影像对话分析。具体方案：1) 将遥感影像的时间序列作为情景记忆存储，支持跨时相变化检测的检索与推理；2) 感知抽象引擎可定制为遥感专用特征提取（如地物分类、变化向量提取）；3) 统一场景引擎可生成遥感领域的多轮问答数据（如"2020年与2023年该区域的植被覆盖变化如何？"），支持强化学习优化；4) 解决遥感长时序分析中因大量影像token导致的上下文窗口溢出问题。

Abstract (英文): Recent unified multimodal models show a single architecture can jointly perform vision/language understanding and image generation/editing. However, they repeatedly feed all historical visual and textual inputs into a shared context window, limiting long-horizon multimodal dialogue due to visual token explosion and unreliable cross-turn referencing. We propose a Cognitive-structured Multimodal Agent that externalizes visual information into an Episodic Visual Memory and selectively reactivates relevant episodes during reasoning. The agent consists of a Perceptual Abstraction Engine for structured visual abstraction, a Cognitive Retrieval Engine for cross-turn memory retrieval, and a Multimodal Executive Controller for autonomous task inference and action planning. To address the lack of turn-level retrieval supervision in existing datasets, we develop a Unified Scenario Engine that programmatically generates structured multi-turn conversations with fine-grained retrieval annotations, enabling reinforcement learning to optimize abstraction and retrieval policies. We also construct a long-horizon visual-dialogue benchmark stratified by difficulty to evaluate episodic visual recall. Our 8B agent achieves 91.4% retrieval accuracy over 20-turn sessions, surpassing 32B baselines by +8.2% while nearly halving per-turn inference time (23.1s -> 12.7s). We further present the Cognitive-structured Multimodal Agent Harness (CMA-Harness), a tool-augmented deployment of the same cognitive structure integrating persistent multimodal memory, web access, image generation/editing/composition tools, and OpenAI-compatible serving. Structured memory and modular decision-making offer a more scalable, efficient paradigm for long-horizon multimodal agents than monolithic parameter scaling. Code: https://github.com/caseclose/cma-harness ; Project page: https://caseclose.github.io/cma-harness/

</details>


### [52] [CT-CLIP Representations for Multimodal Lung Cancer Survival Prediction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08503)
*Sofie Allgöwer,Mikael Johansson,Andreas Hallqvist,Jonas Andersson,Åse Johnsson,Ida Häggström,Jennifer Alvén*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本研究评估了领域特定的基础模型CT-CLIP作为特征提取器，在数据受限的肺癌预后预测场景中，结合冷冻编码器和轻量级生存头，在多模态生存预测中取得了优于临床基线且可与其他多模态方法媲美的效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 肺癌预后预测对治疗规划至关重要，但深度学习生存模型常受限于缺乏带有可靠结果数据的精心筛选影像队列。本研究旨在探索能否利用领域特定的基础模型表征，在数据受限的临床环境中实现多模态生存预测。

Method: 采用CT-CLIP作为预训练基础模型，从242名肺癌患者的预处理CT图像和临床变量中提取特征。评估了三种适应策略：冷冻编码器、全参数微调和低秩适应（LoRA），并结合模态消融实验，与临床基线和多模态基线进行比较。

Result: 冷冻CT-CLIP模型结合可训练的轻量级生存头，性能优于临床基线，与其他多模态方法相比表现相当或更优，并能将患者区分为具有临床意义的高风险和低风险组。

Conclusion: 领域特定的基础模型CT-CLIP在数据受限的临床场景下，通过冷冻编码器加轻量生存头的策略，能够有效进行多模态肺癌生存预测，降低了对大规模标注数据集的依赖。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感领域同样面临标注数据稀缺的问题，CT-CLIP的冷冻编码器+轻量头策略可直接迁移至遥感图像（如高分辨率卫星影像）与地理/气象多模态数据的生存/灾害预测任务中。具体方案：1）使用遥感预训练基础模型（如SatMAE、SwinUNETR等遥感领域基础模型）替代CT-CLIP作为特征提取器；2）结合遥感影像与地面观测数据（如气象、地形等）构建多模态输入；3）在小型标注遥感数据集上采用冷冻编码器+轻量预测头或LoRA微调，实现数据受限条件下的高效预测。

Abstract (英文): Accurate prognosis prediction is important for treatment planning in lung cancer, but deep learning-driven survival modelling is often limited by the scarcity of curated imaging cohorts with reliable outcome data. This study evaluates whether representations from a domain-specific foundation model can be used for multimodal survival prediction in data-constrained clinical settings. We assess the foundation model CT-CLIP as a feature extractor for pretreatment computed tomography images and clinical variables from 242 diagnosed lung cancer patients. The evaluation includes adaptation strategies based on frozen encoders, full fine-tuning, and low-rank adaptation, together with modality ablations and comparisons with clinical and multimodal baselines. The results show that a frozen CT-CLIP model combined with a trainable lightweight survival head outperforms the clinical baseline and achieves comparable or improved performance relative to other multimodal approaches, and separates patients into clinically meaningful high- and low-risk groups.

### [53] [Do Egocentric Video-Language Models Capture Both Hand- and Object-Centric Cues?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08514)
*Masatoshi Tateno,Alexandros Stergiou,Risa Shinoda,Yoichi Sato,Dima Damen*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出一种新的手-物交互（HOI）识别学习范式，包含手-物掩码训练和HOI动态感知解码器，以解决现有视频-语言模型依赖虚假相关性的问题。同时引入CI-HOI评估基准和DEHOI测试集，用于独立评估模型对手部与物体线索的推理能力。实验表明该方法在多个任务上优于现有模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视频-语言模型在HOI识别中常利用手、物体或环境背景间的虚假相关性（shortcut），而非真正基于手和物体的外观与动态进行推理，导致泛化能力不足。

Method: (i) 手-物掩码训练（hand-object masked training）：从部分手或物体观测中学习鲁棒推理；(ii) HOI动态感知解码器（HOI-dynamics-aware decoder）：通过辅助预测手和物体的位置与语义，显式学习以手和物体为中心的嵌入表示，增强对两类线索的敏感性。

Result: 在DEHOI测试集、标准动作识别、物体状态识别以及机器人操作动作识别等任务上，该方法均优于现有模型，实现了更鲁棒的HOI理解。

Conclusion: 结合掩码训练与动态感知解码器的学习范式能更有效地利用手部和物体中心信息，克服虚假相关性，提升HOI识别模型的泛化性与鲁棒性。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：75%。遥感场景中目标-背景交互（如车辆-道路、船舶-水面）的识别同样易受背景虚假相关性干扰，可将本文的手-物掩码训练思想迁移为"目标-上下文掩码训练"，结合动态感知解码器预测目标位置与语义，增强遥感模型对目标外观与运动信息的依赖，减少对背景的捷径学习。

Abstract (英文): Hand-object interaction (HOI) recognition requires capturing both hand manipulations and object transformations. However, existing video-language models often fall into shortcuts by relying on spurious correlations among hands, objects, or environmental context, rather than reasoning from the appearance and dynamics of hands and objects themselves. To address this limitation, we propose a new learning paradigm that combines (i) hand-object masked training, which enables robust reasoning from partial hand or object observations, and (ii) an HOI-dynamics-aware decoder that explicitly learns hand- and object-centric embeddings through auxiliary predictions of their locations and semantics, enhancing sensitivity to both cues. To systematically evaluate such cue-specific reasoning, we introduce Cue-Isolated HOI (CI-HOI), a new evaluation that assesses models' ability to predict actions from hand- and object-related cues independently. To enable CI-HOI, we curate the DEHOI testbed, which separates hand- and object-related observations for disentangled HOI evaluation through inpainting. Using DEHOI, we demonstrate both quantitatively and qualitatively that our training strategy exploits hand- and object-centric information more effectively than existing models. Our approach improves over existing models on DEHOI, standard action recognition, object state recognition, and even robot manipulation action recognition, leading to more robust HOI understanding.

### [54] [Beyond wheelchairs and blindfolds: Investigating disability stereotypes in T2I models with INCLUDE-BENCH](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08515)
*Sophia Lichtenberg,Albert Gatt,Judith Masthoff*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出INCLUDE-BENCH基准，首个大规模评估文生图模型在残疾相关偏见方面的基准，包含119K生成图像，评估15个开源和2个闭源模型，发现模型普遍将残疾描绘为轮椅使用者、缺乏多样性、强化刻板印象，并引入SCM分数证明模型反映现实世界的刻板关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建INCLUDE-BENCH基准，包含119K生成图像，跨多个偏见维度设计提示词，涵盖静态和动态上下文；引入Stereotype Content Model (SCM)分数定量评估模型反映现实刻板关联的程度；评估15个开源和2个闭源T2I模型。

Result: (1) 行动障碍和默认残疾提示在所有模型中普遍生成轮椅图像；(2) 残疾条件下的生成图像多样性显著更低；(3) 刻板印象式的描绘具有更强的残疾-文本对齐；(4) T2I模型反映现实世界中的刻板关联（由SCM分数支持）。

Conclusion: 当前T2I模型在残疾表征方面存在系统性偏见，倾向于单一化、刻板化的描绘，缺乏对残疾多样性的真实反映；INCLUDE-BENCH为未来模型评估和缓解残疾偏见提供了标准化工具。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。该工作为遥感领域生成式模型（如文本生成遥感图像、遥感视觉语言模型）的偏见评估提供了方法论框架：(1) 可直接迁移INCLUDE-BENCH的提示词设计方案，构建遥感场景下针对特定群体（如不同地貌类型、建筑风格、土地利用类别）的表征公平性基准；(2) SCM分数可适配用于评估遥感生成模型是否过度偏向某些典型场景（如城市而非乡村、发达地区而非欠发达地区）；(3) 遥感数据中同样存在对特定区域/人群的系统性表征偏差（如忽视边缘地带），该方法的偏见评估框架可有效支撑遥感AI公平性研究。

Abstract (英文): Text-to-image (T2I) models have been shown to exhibit social biases. Prior work has mainly focused on gender, skin tone, and cultural representation within restricted occupational associations, and emerging benchmarks increasingly incorporate these dimensions. However, disability remains systematically underexplored. Current evaluation practices often fail to align with sociologically grounded definitions of stereotyping, limiting principled assessment of representational harms toward people with disabilities (PWD). To address this, we introduce INCLUDE-BENCH, the first large-scale benchmark for evaluating disability-related bias in T2I models. INCLUDE-BENCH comprises 119K generated images based on prompt design across multiple bias dimensions and both static and dynamic contexts. We evaluate 15 open-source and 2 closed-source models. Our key findings reveal that: (1) mobility-impaired and default disability prompts predominantly yield wheelchair depictions across all models; (2) disability-conditioned generations consistently exhibit less diversity; (3) stereotypical portrayals demonstrate stronger disability-text alignment; and (4) we introduce the Stereotype Content Model (SCM) Score, demonstrating that T2I models reflect real-world stereotypical associations.

### [55] [Whareformer: Learning to Track What is Where in Long Egocentric Videos](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08537)
*Jacob Chalk,Saptarshi Sinha,Dima Damen,Yannis Kalantidis,Diane Larlus*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出首个基于学习的OSNOM任务解决方案Whareformer，利用Transformer架构联合推理物体外观和3D位置，通过可更新记忆和新轨迹令牌实现视频中物体（包括移出视野或被遮挡时）的持续追踪，在少量训练数据下取得SOTA性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: OSNOM任务旨在解决第一人称视频中由佩戴者移动的物体在离开视野或严重遮挡后仍需持续追踪的问题，现有方法缺乏学习能力，因此需要首个基于学习的解决方案。

Method: 提出Whareformer，一种基于Transformer的模型，包含两个组件：可更新的已建立轨迹记忆和轨迹分配模块。模型联合推理物体外观（what）和更新的3D位置（where），并采用专用New Track令牌来处理新出现的物体。

Result: 仅用56个视频训练，在EPIC-KITCHENS-100（未见视频）、IT3DEgo和HD-EPIC三个数据集的260个长测试视频上达到SOTA性能，显著优于先前工作。

Conclusion: Whareformer通过相对距离和演化轨迹表示的设计选择，在少量训练数据下实现了高效的学习和泛化能力，验证了基于学习的方案在OSNOM任务上的有效性。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：75%。遥感视频中目标（如车辆、船只）常因云层遮挡或移出传感器范围而丢失，可借鉴Whareformer的联合外观-3D位置推理和可更新记忆机制，实现遥感视频中目标跨视野/跨遮挡的持续跟踪；其中的New Track令牌可适配遥感场景中突然出现的新目标。

Abstract (英文): The recently established 'Out of Sight, Not out of Mind' (OSNOM) task for egocentric videos focuses on tracking objects that are moved by the camera wearer, online, maintaining knowledge of instance locations throughout the video even when they leave the field of view or become heavily occluded. In this paper, we propose the first learning-based solution to the OSNOM task: Whareformer, a transformer-based model with two components: an updatable memory of established tracks and a track assignment module that associates observations with existing tracks in a feed-forward manner. Whareformer jointly reasons over evolving object appearance (what) and updated 3D location (where), and employs a dedicated New Track token to reason about novel objects.
  Thanks to its design choices of using relative distances and evolving track representations, Whareformer is trained on a small set of 56 videos but achieves SOTA performance on 260 long test videos from three datasets: EPIC-KITCHENS-100 (unseen videos), IT3DEgo, and HD-EPIC, with significant absolute improvements over prior work.

### [56] [VocaDet: Sample-Driven Open-Vocabulary Object Detection and Segmentation via Visual Tokenization and Vector Database Retrieval](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08541)
*ZhiXin Sun*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: VocaDet是一个基于样本驱动的开放词汇目标检测与分割框架，通过将连续视觉表示转化为离散视觉词汇，并利用向量数据库进行可扩展的检索式识别，无需模型重新训练即可从用户提供的正负样本集合中学习目标概念。在UA-DETRAC数据集上验证了其有效性和持续扩展能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有开放词汇检测方法依赖文本提示、有限视觉示例或昂贵的特征匹配过程，难以扩展到大规模且持续增长的物体库。本文旨在提出一种无需模型重训练、可直接从用户提供的正负样本集合中学习目标概念的检测与分割框架。

Method: 采用DINOv3作为视觉特征提取器，通过凝聚聚类（agglomerative clustering）和自适应聚类敏感性生成多粒度视觉token；将视觉token与位置去偏表示和空间拓扑信息一起存入向量数据库作为可扩展的目标记忆；推理时将查询图像转化为视觉token，与存储的目标记忆进行高效匹配，并引入背景过滤机制去除频繁出现的背景模式。

Result: 在UA-DETRAC数据集上，VocaDet无需传统检测器训练即可实现有效的开放词汇检测性能，并支持随着正负样本积累而持续扩展的识别能力。

Conclusion: 本文验证了基于离散视觉词汇和向量数据库检索的样本驱动开放词汇检测框架的有效性，为大规模、持续扩展的物体识别提供了一种无需重训练的可扩展解决方案。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感场景中存在大量细粒度目标（如不同型号的飞机、船只、车辆）且类别持续增加，VocaDet的样本驱动机制无需重新训练即可扩展类别，非常适合遥感领域的动态目标识别需求。具体方案：1) 将DINOv3替换为遥感预训练的视觉基础模型（如RSGPT、RemoteCLIP的特征提取器）以提升对遥感目标的特征判别力；2) 利用遥感影像的GPS坐标信息增强空间拓扑编码，提升目标定位精度；3) 结合遥感场景中的背景多样性（如不同季节、光照条件）优化背景过滤机制，减少误检。

Abstract (英文): Open-vocabulary object detection and segmentation aim to recognize arbitrary objects beyond predefined categories. Although recent vision-language and reference-based approaches have significantly advanced this field, they often rely on text prompts, limited visual examples, or expensive feature matching procedures, making them difficult to scale to large and continuously expanding object repositories. In this work, we propose VocaDet, a sample-driven open-vocabulary object detection and segmentation framework that learns object concepts directly from user-provided positive and negative sample collections without model retraining. The key idea is to transform continuous visual representations into discrete visual vocabularies and perform efficient retrieval-based recognition through a scalable vector database. Specifically, we employ DINOv3 as the visual feature extractor and apply agglomerative clustering with adaptive clustering sensitivity to generate multi-granularity visual tokens. These visual tokens, together with position-debiased representations and spatial topology information, are stored as expandable object memories in a vector database. During inference, query images are converted into visual tokens and efficiently matched against the stored object memories for object localization and segmentation. Furthermore, a background filtering mechanism is introduced to remove frequently occurring background patterns and reduce redundant retrieval operations in practical fixed-camera scenarios. Experiments on the UA-DETRAC dataset demonstrate that VocaDet achieves effective open-vocabulary detection performance without conventional detector training, while supporting continuously expandable recognition capability as additional positive and negative samples are accumulated.

### [57] [Switch-Reasoner: Learn When to Think in Multitask Mixtures via Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08572)
*Yiyang Fang,Pei Fu,Jinjie Li,Jian Liang,Wenke Huang,Ruijie Luo,Shaojie Zhang,Jian Luan,Yi R. Fung,Mang Ye*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出Switch-Reasoner框架，基于GRPO让多模态大模型自适应选择是否进行显式推理，通过双层调节机制平衡推理与直接回答，在11个任务上实现了更好的精度-效率权衡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有MLLM采用固定的"先思考再回答"范式，在异构多任务场景下效率低下——简单输入不需要显式推理，困难输入则需要；且后训练中学"何时思考"不稳定，不平衡的rollout会导致模型倾向于总是思考或总是直接回答。

Method: 提出Switch-Reasoner框架：1) 将思考视为虚拟工具调用，模型可选择直接回答或先调用显式推理再回答；2) 采用GRPO进行训练；3) 引入双层调节机制——全局层平衡两种模式的整体使用比例，样本层基于两种选择的相对收益提供监督信号，从而稳定决策学习。

Result: 在11个多模态任务上的实验表明，Switch-Reasoner减少了不必要的推理同时保持强性能，实现了更好的精度-效率权衡。

Conclusion: 通过自适应推理模式选择，可以有效提升MLLM在多任务场景下的效率，双层调节机制是稳定决策学习的关键。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感领域存在大量异构任务（如场景分类、目标检测、变化检测、语义分割），不同任务对推理深度的需求差异显著。具体交叉方案：1) 将Switch-Reasoner应用于遥感MLLM，使模型在简单场景分类任务上直接输出，在复杂变化检测或目标识别任务上调用显式推理；2) 引入遥感领域特有的"空间推理"作为工具调用选项（如地理空间关系推理、多时相分析）；3) 利用GRPO框架优化遥感任务间的学习平衡，避免模型在某些简单视觉任务上过度推理。

Abstract (英文): Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) often follow a fixed Think-then-Answer paradigm, which is inefficient in heterogeneous multitask settings because simple inputs may not require explicit reasoning while difficult ones can benefit substantially from it. Learning when to think is also unstable during post-training, where imbalanced rollouts can drive the model toward always-thinking or always-direct behavior. We propose Switch-Reasoner, a GRPO-based framework that learns to adaptively select reasoning modes for MLLMs. It treats thinking as a virtual tool invocation and allows the model to either answer directly or invoke explicit reasoning before answering. To stabilize this decision, we introduce a dual-level regulation mechanism that balances the overall use of Thinking Mode and Direct Mode while providing sample-level supervision based on the relative benefit of the two choices. Experiments on 11 multimodal tasks show that Switch-Reasoner reduces unnecessary reasoning while maintaining strong performance, achieving a better accuracy-efficiency trade-off.

</details>


### [58] [When Structured Sparse Autoencoders Learn Consistent Concepts Across Modalities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08605)
*Weiduo Liao,Yunqiao Yang,Ying Wei*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出结构化稀疏自编码器(S²AE)，通过在视觉模态中引入语义和空间一致性约束（基于Transformer注意力相似性和空间邻近性对图像块分组，并设计组间独占稀疏与组内组稀疏正则化），解决了视觉-语言模型中稀疏自编码器难以学习模态一致概念的问题。在Qwen2.5-VL-7B-Instruct模型上，该方法在语义对齐(mIoU)上平均提升6.06%，表示效率(更低的l0范数)提升60.81，重构保真度(解释方差>99%)几乎无损，跨模态分析表明视觉结构先验增强了神经元单语义性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在视觉-语言模型(VLM)中，传统的稀疏自编码器(SAE)难以学习到模态一致的概念，视觉模态中的概念往往呈现碎片化覆盖（即不连续的区域），导致多模态特征缺乏语义连贯性与可解释性。

Method: 提出结构化稀疏自编码器(S²AE)，首先基于Transformer注意力相似性和空间邻近性对图像块进行分组，然后在训练SAE时引入结构化稀疏正则化，包含两部分：组间独占稀疏(exclusive sparsity)用于解耦不同组的概念，组内组稀疏(group sparsity)用于保持组内概念的一致性，从而驱动SAE的潜在神经元专注于不同的、语义基础一致的概念。

Result: 在Qwen2.5-VL-7B-Instruct模型上，语义对齐(mIoU)平均提升6.06%，表示效率(l0范数)提升60.81，解释方差>99%保持近乎完美重构；跨模态分析中，语义一致性平均提升3.08%，单语义性得分平均提升2.37%。

Conclusion: S²AE通过视觉结构先验有效地增强了多模态特征的神经元单语义性，促进了更连贯和更解耦的多模态表示，解决了VLM中SAE学习模态一致概念的难题。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感图像具有高度结构化特征（如地物边界明确、空间分布规律性强），S²AE基于注意力相似性和空间邻近性进行分组的思路非常适合遥感场景。具体方案：(1)利用遥感影像的地理空间先验（如道路、建筑物、植被区域的连续性）增强分组质量，替代原始分组中的纯注意力相似性；(2)稀疏正则化可应用于遥感多模态模型（如遥感图像-文本描述、遥感图像-LiDAR点云）的特征对齐与解耦；(3)可用于遥感变化检测中的语义一致特征提取，减少不同时相影像间的概念碎片化问题。

Abstract (英文): Sparse autoencoders (SAEs) have emerged as a promising technique for mechanistic interpretability by learning a set of sparse latent features in large models, each of which encodes a distinct concept. However, in vision-language models (VLMs), vanilla SAEs struggle to learn modality-consistent concepts, with concepts often exhibiting fragmented coverage (i.e., disjoint regions) in the visual modality. To address this challenge, we propose a Structured Sparse AutoEncoder ($S^2AE$) that enforces concept consistency from both semantic and spatial perspectives in the visual modality. Specifically, we group image patches based on Transformer attention similarity and spatial proximity, and introduce a structured sparsity regularization when training the vanilla SAE. The regularization consists of exclusive sparsity for inter-group concept disentanglement and group sparsity for intra-group concept consistency, which drives the latent neurons by SAEs to specialize in distinct, semantically grounded concepts. Evaluated on the \texttt{Qwen2.5-VL-7B-Instruct} model, the method achieves 6.06% average improvement in semantic alignment (mIoU) and 60.81 in representational efficiency (lower l0 norm) while maintaining near-perfect reconstruction fidelity with an Explained Variance above 99%. Cross-modal analysis further demonstrates that $S^2AE$ enhances neuronal monosemanticity by this visual structural prior, achieving a 3.08% average gain in semantic consistency and a 2.37% average gain in monosemanticity scores for both modalities of multimodal features, thereby fostering more coherent and disentangled representations.

</details>


### [59] [Do Transformations Reveal the Truth? Generative Residual Learning for Generalized AI-Generated Image Detection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08674)
*Kutub Uddin,Nusrat Tasnim,Awais Khan,Mohammad Umar Farooq,Khalid Malik*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出 GenRes 和 GenRes++ 框架，通过神经张量网络进行生成残差学习，并结合可学习的注意力机制聚合多变换样本的关系特征，利用 PE-Core 特征提取器，有效检测 AI 生成图像，在多个基准数据集上优于现有方法。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生成式 AI 的快速发展使得深度伪造媒体高度逼真，带来了虚假信息、数字身份盗窃、欺诈和操纵公众舆论等严重威胁。由于生成方法的多样性和伪影的细微性，AI生成图像检测面临可靠挑战。

Method: 提出 GenRes 框架，通过神经张量网络对原始样本与变换样本之间的细粒度关系特征进行生成残差学习以增强泛化能力；针对多生成变换场景，提出 GenRes++，采用可学习的注意力机制聚合多个变换样本的关系特征，使模型关注最具信息量的线索。两者均使用 PE-Core 作为特征提取器，提供通用且语义丰富的嵌入以提升跨域性能。

Result: 在多个基准数据集上的综合实验表明，提出的 GenRes++ 方法优于现有方法。

Conclusion: GenRes 系列框架通过生成残差学习和注意力机制有效提升了 AI 生成图像检测的泛化能力和跨域性能，能够检测未见过的生成方法产生的图像。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感图像中存在大量由 GAN、扩散模型等生成的伪造地貌或地物目标，可借鉴 GenRes 的生成残差学习框架用于遥感伪造图像检测。具体方案：1) 将 PE-Core 替换为遥感领域预训练骨干（如 ResNet-RS、Swin Transformer），保留神经张量网络的关系建模能力；2) 针对遥感场景（多光谱、多尺度、不同分辨率），扩展 GenRes++ 的注意力机制以融合多波段变换样本的特征；3) 可应用于遥感数据集的真伪鉴别、对抗样本防御以及图像生成溯源。

Abstract (英文): The rapid advancement of generative AI has enabled the creation of highly realistic deepfake media, posing significant threats, including misinformation, digital identity theft, fraud, and manipulation of public opinion. AI-generated image (AIGI) detection is reliably challenging due to the diversity of generative methods and the subtle artifacts they leave behind. In this work, we propose GenRes, a novel framework for generative residual learning via a neural tensor network, which models fine-grained relational features between original and transformed samples to enhance generalization. To address scenarios involving multiple generative transformations, we introduce GenRes++, which employs a learnable attention mechanism to aggregate relational features across multiple transformed samples and enables the model to focus on the most informative cues. Both models leverage PE-Core as a feature extractor, providing generalized and semantically rich embeddings that improve cross-domain performance and enable the detection of AIGI generated by unseen methods. Comprehensive experiments on multiple benchmark datasets demonstrate that the proposed GenRes++ approach outperforms existing methods.

### [60] [Multi-Resolution Feature Stem for Diabetic Retinopathy lesion segmentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08679)
*Indranil Dutta,Taehee Jeong*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文发现糖尿病视网膜病变分割中，提高输入分辨率会改善微小动脉瘤的分割，但意外地降低了较大出血灶的性能。为解决这一分辨率权衡问题，提出了一种多分辨率特征茎（Multi-Resolution Feature Stem），将其与UNet++骨干集成，实现多尺度并行处理，在保持上下文信息的同时捕获细粒度细节。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: DR病变大小差异巨大（从微小的微动脉瘤到大面积出血和渗出），高分辨率对小病变重要但可能对大病变有害，现有研究缺乏对输入分辨率与不同病变类型之间复杂关系的系统探究。

Method: 1) 系统实验：在U-Net、UNet++、Vision Transformers、DeepLabV3+等多种架构上对比512×512和1024×512分辨率。2) 提出Multi-Resolution Feature Stem：一种输入级金字塔结构，集成到UNet++骨干中，并行处理多个尺度。

Result: 验证了提高分辨率对微动脉瘤有利但对大出血有害这一反直觉现象；提出的多分辨率特征茎有效解决了这一分辨率权衡问题。

Conclusion: 挑战了"高分辨率总是有益的"常见假设，提供了一种参数高效、能同时兼顾不同尺度病变分割需求的实用架构。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：90%。遥感图像中目标尺度差异极大（如小目标车辆与大面积水体/建筑区），与DR病变的尺度多样性高度相似。具体方案：1) 将Multi-Resolution Feature Stem直接迁移至遥感语义分割模型（如U-Net、DeepLabV3+），用于处理遥感图像中多尺度地物分割。2) 在遥感变化检测任务中，不同尺度的变化目标（小范围新建建筑 vs 大面积植被变化）也可受益于此方法。3) MFS可作为即插即用模块嵌入遥感专用分割网络（如ResUNet、MANet），提升多尺度分割性能而几乎不增加参数量。

Abstract (英文): Diabetic Retinopathy (DR) is a leading cause of preventable blindness worldwide, requiring automated lesion segmentation using deep learning models for early detection and monitoring. However, DR lesions vary dramatically in size from tiny microaneurysms to large hemorrhages and exudates. This variability creates conflicting demands on the model architecture and input resolution, posing a challenge for effective design. This work investigates the impact of input resolution on different lesion types. Through systematic experimentation with multiple architectures (U-Net, UNet++, Vision Transformers, DeepLabV3+) at $512 \times 512$ and $1024 \times 1024$ resolutions, we identify a critical, counter-intuitive phenomenon where increasing input resolution has opposing effects on different lesion types. We demonstrate that while higher resolution is essential for resolving fine-grained microaneurysms, it can unexpectedly degrade performance on larger hemorrhages. This finding challenges the common assumption that higher resolution is uniformly beneficial. To address this, we propose a novel Multi-Resolution Feature Stem, an input-level pyramid integrated with a UNet++ backbone. This architecture processes multiple scales in parallel, capturing fine-grained details without sacrificing contextual information. This work contributes crucial empirical evidence of this complex, resolution-dependent behavior and a practical, parameter-efficient architecture that successfully resolves this trade-off.

### [61] [SAM-MT: Real-Time Interactive Multi-Target Video Segmentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08688)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有VOS方法在多目标场景下需为每个目标复制单目标处理流程，导致FPS下降且延迟随目标数增加而无限增长。

Method: 1) 显式查询表征不同目标 + 共享全局上下文表示；2) 解耦掩码注意力避免跨目标干扰；3) 稀疏记忆实现稳定时序演化；4) 遮挡处理与重叠预防策略。

Result: 10个目标下>36 FPS，延迟与目标数量解耦，性能与SAM2单目标基线持平。

Conclusion: 成功将多目标VOS的延迟与目标数量解耦，在实时性和分割性能之间取得良好平衡。

Abstract (英文): Modern Video Object Segmentation (VOS) involves tracking and segmenting user-specified targets. While recent approaches have achieved remarkable performance in single-target scenarios, extending them to multi-target settings typically involves replicating the single-target processing for each individual object, resulting in reduced frame rates (FPS) with unbounded latency as target count increases. Built upon Segment Anything 2 (SAM2), we propose SAM-MT, which addresses this by transforming the model into an interactive framework for real-time Multi-Target video segmentation. SAM-MT uses explicit queries to represent different individual targets, in parallel with a shared representation for global context. It employs decoupled masked attention to keep individual identities distinct from cross-target interference, and sparse memory for stable temporal evolution, along with specialized strategies for occlusion handling and overlap prevention. SAM-MT successfully decouples latency from the number of targets, achieving real-time speed on par with single-target baselines (>36 FPS for 10 targets) while maintaining SAM2's robust video segmentation performance.

*Wenbo Xu,Zhimin Chen,Xiaojie Liang,Hengrui Liu,Wei Lu*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: HumanForge是一个大规模、多范式的人体中心视频伪造数据集，结合Gen2Anno多智能体流水线自动生成18K+高质量伪造视频片段及结构化标注。基准测试表明现有检测器和多模态大模型在该数据集上的零样本泛化与细粒度推理仍面临显著挑战。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract (英文): Rapid advancements in video diffusion models and temporal editing tools have enabled the generation of highly realistic human-centric videos, posing unprecedented challenges to digital content forensics. Existing benchmarks primarily focus on either face-swapping or global text-to-video synthesis, overlooking the crucial dimensions of human-object or human-human interactions and multi-modal alignment. To address these limitations, we introduce HumanForge, a unified, large-scale, and multi-paradigm human-centric video forgery dataset. To construct and annotate this dataset without labor-intensive manual labeling or hallucinated monolithic prompts, we propose Gen2Anno, a modular active multi-agent pipeline built on LangGraph. Gen2Anno coordinates six specialized agents-ranging from source profiling to MoE-based reference analysis and closed-loop forensic verification-to generate over 18K high-fidelity video segments and produce structured, contrastive omni-annotations containing binary decisions, fine-grained artifact categories, and spatio-temporal localization. Code and dataset will be publicly released.

Abstract (英文): Accurate 3D terrain maps are essential for emergency response when assessing wildfire hazards. However, wildfire-prone regions often span vast areas where conventional reconstruction methods underperform. Airborne LiDAR systems provide high-resolution terrain data, but they are expensive and infrequently updated. Image-based methods offer a lower-cost alternative, but struggle due to sparse visual features and limited image overlap. We propose a multi-modal reconstruction framework leveraging outdated Digital Elevation Models (DEMs) as geometric priors for image-based 3D reconstruction. Our key innovation is physics-based pixel-pixel alignment between images and DEM data, dramatically reducing computational complexity by eliminating expensive feature matching procedures. *Ayda Eghbalian,Kevin Desai*

TL;DR: 本文提出BioModule，一种轻量级时序Transformer插件，可附加在任何3D姿态估计器下游，从标准17关节点骨架预测生物力学属性。通过构建Human3.6M与Human3.6Mplus的对齐数据集进行训练，实现了从视觉姿态估计到生物力学有意义的人体运动分析的模块化桥梁。

Abstract (英文): Recent progress in 3D human pose estimation has made markerless recovery of skeletal motion increasingly accurate and scalable. In this work, we propose BioModule, a lightweight plug-in temporal transformer that attaches downstream of any 3D pose estimator and predicts biomechanical attributes from standard 17-joint 3D skeletons. BioModule is estimator-agnostic and requires no modification of the upstream pose model, enabling existing pose estimators to be extended toward physically interpretable motion analysis.
  To train and evaluate BioModule, we construct a large-scale aligned dataset pairing Human3.6M video and 3D keypoints with the biomechanical label space of Human3.6Mplus. We establish and verify anatomical correspondence between coordinate systems of the two datasets, enabling frame-accurate cross-modal supervision. Using this aligned supervision, BioModule predicts biomechanical quantities. We further benchmark BioModule across seven state-of-the-art 3D pose estimators, providing the first systematic analysis of how upstream pose estimation quality propagates to downstream biomechanical prediction fidelity. The results position BioModule as a compact, modular bridge between vision-based pose estimation and biomechanically meaningful human motion analysis.

### [65] [WaspMOT: A Benchmark for Long-Term Multi-Object Tracking of Trichogramma Wasps](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08729)
*Tomasz Stanczyk,Yuan Gao,Hardik Agarwal,Seongroo Yoon,Tiantao Zhang,Vincent Calcagno,Francois Bremond*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有MOT基准以短视频序列为主，无法充分评估长时间身份保持能力。为填补这一空白，作者引入WaspMOT，通过长时间（超8分钟）的赤眼蜂跟踪实验来暴露传统数据集无法观察到的长时关联问题。

Method: 构建了一个闭环跟踪场景数据集：10段序列，每段约12,000帧，所有个体全程存在，需跨数千帧保持身份一致。提供密集MOTChallenge标注和oracle检测以隔离关联性能。采用统一的跟踪-检测协议评估ByteTrack、BoT-SORT、C-BIoU、OC-SORT和McByte五种方法，并提出空间轨迹片段拼接基线。

Result: 所有评估方法均出现显著的轨迹碎片化，即使使用完美检测也表现不佳；简单的空间轨迹片段拼接基线可一致性地提升跟踪性能，表明长时关联任务仍有巨大提升空间。

Conclusion: WaspMOT为研究长时关联提供了新的基准，揭示了传统数据集无法观察到的现有跟踪方法的局限性，为未来改进长期身份保持技术指明了方向。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。该文的长时身份保持问题与遥感中的长时序目标跟踪（如卫星视频中的车辆/飞机长时间跟踪、无人机航拍视频的目标持续监测）高度相关。具体交叉方案：(1) 直接将WaspMOT中的空间轨迹片段拼接方法迁移到遥感长时序视频跟踪任务中，解决因遮挡、旋转导致的目标ID跳变问题；(2) 借鉴WaspMOT的闭环场景设计思路，构建遥感领域的长时闭环跟踪基准（如机场内所有飞机从进港到出港的全过程跟踪）；(3) 将WaspMOT中用于隔离关联性能的oracle检测思想引入遥感评估，区分检测误差与关联误差的贡献。

Abstract (英文): Multi-object tracking (MOT) has achieved strong performance on benchmarks dominated by short video sequences. However, such datasets do not adequately evaluate long-term identity preservation, where objects must be tracked consistently over extended durations. We introduce WaspMOT, a benchmark designed to address this gap through long-duration tracking of Trichogramma wasps in controlled ecological experiments. The dataset contains 10 sequences of approximately 12,000 frames each (over 8 minutes at 25 FPS), with dense MOTChallenge annotations and oracle detections to isolate association performance.
  Unlike existing benchmarks, WaspMOT forms a closed-set tracking scenario where all individuals remain present throughout the sequence, requiring consistent identity assignment across thousands of frames despite abrupt jumps, occlusions, and highly similar appearance. We establish a benchmark by evaluating five tracking-by-detection methods, including ByteTrack, BoT-SORT, C-BIoU, OC-SORT, and McByte, under a unified protocol. Results show that all methods suffer from significant trajectory fragmentation, highlighting the difficulty of long-term identity preservation even with perfect detections. A simple spatial tracklet stitching baseline consistently improves performance, indicating that substantial gains remain possible.
  WaspMOT provides a new benchmark for studying long-term association and reveals limitations of current tracking approaches that are not observable on conventional datasets. The benchmark will be made publicly available at the project repository: https://github.com/tstanczyk95/WaspMOT/ .

</details>


### [66] [OpenCoF: Learning to Reason Through Video Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08763)
*Xinyan Chen,Ziyu Guo,Renrui Zhang,Dongzhi Jiang,Hongsheng Li*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出OpenCoF框架，包含OpenCoF-17K推理视频数据集和基于Wan2.2微调的Wan-CoF模型，通过时间帧链（Chain-of-Frame）推理实现视频生成中的逻辑推理能力，并引入视觉和文本推理token机制提升时空推理性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视频生成模型主要基于通用视频语料训练，缺乏针对Chain-of-Frame推理的多样化监督数据和专门设计，因此需要构建专门的推理视频数据集和模型来探索时间帧推理能力。

Method: 1) 构建OpenCoF-17K数据集，涵盖11个任务族；2) 在Wan2.2-I2V-A14B基础上微调得到Wan-CoF；3) 设计视觉推理token和文本推理token分别捕获低层视觉线索和高层语义先验，以支持时空推理。

Result: 在四个视频推理基准上，Wan-CoF相比基线Wan2.2-I2V-A14B取得显著提升；通过注意力分析和性能对比验证了推理token机制在模型深度、去噪步数、空间和时间维度上的有效性。

Conclusion: 更强的视频推理能力需要广泛的时间监督和显式的中间推理状态组织机制，开源数据集、模型和代码以促进推理导向的视频生成研究。

Abstract (英文): Reasoning has become a core capability for large models, especially when reliable decisions require understanding logical consequences. Recent video generation models offer a reasoning path distinct from previous Chain-of-Thought (CoT): reasoning can unfold through temporally connected frames, known as Chain-of-Frame (CoF) reasoning. However, existing video generators are primarily trained on general video corpora, still lacking diverse supervision and dedicated designs for CoF reasoning. To address this gap, we introduce OpenCoF, a framework comprising the OpenCoF-17K dataset, a reasoning video dataset spanning 11 task families, and Wan-CoF, a fine-tuned video model for studying whether diverse temporal supervision improves CoF behavior. Across four video reasoning benchmarks, Wan-CoF achieves considerable gains over the Wan2.2-I2V-A14B baseline. Building on this, we empirically explore more advanced designs for CoF capabilities, i.e., equipping the model with visual and textual reasoning tokens. This mechanism respectively captures low-level visual cues and high-level semantic priors for spatial and temporal reasoning. Through performance comparisons and attention analysis, we examine how these tokens contribute across model depth, denoising steps, space, and time. Our results suggest that stronger video reasoning requires both broad temporal supervision and explicit mechanisms for organizing intermediate reasoning state. We open-source the dataset, model, and code to facilitate future research on reasoning-oriented video generation.

Abstract (英文): In this work, we present Canvas360, a two-stage framework for in-context panoramic generation that combines geometry-aware pretraining with downstream task-specific fine-tuning. To address the lack of large-scale, high-quality training data tailored to in-context panoramic tasks, we propose Canvas360Dataset, a collection of 1M high-quality paired panoramic samples for style transfer, inpainting, outpainting, and editing, enabling effective supervision across diverse in-context generation scenarios. On the modeling side, Canvas360 enhances text-to-panorama generation through parallel depth generation, velocity circular padding, and similarity loss regularization, enabling the model to learn geometry-aware representations, capture object distortion details, and improve geometric consistency and global coherence. Furthermore, empowered by strong panoramic priors, Canvas360 enables a unified in-context panoramic generation framework that supports diverse downstream tasks via token-level concatenation, surpassing prior methods in both task coverage and modeling flexibility. Extensive experiments show that Canvas360 improves panoramic image fidelity, achieving particularly strong performance on the panorama-specific FAED metric and competitive or leading results across the reported quantitative evaluations. More information can be found on our project page: https://zry000.github.io/Canvas360/

### [68] [OPSD-V: On-Policy Self-Distillation for Post-Training Few-Step Autoregressive Video Generators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08766)
*Hongyu Liu,Chun Wang,Feng Gao,Xuanhua He,Yue Ma,Ziyu Wan,Yong Zhang,Xiaoming Wei,Qifeng Chen*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 提出OPSD-V，一种基于同策略自蒸馏的后训练范式，用于改进少步自回归视频扩散模型的长视频生成质量，通过引入真实长视频作为时间上下文并提供密集轨迹级监督，在不改变推理机制的情况下减少误差累积并增强运动动态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有少步自回归视频生成器虽能低延迟生成长视频，但在长自回归展开过程中存在误差累积和运动动态弱化的问题。

Method: 采用同策略自蒸馏范式：学生模型遵循推理时的自回归展开方式，基于自身生成的KV缓存生成每个片段；教师模型在同一去噪状态下评估，但使用更干净的、由真实视频上下文替代旧历史信息的自回归一致性时间缓存，从而提供密集的去噪级校正目标。

Result: 在Self-Forcing和LongLive等少步自回归视频模型上取得一致改进，视觉质量、运动动态和VBenchLong分数均有提升。用户研究中，OPSD-V在66.0%的整体偏好判断中优于基线模型（排除平局时为82.5%）。

Conclusion: OPSD-V通过同策略自蒸馏有效缓解了少步自回归视频扩散模型的长时序退化问题，且不改变采样器、去噪步数或推理缓存机制，是一种轻量级且有效的后训练改进方法。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：75%。遥感视频生成或时序预测任务中，长时序自回归同样面临误差累积问题。OPSD-V的自蒸馏框架可直接迁移至遥感卫星视频生成（如云层运动、植被变化序列），利用真实遥感时序数据作为教师上下文来校正自回归推理。具体方案：将遥感时序影像（如多时相NDVI序列或SAR影像）作为教师缓存中的"真实上下文"，指导学生模型生成长时序遥感变化视频，减少长序列中的漂移和运动失真。需注意遥感数据的地面真值获取成本较高，但少量长时序样本即可提供有效监督。

Abstract (英文): We propose OPSD-V, an on-policy self-distillation paradigm for post-training few-step autoregressive (AR) video diffusion models. Existing few-step AR video generators can produce long videos with low latency, but still suffer from error accumulation and weakened motion dynamics during long autoregressive rollout. OPSD-V reduces long-horizon degradation while preserving the original few-step inference path. The key idea is to introduce real long-video data as temporal context during training and use it to provide dense trajectory-level supervision. Specifically, the student follows the exact inference-time rollout, generating each chunk conditioned on its own previously generated KV cache. In parallel, the teacher is evaluated at the same student-visited denoising states, but uses a cleaner AR-consistent temporal cache in which older history can be replaced by real-video context. This provides dense denoising-level corrective targets under on-policy AR cache dynamics, without changing the sampler, number of denoising steps, or inference-time cache mechanism. We apply OPSD-V to representative few-step AR video models, including Self-Forcing and LongLive. Experiments show consistent improvements in visual quality, motion dynamics, and VBenchLong scores. A user study with 10 participants comparing 20 video pairs shows that OPSD-V is preferred over the base models in 66.0% of overall-preference judgments (82.5% excluding ties).

</details>


### [69] [Geometry and Gradient-based Partitioning for Panoramic Outdoor Reconstruction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08769)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将3DGS扩展到大规模户外场景存在数据采集和计算成本高昂的问题。虽然全景图像（ERP）能通过360°视场降低采集成本，但其全向可见性使得依赖局部相机截锥体的现有分区策略失效，导致分块优化退化为全局训练。

Method: 提出两阶段粗到细框架PanoLOG：1）全局粗阶段：利用天球建模和全景单目深度监督获得可靠几何；2）细化阶段：采用G²PS（几何与梯度引导分区策略），通过视差驱动的不确定性构建自适应包围体，并基于梯度的重要性评分分配相机。

Abstract (英文): Scaling 3D Gaussian Splatting (3DGS) to large outdoor scenes is costly in both data acquisition and computation. Adopting panoramic images with equirectangular projection (ERP) can reduce capture effort via their full $360^{\circ}$ field of view, yet the resulting omnipresent visibility invalidates existing partitioning strategies that rely on local camera frustums, causing block-wise optimization to degenerate into global training. Thus, we propose PanoLOG, a two-stage coarse-to-fine framework equipped with a Geometry and Gradient-based Partitioning Strategy tailored for large-scale panoramic 3DGS reconstruction. In the global coarse stage, PanoLOG leverages sky-sphere modeling and panoramic monocular depth supervision for reliable geometry, while in the refinement stage, G$^2$PS builds adaptive bounding volumes via parallax-driven uncertainty and assigns cameras via gradient-based importance scoring. Furthermore, we construct Pano360, the first benchmark on large-scale panoramic dataset for outdoor scene reconstruction. Extensive experiments demonstrate that G$^2$PS achieves state-of-the-art rendering quality while maintaining scalable, block-parallel training. Our models, training code, and dataset are publicly available.

Abstract (英文): Recovering high-quality video from sparse event streams is a challenging task. Regression methods often blur textures, while existing generative models struggle with long-term stability. We propose LongE2V, a novel approach that leverages pre-trained video diffusion priors to jointly handle event-based video reconstruction, prediction, and frame interpolation. By fine-tuning a foundational video model, our approach achieves high data efficiency and superior perceptual quality. We introduce Autoregressive Unrolling and Adaptive Context Switching to mitigate temporal drift in extremely long sequences. We also propose Reencoding Alignment with Cross Residual Correction to ensure precise bidirectional consistency during frame interpolation. Furthermore, Event Voxel Density Augmentation ensures robustness across varying sensor resolutions. Extensive experiments on real-world benchmarks demonstrate that LongE2V outperforms state-of-the-art methods across all three tasks, exhibiting exceptional temporal coherence and zero-shot generalization. ### [71] [ZipDepth: Bringing Lightweight Zero-Shot Monocular Depth Anywhere, on Any Device](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08771)
*Fabio Tosi,Luca Bartolomei,Matteo Poggi,Stefano Mattoccia*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: ZipDepth是一个6.1M参数的轻量级单目深度估计网络，通过高效可重参数化编解码器设计与大规模多域知识蒸馏，在五类基准上实现了零样本准确率与部署效率的最佳平衡，性能接近参数多50倍的基础模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基础模型零样本泛化能力强但计算开销巨大，无法部署到嵌入式与移动平台；而轻量级模型仅在单域自监督范式下开发，在域迁移时失效。亟需一个既轻量又具备跨域零样本能力的深度估计方案。

Method: 提出ZipDepth，核心由两部分构成：(1) 高效可重参数化编解码器架构，压缩至6.1M参数；(2) 从大型基础模型进行大规模多域知识蒸馏，使小模型继承跨域零样本泛化能力，并在大规模多域训练集上联合训练。

Result: ZipDepth仅6.1M参数，在服务器GPU至功耗受限设备上均能达到实时推理速度。在五个基准数据集上，于轻量级模型中取得了零样本准确率与部署效率的最佳权衡，准确率显著接近参数多50倍的基础模型。

Conclusion: ZipDepth证明了通过高效架构设计与大规模多域知识蒸馏的结合，可以在极轻量化前提下实现接近大模型的跨域零样本深度估计性能，为深度估计在边缘设备上的部署提供了可行方案。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：90%。遥感领域常面临多源影像（光学、SAR、多光谱）的域差异问题，且机载/星载平台计算资源受限。具体方案：(1) 直接迁移ZipDepth至遥感单目深度估计，利用其多域蒸馏优势适应不同传感器、不同分辨率下的深度预测；(2) 将可重参数化编解码器适配为遥感专用的多尺度特征提取结构，处理大尺度地物与细节纹理的共存问题；(3) 在知识蒸馏阶段引入遥感特有的大规模无标签数据集（如卫星立体像对、LiDAR点云伪标签），进一步提升零样本泛化至未见地理场景的能力。

Abstract (英文): Monocular depth estimation has seen remarkable progress through foundation models achieving robust zero-shot generalization, yet their computational demands place them far beyond the reach of embedded and mobile platforms. Lightweight alternatives exist, but have been developed almost exclusively within single-domain, self-supervised paradigms, failing silently under domain shift. We present ZipDepth, a compact monocular depth network that bridges this gap by combining an efficient reparameterizable encoder-decoder with large-scale knowledge distillation from a foundation model over a large multi-domain training set. Comprising just 6.1M parameters, ZipDepth runs at real-time rates from server GPUs to power-constrained devices, achieving the best trade-off between zero-shot accuracy and deployment efficiency among lightweight models across five benchmarks, taking a significant step towards the accuracy of foundation models with 50x more parameters.

</details>


### [72] [Wat3R: Underwater 3D Geometry Learning without Annotations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08772)
*Jiangwei Ren,Xingyu Jiang,Zijie Song,Wei Xu,Hongkai Lin,Dingkang Liang,Xiang Bai*

Main category: cs.CV

TL;DR: 本文提出Wat3R，一种跨域半监督学习框架，用于将前馈式3D重建模型从空气域迁移到水下场景。该方法采用教师-学生架构，无需任何标注水下数据，仅利用未标注的真实水下视频学习鲁棒几何表示，并设计跨视角一致性损失补偿水体衰减与散射导致的信息退化。同时构建了Water3D数据集用于几何评估。实验表明Wat3R在水下多视图深度估计和点云重建上优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 水下环境存在光衰减、散射等独特挑战，且缺乏大规模高质量3D标注数据。现有前馈式3D重建方法依赖大量密集标注，这在水下场景中不可行。

Method: 提出Wat3R框架：(1) 采用教师-学生半监督学习架构，无需水下标注数据；(2) 利用大量未标注真实水下视频进行几何表示学习；(3) 设计跨视角一致性损失，利用其他视图的几何线索补偿当前视图因水体衰减和散射导致的信息退化；(4) 构建Water3D数据集用于评估。

Result: 在水下多视图深度估计和点云重建任务上，Wat3R优于当前最先进方法。

Conclusion: Wat3R成功实现了从空气到水下场景的跨域3D重建适应，无需任何水下标注数据，验证了半监督学习框架在水下几何任务中的有效性。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。与遥感的交叉方案：(1) 水下和遥感水色图像共享相似的大气/水体散射和衰减物理模型，Wat3R的跨视角一致性损失可直接用于多角度遥感水色图像的几何重建；(2) 教师-学生半监督框架可用于遥感领域缺乏3D标注的场景（如浑浊水体、大气雾霾环境下的卫星或无人机航拍），无需密集人工标注；(3) 构建的Water3D数据集的构建思路可借鉴到遥感水体/水下地物3D评估基准的建立；(4) 该框架可扩展到遥感中的水下地形重建、浅海水深反演等任务。

Abstract (英文): Estimating 3D geometry in underwater environments presents unique challenges due to light attenuation, scattering, and the absence of large-scale, high-quality 3D annotations. Pioneering methods rely on massive dense annotations that are impractical in underwater settings. In this paper, we propose Wat3R, a cross-domain semi-supervised learning framework designed to adapt feed-forward 3D reconstruction models from air to underwater scenes. Uniquely, our method eliminates the need for any annotated underwater data following a teacher-student architecture, that learns robust geometry representations merely on abundant unlabeled real underwater video footage. We also design a cross-view consistency loss that leverages geometric cues from other views to compensate for the information degradation in the current view caused by water attenuation and scattering. Furthermore, considering the lack of comprehensive evaluation benchmarks, we construct Water3D, a diverse dataset covering various water bodies and underwater scenarios, designed for geometric task evaluation. Experimental results demonstrate that Wat3R outperforms current state-of-the-art methods in underwater multi-view depth estimation and point cloud reconstruction. The dataset and code are available at https://github.com/LSXI7/Wat3R .
