### [74] [A unified kernel-driven modeling framework adapted to continuous, discrete and row-planted canopies in the thermal infrared domain](https://doi.org/10.1016/j.rse.2026.115548)
*Biao Cao,Yingjie Wang,Jean‐Philippe Gastellu‐Etchegorry*

Main category: RSE

TL;DR: 本文针对行播作物和果园的热红外辐射角度效应，提出了一种统一的核驱动建模框架，包含各向同性核、基形核、热点核和热带核，并实例化了两个新模型（Kimes-RL-Ganis和Kimes-Chen-Ganis）。通过三个DART模拟数据集和三个机载多角度实测数据集验证，新模型相比六种现有模型，RMSE降低幅度达42.5–84.9%，在连续和离散冠层中均表现出良好的适应性，为地表温度角度归一化提供了新方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有核驱动模型仅针对离散和连续冠层设计，未考虑行播结构特有的辐射角度依赖性，而物理模型参数过多难以校准。因此需要发展能够适应行播冠层结构的热红外核驱动模型，以实现地表温度的精确角度归一化，服务于水分管理和产量预测。

Method: 提出统一核驱动建模框架，包含四个核：各向同性核、基形核（表示行结构角度效应）、热点核和热带核（表示行结构产生的热辐射增强带）。在此框架下实例化两个模型（Kimes-RL-Ganis和Kimes-Chen-Ganis），利用DART模拟数据和机载实测多角度数据，与Vinnikov、RL、Vinnikov-RL、Vinnikov-Chen、LSF-RL、LSF-Chen六种现有模型进行对比验证。

Result: 三个模拟场景中，RMSE从1.105–2.047 K降至0.265–0.349 K，降幅71.0–84.9%；三个实测场景中，RMSE从1.316–2.227 K降至0.614–0.909 K，降幅42.5–61.2%。新模型在连续和离散冠层均表现优越。

Conclusion: 新提出的核驱动模型框架能有效表征行播冠层的热辐射角度效应，显著提升角度归一化精度，且兼具物理模型的泛化能力和经验模型的简洁性，适用于多种植被类型。该框架还可拓展至光学域的行播场景BRDF模拟。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。本文本身就是遥感热红外领域的重要进展。改进方案：(1) 将本框架扩展到光学多光谱/高光谱域，利用核驱动思想实现行播作物BRDF和 emissivity 的同时反演；(2) 引入机器学习（如高斯过程回归）对核参数进行先验约束，进一步提升在复杂行结构场景下的鲁棒性；(3) 结合无人机热红外多角度观测数据，开发实时角度归一化业务化算法；(4) 将框架与作物生长模型耦合，实现基于归一化地表温度的作物水分胁迫动态监测。

Abstract (英文): To make better use of solar energy, many crops and orchards are planted in rows around the world. Accurate monitoring of the heat radiation status of row-planted crops and orchards is important for water management and yield forecasting. However, the radiation observed by a sensor is generally angle-dependent due to the complex architecture of the canopy, which must be normalized with respect to a reference direction (e.g., the nadir direction). Compared to physical models with numerous input parameters about the canopy structure and thermal property (e.g. canopy height, leaf area index, leaf emissivity and leaf temperature), semi-empirical kernel-driven models are much easier to be calibrated using only multi-angle sensor observations. However, all existing kernel-driven models have been developed for discrete and continuous canopies, without considering the specific architecture of row structure. To extend the fitting ability to row-planted canopies, a unified kernel-driven modeling framework in the thermal infrared domain has been developed in this study. It includes an isotropic kernel, a base shape kernel, a hotspot kernel and a hot belt kernel. Both base shape and hot belt kernels can represent the angular effect of row structure. Two instantiated models (i.e., Kimes-RL-Ganis and Kimes-Chen-Ganis) are proposed within this unified framework. Then, three DART (Discrete Anisotropic Radiative Transfer)-simulated datasets and three airborne-measured multi-angle datasets have been adopted to evaluate our two new models against six existing models (i.e., Vinnikov, RL, Vinnikov-RL, Vinnikov-Chen, LSF-RL and LSF-Chen). Results show RMSE reduction percentages as large as 71.0–84.9% for the three simulated scenes (1.322–1.445 K to 0.300–0.349 K, 1.105–1.263 K to 0.265–0.321 K, and 1.926–2.047 K to 0.269–0.291 K) and 42.5–61.2% for the three measured scenes (2.043–2.227 K to 0.78–0.792 K, 1.316–1.426 K to 0.614–0.649 K, and 1.580–1.654 K to 0.882–0.909 K). Given the demonstrated adaptability of these new models to both continuous and discrete canopies, they offer significant potential for advancing angular normalization of land surface temperature across diverse vegetation types in applications. This framework is well suited for the bi-directional reflectance distribution function simulation over row-planted scenes in the optical domain.

### [75] [Differences and Driving Mechanisms of the Vegetation Dual-Track Recovery Process After Forest Fires Based on the Vegetation Index](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132175)
*Sen Wang,Xingpeng Liu,Rima Ga,Bing Ma,Nile Wu,Zhijun Tong,Jiquan Zhang*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文利用EVI（结构恢复）和SIF（功能恢复）两种指标，结合Transformer和随机森林模型，分析火灾后植被恢复的时空动态及驱动因素。结果表明SIF恢复慢于EVI，三年后约78%过火区EVI恢复至灾前80%以上，而SIF仅达70%；降水与温度促进恢复，地形和燃烧严重度（dNBR）则起抑制作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 火灾后植被的结构恢复与功能恢复之间的具体差异尚不明确，亟需从双重视角量化比较二者差异，以更全面理解生态系统恢复力。

Method: 使用EVI表征结构恢复、SIF表征功能恢复；采用Transformer模型模拟灾前灾后EVI和SIF的变化；利用随机森林模型识别恢复的关键驱动因子；通过双变量依赖分析探讨降水、温度、地形、dNBR等因素的影响。

Result: 火灾后EVI和SIF均急剧下降，但SIF恢复速度慢于EVI；三年后约78%过火区EVI恢复至灾前水平的80%以上，而SIF仅恢复至70%；降水与温度促进恢复，地形和dNBR则起抑制作用。

Conclusion: 本研究提出了一种分阶段、分析性的火灾后森林植被恢复方法，提供了结构-功能双视角的框架，为理解森林恢复力和可持续恢复管理提供了 actionable insights。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。该研究已充分利用遥感指标（EVI和SIF）进行火灾后恢复分析，可直接应用于遥感领域的林火恢复监测。改进方向：（1）可引入更多遥感指标如NDVI、NBR、LAI等，丰富结构-功能多维度评估；（2）将Transformer与随机森林结合的方法迁移至其他生态扰动（如干旱、虫害）的遥感恢复评估中；（3）可结合高空间分辨率遥感数据（如Sentinel-2、Landsat融合数据）提升恢复时空精细度；（4）将SIF与光合模型耦合，进一步区分植被恢复中光合能力与绿度恢复的内在机制。

Abstract (英文): Vegetation recovery after forest fires is a vital indicator of ecosystem resilience. However, the specific differences between structural and functional recovery after fire have remained unclear. In this study, we quantified and compared post-fire recovery using two distinct vegetation indicators: the Enhanced Vegetation Index (EVI) for structural recovery and Solar-Induced Chlorophyll Fluorescence (SIF) for functional recovery. We analyzed the spatiotemporal dynamics and drivers of post-fire recovery. A Transformer model was used to simulate pre- and post-fire variations in EVI and SIF, while a Random Forest model was employed to identify the key drivers of recovery. We analyze the spatiotemporal dynamics and drivers of post-fire recovery. A Transformer model simulates pre- and post-fire variations in EVI and SIF, while a Random Forest model identifies key drivers of recovery. Our results show a steep decline in both indicators after fires, with SIF recovering more slowly than EVI. Three years after the fire, about 78% of burned areas regain at least 80% of their pre-fire EVI levels, but SIF recovery reaches only 70%. Bivariate dependency analysis indicates that precipitation and temperature promote recovery, whereas topography and the Differenced Normalized Burn Ratio (dNBR) have the opposite effect. This study advances a phased, analytical approach to post-fire forest vegetation recovery, offering a dual-perspective framework for understanding forest resilience and providing actionable insights for sustainable restoration and management.

### [76] [Trend Pattern (1980–2025) of Total Ozone Column over Antarctica in Winter–Spring Season, Derived from Heatmap Analysis—A New Approach to Detecting Ozone Hole Recovery](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132174)
*Agnieszka Czerwińska,Janusz W. Krzyścin*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文通过分析南极昭和站和阿蒙森-斯科特站1980-2025年冬季-春季期间总臭氧柱（TOC）趋势的红-蓝热力图模式，提出了一种检测臭氧层恢复的替代方法。研究发现，无论数据来源如何，2000年之前热力图以蓝色（负趋势）为主，2000年之后以红色（正趋势）为主，证实了臭氧层在21世纪初开始恢复的假设。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 南极臭氧层恢复的检测因大气动力学引起的大幅年际变率而困难重重，难以得出确定结论。现有方法无法有效从噪声数据中辨别恢复信号，需要一种更具鲁棒性的替代分析手段。

Method: 采用红-蓝热力图对1980-2025年冬季-春季TOC趋势进行可视化分析；选取三个年度TOC时间序列（冬季平均值、9月15日值、春季最小值）监测南极昭和站和阿蒙森-斯科特站的臭氧空洞发展；综合使用再分析数据、地面测量和卫星观测等多源日TOC数据。

Result: 无论数据来源和站点如何，2000年之前热力图以蓝色（负趋势）区域为主，2000年之后红色（正趋势）区域显著出现；这种模式在原始噪声TOC时间序列中被掩盖。

Conclusion: 热力图分析证实了趋势反转的假设，即臭氧层恢复始于21世纪初，该方法能有效从噪声数据中提取恢复信号。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。该论文本身即属于遥感应用领域。改进方案：（1）可将热力图分析方法扩展到全球其他区域的臭氧监测，如北极或中纬度地区；（2）结合机器学习聚类算法自动识别热力图中趋势转折点，减少主观判断；（3）引入多光谱或超光谱遥感数据（如OMI、TROPOMI）进行更精细的垂直臭氧分布趋势分析；（4）将热力图方法应用于其他大气成分（如NO₂、SO₂、CH₄）的趋势反转检测。

Abstract (英文): Numerous attempts have been made to detect signs of ozone layer recovery over Antarctica, which has been expected since the beginning of the 21st century as a result of the reduction in concentrations of ozone-depleting substances in the Antarctic stratosphere, in accordance with the provisions of the 1987 Montreal Protocol and subsequent amendments aimed at protecting the ozone layer. Large year-to-year variability in the Antarctic ozone, driven by changes in atmospheric dynamics, has made it difficult to draw definitive conclusions about the rate of Antarctic ozone recovery. In this paper, we present an alternative approach to analyse ozone recovery by examining patterns in blue–red heatmaps of total ozone column (TOC) trends during the winter–spring period from 1980 to 2025. Three annual TOC time series (winter average, 15 September value, and spring minimum) were analysed to monitor the ozone hole development over the Syowa and Amundsen–Scott stations. Various sources of the daily TOC data were examined, including reanalysis data, ground-based measurements, and satellite observations. Regardless of the data source, we found that, for both stations, blue cells (negative trends) dominated in the areas of the heatmap where the TOC trends ended before 2000, while red cells (positive trends) appeared mostly afterwards. These results confirm the hypothesis of a trend reversal, i.e., a recovery beginning in the early 2000s, which was obscured in the original, noisy TOC time series.

### [77] [Landslide Susceptibility Assessment in a Complex Mountain Basin Transition Zone by Integrating Mamba and SBAS-InSAR Deformation Evidence: A Case Study of the Xining Basin, China](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132170)
*Heming Yang,Wenhui Liu,Y Y Liu*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种将Mamba-LSM模型与SBAS-InSAR形变信息双向重分类相结合的滑坡易发性制图框架，在西宁盆地验证表明该方法能有效提升高易发区内滑坡的聚集度和物理可解释性，AUC达0.9011。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 山盆地过渡带的滑坡易发性制图仍具挑战，传统方法主要依赖历史编录和静态条件因子，很少引入独立形变证据来优化易发性分区。

Method: 提出Mamba-LSM与SBAS-InSAR形变信息双向重分类耦合的集成框架。Mamba-LSM融合六通道邻域块、CNN局部空间编码和Mamba潜在特征变换；再通过SBAS-InSAR形变热点进行双向重分类修正易发性分区。

Result: Mamba-LSM的AUC达0.9011，F1分数0.7431，均优于对比模型。重分类后高和极高易发区仅占研究区25.31%，但包含69.84%的滑坡，且集中在山谷过渡带、河流侵蚀坡和工程扰动区。

Conclusion: 将独立SBAS-InSAR形变证据集成到易发性制图中，能同时提升滑坡在高易发区的空间集中度和易发性分区的物理可解释性。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。本文本身就是遥感与地质灾害交叉的典型工作。改进方向：(1) 可引入多时相InSAR（如PS-InSAR、DS-InSAR）提供更密集的形变监测点，提升重分类精度；(2) 结合光学遥感影像（如Sentinel-2）提取地表覆盖和植被变化信息作为动态因子输入Mamba-LSM；(3) 可尝试将形变速率作为连续特征直接嵌入Mamba-LSM的输入通道，而非仅用于后处理重分类；(4) 在不同地质环境（如黄土高原、青藏高原边缘）验证框架迁移性。

Abstract (英文): Landslide susceptibility mapping (LSM) in mountain–basin transition zones remains challenging because conventional approaches rely mainly on historical inventories and static conditioning factors, whereas independent deformation evidence is seldom incorporated to refine susceptibility zonation. This study proposes an integrated LSM framework for the Xining Basin by coupling a Mamba-based model (Mamba-LSM) with SBAS-InSAR-based deformation-informed bidirectional reclassification, with the key innovation lying in the use of independent deformation evidence to refine susceptibility zonation after model prediction. Specifically, Mamba-LSM integrates six-channel neighborhood patches, CNN-based local spatial encoding, and Mamba-based latent feature transformation to improve the representation of local terrain context for landslide susceptibility assessment. Results show that Mamba-LSM achieved the highest AUC among the evaluated models, reaching 0.9011 with an F1-score of 0.7431. After deformation-informed bidirectional reclassification, the high- and very-high-susceptibility classes occupied only 25.31% of the study area but contained 69.84% of the mapped landslides, and were concentrated mainly in valley–mountain transition belts, river-incised slopes, and engineering-disturbed sectors where SBAS-InSAR deformation hotspots were also preferentially distributed. These findings demonstrate that integrating independent SBAS-InSAR deformation evidence can improve both the spatial concentration of landslides in high-susceptibility zones and the physical interpretability of susceptibility zonation.

</details>


### [78] [Comprehensive Validation of ICESat-2 ATL08 Terrain Height Product Using High-Resolution DSM: A Multi-Site Study in Central-South China](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132160)
*J Y Chen,Wei Wang,Jingqi Liu,Mingjun Deng,Guoshi Liu,Yingfei Gao*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本研究以高分辨率数字表面模型为参考数据，在中国中南部18个典型地貌区（涵盖平原、丘陵、山地和高山峡谷）对ICESat-2 ATL08地表高程数据进行了系统验证。结果表明，所有站点平均RMSE为3.318 m（范围1.044–5.120 m），精度呈现明显的地形依赖性：平原最高（RMSE=1.044 m），丘陵次之（RMSE≈1.610–3.871 m），山地和高山峡谷最差（RMSE≈2.374–5.120 m）。整体平均误差为−1.032 m。建议在复杂地形区域使用该产品时考虑地形因素，并在高山峡谷区（RMSE>5 m）进行结合地形信息的后处理校正。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: ICESat-2 ATL08是全球地表高程监测的重要数据源，但其在中国中南部复杂地形区域的精度尚未被系统评估，现有研究缺乏对这一关键区域多地形类型覆盖的全面验证。

Method: 选取中国中南部18个典型地貌区共949个有效验证点，以高分辨率数字表面模型（DSM）为参考数据，通过计算RMSE和ME等指标，对ICESat-2 ATL08高程产品进行系统验证，并按平原、丘陵、山地和高山峡谷四种地形类型进行分类精度评估。

Result: 所有站点平均RMSE为3.318 m（范围1.044–5.120 m），整体ME为−1.032 m（范围−4.575至+2.548 m）。平原区精度最高（RMSE=1.044 m），丘陵区RMSE约1.610–3.871 m，山地和高山峡谷区精度相对较差（RMSE约2.374–5.120 m）。

Conclusion: ICESat-2 ATL08在中国中南部的精度具有高度地形依赖性，用户在使用时应考虑地形复杂度；对于RMSE超过5 m的高山峡谷区域，建议结合地形信息进行后处理校正以提高精度。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：90%。该研究本身就是遥感领域的地形数据精度验证工作，可从以下方面改进：(1) 引入更多地形因子（如坡度、坡向、粗糙度）与误差的定量回归分析，构建地形自适应校正模型；(2) 结合多源遥感数据（如Sentinel-2光谱信息、SRTM/ASTER DEM）进行地形分类辅助的误差分区校正；(3) 利用机器学习方法（随机森林、XGBoost）建立地形参数与ATL08高程误差的非线性预测模型；(4) 扩展验证区域至其他复杂地形区（如青藏高原、黄土高原），提升结论普适性；(5) 与GEDI等其他星载激光雷达数据进行交叉验证与融合分析。

Abstract (英文): ICESat-2 ATL08 is an important data source for global land surface elevation monitoring, while its accuracy has not been systematically evaluated in the complex terrain areas of central and southern China. Taking high-resolution digital surface models as reference data, this study carries out systematic verification with a total of 949 valid verification points covering 18 typical geomorphological areas in central and southern China. The verification sites cover various terrain types including plains, hills, mountains and alpine canyons. The results show that the average root mean square error of all sites is 3.318 m, ranging from 1.044 m to 5.120 m. Among them, plain areas have the highest accuracy (HS, RMSE = 1.044 m), followed by hilly areas with RMSE of approximately 1.610–3.871 m, and mountainous and alpine canyon areas show relatively poorer accuracy with RMSE of approximately 2.374–5.120 m. The overall mean error (ME) is −1.032 m, with ME values ranging from −4.575 m to +2.548 m across sites. The accuracy of ICESat-2 ATL08 in central-southern China is highly terrain-dependent: RMSE is 1.044 m in the plain site and ranges from 1.610 to 3.871 m in hilly areas and from 2.374 to 5.120 m in mountainous and alpine canyon areas. Therefore, users should consider terrain complexity when applying this product, and post-processing correction incorporating topographic information is recommended for alpine canyon areas where RMSE exceeds 5 m.

### [79] [A Lightweight Small-Object Detector for UAV Imagery via Multi-Scale Feature Enhancement and Saliency-Guided Cross-Layer Fusion](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132164)
*Hao Zhen,Guijun Chen,Fangli Guan,Liqi Yan,Zhixiang Fang,Jianhui Zhang,Haosheng Huang,Pan Li*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文针对无人机航拍图像中的细节丢失、跨尺度融合失效和环境干扰三大挑战，基于YOLOv8s框架提出了一种结合多尺度特征增强和显著性引导跨层融合的优化检测器。通过引入RFCAConv和RGCSP模块增强局部细节与空间结构建模，设计多尺度自适应融合模块(MSAFM)对齐深浅层特征，以及显著性引导上下文注意力模块(CASM)抑制背景干扰，在VisDrone2019数据集上达到48.3% mAP@0.5和29.0% mAP@[0.5:0.95]，远超YOLOv8s，同时保持7.2M参数和14.4MB模型大小的轻量化优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无人机航拍图像存在三个关键问题：1) 小目标像素少、弱边缘被下采样稀释导致细节丢失；2) 浅层与深层特征之间的语义鸿沟导致尺度错配和小目标被抑制，跨尺度融合失效；3) 杂波、遮挡和密集布局导致定位偏移的环境干扰。现有方法在精度与实时性的平衡上仍显不足。

Method: 基于YOLOv8s框架进行三方面改进：1) 在主干网络集成RFCAConv和RGCSP模块，增强局部细节与空间结构建模能力；2) 设计多尺度自适应融合模块(MSAFM)，通过双池化和自适应通道重校准对齐深浅层特征；3) 引入显著性引导上下文注意力模块(CASM)突出目标区域，结合动态检测头实现自适应特征调制。

Result: 在VisDrone2019数据集上，该方法达到48.3% mAP@0.5和29.0% mAP@[0.5:0.95]，相比YOLOv8s分别提升10.2和6.3个百分点，模型仅7.2M参数、14.4 MB大小。

Conclusion: 所提出的多尺度特征增强与显著性引导跨层融合策略有效解决了无人机航拍图像的三项主要挑战，在保持模型轻量化的前提下显著提升了检测精度，适用于无人机实时环境感知任务。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。本文本身就是针对无人机遥感图像检测的论文，可直接应用于遥感目标检测。改进方案：1) 可将RFCAConv替换为更适合遥感大尺度变化场景的改进卷积如DCNv3；2) MSAFM可引入遥感多模态数据（如红外+可见光）的跨模态特征对齐；3) CASM可扩展为全局-局部显著性联合建模以适应遥感图像的大视野与高分辨率特性；4) 动态检测头可针对遥感旋转目标检测（OBB）任务进行适配优化。

Abstract (英文): As unmanned aerial vehicles (UAVs) become central to traffic inspection, urban security, and emergency response, UAV-based environmental perception requires both high accuracy and real-time efficiency. However, UAV imagery remains challenging due to three primary factors: detail loss, where small targets occupy minimal pixels and weak edges are diluted by downsampling; ineffective cross-scale fusion, where semantic gaps between shallow and deep features lead to scale misalignment and small-object suppression; and environmental interference, where clutter, occlusion, and dense layouts cause localization drift. To address these challenges, we propose an optimized efficient detector built upon the YOLOv8s framework, incorporating multi-scale feature enhancement and saliency-guided cross-layer fusion. Specifically, we integrate RFCAConv and RGCSP modules into the backbone to strengthen local detail and spatial structure modeling. Furthermore, we design a Multi-Scale Adaptive Fusion Module (MSAFM) to align deep and shallow cues through dual-pooling and adaptive channel recalibration. To handle complex backgrounds, a Saliency-Guided Contextual Attention Module (CASM) is introduced to emphasize target regions, alongside a dynamic detection head for adaptive feature modulation. Evaluated on the VisDrone2019 dataset, our method achieves 48.3% mAP@0.5 and 29.0% mAP@[0.5:0.95], outperforming YOLOv8s by 10.2 and 6.3 points, respectively, while keeping the model compact with 7.2M parameters and a 14.4 MB model size.

</details>


### [80] [A Spectrally Enhanced Multi-Scale CNN for Limited-Sample Lithological Mapping Using Band-Integrated ASTER and Sentinel-2A Imagery](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132163)
*Qiuming Pei,Jiale Shen,Li Zhang,Yifei Zhang,Sergei Krivonogov,Shiming Wang,Daren Fang*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于ASTER与Sentinel-2A波段集成多光谱数据与轻量化光谱-空间CNN的有限样本岩性制图框架，在甘肃肃北县石板墩地区实现了八类岩性的高精度分类，总体精度达94.12%，优于单传感器数据及传统方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多光谱遥感岩性制图面临光谱信息有限和标记样本稀缺的双重挑战，限制了CNN学习判别性光谱-空间特征的能力，亟需一种既充分利用多传感器互补信息又能在小样本条件下有效训练的轻量化方法。

Method: 1) 将ASTER SWIR波段配准重采样至Sentinel-2A，与Sentinel-2A的VNIR和红边波段集成构建互补多光谱数据集；2) 设计紧凑型光谱增强多尺度CNN，包含残差光谱特征增强模块（学习波段间表示）和并行多尺度混合卷积模块（捕获光谱-空间特征）；3) 使用8158训练样本和3497独立验证样本对8种岩性单元进行分类。

Result: 波段集成数据集相比单传感器数据显著提升分类性能；提出模型在集成数据集上OA达94.12%、AA达94.04%、Kappa为0.932；t-SNE可视化显示融合空间纹理特征后岩性聚类更紧凑可分；消融实验验证了所提两个模块的有效性。

Conclusion: 集成免费多光谱数据与轻量化光谱-空间CNN为基岩裸露干旱-半干旱区岩性制图提供了实用且经济的解决方案，尤其适用于缺乏高光谱影像和密集野外样本的场景。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。本文本身就是遥感岩性制图论文。改进方向：1) 可将该波段集成策略扩展至其他多传感器组合（如Landsat-8/Sentinel-1 SAR与Sentinel-2融合），增加纹理和结构信息；2) 光谱增强模块可引入可变形卷积或注意力机制以更好地建模波段间非线性关系；3) 多尺度混合卷积可替换为更轻量的MoblieNet或ShuffleNet单元以降低参数量；4) 可引入半监督或自监督学习进一步缓解小样本问题；5) 将该框架迁移至其他地质条件复杂地区或植被覆盖区进行泛化性验证。

Abstract (英文): Lithological mapping with multispectral remote sensing remains challenging when diagnostic spectral information is limited and reliable labeled samples are scarce. This problem is particularly relevant when convolutional neural networks (CNNs) are applied to lithological classification, because limited spectral dimensionality and scarce training samples may hinder the learning of discriminative spatial–spectral features. In this study, we developed a limited-sample lithological mapping framework for the Shibaocheng area of Subei County, Gansu Province, China, using band-integrated ASTER and Sentinel-2A multispectral imagery. ASTER shortwave infrared (SWIR) bands were co-registered and resampled to Sentinel-2A imagery, and then integrated with Sentinel-2A visible and near-infrared (VNIR) and red-edge bands to construct a complementary multispectral dataset. A compact spectrally enhanced multi-scale CNN was designed, incorporating a residual spectral feature enhancement module for inter-band representation learning and a parallel multi-scale hybrid convolution module for capturing spatial–spectral features. Eight lithological units were classified under limited-label conditions using 8158 training samples and 3497 spatially independent validation samples. Experimental results show that the band-integrated ASTER–Sentinel-2A dataset improved classification performance compared with single-sensor inputs. Using the proposed model, the band-integrated dataset achieved an overall accuracy (OA) of 94.12%, average accuracy (AA) of 94.04%, and Kappa coefficient of 0.932, compared with OA values of 93.14% and 92.40% obtained using ASTER and Sentinel-2A alone, respectively. The positive effect of band-level integration was also observed for spectral angle mapper (SAM), support vector machine (SVM), and 3D-CNN, whose OA values increased to 54.33%, 86.12%, and 92.29%, respectively. The proposed CNN achieved the highest OA among the evaluated methods, outperforming SAM, SVM, and the conventional 3D-CNN. In addition, t-SNE visualization indicated that incorporating spatial texture features produced more compact and better-separated lithological clusters than using spectral features alone. Ablation experiments further demonstrated that the proposed spectral feature enhancement and multi-scale hybrid convolution modules each contributed to improving lithological classification performance. These results demonstrate that integrating freely available multispectral data with a lightweight spectral–spatial CNN provides a practical and cost-effective solution for lithological mapping in bedrock-exposed arid to semi-arid regions, especially where hyperspectral imagery and dense field samples are unavailable.

### [81] [Beyond NDVI: A Multi-Index Remote Sensing Analysis of Wetland Marsh Recovery Following the Mississippi River Gulf Outlet Closure](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132159)
*Lloyd Ndlovu,Robert W. Whalin,Rocky Talchabhadel*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文利用1984–2025年Landsat卫星数据，通过受控中断时间序列（CITS）分析，量化了2009年密西西比河航道（MRGO）关闭对路易斯安那州Shell Beach沿海湿地植被的因果影响。研究发现，整体上湿地植被持续衰退，但淡水沼泽表现出显著的恢复，差异中的差异（DiD）分析确认了NDII和kNDVI的下降是MRGO关闭特异的。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 评估大型水利工程（MRGO关闭）对沿海湿地植被的长期因果影响，区分自然变异与人类干预效应，为湿地恢复管理提供科学依据。

Method: 使用42年Landsat时序数据（1984–2025），结合NDVI、kNDVI、NDII、NDRE多指数，通过STL分解提取去季节化植被异常，采用CITS（包括单组ITS和CITS-DiD）框架，以Northern Barataria Bay为未处理对照区，使用Newey–West HAC标准误的分段OLS回归。

Result: 单组ITS显示整体NDVI（β3=−0.0034/yr）、NDII（β3=−0.0032/yr）、kNDVI（β3=−0.0016/yr）显著负向斜率变化。分层分析显示淡水沼泽NDVI显著恢复（β3=+0.0190/yr），而咸水、半咸水和中间群落持续衰退。CITS-DiD确认NDII（−0.00313/yr）和kNDVI（−0.00123/yr）下降为MRGO特异，淡水NDVI恢复（+0.02071/yr）亦为MRGO特异。

Conclusion: 多指数、长时序Landsat监测结合季节分解与传感器间完全归一化，是评估管理沿海湿地恢复轨迹的必要手段；MRGO关闭对湿地植被的影响具有群落特异性，淡水沼泽表现出恢复能力。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。本文方法可直接迁移至中国沿海湿地（如黄河三角洲、崇明东滩）的水利工程（如调水、闸坝关闭）生态效应评估。改进方向：（1）引入Sentinel-1 SAR数据补充云雨天气下的结构信息；（2）增加高光谱指标（如REIP、红边位置）以提升植被胁迫早期检测能力；（3）结合LSTM或贝叶斯时空模型替代OLS回归，以更好捕捉非线性趋势和不确定性。

Abstract (英文): We present a 42-year (1984–2025) Landsat consistent satellite vegetation trajectory for coastal wetlands in the Shell Beach area in the Breton Sound estuary, Louisiana. We applied the Controlled Interrupted Time Series (CITS) analysis to the satellite record to quantify the causal effect of the 2009 Mississippi River Gulf Outlet (MRGO) closure on the coastal wetland vegetation. The analysis used NDVI, kNDVI, and NDII across 88 vegetation transect plots located within five Coastal Reference and Monitoring Systems (CRMS) stations in the Shell Beach wetlands. Vegetation communities identified included Saline, Brackish, Freshwater, and Intermediate marsh. Sentinel-2 data from 2015 to 2025 were retained as an independent parallel record for NDRE analysis only. Quarterly median composites were decomposed using the Seasonal-Trend decomposition using LOESS (STL) to isolate de-seasonalized vegetation anomalies. The CITS design used segmented Ordinary Least Squares (OLS) regression with Newey–West HAC standard errors (lag = 3) at the study area. Northern Barataria Bay was used as an untreated regional control site to remove concurrent climate and sea level rise confounders. Whilst Hurricane Katrina and subsequent years (2005–2008) were excluded from the models, the single group ITS identified significant negative post-closure slope change across three indices. These were NDVI (β3 = −0.0034 yr−1, p = 0.000), NDII (β3 = −0.0032 yr−1), and kNDVI (β3 = −0.0016 yr−1). These values indicated continued site-level decline relative to the pre-closure trend. Community-stratified ITS analysis showed a distinct divergent pattern with Freshwater marshes demonstrating significant recovery, with NDVI β3 = +0.0190 yr−1, p = 0.000, whilst Saline, Brackish, and Intermediate communities continued to decline. CITS Difference-in-Differences (DiD) confirmed that site-level NDII and kNDVI declines were MRGO-specific. The DiD findings were that NDII = −0.00313 yr−1, p &lt; 0.001; kNDVI = −0.00123 yr−1, p = 0.008. These findings isolated that physiological water stress and the non-linear biomass losses were a result of the MRGO-closure. The Freshwater DiD for NDVI (+0.02071 yr−1, p = 0.000) was the strongest evidence of MRGO-specific recovery. Barataria Freshwater declined, whilst the Shell Beach Freshwater recovered. The results demonstrated that multi-index decadal Landsat monitoring with seasonal decomposition and full inter-sensor harmonization is essential for restoration trajectory assessment in managed coastal wetlands.

### [82] [Environmental Controls and Transition of the Baige Landslide Deformation Revealed by Time-Series Remote Sensing Observations](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132169)
*Shuolong Huang,Gang Mei,Yingjie Sun*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文利用SBAS-InSAR、STL时间序列分解、PCA-ICA信号分析和坡单元空间统计等方法，研究了青藏高原东部高山峡谷区发生的白格滑坡的时空演化特征及环境控制机制。结果表明：滑坡变形可分为三个阶段（缓慢滑动、残余蠕变、长期持续加速）；失稳导致变形场系统性重构，有效像素从2766降至560，变形从轻微正LOS位移转为显著负LOS位移，全局标准差从21.40 mm增至40.55 mm；驱动机制从短期多因素控制转变为以温度为主的长期环境控制，重力驱动蠕变和失稳后结构调始终保持重要背景作用，坡体破碎化和结构重组可能是该转变的原因。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高山峡谷区高位岩质滑坡频发，但对其时空演化的定量理解及阶段依赖驱动机制的认识尚不充分，亟需揭示滑坡失稳前后变形场演化规律及环境控制机制的转变。

Method: 采用小基线子集干涉合成孔径雷达（SBAS-InSAR）、基于Loess的季节-趋势分解（STL）、主成分分析-独立成分分析（PCA-ICA）信号分析以及坡单元空间统计方法。

Result: (1) 变形分为三个阶段：缓慢滑动（失稳前）、残余蠕变（失稳后）、长期持续加速；(2) 失稳导致变形场系统性重构，有效像素减少，变形方向反转，离散度增大；(3) 驱动机制从短期多因素控制转变为以温度为主的长周期环境控制，重力蠕变和结构调始终是重要背景因素。

Conclusion: 揭示了白格滑坡失稳前后变形阶段划分、变形场重构特征及驱动机制转换规律，指出坡体破碎化和结构重组是驱动机制转变的关键因素。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。该论文本身就是遥感（InSAR）在滑坡灾害中的典型应用。改进方案：(1) 可引入多源遥感数据（如光学影像偏移量追踪、激光雷达点云）与InSAR结合，弥补SAR在大梯度形变区的失相干问题；(2) 可结合深度学习（如LSTM、Transformer）对STL分解后的残差序列进行预测，提升形变预警能力；(3) 可在坡单元统计中加入三维离散元数值模拟，实现遥感观测与物理机制的耦合分析。

Abstract (英文): High-altitude rock slides frequently occur in the high-mountain canyon regions of the eastern Tibetan Plateau, posing significant disaster risks. The Baige landslide catastrophically failed in October 2018, blocking the Jinsha River and forming a major landslide-dammed lake. However, quantitative understanding of the spatiotemporal evolution and environmental control mechanisms remains insufficient, particularly regarding stage-dependent driving mechanisms. This study investigates the Baige landslide using mall Baseline Subset Interferometric Synthetic Aperture Radar (SBAS-InSAR), Seasonal-Trend decomposition based on Loess (STL) time-series decomposition, Principal Component Analysis–Independent Component Analysis (PCA-ICA) signal analysis, and slope-unit spatial statistics. Results indicate that: (1) deformation exhibited three stages separated by October 2018: slow pre-slide deformation, post-slide residual creep, and long-term sustained acceleration; (2) instability caused systematic restructuring of the deformation field, with valid pixels decreasing from 2766 to 560, deformation changing from slight positive line-of-sight (LOS) displacement to pronounced negative LOS displacement, and global standard deviation increasing from 21.40 mm to 40.55 mm, with stronger disturbances in the steep front zone; and (3) the driving mechanism shifted from short-term multi-factor control to a temperature-dominated long-term environmental control regime after failure, while gravity-driven creep and post-failure structural adjustment remained important background controls. Slope fragmentation and structural reorganization likely contributed to this transition.

Abstract (英文): The rapid development of deep learning methods has significantly improved the effectiveness of object detection in Earth Observation (EO) imagery. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出VCPSun专用太阳扫描模式，采用高密度太阳扫描策略，结合中点时间对齐与前馈控制太阳视运动；通过太阳样本识别、传播路径校正、二维高斯曲面拟合，以及太阳源展宽和扫描模糊的去卷积处理，联合反演波束指向、波束宽度和天线增益。

Result: 质量控制的太阳样本保留率85.7%；波束指向偏差在±0.05°以内；H极化方位/俯仰波束宽度相对差异3.26%/1.52%，V极化2.09%/1.84%，整体均值<3.5%；H/V极化天线增益差异分别为-0.062 dB和-0.144 dB，均小于0.2 dB。

Abstract (英文): The calibration accuracy of key weather radar antenna parameters, including beam pointing, beamwidth, and antenna gain, directly affects quantitative precipitation estimation (QPE) and multi-radar network products. Conventional calibration approaches such as external field beacons and far-field tests are often constrained by site conditions and high implementation costs, making them difficult to apply routinely in operational radar networks. To address this limitation, this study proposes a robust solar calibration method for key antenna parameters of weather radars based on a dedicated Volume Coverage Pattern for Sun calibration, hereafter referred to as VCPSun. The proposed method uses a high-density solar scanning strategy with midpoint time alignment and feed-forward control of solar apparent motion. Combined with solar sample identification, propagation path correction, two-dimensional Gaussian surface fitting, and deconvolution of solar-source broadening and scan-smearing effects, the method enables reliability retrieval of beam pointing, beamwidth, and antenna gain. A high-frequency intensive observing experiment was conducted using a China New Generation Weather Radar, model SA-D (CINRAD/SA-D), deployed at the Changsha Meteorological Radar Calibration Center, with independent far-field test results used for validation. The results show that the retention rate of quality-controlled solar samples reached 85.7%, supporting stable reconstruction of the main-lobe power pattern. The retrieved mean beam pointing biases for both polarizations were within ±0.05°. After correction, the relative differences in beamwidth with respect to far-field measurements were respectively 3.26% and 1.52% for the H-polarization azimuth and elevation directions and 2.09% and 1.84% for the V-polarization azimuth and elevation directions, with the overall mean relative difference being less than 3.5%. The antenna gain differences relative to the independent far-field reference values were within 0.2 dB, at −0.062 dB for H-polarization and −0.144 dB for V-polarization. Comparative analysis with historical one-dimensional SunCheck records and an ablation test of the beamwidth correction chain further demonstrate that high-density two-dimensional sampling and physical deconvolution corrections improve the robustness and quantitative accuracy of the solar-based retrieval. These results demonstrate the feasibility of reliable in situ calibration of key antenna parameters for operational weather radars. The proposed method provides a potential technical pathway for in situ quantitative assessment of antenna performance in S-band CINRAD/SA-D radars, although further validation using additional radars and longer observation periods is required prior to network-wide application.

### [85] [Diffusion-Driven Relative Radiometric Normalization with Spatial–Spectral Attention Residual Network for Multi-Temporal Remote Sensing Imagery](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132156)
*Liyao Song,Chunyan Liu,Ma Jx,Haiwei Li,Long Ma,Ruofeng Wang*

Main category: Remote Sensing

Method: 提出扩散概率RRN框架：1）前向过程注入结构化噪声+随机扰动模拟辐射不一致性；2）反向过程通过双目标变分公式恢复一致性；3）核心为空间-光谱注意力残差网络（SSARN），集成残差学习与双重注意力机制；4）SSIM引导的预处理自动选取稳定伪不变区域用于训练。

Abstract (英文): Relative radiometric normalization (RRN) is fundamental to multi-temporal remote sensing analysis; however, conventional techniques often struggle with nonlinear distortions, outlier contamination, and heterogeneous land-cover conditions. To address these challenges, we propose a diffusion-based probabilistic framework that models radiometric inconsistency as a combination of deterministic residuals and stochastic perturbations. In this framework, the forward process injects structured noise and stochastic perturbations, while the reverse process restores radiometric consistency through a dual-objective variational formulation. At the core of this framework is a spatial–spectral attention residual network (SSARN), which integrates residual learning with dual attention mechanisms to capture cross-band dependencies and multi-scale spatial context. A preprocessing stage guided by the structural similarity index (SSIM) further enhances robustness by automatically selecting stable pseudo-invariant regions for model training. Comprehensive experiments on multi-temporal Sentinel-2 datasets demonstrate that the proposed method consistently outperforms existing approaches, achieving higher accuracy and enhanced spectral fidelity. Moreover, the framework ensures greater consistency of the normalized difference vegetation index (NDVI) and preserves fine-grained textural details, underscoring its potential as a scalable and resilient solution for large-scale RRN in remote sensing applications.

### [86] [Anchor-Level Spectral–Spatial Graph Clustering for Hyperspectral Images](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132172)
*Chaodie Liu,Jianxiong Luo,Fei Li,Qianyao Qiang,Feiping Nie*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种锚点级光谱-空间图聚类（ASSGC）模型，通过超像素内逐波段中值策略生成代表性锚点以抑制噪声，并设计融合光谱与空间位置的新距离度量来构建锚点级亲和矩阵，降低计算开销。在四个高光谱数据集上的实验表明，该方法在保持低时间复杂度的同时优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高光谱图像聚类面临高光谱变异性、复杂空间分布和噪声干扰等挑战，现有基于图的聚类方法大多忽略空间信息且计算成本高，无法有效处理大规模HSI数据。

Method: 1) 在超像素内采用逐波段中值策略生成代表性锚点以抑制噪声和离群点；2) 设计融合光谱特征与空间位置的新距离度量，在锚点级构建光谱-空间联合亲和矩阵；3) 对锚点应用谱聚类获取标签，再传播至对应超像素实现全图聚类。

Result: 在Indian Pines（64.13%）、Pavia University（71.33%）、Salinas（87.86%）和Salinas A（99.23%）四个数据集上取得了优于现有方法的聚类精度，且时间复杂度低。

Abstract (英文): Hyperspectral image (HSI) clustering aims to partition pixels into distinct clusters by leveraging spectral and spatial features, thereby providing crucial support for the interpretation and information extraction of hyperspectral data. However, due to high spectral variability, complex spatial distribution, and noise interference, HSI clustering still faces considerable challenges. Graph-based clustering represents a prominent learning framework and achieves competitive performance on HSI analysis. However, most existing methods ignore spatial information and suffer from high computational cost, rendering them incapable of effectively dealing with large-scale HSIs. To address the aforementioned challenges, this paper proposes an anchor-level spectral–spatial graph clustering (ASSGC) model for HSIs. The proposed ASSGC employs a band-wise median strategy within each superpixel to generate representative anchors to suppress noise and outlier effects. A novel distance metric is designed to integrate spectral features and spatial positions to effectively identify neighbors and construct a spectral–spatial joint affinity matrix at the anchor-level, thereby reducing computational burden and memory consumption. Subsequently, spectral clustering is applied to obtain anchor labels, which are propagated to the corresponding superpixels to achieve full-image clustering. Experiments on four HSI datasets yield ACC of 64.13% on Indian Pines, 71.33% on Pavia University, 87.86% on Salinas, and 99.23% on Salinas A, demonstrating that the proposed ASSGC outperforms several existing state-of-the-art methods while maintaining low time complexity.

### [87] [A Deep Learning-Based Method for Enhancing the Signal-to-Noise Ratio of Star Sensor Images](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132178)
*Jian Guan,Hanye Yu,Yanpeng Wu,X Li,Rongzheng Cao*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 针对星敏感器在窗跟踪模式下星点信号被杂散光和读出噪声淹没的问题，该文以自监督时空去噪模型ASTERIS为基础，引入逐帧空间可变形卷积补偿亚像素抖动并抑制背景噪声，同时设计复值频域损失联合约束幅值和相位谱以保留星点高频细节。实验表明，在极低信噪比下，该方法相比ASTERIS和堆叠法显著提升去噪和质心提取精度（PSNR提升约17.8 dB，质心误差约0.1像素）。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1) 在ASTERIS解码器上采样阶段引入逐帧空间可变形卷积，自适应补偿亚像素偏移并抑制背景噪声，同时降低参数量。2) 设计复值频域损失函数，结合高频加权掩码联合约束幅值和相位谱，保留星点高频细节。

Result: 在极低信噪比星图上，所提方法PSNR提升约17.8 dB，质心定位误差约0.1像素；原始ASTERIS模型PSNR提升约9.5 dB，误差约0.4像素；多帧堆叠法PSNR提升约6.0 dB，误差约0.5像素。

Conclusion: 该方法在模拟强噪声条件下实现了有效的质心提取，展示了在轨星敏感器数据处理的潜力，未来工作将进一步解决工程部署问题。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：100%。该文本身就是遥感领域（星敏感器）论文。改进方案：1) 可变形卷积与频域损失可推广至其他遥感影像的去噪任务（如高光谱图像、SAR图像），特别是需要亚像素级配准和细节保留的场景；2) 自监督训练策略可减少对干净参考数据的依赖，适用于缺乏真实标签的遥感任务；3) 可考虑将复值频域损失扩展至多尺度频域约束，进一步提升复杂地物目标的边缘保持能力；4) 工程部署方面可探索模型量化剪枝等轻量化方案以适应星上计算资源约束。

Abstract (英文): In window tracking mode, stray light and detector readout noise can submerge star spot signals in star sensor images. The resulting degradation reduces centroid extraction accuracy and may even cause extraction failure, thereby preventing precise attitude determination. This study uses the self-supervised spatiotemporal denoising model ASTERIS as the baseline. ASTERIS integrates 3D spatiotemporal inputs with a global attention mechanism for joint noise modeling, thereby providing stronger denoising and restoration capability than conventional methods such as multi-frame stacking. However, ASTERIS lacks adaptive compensation for subpixel jitter in on-orbit star images and has difficulty preserving the high-frequency morphology of star spots, affecting denoising performance and centroiding accuracy. To address these limitations, this study introduces two improvements: First, frame-by-frame spatial deformable convolution is incorporated into the decoder upsampling stage to adaptively compensate for subpixel offsets, actively suppress background noise, and lower the parameter count. Second, a complex-valued frequency domain loss with a high-frequency weighted mask is designed to jointly constrain the amplitude and phase spectra, thereby preserving high-frequency star spot details. Experimental results show that, for star images with extremely low signal-to-noise ratios, the proposed method improves the peak signal-to-noise ratio by approximately 17.8 dB and reduces the centroid localization error to approximately 0.1 pixels. This performance is substantially better than that of the original ASTERIS model, which improves the peak signal-to-noise ratio by approximately 9.5 dB and yields an error of approximately 0.4 pixels, and the multi-frame stacking method, which improves the peak signal-to-noise ratio by approximately 6.0 dB and yields an error of approximately 0.5 pixels. Under the simulated strong noise conditions considered in this study, the proposed method achieves effective centroid extraction, demonstrating its potential for on-orbit star sensor data processing. Future work will further address its engineering deployment.

*Y ouzhong Guo,Z H E N G M Jiang,Yuxuan Lin,Ge Qu,Weile Li,Xiaoai Dai*

Motivation: 高山峡谷流域的滑坡易发性制图常受限于稀疏且不完整的局部编录数据，而国家尺度的滑坡信息能否转化为可靠的局部知识尚不明确，尤其在强地形与环境异质性区域，大尺度模型的直接迁移效果受限。

Method: 以帕隆藏布流域为测试案例，设计四种策略：(1)局部基线建模；(2)国家模型直接迁移；(3)加权源-目标联合训练；(4)先验信息引导的局部建模。采用相同条件因子、数据处理流程、空间独立测试集和评估指标进行控制对比。

Result: 先验信息引导策略在独立测试集上AUC达0.901，ECE降至0.055，优于局部基线、直接迁移和联合训练策略。其易发性图呈现广阔的低易发性背景与空间集中的高易发性斑块，减少了过度预测同时保留了局部滑坡易发区。

Conclusion: 国家尺度的滑坡信息转化为局部可重新校准的概率先验比直接迁移更有效，为数据匮乏的山地流域易发性评估提供了实用路径。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。该方法的整体框架（国家模型→局部先验校准）可直接迁移至遥感领域。具体改进方案：(1)将国家尺度遥感滑坡编录（如InSAR、光学影像解译结果）作为外部先验，结合局部高分辨率遥感数据（如无人机、雷达）进行校准，提升局部易发性制图精度；(2)利用遥感多源数据（DEM、光学、SAR）提取更丰富的条件因子，增强先验信息的物理可解释性；(3)在缺少地面实测的偏远山区，该策略可有效利用已有遥感大数据资源，降低对密集局部样本的依赖。

Abstract (英文): Landslides pose widespread threats to mountainous communities and infrastructure worldwide, yet susceptibility mapping in alpine gorge basins is often constrained by sparse and incomplete local inventories. Whether national-scale landslide information can be transformed into reliable local knowledge remains unclear, particularly where strong topographic and environmental heterogeneity limits the direct transfer of broad-scale models. Here, we use the Parlung Tsangpo Basin on the southeastern Tibetan Plateau as a test case and compare four strategies for introducing national-scale information: local baseline modelling, direct national-model transfer, weighted source–target joint training, and prior-informed local modelling. The experiments use the same conditioning factors, data-processing workflow, spatially independent test set, and evaluation metrics, allowing the transfer strategies to be assessed under controlled conditions. The prior-informed strategy treats the susceptibility probability produced by the national model as a geoscientifically interpretable external prior, which is then relearned and recalibrated by local samples, and achieves the best overall performance. On the independent test set, it reaches an area under the receiver operating characteristic curve (AUC) of 0.901 and reduces the expected calibration error (ECE) to 0.055, outperforming the local baseline, direct transfer, and joint training strategies. Its susceptibility map shows an extensive low-susceptibility background with spatially concentrated high-susceptibility patches, thereby reducing broad-scale overprediction while preserving local landslide-prone zones. These results indicate that national-scale landslide information is more effective when converted into a locally recalibrated probability prior than when transferred directly, providing a practical pathway for susceptibility assessment in data-scarce mountainous basins.

### [89] [A Vertically Structured Machine Learning Approach for Cloud Liquid and Ice Water Content Profiling](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132177)
*Zhengyu Pan,Yansong Bao,Wei Hong,Haoran Li,Fang Pang,Wei Tao*

Main category: Remote Sensing

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有云水含量反演受限于垂直方向强变异性和观测量间的非线性依赖，地基云雷达与微波辐射计联合使用需解决时空匹配和偏差控制问题，亟需能显式建模垂直结构依赖的反演框架。

Method: 提出垂直结构化机器学习框架，包含三个核心步骤：(1) 构建垂直结构增强特征，编码局部梯度和上下文信息；(2) 通过廓线感知堆叠策略集成多个异构树学习器；(3) 引入廓线级精炼步骤抑制层间不一致性。

Result: 基于Lindenberg站点全年Cloudnet观测验证，IWC的RMSE从0.0152降至0.0092 g m−3，R²从0.412提升至0.784；LWC的RMSE从0.0786降至0.0591 g m−3，R²从0.303提升至0.606；边界区域改进尤为显著。

Conclusion: 将云反演视为垂直结构化学习问题可减少逐点模型固有的不一致性，建立了将垂直约束融入大气廓线反演的数据驱动基线。

Abstract (英文): Accurate retrieval of cloud liquid water content (LWC) and ice water content (IWC) vertical profiles remains limited by strong vertical variability and nonlinear dependencies among observed variables. Ground-based cloud radar reflectivity and microwave radiometer-derived thermodynamic profiles provide complementary constraints, but their joint use requires consistent time–height matching and bias-controlled predictors. This study develops a vertically structured machine-learning framework that explicitly represents profile-level dependencies by constructing vertical-structure-enhanced features to encode local gradients and contextual information, integrating multiple tree-based learners with heterogeneous configurations through a profile-aware stacking strategy, and introducing a profile-level refinement step to suppress layer-to-layer inconsistencies. The framework is evaluated using year-round Cloudnet observations from the Lindenberg site, where IWC RMSE decreases from 0.0152 g m−3 to 0.0092 g m−3 with R2 increasing from 0.412 to 0.784, and LWC RMSE decreases from 0.0786 g m−3 to 0.0591 g m−3 with R2 increasing from 0.303 to 0.606. Additional boundary-region evaluation shows that the improvement is particularly evident near radar-derived cloud boundaries, where cloud structure and hydrometeor content may vary rapidly with height. These results indicate that treating cloud retrieval as a vertically structured learning problem reduces inconsistencies inherent in pointwise models and establishes a data-driven baseline for incorporating vertical constraints into atmospheric profile retrieval.

### [90] [MIGA-Net: A Graph Interaction and Gated Context Network for High-Resolution Remote Sensing Change Detection](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132155)
*Jingtong Yang,Xiaorong Xue,Yishuo Tian,Wen Zhang,Bingyan Lu,Xin Zhao,W X Wang*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: MIGA-Net是一种端到端的遥感变化检测框架，通过时空图交互模块(ST-GIM)、自适应门控上下文金字塔模块(AGCP)和层次化边界感知细化模块(HBAR)分别抑制伪变化、多尺度聚合特征和恢复边界轮廓，在三个数据集上取得了SOTA性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高分辨率遥感变化检测面临三个核心挑战：(1)跨时相外观不一致(如光照、季节变化)导致的伪变化；(2)目标尺度变化大；(3)多层级解码引入的边界模糊问题。现有方法未能同时有效解决这三个问题。

Method: 提出MIGA-Net端到端框架，包含三个创新模块：(1) ST-GIM：结合交互式注意力与图推理，抑制光照或季节引起的伪变化；(2) AGCP：通过内容驱动的尺度选择与门控残差机制调节上下文注入，减少噪声放大；(3) HBAR：整合语义通道滤波与显式边界注意力，实现渐进式轮廓恢复。

Result: 在LEVIR-CD、WHU-CD和SYSU-CD上分别达到F1=91.84%/92.52%/82.92%，IoU=84.91%/86.08%/70.83%，在定量指标和边界质量上均取得一致性改进。

Conclusion: MIGA-Net通过联合建模时空交互、自适应多尺度聚合和层次化边界细化，有效抑制伪变化并生成结构保真度高的变化检测结果，验证了其在鲁棒伪变化抑制和结构忠实预测方面的有效性。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。改进方案：(1) ST-GIM中的图推理可引入图卷积网络(GCN)的变体(如GraphSAGE)以增强对不规则地物边界的建模能力；(2) AGCP的门控机制可扩展为动态卷积或可变形卷积，以更好适应遥感地物几何形变；(3) HBAR的边界注意力可与遥感影像的多光谱或SAR特征融合，提升多模态变化检测的边界恢复质量；(4) 可引入对比学习或自监督预训练策略，进一步提升在标注数据稀缺场景下的泛化性能。

Abstract (英文): Remote sensing change detection (CD) aims to localize land-surface changes from bi-temporal imagery and plays an important role in applications such as urban monitoring, disaster assessment, and environmental analysis. In high-resolution scenarios, CD performance is often degraded by cross-temporal appearance inconsistency, large variations in target scale, and boundary ambiguity introduced during multi-level decoding. To address these challenges, we propose MIGA-Net, an end-to-end framework that jointly models spatio-temporal interaction, adaptive multi-scale context aggregation, and hierarchical boundary refinement. Specifically, the Spatio-Temporal Graph Interaction Module (ST-GIM) combines interactive attention and graph reasoning to suppress pseudo-changes caused by illumination or seasonal shifts; the Adaptive Gated Context Pyramid Module (AGCP) performs content-driven scale selection and regulates context injection through a gated residual mechanism to reduce noise amplification; and the Hierarchical Boundary-Aware Refinement Module (HBAR) integrates semantic channel filtering and explicit boundary attention for progressive contour recovery. Experiments on LEVIR-CD, WHU-CD, and SYSU-CD demonstrate that MIGA-Net achieves F1 scores of 91.84%, 92.52%, and 82.92%, and IoU scores of 84.91%, 86.08%, and 70.83%, respectively. The proposed method yields consistent improvements in both quantitative metrics and structural boundary quality, indicating its effectiveness for robust pseudo-change suppression and structurally faithful prediction in high-resolution remote sensing CD.

### [91] [Assessing the Reliability of Sentinel-2 for Turbidity Estimation in a Shallow Coastal Lagoon](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132176)
*Adriana Castro,Humberto Pereira,João Miguel Días,Carina L. Lopes*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 沿海系统浊度监测对可持续管理至关重要，但现有卫星遥感算法在浅海泻湖等复杂水体中适用性不足，尤其缺乏针对特定区域（如Aveiro泻湖）的局部校准模型。

Method: 在2025年5月28日与Sentinel-2卫星过境同步开展现场测量，采集近表层浊度与Secchi深度数据；利用ACOLITE软件(v20250114.0)提取遥感反射率（Rrs）并测试多种算法；基于Rrs数据开发并经验调整新浊度模型，通过决定系数（R²）和均方根误差（RMSE）评估性能。

Result: 现有ACOLITE算法不适用于Aveiro泻湖，严重低估高浊度值；665 nm与560 nm波段比值（RGratio）是最优光谱指数，浊度估算R²=0.822，RMSE=1.77 NTU。

Conclusion: 局部校准模型优于标准ACOLITE算法，对浅海泻湖浊度反演至关重要；但模型仅基于单次潮汐、风和河流排放条件下的采样，尚未经过独立验证，需进一步评估其时空泛化能力。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。改进方案：（1）引入多时相数据（不同潮汐、季节）增强模型鲁棒性；（2）结合Sentinel-2红边波段（如705 nm）提升高浊度水体的区分能力；（3）加入大气校正后验质量控制（如AERONET-OC验证）减少Rrs误差；（4）尝试机器学习（如随机森林、神经网络）融合多波段信息替代简单比值模型；（5）扩展至其他类似浅海泻湖（如中国杭州湾、荷兰瓦登海）进行迁移学习验证。

Abstract (英文): Understanding turbidity in coastal systems is essential to ensure the sustainable management of these ecosystems, which are increasingly under pressure from natural factors and human activities. Thus, this study aims to develop a local Sentinel-2-based turbidity model for the Aveiro lagoon (Portugal) by combining Sentinel-2 records with in situ measurements. A field campaign synchronized with a Sentinel-2 overpass was conducted across the lagoon channels on 28 May 2025, to capture spatial variability by measuring near-surface turbidity and Secchi depth, for correspondence with the spectral records of satellite. Remote Sensing Reflectance (Rrs) and turbidity were derived using various algorithms integrated within the ACOLITE software (v20250114.0). Additionally, new turbidity models were developed and empirically adjusted based on the Rrs data, with their performance quantified through the coefficient of determination (R2) and Root Mean Square Error (RMSE). The results showed that the existing algorithms are not directly suitable for the Aveiro lagoon, as they underestimate the highest turbidity values. The ratio between 665 and 560 nm bands (RGratio) proved to be the most suitable spectral index, performing best in estimating turbidity (R2 = 0.822 and RMSE = 1.77 NTU). This study highlights the importance of locally calibrated models over standard ACOLITE algorithms for turbidity retrieval in shallow coastal lagoons, while emphasizing that the proposed model was calibrated for the tidal, wind, and river discharge conditions sampled during the campaign and has not yet been independently validated.

### [92] [Local Calibration Enhances the Transferability of UAV-LiDAR Models for Tree-Level Carbon Estimation in Radiata Pine Plantations](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132161)
*Michael S. Watt,Sadeepa Jayathunga*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本研究比较了线性混合效应模型、广义加性模型和随机森林三种方法，在新西兰20个辐射松人工林站点的35,201棵树中评估UAV-LiDAR估算树木碳储量的模型迁移性。结果表明，多站点模型泛化能力差（相对RMSE 35.9-56.9%），但使用50棵树的局部后验校准可将误差降低30-60%（相对RMSE 22.8-25.0%），接近全局部模型（21.9-23.1%），且50棵以上样本量收益递减。后验校准多站点UAV-LiDAR模型是一种实用高效的碳估算方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 森林碳的准确、可迁移估算对森林经营和温室气体报告至关重要，但由于林分结构和立地条件差异，现有模型跨站点迁移性差，亟需一种兼具准确性和实用性的建模策略。

Method: 基于20个站点35,201棵辐射松数据，采用留一站点外（LOSO）框架评估多站点模型迁移性；比较LMM、GAM、RF三种方法在三种策略（多站点、局部后验校准、全局部模型）下的表现；分析样本量增加对精度的影响及随机采样与样地采样的差异。

Result: 多站点模型表现差（相对RMSE 35.9-56.9%）；50棵树的后验校准可将误差降低30-60%（相对RMSE 22.8-25.0%），显著减少站点偏差；全局部模型仅有微小提升（21.9-23.1%）；后验校准在50棵树以上、全局部模型在175棵树以上精度增益递减；采样策略间差异小。

Conclusion: 后验校准多站点UAV-LiDAR模型结合少量局部样本（约50棵树），能够在保持较高精度的同时大幅提升模型迁移性，为人工林树木碳估算提供了一种实用高效的方法。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：90%。该论文本身就是遥感（UAV-LiDAR）在林业碳估算中的应用研究。改进方向：1) 可引入深度学习（如PointNet++、Graph Neural Networks）替代传统机器学习方法，更好地捕捉树木点云的空间拓扑结构；2) 可结合多源遥感数据（如高光谱、SAR）对林分类型和树种多样性进行先验分类，从而减少因树种差异导致的迁移误差；3) 后验校准策略可扩展到半监督或主动学习框架，自动化最优局部样本选择和模型更新；4) 可探索贝叶斯方法量化模型不确定性，为碳估算提供置信区间。

Abstract (英文): Accurate and transferable estimation of forest carbon is essential for operational forest management and national greenhouse gas reporting, yet it remains challenging because of variation in stand structure and site conditions. Unmanned aerial vehicle-based light detection and ranging (UAV-LiDAR) provides detailed structural information for modelling tree-level carbon, but model transferability across sites is often limited. In this study, we compared three modelling approaches—a linear mixed-effects model (LMM), a generalised additive model (GAM), and Random Forest (RF)—within a unified framework of multi-site, locally post hoc calibrated, and fully local model-fitting strategies. Using data from 20 radiata pine (Pinus radiata D. Don) plantation stands across New Zealand (35,201 trees), a leave-one-site-out (LOSO) framework was used to assess multi-site model transferability and support post hoc calibration, while local models were evaluated using repeated within-site train/test splits. We also evaluated how prediction accuracy changed with increasing local sample size and compared random tree selection with plot-based sampling. Multi-site models showed poor generalisation, with mean relative RMSE ranging from 35.9% to 56.9% and substantial site-level bias. Applying post hoc calibration to the multi-site model using a 50-tree sample reduced prediction error by 30 to 60% (mean relative RMSE 22.8–25.0%) and substantially reduced bias across sites. The fitting of fully local models with the same sample size yielded only modest further improvements (mean relative RMSE 21.9–23.1%). Gains in accuracy were minimal with increasing sample sizes above 50 trees for post hoc calibration and 175 trees for the fully local models, and differences in accuracy between sampling strategies were small. These results show that post hoc calibration of multi-site UAV-LiDAR models with a small local sample provides a practical and efficient approach for tree-level carbon estimation in plantation forests.

### [93] [Cloud Microphysical Characteristics in the Northeast China Cold Vortex Derived from Satellite Measurements](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132165)
*Qin Zheng,Qi Liu,Yuan Li,Zhenci Lu,Jiahao Cheng*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 利用MODIS云产品分析东北冷涡（NCCV）条件下云的类型频率及液态有效半径、冰有效半径、液态水路径、冰水路径等微物理特性，发现NCCV与非NCCV云系统在云类型组成上相似（以层积云为主），但微物理特性差异显著，尤其液态水路径明显更大，且液态水路径和冰水路径的空间异质性更强。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 东北冷涡常引发雷暴、大风、强降水等天气，但与之相关的云系统微物理特性长期缺乏观测表征，现有研究不足。

Method: 利用MODIS云产品，对比分析NCCV与非NCCV条件下的云类型频率及四种关键微物理参数（Re_liq、Re_ice、LWP、IWP），并进一步分析NCCV域内云微物理的空间结构。

Result: NCCV与非NCCV云类型组成相似，层积云占比超40%；但NCCV云系统的LWP显著更大；空间上，LWP和IWP的异质性高于Re_liq和Re_ice，LWP在北部至西北部区域明显增大。

Conclusion: 揭示了NCCV相关云系统的统计微物理特征，为深入理解其独特的云和降水物理过程提供了卫星观测角度的参考。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：90%。该论文已以MODIS卫星遥感数据为核心方法，可直接拓展至其他卫星传感器（如VIIRS、葵花8/9号AHI）进行交叉验证；未来可与主动遥感（如CloudSat/CALIPSO的雷达-激光雷达联合产品）结合，获取垂直廓线信息以弥补MODIS仅提供柱积分量的局限；此外，可将云微物理参数与再分析资料或数值模式输出进行对比，改进NCCV云微物理参数化方案。

Abstract (英文): The Northeast China Cold Vortex (NCCV), a typical synoptic-scale system in Northeast China, North China, and the Jianghuai region, frequently triggers thunderstorms, strong winds, and heavy precipitation, making it significant for meteorological monitoring and operational forecasting. However, the cloud microphysical properties of NCCV-associated cloud systems remain poorly characterized, as long-term cloud microphysical observations are limited. This study utilizes cloud products from the Moderate Resolution Imaging Spectroradiometer (MODIS) to analyze cloud-type frequencies and four key cloud microphysical properties under NCCV conditions: liquid effective radius (Re_liq), ice effective radius (Re_ice), liquid water path (LWP), and ice water path (IWP). Nearly identical cloud-type compositions are found for the two groups, NCCV and non-NCCV samples with similar cloud fractions on the regional scale, which are dominated by stratocumulus (Sc), altostratus (As), cumulus (Cu), and stratus (St), with Sc accounting for above 40% of total cloud occurrence. Yet microphysical properties differ markedly between these two groups. LWP shows the most contrast and it is evidently larger in NCCV than in non-NCCV cloud systems. As for the spatial structure of cloud microphysics in the NCCV domain, it is found that Sc, As, St, and nimbostratus (Ns) constitute the primary background, and Sc remains the dominant cloud type in almost all spatial sectors. LWP and IWP tend to have stronger spatial heterogeneity than Re_liq and Re_ice. LWP gets notably larger in the northern to northwestern sectors, whereas IWP shows much higher variations in both radial and azimuthal dimensions. These results reveal the statistical microphysical characteristics of cloud systems associated with NCCV from the perspective of satellite observations, providing a reference for a deeper understanding of their unique cloud and precipitation physical processes.

</details>


### [94] [YOLO-Based Landslide Identification and Causal Inference Using Double Machine Learning in Longyan, Fujian](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132157)
*Jiaqi He,Lingsheng Luo,Weiwei Li,Yuedan Luo,Xinyi Huang,H Wang,CL Guo,Shengdong Chen,Chuanan Xia*

Method: 采用YOLO深度学习模型基于2024年福建龙岩卫星影像构建训练数据集进行滑坡识别；采用双机器学习模型（Double Machine Learning）分析降雨、NDVI、距道路距离等致灾因子与滑坡之间的因果推断关系；利用SHAP值评估各因子的重要性排序。

Result: 2024年共识别滑坡1185处，总面积约31.02 km²，主要集中于上杭、武平、长汀及新罗南部；滑坡主要分布在海拔300-500 m、坡度10°-25°、年降雨量1600-1700 mm的区域；SHAP值显示关键因子排序为：NDVI > 降雨 > 距道路距离 > 距河流距离 > 坡向；因果推断表明6-7月降雨对滑坡有显著正向因果效应，与降雨型滑坡物理机制及政府报告数据一致。

Conclusion: 本文提出的框架和研究成果为闽西南地区滑坡识别与风险评估提供了有价值的技术和理论支持。

Abstract (英文): Landslides and their associated secondary hazards present substantial threats to both public infrastructure and resident safety. The rapid and accurate identification of large-scale landslide events remains a critical challenge in the field of engineering geology. In this study, a YOLO-based deep learning model is developed for landslide identification relying on a training dataset constructed using the satellite imagery of Longyan City, Fujian Province, in 2024. Adopting the double machine learning model, we examine the causal inference relationships between landslide and causative factors, including rainfall (R), mean Normalized Difference Vegetation Index (NDVI) and Distance to roads (DRoa). A total of 1185 landslides is identified in 2024, covering an area of approximately 31.02 km2. The landslides are predominantly concentrated in Shanghang, Wuping, Changting, and the southern part of Xinluo. The landslides mainly correspond to elevations around 300–500 m, slopes among the interval of [10°, 25°], and annual rainfall intensities ranging from 1600 m to 1700 mm. The top five key factors for landslide occurrence in descending order are NDVI, R, DRoa, Distance to Rivers (DRiv) and Aspect (A), in terms SHAP values. Causal inference analysis reveals that the rainfall in June and July shows significant positive causal effects to landslide, which is consistent with the physical mechanism of rainfall-induced landslide and the landslide data reported by the government. The framework proposed and the findings in this study offer valuable technical and theoretical support for landslide identification and risk assessment in southwestern Fujian.

### [95] [MS3CHFormer: A Multi-Scale Spatial–Spectral Convolutional Hybrid Transformer for Hyperspectral Image Classification](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132173)
*Jian Yu,Haixin Sun,Fanlei Meng,Jiaqi Liang,Xing Zhou*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为MS3CHFormer的多尺度空间-光谱卷积混合Transformer模型，通过多分支多感受野的卷积模块、Token选择性稀疏Transformer编码器、局部-全局特征融合模块和细节保持增强模块，有效解决了高光谱图像分类中多尺度特征建模不足、局部与全局特征交互低效以及Transformer计算复杂度高的问题，在四个公开数据集上取得了优于现有方法的分类性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有深度学习方法在高光谱图像分类中仍存在多尺度空间-光谱特征建模不足、局部与全局特征缺乏高效交互机制、Transformer计算复杂度高且存在冗余信息等问题，限制了模型性能。

Method: 1) 多尺度空间-光谱卷积模块(MS3ConvM)：通过多分支多感受野设计联合建模不同尺度的空间和光谱特征；2) Token选择性稀疏Transformer编码器(TSSTE)：通过动态相关性感知注意力(DCAA)自适应选择Token并进行稀疏建模，降低计算复杂度并抑制冗余信息；3) 局部-全局特征融合模块(LGFFM)：将CNN和Transformer特征映射到不同表示空间实现深度互补融合；4) 细节保持增强模块(DPEM)：通过残差连接引入原始细节信息补偿高层语义表示中的细节损失。

Result: 在四个公开高光谱数据集上的实验表明，MS3CHFormer在有限训练样本下优于现有最先进方法，具有优异的分类精度、鲁棒性和泛化能力。

Conclusion: 所提出的MS3CHFormer通过多尺度空间-光谱卷积与稀疏Transformer的高效混合，有效提升了高光谱图像分类性能，在复杂地物表示、计算效率和数据稀缺场景下均表现出显著优势。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：100%。本身就是遥感高光谱图像分类论文。改进方案：1) 可进一步引入光谱波段间的物理相关性先验来指导Token选择策略；2) 可探索更高效的稀疏注意力机制如哈希近似或低秩分解以进一步降低计算开销；3) MS3ConvM可扩展为3D卷积与2D卷积的自适应组合以适应不同地物类型的空间-光谱联合建模需求；4) DPEM可与边缘检测或形态学操作相结合以增强地物边界保持能力；5) 可引入少样本学习或自监督预训练策略进一步降低对标注样本的依赖。

Abstract (英文): Deep learning methods that integrate convolutional neural networks (CNNs) and Transformers have achieved remarkable progress in hyperspectral image (HSI) classification. However, existing methods still suffer from insufficient multi-scale spatial–spectral feature modeling, a lack of efficient interaction mechanisms between local and global features, and the inherent high computational complexity and redundant information of Transformers, which limit model performance. To address these issues, a Multi-Scale Spatial–Spectral Convolutional Hybrid Transformer model (MS3CHFormer) is proposed in this article. Specifically, a Multi-Scale Spatial–Spectral Convolution Module (MS3ConvM) is first constructed. Through a multi-branch and multi-receptive-field design, it jointly models spatial and spectral features at different scales, thereby enhancing the representation capability of complex ground objects. Then, a Token-Selective Sparse Transformer Encoder (TSSTE) is designed, which adaptively selects tokens and performs sparse modeling via a Dynamic Correlation-Aware Attention (DCAA) mechanism, effectively reducing computational complexity while suppressing redundant information and further reinforcing key feature representations. Furthermore, a Local–Global Feature Fusion Module (LGFFM) is designed to achieve deep complementary fusion of CNN and Transformer features by mapping them into different representation spaces. Finally, a Detail-Preserving Enhancement Module (DPEM) introduces original detail information through residual connections to compensate for detail loss in high-level semantic representations, thereby enhancing the representation capability of boundaries and fine-grained structures. Experiments and comparative analyses on four public HSI datasets demonstrate that the proposed MS3CHFormer outperforms state-of-the-art methods and achieves superior classification accuracy under limited training samples, exhibiting excellent robustness and generalization ability.

</details>


### [96] [Fusion of Airborne and Ground-Based Multi-Source Data for High-Precision 3D Real-Scene Modeling of Historic Cultural District](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132171)
*Huineng Yan,Yuan Qi,Yaxin Wen,Yu Li,Zhigang Lu,Rui Wang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统无人机倾斜摄影在历史街区的复杂巷道环境中存在数据空洞、纹理不足和精度较差的问题，阻碍了无人机技术在文化遗产保护中的广泛应用。

Method: 1) 建立基于图像灰度变化范围参数的畸变区域识别算法；2) 融合无人机倾斜摄影、手机近景摄影测量和RTK定位技术；3) 构建三维实景重建技术框架；4) 在真实历史街区进行实地实验验证。

Conclusion: 提出的多源数据融合三维重建技术框架能有效解决传统无人机倾斜摄影在历史街区复杂环境中的局限性，为历史街区的数字化保护、修复规划和智慧文旅提供了可参考的技术方案。

Abstract (英文): Traditional Unmanned Aerial Vehicle (UAV) oblique photogrammetry for 3D real-scene modeling of historic cultural districts suffers from data gaps, insufficient texture, and poor accuracy in complex alleyway environments, hindering the widespread adoption of UAV technology. To address these challenges, this paper establishes a distortion region identification algorithm based on image grayscale variation range parameters. Then, through fusing UAV oblique photogrammetry, close-range smartphone photogrammetry, and Real-Time Kinematic (RTK) positioning technology, it ultimately constructs a 3D real-scene reconstruction technical framework. To validate the method’s effectiveness and reliability, a field experiment was conducted in the Zaoerxiang Historic Cultural District of Zhanggong District, Ganzhou City, Jiangxi Province, China. The experimental results demonstrate that the proposed algorithm can effectively identify distortions in the modeling results from UAV images. After fusing smartphone images from distorted regions and RTK measurements from ground control points (GCPs), the discrepancies in X, Y, and Z coordinates between the results and verification points mostly fall within 10 to 25 mm, while the differences from the measured lengths using a steel tape measure and a leveling rod were within the range of 10 to 20 mm. Furthermore, compared to approaches that rely solely on UAV images or on the fusion of UAV and all ground-based images for modeling, the method proposed in this paper restores building texture information in occluded areas and improves the accuracy of 3D real-scene modeling while simultaneously reducing data-processing and storage requirements and enhancing operational efficiency. It provides a referenceable technical framework for digital preservation, restoration planning, and smart cultural tourism of historic districts.

### [97] [A Scalable Clustering-Based Method for Vegetation Mapping in Large Areas Using Satellite Image Time Series](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132162)
*Baggio Luiz de Castro e Silva,Karine Reis Ferreira,Gilberto Ribeiro de Queiroz,Juliana Santos da Mota,Erison Carlos dos Santos Monteiro,Mayara Teodoro,Isabel Cristina de Oliveira Silva,Murilo Brasil da Silva,Rodrigo Delgado Inácio,Rafael Andrade Aluvei,Agata Fabielle Gomes,Cláudio Almeida,Marcos Adami*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于聚类（GPU加速SOM+层次聚类+DTW）的半自动方法，用于在巴西塞拉多生物群落中快速、低成本地绘制次生植被图。该方法将专家标注从像素级别缩减到约3000个聚类级别，使制图时间从2年缩短至6个月，总体精度达96.45%，次生植被面积约9.87万平方公里。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 巴西塞拉多生物多样性热点受到农业扩张和原生植被转化的严重威胁，需要高效监测支持保护与环境政策。在异质景观中，基于监督分类的LULC制图面临大量高质量训练样本的需求瓶颈，亟需开发减少训练样本需求、可扩展的次生植被制图方法。

Method: 两阶段方法：第一阶段为无监督过程，利用GPU加速的自组织映射（SOM）和基于动态时间弯曲（DTW）的层次聚类，对卫星影像时间序列进行聚类，生成光谱-时间聚类；第二阶段由专家通过目视解译对聚类进行标注和精化，将专家知识从像素级别转移到分组的光谱-时间模式上。

Result: 应用于塞拉多69.2万平方公里区域，次生植被面积81,209 km²（11.74%）；设计估算面积98,683±10,071 km²；总体精度96.45±1.52%，用户精度96.27±2.40%，生产者精度79.22±7.94%，F1-score 86.90%。初始聚类标注覆盖86.3%的次生植被面积，仅需约3000次聚类级决策。制图时间从2年缩短至6个月。

Conclusion: 本文提出的半自动聚类方法能在大幅减少人力投入的同时保持所需专题精度，已成功应用于TerraClass Cerrado 2024业务化监测周期，证明了该方法在大尺度异质景观次生植被制图中的有效性和实用性。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。1）对于遥感领域类似异质景观（如中国南方喀斯特、东南亚热带雨林）的次生植被/森林恢复监测，可直接迁移该SOM+DTW聚类框架；2）可引入主动学习策略，在聚类标注阶段优先选择不确定性高的聚类进行专家标注，进一步提升效率；3）可将DTW替换为更高效的时序相似性度量（如ShapeDTW或时间序列Transformer嵌入），加速大规模处理；4）未来可引入弱监督或自监督学习方法自动标注部分聚类，进一步减少人工标注量。

Abstract (英文): The Brazilian Cerrado, a global biodiversity hotspot, is under increasing pressure from agricultural expansion and native vegetation conversion, underscoring the need for efficient monitoring to support conservation and environmental policies. In heterogeneous landscapes, land use and land cover (LULC) mapping using supervised classification methods faces a major bottleneck: the need for extensive and high-quality training datasets. To address this challenge, we propose a semi-automated, clustering-based methodology for mapping secondary vegetation within previously deforested areas, reducing training-sample requirements and enabling scalable mapping through the clustering of satellite image time series. In the first stage, an unsupervised process integrates graphics processing unit (GPU)-accelerated Self-Organizing Maps and hierarchical clustering with Dynamic Time Warping to produce spectro-temporal clusters. In the second stage, specialists label and refine these clusters by visual interpretation, transferring expert knowledge from individual pixels to grouped spectro-temporal patterns. Applied to 692,000 km2 of previously deforested land in the Cerrado biome, the methodology produced a mapped secondary vegetation area of 81,209 km2 (11.74%). The design-based estimated area was 98,683 ± 10,071 km2, with an overall accuracy of 96.45 ± 1.52%, a user’s accuracy of 96.27 ± 2.40%, a producer’s accuracy of 79.22 ± 7.94%, and an F1-score of 86.90%. The initial cluster labeling accounted for 86.3% of the final secondary vegetation area and limited the interpretation task to approximately 3000 cluster-level decisions. Implemented in the TerraClass Cerrado 2024 cycle, the workflow reduced the secondary vegetation mapping phase from approximately two years to six months while maintaining the thematic accuracy required for large-scale operational monitoring.

### [98] [Integrating Gross Error Identification with Deep Learning for InSAR Topography-Dependent Delay Correction: A Case Study of the Baihetan Hydropower Station Area](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132168)
*Yuanyuan Liu,H T Chen,Dan Liu,Bo Liu*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出一种结合粗差识别与多层感知机（EiMLP）的组合模型，用于校正地形相关对流层延迟。该方法通过相位梯度检测解缠相位跳变，并利用MLP从单幅干涉图中重建大气相位。在白鹤滩水电站区域的实验表明，该方法模拟大气相位的SSIM达0.970，RMSE为0.673 rad，校正后干涉图相位标准差平均降低83%，显著抑制了地形相关相位，并能揭示被大气误差掩蔽的斜坡失稳信号。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对流层延迟严重制约高精度InSAR观测，特别是在高山峡谷区域。现有校正方法在处理地形复杂区域时存在局限性，亟需一种基于单幅干涉图、不依赖外部数据且能有效处理粗差的大气校正方法。

Method: 提出EiMLP组合模型：(1) 粗差识别模块：基于相位梯度检测解缠相位中的跳变；(2) MLP模块：利用单幅干涉图的解缠相位和DEM高程信息重建大气相位。整个过程仅需单幅干涉图，无需外部气象数据或多时相统计。

Result: 模拟大气相位SSIM达0.970，RMSE为0.673 rad；实际干涉图校正后相位标准差平均降低83%；地形相关相位得到显著抑制；原始干涉图中被大气误差掩盖的斜坡失稳信号在校正后清晰显现。

Conclusion: EiMLP模型基于单幅干涉图即可实现有效的对流层延迟校正，具有稳健的适用性，为未来InSAR对流层延迟校正提供了可靠参考。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。本文本身就是InSAR遥感领域的论文。改进方向：(1) 可将MLP替换为更先进的深度学习模型（如Transformer、CNN-LSTM混合架构）以提升大气相位重建精度；(2) 引入多源辅助数据（如GNSS PWV、气象再分析资料）作为MLP输入特征；(3) 粗差识别模块可结合空间统计或聚类方法提升跳变检测鲁棒性；(4) 可扩展至时序InSAR处理框架，实现时序大气校正；(5) 在复杂地形区域（如青藏高原、横断山脉）进行跨区域验证以评估泛化能力。

Abstract (英文): Tropospheric delay poses a major limitation to high-precision InSAR observations, particularly in high mountain and canyon regions. To address this issue, this study proposes a combined model (EiMLP) that integrates gross error identification with a multilayer perceptron (MLP) for topography-dependent tropospheric delay correction. The gross error identification module detects unwrapped phase jumps based on phase gradients, followed by an MLP model that reconstructs the atmospheric phase using unwrapped phase and elevation information from a single interferogram. The proposed method is validated in the Baihetan Hydropower Station area and compared with traditional correction methods. Experimental results demonstrate that the proposed method achieves a Structural Similarity Index Measure (SSIM) of 0.970 and a Root Mean Square Error (RMSE) of 0.673 rad for the simulated atmospheric phase. After atmospheric correction, the average phase standard deviation of the interferograms is reduced by 83%, and the topography-related correlation is significantly suppressed. Furthermore, after correction by the proposed method, the signals that are masked by atmospheric errors in the original interferograms can be clearly revealed, indicating the potential for slope instability. These findings indicate that the EiMLP model, operating on a single interferogram, exhibits robust applicability and provides a reliable reference for future InSAR tropospheric delay correction.

### [99] [Trait-Dependent Effects of Band Selection on Predicting Soybean Biomass, Leaf Area Index, and Canopy Cover from Hyperspectral Reflectance](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132179)
*Etsushi Kumagai,Takayuki Yabiku,Yusuke Masuya,Kensuke Kimura,Erina Fushimi,Ryosuke Nomiyama*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本研究评估了不同波段选择算法（全波段PLS、PLS-VIP、BoLASSO和集成方法）对大豆冠层高光谱反射率（501-801 nm）预测地上生物量（AGB）、叶面积指数（LAI）和冠层覆盖度（CC）的影响。结果表明，波段选择的有效性取决于目标性状：全波段PLS对AGB预测效果较好，而BoLASSO在减少波段数量的情况下对LAI和CC达到了与PLS相当的精度。年际间迁移性对AGB比LAI和CC更困难，所选波长主要集中在可见光、红边和近红外区域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 冠层性状的非破坏性预测对理解作物生长和提高表型分析效率至关重要。高光谱反射率提供了详细光谱信息，但波段选择在回归-based性状预测中的作用尚不清楚，尤其是在冠层尺度上。

Method: 使用大豆冠层高光谱反射率（501-801 nm，VNIR范围），数据集涵盖多个地点、年份、品种和灌溉处理。比较了全波段偏最小二乘回归（PLS）与三种波段选择方法：PLS-变量重要性投影（VIP）、自助LASSO（BoLASSO）和集成方法。模型性能通过Kennard-Stone验证和留一年交叉验证评估。

Result: 全波段PLS在Kennard-Stone验证下对AGB表现良好；BoLASSO在减少波段数量下对LAI和CC达到与PLS相当的精度。留一年交叉验证显示AGB的年际迁移性比LAI和CC更困难。所选波长主要集中在可见光、红边和近红外区域。

Conclusion: 波段选择策略应根据目标性状定制，选定的VNIR波段可为大豆冠层性状的简化传感提供候选光谱区域。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。1）可将该方法推广至其他作物（如小麦、玉米、水稻）的冠层性状估测，验证波段选择策略的普适性；2）可结合卫星/无人机高光谱影像（如Sentinel-2、PRISMA、EnMAP），将地面冠层尺度结论向遥感像元尺度扩展；3）可引入深度学习（如1D-CNN、注意力机制）进一步优化波段选择与特征提取；4）可扩展到更多冠层生化参数（如叶绿素、氮含量、水分含量）的预测；5）可探索将选出的关键波段（可见光+红边+NIR）用于多光谱传感器的波段设计，实现低成本、高通量的表型监测。

Abstract (英文): Predicting canopy traits non-destructively is important for understanding crop growth and improving phenotyping efficiency. Hyperspectral reflectance provides detailed spectral information, but the role of band selection in regression-based trait prediction at the canopy scale remains unclear. In this study, we evaluated the effects of different band-selection algorithms on the prediction accuracy of aboveground biomass (AGB), leaf area index (LAI), and canopy cover (CC) in soybeans using canopy hyperspectral reflectance in the visible to near-infrared (VNIR) range from 501 to 801 nm. The dataset included multiple sites, years, cultivars, and irrigation treatments. We compared a full-band partial least squares regression (PLS) model with three band-selection methods (PLS-Variable Importance in Projection (VIP), Bootstrapped least absolute shrinkage and selection operator (LASSO) (BoLASSO), and an ensemble approach). Model performance was assessed using Kennard–Stone validation and leave-one-year-out cross-validation. The results showed that the effectiveness of band selection depended on the target trait. Full-band PLS performed well for AGB under Kennard–Stone validation, whereas BoLASSO achieved comparable accuracy to PLS for LAI and CC using a reduced number of selected bands. Leave-one-year-out cross-validation showed that year-to-year transferability was more difficult for AGB than for LAI and CC. The selected wavelengths were located mainly in the visible, red-edge, and near-infrared regions. These results indicate that band-selection strategies should be tailored to the target trait and that selected VNIR bands can provide candidate spectral regions for simplified sensing of soybean canopy traits.

### [100] [Spatial and Temporal Variability of Terrestrial Water Storage and Their Relationship with Groundwater Level with GRACE, GLDAS and Observations: A Case Study of Murray–Darling Basin](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132206)
*Chongya Ma,Jiping Liu,Guobin Fu*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本研究利用GRACE卫星数据、GLDAS陆面模型和气候观测数据，分析了Murray-Darling流域2002-2025年陆地水储量的时空变化、与地下水位的关联，发现TWS具有明显年际波动，与降雨、蒸发和径流显著相关，为地下水资源管理提供了重要参考。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 揭示Murray-Darling流域陆地水储量的时空变化规律及其与地下水位的关联，以支持基于GRACE卫星信息的地下水管理决策。

Method: 综合使用GRACE卫星反演的陆地水储量数据、GLDAS陆面模型模拟结果（包括蒸散发和径流）、以及气候观测数据，通过聚类分析识别TWS空间模式，通过相关分析和组合模型评估降雨、蒸发和径流对TWS变化的解释能力，并对比TWS反演的地下水储量变化与实测地下水位变化。

Result: (1) TWS呈现2002-2009年负异常下降、2010-2017年正异常下降、2018-2025年正负混合上升的三阶段演变；(2) 识别出5个主导聚类模式解释TWS空间变异性；(3) TWS与降雨强相关但局部较弱；(4) 联合蒸发和径流的组合模型显著提升对TWS变异的解释能力；(5) TWS反演与实测地下水变化既有相似性也有差异。

Conclusion: GRACE结合陆面模型和气候数据能够有效揭示流域尺度水储量时空动态，对改进地下水资源管理具有重要价值。

Abstract (英文): Spatial and temporal patterns of terrestrial water storage (TWS), and their relationship with groundwater levels, were investigated with the Gravity Recovery and Climate Experiment (GRACE) satellite data, the Global Land Data Assimilation System (GLDAS) land surface model results, and climate observations for the Murray–Darling Basin (MDB). The results show that: (1) TWS displays a clear temporal variability: a negative TWS anomaly with a declining trend during 2002–2009, a positive TWS anomaly with a decreasing trend during 2010–2017, and a period of mixed positive and negative TWS anomalies being accompanied by an increasing trend from 2018 to 2025; (2) five dominant cluster patterns were identified that explain the spatial variability of temporal TWS across the MDB; (3) overall, TWS temporal variability is strongly correlated with rainfall, although it is weak at certain locations; (4) TWS is also influenced by evaporation (both actual and potential evapotranspiration, AET and PET) and runoff, and a combined model significantly improves the overall performance in explaining TWS temporal variability; and (5) TWS-derived groundwater storage changes show both similarities and differences in comparison with groundwater level observation changes, reflecting complex hydrogeological processes and the influence of human activities such as groundwater extraction. These findings provide valuable insights to support improved groundwater resource management with GRACE satellite information and land surface models.

### [101] [S2M-Net: Dynamic Hyperspectral Unmixing Network Integrating Spectral Sequence Mamba and Local Spatial–Spectral Awareness](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132228)
*Yi Yang,Mei‐Yan Xu,Weidong Zhang,Ji Zhang,Yuquan Gan*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出一种结合光谱序列Mamba与局部空谱感知的动态高光谱解混网络，通过非对称双流协作架构（全局光谱Mamba分支+局部空谱CNN分支）和空间自适应门控融合模块，在多个公开数据集上实现了更优的解混精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于深度学习的高光谱解混方法中，CNN感受野有限，难以捕获全光谱序列的长程依赖；Transformer虽具备全局建模能力，但计算复杂度为二次方，且无法在连续光谱波段中自适应滤除冗余噪声。为此，本文旨在设计一种兼具线性复杂度全局建模与局部空谱细节感知的解混网络。

Method: 提出非对称双流协作架构：(1) 光谱序列Mamba分支：将高光谱数据建模为一维连续序列，利用选择性状态空间模型以线性复杂度进行全局扫描，自适应滤除冗余光谱波段，提取高纯度全局光谱语义；(2) 局部空谱感知分支：采用注意力增强的CNN捕获局部连续光谱变化和空间纹理，为丰度估计提供细粒度几何边界约束；(3) 空间自适应门控融合模块：根据不同空间区域的像素混合复杂度，动态平衡全局光谱语义与局部空谱细节。

Result: 在多个公开高光谱数据集上的大量实验表明，所提方法在解混精度上相较于对比方法取得了显著提升。

Conclusion: 本文验证了将状态空间模型（Mamba）引入高光谱解混任务的有效性，通过双流架构协同全局光谱建模与局部细节感知、并辅以自适应融合机制，为高光谱解混提供了一种新的高效方案。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。作为一篇直接面向高光谱遥感解混的论文，可从以下方面改进：(1) 将现有的像素级解混扩展为亚像素级或超像素级解混，进一步提升空间分辨率鲁棒性；(2) 引入多时相或高光谱-多光谱融合数据以增强丰度估计的时-空一致性；(3) 将Mamba分支替换为双向Mamba或2D Mamba以增强空谱联合建模；(4) 结合自监督或弱监督学习范式，减少对纯像元先验的依赖；(5) 探索将门控融合模块替换为神经架构搜索（NAS）自动寻优的融合策略。

Abstract (英文): Hyperspectral unmixing aims to extract pure endmembers and their corresponding abundance from mixed pixels. Existing deep learning-based unmixing methods predominantly rely on convolutional neural networks (CNNs) or Transformer architectures. However, CNNs suffer from limited receptive fields and struggle to capture long-range spectral dependencies across the entire spectral sequence. While Transformers possess global modeling capabilities, they are constrained by quadratic computational complexity and lack the ability to adaptively filter redundant noise in consecutive spectral bands. To address these limitations, this paper proposes a dynamic hyperspectral unmixing network integrating a spectral sequence Mamba with local spatial–spectral awareness. Specifically, the network features a novel asymmetric dual-stream collaborative architecture. The first branch, the spectral sequence Mamba, models hyperspectral data as a one-dimensional continuous sequence and employs the selective state space model to perform global scanning with linear complexity. This adaptively filters redundant spectral bands to accurately extract high-purity global spectral semantics. The second branch, dedicated to local spatial–spectral awareness, uses an attention-augmented CNN to capture local continuous spectral variations and spatial textures, providing fine-grained geometric boundary constraints for abundance estimation. Furthermore, a spatially adaptive gated fusion module is designed to dynamically balance global spectral semantics and local spatial–spectral details according to the pixel mixing complexity of varying spatial regions. Extensive experiments on multiple public hyperspectral datasets demonstrate that the proposed method achieves significant improvements in unmixing accuracy over comparative methods.

### [102] [Spatiotemporal Evolution of Ecological Environment Quality and Driving Factors in the Loess Plateau of Northern Shaanxi](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132219)
*Ruize Tang,Z L Li,Shuangcheng Zhang,Junkai Gu,Jiandong Xiao*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本研究基于遥感生态指数（RSEI）模型，系统评估了2000-2024年陕北黄土高原生态环境质量的时空演变，发现EEQ呈波动上升趋势（RSEI均值从0.376升至0.545），空间上呈现“南高北低、西北最低”的格局，改善区域占比91.21%，地貌类型是影响EEQ空间异质性的主导因子（平均q值0.701）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
