Method: (1) 构建遥感生态指数（RSEI）模型进行综合评估；(2) 采用Theil–Sen估计量、Mann–Kendall检验和Hurst指数检测变化显著性并预测未来趋势；(3) 运用Geodetector模型探究驱动因子。

Result: (1) EEQ呈波动上升趋势，RSEI均值从0.376升至0.545，年均增长约0.00569；(2) 空间呈“南高北低、西北最低”格局，“优”和“良”等级占比提升约20个百分点，“中”等级从13.61%扩至47.12%；(3) 改善区域占91.21%，与未来预测改善区域高度重叠；(4) 地貌类型对EEQ空间异质性影响最大（多年平均q值0.701），地貌-土地利用交互作用持续塑造区域EEQ空间分布。

Conclusion: RSEI模型能有效评估陕北黄土高原生态环境质量的时空演变，地貌类型是主导驱动因子，研究成果可为该区域精准生态修复规划和空间优化提供科学依据。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。改进方案：(1) 可引入植被生产力（如GPP/NPP）、土壤水分遥感产品等更多生态参量丰富RSEI指标体系；(2) 可结合Sentinel-1 SAR数据补充地表形变/侵蚀信息，增强对黄土高原水土流失的监测能力；(3) 可尝试引入机器学习方法（如随机森林、XGBoost）优化Geodetector模型中的因子交互检测；(4) 可结合高时间分辨率遥感数据（如MODIS每日产品）开展更细尺度的年内/季节动态分析；(5) 可引入大气校正预处理步骤（如6S模型）提升遥感指数计算精度。

Abstract (英文): Accurately assessing the spatiotemporal evolution of ecological environment quality (EEQ) on the Loess Plateau of Northern Shaanxi is of great significance for consolidating the ecological security barrier of the Yellow River Basin. Most of the existing research focuses on a single ecological theme, which does not reflect the overall ecological status of the region. In this study, a remote sensing ecological index (RSEI) model was constructed to systematically assess the EEQ from 2000 to 2024. The Theil–Sen estimator, Mann–Kendall test, and Hurst exponent were jointly employed to detect change significance and predict future trends, while the Geodetector model was applied to explore driving factors. The results were as follows: (1) EEQ exhibited a fluctuating but overall upward trend, with the mean RSEI rising from 0.376 in 2000 to 0.545 in 2024—an average annual increase of approximately 0.00569. (2) Spatially, a distinct pattern of “higher in the south, lower in the north and the lowest in the northwest” was observed. Over the 25-year period, the combined proportion of “excellent” and “good” grades increased by roughly 20 percentage points, and the “moderate” grade expanded from 13.61% to 47.12%. (3) Areas showing an improving trend accounted for 91.21% of the total area and highly overlapped with those projected to improve in the future. (4) Single-factor detection revealed that geomorphological type exerted the greatest influence on the spatial heterogeneity of EEQ, with a multi-year mean q-value of 0.701. Interaction detection further indicates that the geomorphology–land use interaction may continue to shape the regional EEQ’s spatial distribution. These findings provide a scientific basis for precise ecological restoration planning and spatial optimization on the Loess Plateau of Northern Shaanxi.

### [103] [Automated On-Orbit Absolute Radiometric Calibration: A Preliminary Method and Results](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132186)
*Xiaojie Yang,Qiuyan Liu,Song Yang,Yang Bai,Shuai Huang,Yingshan Sun,Jiangpeng Li,Hongyu Wu,Xing Zhong,Weibin Wang*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 针对缺乏星上定标系统的低成本商业卫星（如吉林一号星座），本文提出了一种基于MCD43A2/MCD12Q1产品生成定标区域矢量、结合MODTRAN查找表实现全自动在轨绝对辐射定标的方法，无需地面同步实验和成像资源消耗，精度优于4%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 低成本商业卫星（如吉林一号星座）缺乏昂贵的星上定标系统，传统替代方法难以对大规模卫星星座实现低资源消耗的自动化可靠定标，而伪不变定标场（PICS）方法因商业卫星密集成像计划而难以频繁观测，亟需一种适用于大量成像仪、依赖广泛可用的晴空地面目标的自动化定标方法。

Method: 利用MCD43A2（BRDF/反照率产品）和MCD12Q1（土地利用分类）生成定标区域矢量，将MODIS辐射基准传递至吉林一号；构建MODTRAN模型输入参数的查找表（LUT）；从吉林一号影像中提取定标像元和模型输入参数，通过对LUT插值获取各像元/波段的入瞳辐亮度，计算在轨绝对辐射定标系数。

Result: 基于RadCalNet对JL1GF02F PMS1传感器进行场地定标验证，所有波段的相对差异最大不超过4%。

Conclusion: 该方法无需地面同步实验、自动化程度高、不消耗商业成像资源，可为大规模商业卫星星座提供高效可靠的在轨定标方案。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：90%。改进方案：（1）可将该方法扩展至其他无星上定标系统的商业遥感星座（如高景一号、北京二号等），仅需适配对应传感器的光谱响应函数；（2）可引入国产卫星数据产品（如FY-3 MERSI或高分系列）替代MODIS作为辐射基准，减少对境外传感器的依赖；（3）可结合深度学习模型动态优化定标区域选择，进一步提升自动化与鲁棒性；（4）LUT插值可引入高斯过程回归等替代线性插值，提升辐亮度估计精度；（5）可考虑植被物候变化对地表BRDF的影响，引入时序模型自适应更新定标区域矢量。

Abstract (英文): On-orbit absolute radiometric calibration tracks sensor radiometric degradation and ensures accuracy for quantitative applications. Low-cost commercial satellites lack expensive on-board calibration systems, and traditional alternative methods cannot achieve automated, reliable calibration for large sensor fleets with low resource consumption. Pseudo-invariant calibration sites require no ground instruments, but commercial satellites’ heavy imaging schedules hinder frequent PICS observations. The Jilin-1 constellation is a large commercial constellation composed of satellites carrying multispectral imagers with resolution better than 1 m, and it has no on-board calibration system. Thus, an automated calibration method applicable to numerous imagers is needed, one that requires widely available clear-sky ground targets. Using MCD43A2 and MCD12Q1 products, we generate calibration region vectors to transfer the MODIS radiometric reference to Jilin-1. A look-up table (LUT) is constructed for the input parameters of the MODTRAN model. Calibration pixels and model input parameters are then extracted from Jilin-1 imagery using the region vectors, the LUT is interpolated to obtain the at-aperture radiance for each pixel and band, and on-orbit absolute radiometric calibration coefficients are calculated. The proposed method requires no ground-based synchronous experiments, achieves a high level of automation, and does not consume commercial imaging resources. The site calibration validation based on RadCalNet for the JL1GF02F PMS1 sensor shows that the maximum relative difference in the method across all bands is less than 4%.

</details>


### [104] [Assessing the Potential of EMIT Hyperspectral Data Combined with DEM-Derived Terrain Variables for Predicting Soil As, Cu and Zn Concentrations in a Mountainous Region of Southwest China](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132211)
*Guangping Qie,Minzi Wang,Ziping Pan,Z X Sun,Wenjin Xie,Zhiyi Liu,Guangxing Wang*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本研究利用EMIT高光谱数据结合DEM地形变量，通过随机森林和XGBoost模型预测贵州仁怀山区土壤砷(As)、铜(Cu)、锌(Zn)浓度。结果表明：As预测效果中等(验证R²=0.460)，Cu预测效果较差(R²=0.188)，Zn预测无效(R²=-0.028)，EMIT高光谱数据在山区重金属预测中能力有限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 星载成像光谱学为区域尺度土壤属性监测带来新机遇，但其在山区环境中预测土壤重金属浓度的能力尚未得到充分验证，特别是使用EMIT高光谱数据时。本研究旨在填补这一空白，评估EMIT数据在复杂地形条件下预测土壤重金属的可行性。

Method: 采用EMIT Level-2A表面反射率数据与DEM衍生地形变量，对贵州仁怀地区的土壤砷(As)、铜(Cu)、锌(Zn)浓度进行估算。仅使用位于有效EMIT覆盖范围内的土壤样本(As:139个, Cu:136个, Zn:130个)。在模型构建前对EMIT光谱变量和地形因子进行筛选以减少冗余，随后使用重复空间交叉验证测试随机森林和XGBoost模型。

Result: As的最佳模型结合了EMIT预测因子与高程，验证R²为0.460；Cu的模型表现较弱，验证R²为0.188；Zn的模型未能优于均值基准，验证R²为-0.028。空间预测图和残差模式表明：As具有中等预测潜力，Cu的预测价值有限，Zn仅具有探索性而非可靠的制图能力。

Conclusion: 在当前样本和预测因子条件下，EMIT高光谱数据对山区土壤As的预测表现出中等潜力，对Cu的预测价值有限，对Zn的制图能力仅为探索性而非可靠。EMIT数据在山区重金属预测中存在显著局限性，尤其对于某些元素表现不佳。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：75%。改进方案：(1) 引入多时相EMIT数据以捕捉土壤重金属的时间动态特征；(2) 融合Sentinel-1/2等其他遥感数据源，增加光谱与结构信息维度；(3) 采用深度学习方法(如CNN或Transformer)自动提取光谱-空间联合特征；(4) 增加土壤质地、pH、有机质等辅助环境变量；(5) 针对山区地形效应，引入地形辐射校正模型预处理EMIT数据；(6) 采用迁移学习或小样本学习策略缓解样本量不足问题；(7) 探索光谱微分变换(如一阶导数、连续统去除)增强重金属弱吸收特征。

Abstract (英文): Spaceborne imaging spectroscopy has created new opportunities for monitoring soil properties at regional scales. Its use for predicting soil heavy metal concentrations in mountainous environments, however, remains insufficiently tested, especially when EMIT hyperspectral data are used. In this study, EMIT Level-2A surface reflectance data were integrated with DEM-derived terrain variables to estimate soil arsenic (As), copper (Cu), and zinc (Zn) concentrations in Renhuai, Guizhou Province, Southwest China. Only soil samples falling within valid EMIT coverage were used for element-specific modeling, resulting in 139 samples for As, 136 for Cu, and 130 for Zn. To reduce redundancy among predictors, EMIT spectral variables and terrain factors were screened before model construction. Random forest and XGBoost models were then tested using repeated spatial cross-validation. The best-performing model for As combined EMIT predictors with elevation and achieved a validation R2 of 0.460. Model performance was considerably weaker for Cu, with a validation R2 of 0.188. For Zn, the model failed to outperform the mean-based benchmark, producing a negative validation R2 of −0.028. The spatial prediction maps and residual patterns suggested that the EMIT-based prediction showed moderate potential for As, limited predictive value for Cu, and exploratory rather than reliable mapping capability for Zn under the current sample and predictor conditions.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 棋盘格标定法虽然简单易用，但在高精度相机几何建模方面存在局限性，可能影响需要几何精度的下游视觉任务性能，因此需要探索更优的标定方法。

Method: 将相机标定问题重新置于摄影测量自标定（PSC）框架下，系统比较棋盘格标定法与PSC在多项视觉任务（包括基于运动恢复结构的3D重建、视觉SLAM、新视角合成与重建）中的精度和准确性表现。

Conclusion: 研究结果倡导在关键计算机视觉应用中实现范式转变，采用更能反映相机系统物理和投影特性的标定方法。

Abstract (英文): Imagery is fundamental to modern scientific research, making robust intrinsic camera calibration indispensable for accurate visual inference. The checkerboard-based calibration method has long been favored for its simplicity and ease of deployment and is widely used even in mission-critical computer vision pipelines. However, its limitations in modeling high-precision camera geometry can compromise downstream performance in tasks requiring geometric accuracy. In this work, camera calibration is revisited through the lens of photogrammetric self-calibration (PSC), and it is demonstrated that the PSC consistently outperforms the checkerboard method in both accuracy and precision across a range of vision tasks, including 3D reconstruction with structure from motion (SfM), visual simultaneous localization and mapping (SLAM), and novel-view synthesis and reconstruction. Our findings advocate for a paradigm shift toward calibration methods that better reflect the physical and projective properties of camera systems in real-world deployments for critical computer vision applications.

### [106] [Multi-Modal Multi-Scale Mamba with Frequency and Semantics-Guided Spectral Modeling for Hyperspectral Image Classification](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132207)
*Hui Peng,Wenzhun Huang,Kaihong Chen,Zhongyan Zhou,Zhen Wang*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出M3-Mamba框架，通过语言引导的多层次Mamba光谱建模，解决高光谱图像分类中光谱冗余、光谱-空间相关复杂和标注样本有限的问题。该方法利用多模态语义先验引导光谱建模，引入频域感知的Mamba状态空间模块捕获长程光谱依赖，并设计文本引导调制策略抑制噪声波段。在四个基准数据集上取得了竞争性结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高光谱图像分类面临三大挑战：高光谱冗余性、复杂的光谱-空间相关性以及标记样本有限。现有方法在处理长程光谱依赖时计算复杂度高，且缺乏有效的语义引导机制来区分光谱特征。

Method: 提出M3-Mamba框架，包含三个核心组件：1）语言引导机制，利用多模态表示的高层语义先验指导光谱建模；2）频域感知的Mamba状态空间模块，高效捕获长程光谱依赖且避免二次计算复杂度；3）文本引导调制策略，在语义指导下自适应重新加权光谱响应，抑制冗余/噪声波段，增强类别相关响应。

Result: 在Indian Pines、Pavia University、Salinas和Houston四个基准数据集上，M3-Mamba在总体精度、平均精度和Kappa系数上均达到竞争性水平。消融实验验证了各关键组件的有效性。

Conclusion: M3-Mamba框架通过语义到光谱的调制，有效应对光谱变异性与类别间混淆问题，在高光谱图像分类任务中展现出良好的应用前景。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。改进方案：1）当前框架主要在光谱维度建模，可扩展为三维扫描Mamba（空间-光谱联合），同时捕获空间邻域与光谱序列的全局依赖；2）语言引导部分可引入遥感领域专用视觉-语言模型（如GeoChat、RSGPT）的语义先验，提升对地物类别的语义理解精度；3）频域感知模块可结合小波变换或多尺度频域分解，适应不同地物类型的光谱特征尺度差异；4）文本引导调制策略可扩展为多模态融合，将SAR、LiDAR等其他遥感数据源作为额外语义引导，增强复杂场景下的分类鲁棒性。

Abstract (英文): Hyperspectral image (HSI) classification remains a challenging task due to high spectral redundancy, complex spectral–spatial correlations, and the limited availability of labeled samples. To address these issues, this paper proposes a novel framework termed M3-Mamba, which integrates language-guided, multi-level, and Mamba-based spectral modeling for hyperspectral image classification. The proposed M3-Mamba leverages high-level semantic priors derived from multimodal representations to guide discriminative spectral modeling, enabling effective interaction between semantic information and fine-grained spectral features. In addition, a frequency-aware Mamba-based state space module is introduced to efficiently capture long-range spectral dependencies while avoiding the quadratic computational complexity of conventional attention mechanisms. Meanwhile, a text-guided modulation strategy is designed to adaptively reweight spectral responses under semantic guidance, suppressing redundant or noisy bands and enhancing class-relevant spectral responses without compromising spectral fidelity. This semantic-to-spectral modulation allows M3-Mamba to better cope with spectral variability and inter-class confusion. Extensive experiments conducted on four widely used benchmark datasets, including Indian Pines, Pavia University, Salinas, and Houston datasets, demonstrate thatM3-Mamba achieves competitive overall accuracy, average accuracy, and Kappa coefficient under the adopted benchmark settings. Ablation studies further validate the effectiveness of each key component, confirming that the proposed framework demonstrates promising effectiveness for hyperspectral image classification.

### [107] [WASP-Mamba: A Wavelet-Enhanced Mamba Framework for Remote Sensing Semantic Segmentation](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132188)
*Yuhao Zhang,G Zhang,Yi Li,Yongbo Wu,Zhiguo Zhou*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出WASP-Mamba框架，针对高分辨率遥感图像语义分割中的尺度变化和边界退化问题，在编码器瓶颈处引入基于Mamba的空间金字塔池化模块增强多尺度特征聚合，并设计小波启发的Mamba解码器解耦重构低频语义与高频细节信息。在LoveDA、ISPRS Vaihingen和ISPRS Potsdam数据集上分别达到53.90%、84.32%和87.06%的mIoU，优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高分辨率遥感图像语义分割面临严重的尺度变化和复杂边界结构挑战，现有基于状态空间模型（如Mamba）的方法在多尺度上下文捕获和细粒度空间细节方面仍存在局限性。

Method: 提出WASP-Mamba框架：(1) 在编码器瓶颈处引入基于Mamba的空间金字塔池化模块，增强多尺度特征聚合与尺度鲁棒性；(2) 设计小波启发的Mamba解码器，通过解耦与重构低频语义信息和高频细节信息，缓解传统上采样导致的边界退化。

Conclusion: WASP-Mamba通过融合Mamba的高效全局建模能力与多尺度/小波策略，有效解决了遥感图像分割中的尺度变化和边界退化问题，取得了优越的分割性能。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：90%。改进方案：(1) 多尺度特征聚合方面，可引入自适应感受野机制，对不同地物类别动态调整尺度权重；(2) 小波解码器可与边缘检测分支结合，进一步强化建筑物/道路等规则的边界分割；(3) 可尝试将Mamba与卷积混合架构（如VMamba+CNN）结合，平衡局部纹理细节与全局上下文建模；(4) 针对不同遥感传感器（多光谱、高光谱）的多通道特性，可扩展小波变换的通道级分解策略。

Abstract (英文): Semantic segmentation of high-resolution remote sensing (HRRS) imagery is a fundamental task in Earth observation but remains challenging due to severe scale variations and complex boundary structures. Although State Space Models (SSMs), particularly Mamba, have shown strong potential for efficient global modeling with linear complexity, existing methods are still limited in capturing multi-scale context and fine-grained spatial details. To address these issues, we propose a novel framework named WASP-Mamba for HRRS image segmentation. A Mamba-based spatial pyramid pooling module is introduced at the encoder bottleneck to enhance multi-scale feature aggregation and improve robustness to scale variations. In addition, a wavelet-inspired Mamba decoder is designed to decouple and reconstruct low-frequency semantic information and high-frequency details, mitigating boundary degradation caused by conventional upsampling. Extensive experiments on the LoveDA, ISPRS Vaihingen and ISPRS Potsdam datasets demonstrate that the proposed method achieves 53.90%, 84.32% and 87.06% mIoU, respectively. Compared with recent state-of-the-art methods, WASP-Mamba achieves superior segmentation performance.

Method: 以2022年欧盟LUCAS调查数据为参考，辅以波兰S2GLC PL 2021年土地覆盖图，使用精确率、召回率、F1分数和IoU指标，评估GDW、ESA WC、ELC三种10米分辨率全球产品的森林分类精度及其组合方案。

Conclusion: 不同全球产品在波兰森林制图中精度各异，但通过合适的组合策略可以显著提升森林制图精度，优于任何单一产品。

Abstract (英文): Using accurate land cover data is essential to monitor land use and cover changes and assess the effectiveness of various environmental policies. Our results showed that forest mapping accuracy of three global products varies for Poland, with F1-score equal to 72.2% for ELC, 76.9% for ESA WC, and 68.8% for GDW. IoU against S2GLC PL was equal to 82.6%, 82.3% and 75.2%, for ELC, ESA WC and GDW, respectively, and slightly exceeded 70.5% for three global products. A specific combination of binary forest maps from global products, where the output forest area consisted of forests mapped at the same time by all three products and forests mapped at the same time only by GDW and ESA WC yielded better accuracy indicators than any single product and other tested combinations (F1-score equal to 80.4%, and IoU against S2GLC PL equal to 87.1%).

### [109] [SMMNet: A Plug-and-Play Lightweight Detection Framework for UAV Aerial Imagery](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132232)
*Minna Liu,Zhigang Luo,Yaowen Hu,Jialang Liu*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: SMMNet是一个轻量级即插即用的无人机航拍图像目标检测框架，包含三个核心模块：结构扩散特征提取器（SDFE）、Mamba驱动的感受野上下文聚合器（MRCA）和掩码引导的贝叶斯框精炼模块（MBBR）。在YOLOv13-S骨干上，VisDrone2019数据集达到32.8% mAP@0.5:0.95和52.6% mAP@0.5，以87 FPS在A800上运行，并在Jetson Orin NX边缘设备上达到30 FPS。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无人机航拍图像中的目标检测面临密集小目标、尺度变化大、背景复杂以及严格的机载计算资源限制等挑战，现有方法难以在精度与效率之间取得良好平衡。

Method: 提出SMMNet框架，包含三个模块：(1) SDFE利用各向异性扩散在下采样过程中保留边界敏感特征；(2) MRCA通过Mamba驱动的多方向选择性状态空间扫描以线性复杂度捕获长程上下文；(3) MBBR利用MobileSAM掩码证据和ELBO假阳性过滤，基于MAP思想进行置信度自适应的边界框精炼。

Result: 以YOLOv13-S为主检测器，VisDrone2019上mAP@0.5:0.95达32.8%，mAP@0.5达52.6%，在A800上87 FPS，相比基线提升3.6和4.5个点。在DroneVehicle和SeaDronesSee上分别有2.53±0.12和2.77±0.06 mAP提升。Jetson Orin NX边缘部署可达30 FPS（TensorRT FP16, 15W TDP）。

Conclusion: SMMNet作为轻量即插即用框架，在多种YOLO检测器和多个无人机航拍基准上均带来一致性能提升，同时在边缘设备上保持实时推理速度，适合资源受限的无人机感知任务。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。该论文本身即为无人机遥感目标检测研究。改进方向：(1) SDFE的各向异性扩散可进一步结合多尺度特征金字塔增强对极小目标的感知；(2) MRCA的Mamba扫描可与遥感影像中的旋转目标检测（如Oriented R-CNN）结合，处理任意朝向目标；(3) MBBR的贝叶斯框精炼可引入遥感场景下的类别先验知识，提升类别不平衡场景的检测性能；(4) 可扩展至遥感图像中的实例分割或旋转框检测任务，适配更多遥感应用场景。

Abstract (英文): Object detection in UAV aerial imagery is challenged by dense small targets, large-scale variation, complex backgrounds, and strict onboard computation limits. To address these issues, this paper proposes SMMNet (Structured-diffusion Mamba Mixture Network), a lightweight plug-and-play detection framework evaluated with YOLO family detectors. SMMNet contains three modules. The Structured Diffusion Feature Extractor (SDFE) uses anisotropic diffusion to preserve boundary-sensitive features during downsampling. The Mamba-driven Receptive-field Context Aggregator (MRCA) performs multi-directional selective state-space scanning to capture long-range context with linear complexity. The Mask-guided Bayesian Box Refinement (MBBR) applies a MAP-inspired confidence-adaptive box update using MobileSAM mask evidence and ELBO-based false-positive filtering. Using YOLOv13-S as the main detector, SMMNet achieves 32.8% mAP@0.5:0.95 and 52.6% mAP@0.5 on VisDrone2019 at 87 FPS on an NVIDIA A800 GPU, improving the YOLOv13-S baseline by 3.6 and 4.5 points, respectively. The added modules reduce throughput compared with the detector-only baseline (168 FPS), but the resulting 87 FPS remains real-time and provides a favorable accuracy–latency trade-off. Three independent-seed runs further show a mean paired gain of 3.60 ± 0.10 mAP on VisDrone2019, 2.53 ± 0.12 mAP on DroneVehicle, and 2.77 ± 0.06 mAP on SeaDronesSee for the YOLOv13-S setting. Additional experiments on DroneVehicle and SeaDronesSee, together with cross-backbone evaluations on YOLOv5/v6/v7/v8/v10/v11/v13 across different UAV benchmarks, show aligned performance trends under matched settings. Edge deployment on an NVIDIA Jetson Orin NX reaches 30 FPS under TensorRT FP16 inference at 15 W TDP, indicating the suitability of SMMNet for resource-constrained UAV perception.

### [110] [Enhanced DINO for Cross-Domain Transmission Tower Detection Using Remote Sensing Images](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132198)
*Junjie Wang,Jiahe Tian,Lingli Zhao,Ningsheng Liao,Jie Yang,Lei Shi*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于增强DINO的跨域输电塔检测框架，通过查询级目标门控(QOG)、MPDIoU回归和质量感知评分模块(QSM)三个轻量化模块，有效解决了不同地理区域遥感图像中输电塔检测的域偏移问题。在10%目标域标注设置下，该方法在精度、召回率、F1-score和mAP@0.5上分别达到0.8947、0.8199、0.8556和0.8684，优于原始DINO和YOLOv8/9/11等主流检测器。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 不同地理区域的遥感图像中，输电塔的结构、规模和背景纹理差异显著，导致在一个区域训练的模型应用于另一区域时检测精度大幅下降。现有方法缺乏针对输电塔这类细长目标的跨域检测解决方案。

Method: 1) 查询级目标门控(QOG)模块：通过估计每个查询的目标性分数，自适应地重新加权解码器查询，抑制背景主导的查询；2) MPDIoU回归损失：替代标准IoU损失，提升细长输电塔目标的定位精度；3) 质量感知评分模块(QSM)：利用预测的定位质量logits校准分类置信度，减少由边界框对齐不佳导致的高置信度误检。三个模块均为轻量化设计，嵌入DINO框架。

Result: 在两个不同地理区域的遥感数据集上，10%目标域标注设置下，该方法精度0.8947、召回率0.8199、F1-score 0.8556、mAP@0.5 0.8684，全面超越原始DINO基线及YOLOv8/v9/v11等主流检测器。

Conclusion: 提出的增强DINO框架通过三个轻量化模块有效解决了跨域输电塔检测问题，为遥感图像中细长目标的鲁棒跨域检测提供了有效方案。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。作为遥感领域的输电塔检测论文，改进方向包括：1) 将QOG模块扩展到其他细长遥感目标（如桥梁、道路、船舶）的跨域检测；2) 结合多尺度特征融合策略进一步提升对不同分辨率遥感图像的适应性；3) 引入域对抗训练或风格迁移机制，增强模型对更多地理区域的泛化能力；4) 将框架扩展为半监督或自监督学习范式，进一步减少对目标域标注数据的依赖。

Abstract (英文): Transmission towers are fundamental components of electric power networks. However, their structure, scale and background textures vary substantially across remote sensing images acquired from different geographic regions. These discrepancies often reduce the detection accuracy of a model trained in one region when it is applied to another region. This paper proposes an enhanced DINO-based framework for cross-domain transmission tower detection that incorporates three lightweight optimisation modules. First, a Query-level Objectness Gating (QOG) module adaptively reweights decoder queries by estimating per-query objectness scores, thereby suppressing background-dominated queries. Second, MPDIoU regression is used to improve the localisation accuracy of elongated transmission tower targets. Third, a Quality-aware Scoring Module (QSM) calibrates classification confidence using predicted localisation-quality logits, thereby reducing high-confidence false detections caused by poor box alignment. Experiments are conducted on two remote sensing image datasets from different geographic regions. Under the 10% target-domain annotation setting, the proposed method achieves a precision of 0.8947, a recall of 0.8199, an F1-score of 0.8556 and an mAP@0.5 of 0.8684, outperforming the original DINO baseline and mainstream detectors including YOLOv8, YOLOv9 and YOLOv11. The results demonstrate that the proposed framework provides an effective solution for robust cross-domain detection of slender transmission tower targets in remote sensing images.

</details>


### [111] [TreeFlow: Conditional Flow Matching for 3D Tree Point Cloud Generation from Inventory Attributes](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132197)
*Anthony Marcozzi,Johnathan Tenny,Daithi Martin,Juan Castorena,Zachary Crennen,Lucas Wells,Samuel Hillman*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: TreeFlow是一种基于条件流匹配的生成模型，能够从物种、采集平台和树高三个条件属性生成逼真的三维树木点云。该模型使用在FOR-species20K基准数据集上训练的Transformer，学习从高斯分布到真实激光扫描数据分布的 velocity field。生成的树木在六项指标中有五项达到或接近真实树木的类内基线水平（Chamfer距离0.581 m vs 0.559 m），在25米以下表现最佳。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 树木精确的三维结构表示对于火灾建模、辐射传输模拟、合成数据生成和森林数字孪生至关重要，但当前方法通常用光滑几何基元近似树冠，忽略了真实树木中的聚集、间隙和不规则分枝结构，导致缺乏所需尺度上的详细3D结构。

Method: 采用条件流匹配（conditional flow matching）框架，以Transformer为骨干网络，在FOR-species20K基准数据集的真实激光扫描数据上训练，学习一个 velocity field，该场将高斯分布的样本传输到真实树木点云的数据分布。生成过程以树种、采集平台和树高为条件。

Result: 在六项评价指标中，生成树木在五项上达到或接近真实树木的类内基线水平；Chamfer距离为0.581 m（真实树木为0.559 m）；在25米以下高度表现最佳，随高度增加性能下降。

Conclusion: TreeFlow是首个完全基于真实激光扫描数据训练的、以标量清单属性为条件的单木点云生成模型，能够生成保留真实树木冠层复杂结构（聚集、间隙、不规则分枝）的高质量三维点云。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。该模型可直接用于遥感领域的以下方向：（1）合成训练数据生成：为基于LiDAR点云的树种分类、森林参数反演等深度学习任务提供大量带标签的逼真训练样本，解决真实数据标注稀缺问题；（2）辐射传输模拟：生成真实冠层结构的三维场景，替代传统光滑几何体近似，提升辐射传输模型（如DART、LESS）对植被反射率模拟的精度；（3）森林碳储量估算：通过生成单木点云计算精确的树木体积和生物量，辅助遥感反演模型的标定与验证；（4）多源遥感数据融合：可扩展模型条件（如加入光谱信息），实现LiDAR与高光谱/多光谱数据的联合生成与协同分析。

Abstract (英文): Accurate three-dimensional representations of tree structure are essential for fire modeling, radiative transfer simulation, synthetic data generation, and digital twins of forests, yet detailed 3D structure is rarely available at required scales. Current approaches approximate crowns with smooth geometric primitives, discarding the clumping, gaps, and irregular branching present in real trees. We present TreeFlow, a conditional flow matching model that generates realistic 3D tree point clouds from species, acquisition platform, and height. The model uses a transformer trained on real laser scanning data from the FOR-species20K benchmark to learn a velocity field transporting samples from a Gaussian distribution to the source data distribution. We evaluate generation quality by comparing conditioning and distributional fidelity metrics to scans of real trees. Generated trees match or approach the intra-class baseline on five of six metrics, with a Chamfer distance of 0.581 m versus 0.559 m for real trees of the same genus and height class. Performance is strongest below 25 m and degrades with increasing height. TreeFlow generates individual-tree point clouds conditioned on scalar inventory attributes using a model trained entirely on real laser scanning data.

*X Chen,Yi Zhang,Lizhen Hu,Hongyi Zhang,Liangsheng Li,Xupu Geng*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出基于AIS关联的星载SAR船舶细粒度九分类方法，通过全局最优匹配策略将AIS船舶类型标签迁移至SAR检测结果，构建含4472个船舶切片的分类数据集，实验证明该方法能实现可靠的SAR独立船舶分类。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: SAR船舶分类因缺乏可靠类别标签而发展滞后，而AIS系统可提供船舶类型信息，但如何将两者有效关联以生成高质量训练标签是亟待解决的问题。

Method: 1) 将原始AIS船舶类型重组织为九类细粒度SAR船舶类别；2) 采用全局最优匹配策略将AIS类别标签迁移至SAR检测结果；3) 仅保留高置信度SAR-AIS匹配对，裁剪对应SAR船舶切片构建分类数据集（4472个样本）；4) 使用ConvNeXt-Tiny等分类器进行训练与评估。

Result: 蒙特卡洛实验表明，所提关联策略在近距离船舶模糊、空间扰动、干扰AIS候选和AIS静态尺寸误差下均优于对比方法；在构建的分类数据集上，ConvNeXt-Tiny取得最佳分类性能。

Abstract (英文): Spaceborne Synthetic Aperture Radar (SAR) provides all-weather, day and night and wide-area imaging capability, and plays a critical role in maritime surveillance. While substantial progress has been achieved in SAR ship detection, SAR ship classification remains relatively underexplored, mainly due to the scarcity of reliable category labels. Automatic Identification System (AIS) provides vessel identity, type, and dynamic trajectory information, and thus offers vessel type information that is difficult to obtain directly from SAR imagery. This paper proposes a fine-grained nine-category SAR ship classification method based on AIS association, which reorganizes the original AIS vessel types into nine fine-grained categories of SAR ship, transfers AIS vessel type information to SAR detection through a global optimal matching strategy, and supports SAR-only vessel category recognition. By retaining only high-confidence SAR and AIS matched pairs and cropping the corresponding SAR ship chips, an SAR ship classification dataset containing 4472 ship chips across the nine categories is constructed. In Monte Carlo experiments based on real AIS records, the proposed association strategy achieves more reliable high-confidence label generation than the compared association methods under close ship ambiguity, spatial perturbation, distractor AIS candidates, and AIS static size errors. In the benchmark experiment on the constructed classification dataset, ConvNeXt-Tiny achieves the best performance among the compared mainstream classifiers. These results demonstrate that AIS association can provide reliable category supervision for SAR ship classification, and the trained classifier can perform ship classification using SAR imagery alone.

### [113] [Assessing Potential Spatial Conflicts Between Projected Quercus Habitat Suitability and Future Land-Use Patterns in China: A Multi-Scenario MaxEnt–PLUS Simulation](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132195)
*Jiali Duan,Dongdong Zhang,Zhongke Feng,Zhichao Wang*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本研究构建了MaxEnt与PLUS模型的软耦合框架，结合16种SSP气候与土地利用情景，评估了中国栎属未来适宜栖息地与人类土地利用格局的空间重叠，发现气候变暖驱动栖息地向北/向西扩张但南方收缩，而建设用地和耕地侵占将显著减少适宜栖息地的空间可用性，生态保护情景能有效缓解冲突。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 仅基于气候的物种分布评估可能因未考虑动态土地利用变化而高估未来适宜栖息地的空间可用性，亟需评估气候驱动的栖息地变化与人类土地利用格局之间的潜在空间重叠。

Method: 采用MaxEnt模型与PLUS模型的软耦合框架，结合16种SSP气候路径与土地利用情景组合，利用栖息地-土地利用冲突指数（HLCI）在栅格尺度上分类评估未来适宜栖息地与土地利用类别的空间重叠。

Result: (1) 气候变暖重塑栎属栖息地适宜性，呈现北/西扩张和部分低纬地区收缩；(2) 未来土地利用将减少适宜栖息地空间可用性，高排放情景下新建适宜栖息地与建设用地重叠达5.90×10⁴ km²，与耕地重叠达36.42×10⁴ km²；(3) 生态保护情景与非生态用地重叠更低，可实现更大范围的栖息地扩张。

Conclusion: 本研究提供了气候-土地利用耦合情景下未来栎属栖息地适宜性空间评估，为适应性森林保护和国土空间规划提供了大尺度支持。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。该研究已深度融合遥感相关技术（土地利用模拟、MaxEnt模型），可在以下方面进一步强化遥感交叉：(1) 引入多源遥感数据（如Landsat/Sentinel时间序列、植被指数NDVI、叶面积指数LAI）替代或辅助MaxEnt的气候变量，提高栖息地适宜性建模的时空分辨率与精度；(2) 利用遥感反演的植被覆盖度、森林高度、火烧迹地等产品，动态校准PLUS模型中的土地利用转换规则；(3) 结合夜光遥感（NPP-VIIRS）量化人类活动强度，改进HLCI冲突指数中人类干扰因子的空间表征；(4) 利用遥感物候数据（如物候期、生长季长度）作为物种分布模型的补充变量，更精细刻画气候变化对栎属物候适应性的影响。

Abstract (英文): Global warming is driving large-scale shifts in the climatically suitable habitats of many species. However, climate-only species distribution assessments may overestimate the spatial availability of future suitable habitats when dynamic land-use change is not considered. To assess potential spatial overlaps between climate-driven habitat suitability shifts and human land-use patterns, this study focuses on Quercus L. as a widely distributed keystone forest taxon in China. The genus-level assessment was designed to identify broad-scale habitat–land-use conflict patterns under multiple climate pathways and territorial spatial planning scenarios, rather than to predict species-specific distribution responses. We developed a soft-coupled framework integrating the Maximum Entropy (MaxEnt) model and the Patch-generating Land-Use Simulation (PLUS) model, and applied the Habitat–Land-Use Conflict Index (HLCI) as a categorical spatial overlay framework to classify potential overlaps between projected suitable habitats and future land-use categories across 16 exploratory scenario combinations integrating Shared Socioeconomic Pathway (SSP)-based climate projections and land-use/land-cover (LULC) scenarios for the 2040s at the grid scale. The results indicate that: (1) climate warming may reshape Quercus habitat suitability, characterized by northward/westward expansion and southward contraction in some low-latitude regions; (2) future land-use patterns may reduce the spatial availability of projected suitable habitats by increasing their overlap with built-up land and cultivated land. Under high-emission scenarios, potential newly suitable habitats overlapped with built-up land by up to 5.90 × 104 km2 and with cultivated land by up to 36.42 × 104 km2; and (3) the Ecological Protection scenario showed lower overlap with non-ecological land-use categories and a larger area of potentially realizable habitat expansion. This study provides a scenario-based spatial assessment of where future Quercus habitat suitability may overlap with human land-use patterns, offering broad-scale support for adaptive forest conservation and territorial spatial planning.

### [114] [3D Gaussian Splatting for Large-Scale Remote Sensing: A PRISMA-Informed Scoping Review of Scalability, Geometric Reliability, and Benchmarking Across UAV/Aerial and Satellite Imagery](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132224)
*Wenbao Fan,Bo Wang,Junqiang Ye,Ruoyu Zha,H T Chen*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 3DGS在大规模遥感应用中仍呈碎片化状态，缺乏系统的综述和统一的评估基准，阻碍了其在实际遥感任务中的可靠部署。

Method: 采用PRISMA-informed范围综述方法，从Web of Science、Scopus、IEEE Xplore等数据库筛选55篇核心文献，构建分面分类法，从平台、传感器模型、可扩展性策略和几何监督四个维度组织文献，并提出一个联合记录视觉保真度、计算成本、可度量几何、产品实用性、失效行为和可复现性元数据的平台感知基准框架。

Result: 分区、层次化、压缩和前馈推理等方法虽提升了可扩展性，但无法保证可度量几何；可靠部署还需传感器一致性投影、几何/地理参考约束、显式监督标签和产品级评估；在无控制点场景下，需区分内部一致性与独立验证的精度。

Conclusion: 提出了一个面向无人机/航空、卫星及混合场景的平台感知基准框架，为后续3DGS遥感研究提供了系统化的评估标准和发展方向。

Abstract (英文): 3D Gaussian Splatting (3DGS) offers efficient explicit rendering, but large-scale remote-sensing use remains fragmented across UAV/aerial photogrammetry, satellite reconstruction, large-scene scaling, surface modeling, and geospatial evaluation. We present a Preferred Reporting Items for Systematic Reviews and Meta-Analyses (PRISMA)-informed scoping review based on 55 core studies identified through Web of Science, Scopus, IEEE Xplore, and supplementary searches completed on 3 June 2026. A faceted taxonomy organizes the literature by platform, sensor model, scalability strategy, and geometric supervision. The synthesis shows that partitioning, hierarchy, compression, and feed-forward inference improve scalability but do not guarantee metric geometry. Reliable deployment additionally requires sensor-consistent projection, geometric or georeferencing constraints, explicit supervision labels, and product-level evaluation. In control-point-free settings, internal consistency should be distinguished from independently validated accuracy. We therefore propose a platform-aware benchmark framework that jointly records visual fidelity, computational cost, metric geometry, product utility, failure behavior, and reproducibility metadata for UAV/aerial, satellite, and hybrid settings.

### [115] [SC-Net: Structural Constrained Contrastive Learning for Landslide Extraction Toward Power Transmission Corridor Safety Monitoring](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132216)
*Wei Song,S. Liu,S S Wu,Cheng Liao,Zongyuan Wu,Shiming Li,X B Zheng,Yanping Duan*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种结构约束对比学习网络(SC-Net)，用于从遥感影像中提取滑坡信息。该方法通过多结构特征提取模块捕捉滑坡几何特征，利用注意力自适应融合模块融合多尺度语义特征，并引入掩码约束的对比学习策略增强滑坡与非滑坡区域的区分能力。在CAS数据集上，SC-Net在CAS-UAV和CAS-SAT上分别达到89.89%和79.76%的IoU，超越了现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 滑坡是常见且具有破坏性的地质灾害，威胁基础设施稳定。长距离输电走廊常穿越山区和林区，滑坡会危及塔基和线路安全。然而，这些滑坡多发生在植被茂密的坡地，密集植被造成严重遮挡，模糊了滑坡边界，并与周围地物高度相似，导致遥感影像中准确高效的滑坡识别仍是一项重大挑战。

Method: 提出SC-Net，包含三个核心模块：(1) 多结构特征提取模块，用于捕获滑坡特有的几何特征；(2) 基于注意力机制的自适应特征融合模块，融合从预训练骨干网络提取的多尺度语义特征；(3) 掩码约束的物体级对比学习策略，在滑坡物体级别强制执行全局结构一致性，增强滑坡与非滑坡区域的可区分性。

Result: 在公开CAS滑坡数据集上，SC-Net在CAS-UAV和CAS-SAT数据集上分别达到89.89%和79.76%的IoU，比最佳基线分别高出2.09%和0.46%。

Conclusion: 所提方法为大规模滑坡监测提供了有效解决方案，并在输电走廊巡检和基础设施安全评估中展现出应用潜力。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：100%。本文本身就是遥感滑坡提取论文。改进方向：(1) 可引入多模态遥感数据（如InSAR形变信息、LiDAR高程数据）作为辅助输入，提升遮挡区域的识别能力；(2) 对比学习策略可扩展为时空对比学习，利用时序遥感影像捕捉滑坡前后的变化特征；(3) 结构特征提取模块可引入图神经网络建模滑坡与周边地物的拓扑关系；(4) 可考虑在损失函数中加入边界感知损失，进一步优化滑坡边界的精细度。

Abstract (英文): Landslides are among the most common and destructive geological hazards and pose a significant threat to the long-term stability of infrastructure systems. In particular, long-distance power transmission corridors often traverse mountainous and forested regions, where landslides can endanger tower foundations and transmission line safety. Such landslides predominantly occur in sloped forested areas, where dense vegetation causes severe occlusion that blurs landslide boundaries and creates strong visual similarity with surrounding land covers. Consequently, accurate and efficient landslide identification from remote sensing imagery remains a significant challenge. To address these challenges, we propose a structural constrained contrastive learning network (SC-Net) for reliable landslide extraction from remote sensing images. First, a multi-structural feature extraction module is designed to capture landslide-specific geometric characteristics. These features are further enhanced by fusing multi-scale semantic representations extracted from a pretrained backbone network through an attention-based adaptive feature fusion module. Additionally, a mask-constrained object-level contrastive learning strategy is introduced to enforce global structural consistency at the landslide object-level, thereby improving the discriminability between landslide and non-landslide regions. Extensive experiments conducted on the publicly available CAS landslide dataset demonstrate the effectiveness of the proposed method. The proposed SC-Net achieves IoU scores of 89.89% and 79.76% on the CAS-UAV and CAS-SAT datasets, respectively, outperforming the best-performing baseline by 2.09% and 0.46%. The proposed method provides an effective solution for large-scale landslide monitoring and demonstrates potential for applications in power transmission corridor inspection and infrastructure safety assessment.

</details>


### [116] [Multi-Level Classification of Urban Green Space Using Multi-Source Remote Sensing and Geospatial Data](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132192)

Method: 1) 通过BERT模型微调与交叉映射规则注入先验知识，基于POI、OSM和全球城市边界（GUB）将城区分为24个功能类别，生成社会功能底图；2) 设计多形状与光谱感知网络（MSSANet）进行物理层的精细植被分类；3) 建立“功能优先、植被其次”耦合范式，参照中国城市绿地分类标准（CJJ/T 85-2017），形成3个功能属性层，构建5大类、11中类、24小类的多层次UGS分类框架。

Abstract (英文): Urban Green Spaces (UGSs) monitoring usually focuses on the extraction of vegetation in the physical layer, while neglecting their functional attributes. This renders the monitoring results unable to objectively reflect the rationality of UGS planning. To address these issues, this study proposes a multi-level classification method integrating multi-source remote sensing and geospatial big data to bridge the semantic gap between the physical layer and the functional layer. In this method, a strategy of prior knowledge injection and semantic reconstruction was developed through the fine-tuning of a BERT model with cross-mapping rules. This strategy aims to classify the urban area into 24 functional categories, generating the social-functional basemap in a functional layer, based on Point of Interest (POI), OpenStreetMap (OSM), and Global Urban Boundary (GUB). Meanwhile, a novel deep learning architecture, namely the Multi-Shape and Spectral Aware Network (MSSANet), was designed for precise vegetation classification of UGSs in the physical layer. Finally, a “function-first, vegetation-second” coupling paradigm containing three functional attribute layers, referring to the Code for Classification of UGS in China (CJJ/T 85-2017), was established. This paradigm integrates the social-functional basemap with physical vegetation patches to build a multi-level UGS classification framework, i.e., the 5 major UGS categories, 11 intermediate UGS categories, and 24 fine-grained UGS sub-categories. Experiments conducted in Jinan and Qingdao, China, demonstrate the efficacy of the proposed method for refined multi-level UGS mapping.

### [117] [Impacts of Extreme Climate on NDVI in China—Response Patterns and Threshold Effects](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132180)
*Mengwei Li,Rong Li,Rui Zhu,Jianan Shan,Zh. Zhao,Fulong Chen,Zhenliang Yin*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 基于2001-2024年中国NDVI和ERA5-Land极端气候数据，采用Pearson相关、小波分析和XGBoost-SHAP模型，发现NDVI以0.021/10年速率增长，R25（31.6%）和SDII（12.5%）是主要驱动因子，且存在显著阈值效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 极端气候事件频发对植被动态的影响日益显著，理解二者响应关系对维持生态系统稳定性至关重要，但目前缺乏对中国区域NDVI对多维度极端气候指标综合响应的定量分析。

Method: 基于ERA5-Land温度和降水数据及MODIS NDVI数据，采用Pearson相关分析（相关性检验）、小波分析（多尺度时频特征）和XGBoost-SHAP模型（特征重要性归因与阈值识别）进行综合建模。

Result: (1) NDVI以0.021/10年稳定增长，极端气候指数在大部分区域呈上升趋势；(2) NDVI与多数极端温湿指标正相关，仅与霜冻日数(FDO)和连续干日(CDD)显著负相关；(3) R25（贡献率31.6%）和SDII（12.5%）为主要驱动因子，阈值分别为1.85天和4.35 mm/day。

Abstract (英文): Studying the impact of extreme climate events on vegetation dynamics is crucial for maintaining ecosystem stability. The findings reveal the following. (1) NDVI increased steadily at a rate of 0.021/10 yr from 2001 to 2024. Extreme temperature and precipitation indices show an increasing trend in most regions. (2) NDVI was positively correlated with most extreme temperature and precipitation indices, and showed a significant negative correlation exclusively with Frost Days FDO (Frost Days) and CDD (Consecutive Dry Days). (3) R25 (Number of Heavy Precipitation Days) and SDII (Simple daily intensity index) are the primary drivers of nationwide NDVI changes, with contribution rates of 31.6% and 12.5%. Extreme climate indices can significantly affect vegetation growth when surpassing certain thresholds. For instance, the thresholds for R25 and SDII are 1.85 days and 4.35 mm/day. This study provides a scientific basis for understanding and managing vegetation responses to increasing climate extremes.

### [118] [RepLite-YOLO: A Parameter-Efficient Residual-Enhanced Detector for Ship Recognition in Remote Sensing Imagery](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132238)
*Ruijia Fu,Zuomin Wang,Zijun Lin,Ying Li,Bingxin Liu*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出RepLite-YOLO，一种基于YOLOv11n的轻量级遥感船舶检测框架，通过ADown模块、C3k2_OREPA_RS模块、ELANFusion_Block和Detect_DWLite检测头等创新设计，在Vessel和Ship Detection数据集上分别将参数量降低57.4%、GFLOPs降低49.2%，同时mAP@50提升1.2和1.3个百分点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前遥感船舶检测方法在复杂海面背景噪声、目标尺度差异大和边缘硬件受限等场景下性能不佳，现有方法存在下采样过程中空间信息不可逆丢失、模型结构冗余以及多尺度特征聚合瓶颈等问题。

Method: 1) 采用ADown模块（来自YOLOv9的双分支下采样机制）生成空间互补特征，保留船体边缘响应同时抑制海面干扰；2) 设计C3k2_OREPA_RS模块，利用在线重参数化（OREPA）在不引入额外推理开销的情况下高效重构深层；3) 构建ELANFusion_Block，将深度可分离卷积（DSC）融入ELAN范式缓解多尺度聚合瓶颈；4) 设计Detect_DWLite头实现高度压缩的解耦预测。

Result: 与YOLOv11n相比，参数量减少57.4%，GFLOPs减少49.2%；在Vessel数据集上mAP@50提升1.2个百分点，在Ship Detection数据集上mAP@50提升1.3个百分点。

Conclusion: RepLite-YOLO在检测精度和计算效率之间取得了良好的平衡，证明了轻量化设计在遥感船舶检测中的有效性。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。改进方案：1) 可进一步引入注意力机制（如CA或SE）增强ADown模块对海面复杂背景的判别能力；2) C3k2_OREPA_RS模块可适配到其他遥感检测任务（如飞机、车辆检测）中以验证其通用性；3) ELANFusion_Block可结合多尺度特征金字塔（如BiFPN）进一步提升多尺度目标的检测性能；4) 可尝试将RepLite-YOLO部署到无人机或卫星边缘计算平台进行实际场景验证。

Abstract (英文): Remote sensing ship detection plays a pivotal role in maritime surveillance, safety assurance, and traffic management. However, current detection methods often face significant challenges due to complex sea-surface background noise, large target-scale variations, and edge-hardware limitations. In this paper, we propose RepLite-YOLO, a lightweight detection framework based on YOLOv11n. Specifically, to alleviate irreversible spatial information loss during downsampling, we adopt the ADown module, originally introduced in YOLOv9, to generate spatially complementary features through its two-branch downsampling mechanism. This design helps preserve salient hull-edge responses while suppressing part of the random sea-surface interference, thereby improving feature robustness for small ship targets. To achieve substantial structural streamlining while maintaining competitive representational capacity under strict hardware constraints, we design the C3k2_OREPA_RS module, utilizing online re-parameterization (OREPA) to efficiently reconstruct deep layers without additional re-parameterization-induced inference operations. Furthermore, we construct the ELANFusion_Block by integrating Depthwise Separable Convolutions (DSC) into the ELAN paradigm to alleviate the multi-scale aggregation bottleneck, and tailor the Detect_DWLite head for highly compressed decoupled prediction. Experimental results show that RepLite-YOLO achieves a favorable balance between detection accuracy and computational efficiency. Compared with YOLOv11n, it reduces the number of parameters by 57.4% and GFLOPs by 49.2%, while maintaining competitive detection accuracy with slight mAP@50 improvements of 1.2 and 1.3 percentage points on the Vessel dataset and Ship Detection dataset, respectively.

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种分层注意力促进的跨尺度学习框架，用于解决复杂场景下多尺度无人机检测中的漏检、虚警和精度低问题。通过分层注意力机制生成多尺度特征、双分支准残差结构保护目标内容、动态聚焦损失优化边界框回归，在恶劣光照和天气条件下显著提升了小目标无人机的检测精度，mAP较YOLOv6提升18.5%。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1) 在骨干网络中引入分层注意力机制，生成多尺度目标特征；2) 颈部构建双分支特征：目标特定特征算子分支与上采样分支，通过准残差结构连接以保护目标内容并重建细节；3) 提出动态聚焦损失度量用于边界框回归，提升学习效率。

Result: 在自建数据集上，所提方法相较于YOLOv6的mAP提升18.5%，能够在恶劣光照和天气条件下准确检测小型弱小无人机。

Abstract (英文): The accurate detection of unmanned aerial vehicles (UAVs) in various sizes played an important role in the practical applications. Yet the preceding works suffered from the missing inference, the false alarms, and the poor accuracy due to the the adverse scene conditions, as well as the mutable scales. To solve the problems, a hierarchical attention promoted cross-scale learning framework was proposed in this paper. First, the hierarchical attention mechanism was introduced in the backbone to generate the multi-scale features of targets, so they can be discerned and located at different scales. The resulting features were further delivered to the neck, in which two branches of features were built, respectively. The former was obtained by the target-specific feature operator, while the latter was generated by the upsampling operation. The dual branches were further connected in the quasi-residual structure. So the content of targets can be protected well, and the detail information can be reconstructed. Finally, the dynamic focusing loss measurement was presented to regress the bounding box of the target, so the learning effectiveness of presented the architecture can be promoted. To verify the proposed method, multiple rounds of experiments were performed. The results demonstrated that small and weak drones can be detected accurately, especially in adverse lighting and weather conditions. The evaluation metric of mean average precision rate (mAP) can be improved by 18.5% (YOLO6) on the collected dataset.

### [120] [Remote Sensing-Based Identification of Spatial Spillovers and Transmission Pathways in the Heat–Energy–Carbon Nexus: Evidence from the Yangtze River Delta](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132222)
*Gaoneng Lai,Lei Jiang,Yingbiao Chen,Shitai Bao,Jinxin Duan,Zuojie Zhu*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本研究基于2014-2023年长三角城市群多源地理空间数据，构建了融合1km城市群探索性分析与5km空间计量建模的多尺度分析框架，通过构建人为能源活动强度（AEAI）作为代理变量，采用空间杜宾模型结合空间中介方法，揭示了“热-能-碳”关联中的空间效应与统计中介路径。结果表明：碳排放存在显著正向空间溢出效应，AEAI解释了UHI与碳排放之间44.63%的总关联，表明该关联部分嵌入于能源密集型人类活动的空间格局，而非纯粹的直接热效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 热岛效应与碳排放的关联虽已受到关注，但其中行为中介路径和跨区域溢出模式尚不清晰，现有研究缺乏多尺度和空间计量视角的系统分析。

Method: 采用多源地理空间数据，构建多尺度分析框架（1km城市群探索性分析和5km空间计量建模）；构建AEAI作为能源相关人类活动代理变量；运用空间杜宾模型（SDM）和空间中介效应方法分析“热-能-碳”关联。

Result: (1) 碳排放存在显著正向空间溢出效应，与热扩散和社会经济网络交互一致；(2) AEAI是UHI与碳排放之间重要的部分统计中介路径，解释了44.63%的总关联。

Conclusion: 区域气候治理需超越单一城市干预和纯物理降温策略，转向跨区域协调与行为调控相结合的综合路径；倡导被动式降温导向的城市规划和需求侧能源转型，以降低碳锁定风险并建设气候韧性城市群。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：90%。该研究已使用多源地理空间数据（如遥感地表温度数据、夜间灯光数据等），与遥感技术高度交叉。改进方案：(1) 可引入更高时空分辨率的遥感数据（如Landsat 30m或ECOSTRESS 70m地表温度数据）替代1km分辨率数据，提升UHI空间细节刻画能力；(2) 可结合遥感反演的植被指数（NDVI/EVI）、不透水面比例（ISA）等参数作为空间中介变量，进一步解析UHI-碳排放间的生态调控路径；(3) 可引入遥感估算的碳排放数据（如OCO-2/3、GOSAT等卫星观测的XCO₂数据）进行外部验证，增强结论的可靠性。

Abstract (英文): The urban heat island (UHI) effect represents a critical urban climate phenomenon arising from the combined pressures of rapid urbanization and climate warming. Although its association with carbon emissions has received increasing scholarly attention, the underlying behavior-mediated pathways and cross-regional spillover patterns remain insufficiently understood. Using multi-source geospatial data for the Yangtze River Delta urban agglomeration from 2014 to 2023, this study develops a multi-scale analytical framework integrating 1 km urban agglomeration exploratory analysis and 5 km spatial econometric modeling. Anthropogenic Energy Activity Intensity (AEAI) is constructed as a proxy for energy-related human activities, and a spatial Durbin model, combined with a spatial mediation approach, is employed to examine the spatial associations and statistically mediated pathways within the “heat-energy-carbon” nexus. The results indicate that: (1) carbon emissions exhibit significant positive spatial spillover effects, consistent with thermal diffusion processes and socioeconomic network interactions; (2) AEAI represents a substantial partial statistical mediation pathway in the association between UHI and carbon emissions, accounting for 44.63% of the total association. This suggests that the UHI–carbon emission linkage is partly embedded in spatial patterns of energy-intensive human activities rather than reflecting a purely direct thermal effect. These findings suggest that regional climate governance may need to move beyond single-city interventions and purely physical cooling strategies toward integrated approaches that combine cross-regional coordination with behavioral regulation. Promoting passive cooling-oriented urban planning and demand-side energy transitions may help reduce carbon lock-in risks and support the development of climate-resilient urban agglomerations.

### [121] [Integrating Commercial and Public Imagery to Accelerate Deforestation Alerts](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132221)
*Zhiqiang Yang,Eric L. Bullock,Erik Lindquist,Carole Andrianirina,Sean P. Healey*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为DIAS的开源框架，通过将不同传感器的图像转换为可互操作的干扰指数（DI）Z-score流，实现多传感器协同的卫星森林砍伐预警。该方法在马达加斯加验证，结合商业（PlanetScope）和公开（Landsat、Sentinel-1/2）影像，能以20%误报率在一个月内检测到2/3的10米分辨率森林砍伐事件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有卫星砍伐预警系统依赖单一传感器或历史存档，难以实现低延迟预警。不同传感器（商业与公开、光学与雷达）的协同使用面临数据源异构、校准不稳定等问题，亟需一种轻量、灵活、可互操作的多传感器融合框架。

Method: DIAS框架的核心创新在于：不再像传统方法那样将像素与历史状态对比，而是计算每个像素在森林敏感轴上的Z-score（相对于整幅图像中森林像素总体分布的位置）。这种方法：(1)减少对历史存档的依赖；(2)降低对稳定传感器校准的要求；(3)支持不同传感器的Z-score DI值直接融合；(4)可灵活适应传感器组的变化。

Result: 在马达加斯加实验中，DIAS结合PlanetScope（商业每日影像）与Landsat、Sentinel-1/2（公开数据），以约20%的误报率，在一个月内检测到2/3的10米参考像素级别森林砍伐事件。仅使用公开数据时，一个月内检测率为40%。

Conclusion: DIAS提供了一种计算轻量、灵活开源的多传感器融合预警方案，能够有效整合不同校准精度的传感器数据，以支持更及时的热带森林监测。随着商业遥感选项的激增，类似DIAS的框架对于多样化传感器协同具有重要价值。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。该论文本身即为遥感论文，改进方向包括：(1)将Z-score的参考分布从全局森林像素扩展到局部邻域自适应窗口，以应对异质性景观；(2)引入时序上下文信息（如滑动窗口Z-score）替代单期图像的静态Z-score，提高对缓慢退化事件的敏感性；(3)结合深度学习语义分割模型对森林像素的选取进行优化，减少非森林杂波干扰；(4)扩展DI值计算中的森林敏感轴维度，从一维线性投影升级为多光谱/多时相的高维流形空间；(5)将DIAS与现有的近实时监测系统（如GLAD、RADD）集成，提供混合预警输出。

Abstract (英文): Generating satellite-based deforestation alerts with actionable latency requires frequent imaging, creating an imperative to use different sensors together. We introduce a simple and open-source framework called the Disturbance Index Alert System (DIAS), which is based upon transformation of imagery from different sources into an interoperable stream of Disturbance Index (DI) values. Whereas most alert systems target divergence of forested pixels from historical states, DIAS targets movement of a pixel’s Z-score position relative to the image-wide population of forest pixels along a forest-sensitive axis. This strategy provides the following practical benefits: (1) it reduces the need to process the historical archive; (2) it reduces dependence upon stable sensor calibration; (3) it allows Z-score-based DI values to be combined across sensors; and (4) it accommodates changes to the group of sensors providing measurements. We demonstrated in Madagascar that sensor integration through DIAS can provide more timely alerts than both conventional individual-sensor systems and additive combination of such systems. Across our study sites, using a commercial source of daily imaging (PlanetScope) in conjunction with imagery from public sources (Landsat, Sentinels-1 and -2) allowed high-confidence detection (false alert rate of approximately 20%) of two-thirds of deforestation occurring at 10 m reference pixels within one month; 40% were detected in that timeframe with public data alone. As commercial options for Earth observation proliferate, flexible and computationally lightweight approaches such as DIAS are needed to accommodate diverse and sometimes only loosely calibrated instruments in support of timely forest monitoring.

### [122] [Detection of Bark Beetle Attacks Using Time-Aggregated Satellite Data with Machine Learning](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132234)
*S. Zeinali,Per‐Ola Olsson,Ted Kronvall,Magnus Wiktorsson,Johan Lindström*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本研究利用XGBoost分类器，结合每周累积的Sentinel-2卫星数据和静态地理/林业数据，检测早期树皮甲虫攻击。结果表明，红边3和蓝色波段是最重要的卫星特征，土地覆盖和地形是最重要的静态特征，模型在第19、25、31和33周检测效果最佳。结合静态和卫星数据可显著提升早期预警能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 树皮甲虫攻击对森林生态系统造成严重威胁，早期检测对于及时干预和控制虫害扩散至关重要。当前方法在早期阶段检测准确性不足，需要结合多源数据提升预警能力。

Method: 使用XGBoost分类器，对比三种数据组合（仅静态数据、仅卫星数据、两者结合）；基于每周累积的Sentinel-2数据进行训练；追踪模型性能随时间变化；系统性分析特征重要性。

Conclusion: 结合静态特征与每周累积的Sentinel-2数据对提升树皮甲虫攻击检测效果至关重要，该思路是构建早期预警系统的关键组成部分。

Abstract (英文): In this study, we explored how early bark beetle attacks can be detected using weekly aggregated Sentinel-2 data in combination with static data, such as geo- and forestry data. We used an XGBoost classifier, known for its strength and reliability in classification, and compared three sets of data: static data only, satellite data only, and using both together. Having trained the models on cumulative weekly data, we were able to track changes in model performance and feature importance over time, identifying key weeks for the detection of bark beetle attacks. A systematic overview of feature importance identified the Red-edge 3 and blue Sentinel-2 bands as the most important when combined with static data; it also showed changes in feature importance compared to using satellite-only data, e.g., adding static features reduced the importance of red and red-edge 2 bands. Among the static features, land cover and landforms were the most important. Evaluating the temporal features for the combined model highlighted certain weeks as containing key information for detection: week 19, which was the main swarming week; week 25, which is 6 weeks after swarming and just before the second generation is completed; and weeks 31 and 33, more than 3 months after the tree was attacked and well after the new generation has swarmed. The study shows that combining static features with cumulative Sentinel-2, accumulated across weeks, are all important for improving the detection of bark beetle attacks, and that such ideas form an important part of early warning systems.

### [123] [Semantic Consistency and Uncertainty-Driven Small-Object Detection for Class Imbalance](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132208)
*Nuo Chen,Peng Zhao,Shouquan Hou*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出SCUD训练框架，通过标签噪声抑制（LNSS）、尺度感知重采样（SARS）和自适应实例选择（AISM）三种策略，解决航拍图像小目标检测中的样本不平衡问题，在DOTA-v1.0和DIOR数据集上分别达到70.7%和88.1%的mAP50，显著提升了稀有类别的检测精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 航拍图像小目标检测中，复杂成像视角、任意目标朝向和长尾类别分布共同导致严重的样本不平衡，降低了检测稳定性并导致 minority 类别频繁误分类。现有方法未能有效联合解决这些因素带来的噪声和过拟合问题。

Method: 提出SCUD框架，包含三个核心模块：(1) LNSS：基于语义一致性的对比学习机制，约束相似样本在特征空间中的聚合，减少噪声样本对模型优化的负面影响；(2) SARS：尺度感知重采样策略，缓解小目标训练过程中因过度重复导致的噪声放大和过拟合；(3) AISM：自适应实例选择机制，联合建模预测不确定性和全局统计先验，动态强调对信息量丰富样本的学习。

Result: 在DOTA-v1.0数据集上达到70.7% mAP50，在DIOR数据集上达到88.1% mAP50，多个稀有类别的检测精度得到显著提升。

Conclusion: 提出的SCUD框架有效解决了航拍图像小目标检测中的样本不平衡问题，尤其对稀有类别的检测改善明显，验证了噪声抑制、尺度感知重采样和自适应实例选择联合策略的有效性。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。该论文本身就是遥感航拍图像小目标检测领域的工作。改进方向：(1) LNSS中的对比学习可引入多视图增强（如多尺度裁剪、旋转增强）进一步提升特征鲁棒性；(2) SARS可扩展到类别感知的混合精度重采样，结合Focal Loss等损失函数进一步平衡难易样本；(3) AISM可融合在线难例挖掘（OHEM）或梯度引导机制，提升动态选择的精确度；(4) 可引入Transformer或DETR类端到端检测头替代当前检测器，减少NMS后处理带来的小目标漏检。

Abstract (英文): In aerial image small-object detection, complex imaging perspectives, arbitrary object orientations, and long-tailed category distributions jointly exacerbate sample imbalance, which significantly degrades detection stability and leads to frequent misclassification of minority categories. To address these challenges, this paper proposes a novel training framework termed SCUD. Specifically, in the label noise suppression strategy (LNSS), a contrastive learning mechanism based on semantic consistency is introduced to constrain the aggregation of similar samples in the feature space, thereby reducing the adverse impact of noisy samples on model optimization. In addition, a scale-aware resampling strategy (SARS) is designed to alleviate noise amplification and overfitting caused by excessive repetition of small objects during training. Furthermore, an adaptive instance selection mechanism (AISM) is developed by jointly modeling prediction uncertainty and global statistical priors, enabling the model to dynamically emphasize learning from informative samples. Extensive experiments are conducted on two publicly available unmanned aerial vehicle (UAV) aerial image datasets to validate the effectiveness of the proposed approach. The proposed method achieves an mAP50 of 70.7% on the DOTA-v1.0 dataset and 88.1% on the DIOR dataset. Notably, the detection accuracy of several rare categories is significantly improved, further demonstrating the effectiveness of the proposed method in addressing sample imbalance in aerial image small-object detection.

### [124] [Sequence-Aware Deep Learning for Field-Scale Surface Soil Moisture Estimation from Sentinel-1, HLS, and Ancillary Data](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132213)
*Elahe Jahan Nejadi,Ramata Magagi,Kalifa Goı̈ta*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本研究提出融合Sentinel-1 SAR、HLS光学遥感、气象、土壤、地形等65维特征的序列感知深度学习模型（FTA-TCN），实现田间尺度（field-scale）地表土壤水分（SSM）高精度估计，在留出验证年（2016湿年+2023干旱年）上达到R²=0.851、RMSE=0.024 m³/m³，优于传统LSTM和TCN基线模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统卫星SSM产品空间分辨率过粗，无法满足田间尺度的农业水分管理需求，亟需融合多源遥感与辅助数据、利用时序深度学习模型提升SSM估计的精度与时空泛化能力。

Method: 使用2016-2024年生长季（5-9月）Sentinel-1过境时刻的多源数据集（1469样本，65特征/样本），包括SAR特征、HLS光学特征、气象数据、土壤质地/容重、地形、作物标签、灌溉概率标志及不规则时间步编码。构建LSTM、TCN及其注意力增强变体（FA、TA、FTA），以FTA-TCN（特征-时间双注意力时序卷积网络）为最优模型，并用SHAP进行特征重要性解释。

Result: FTA-TCN在留出验证年上R²=0.851、RMSE=0.024 m³/m³、MAE=0.020 m³/m³，显著优于基线LSTM（R²=0.422）和基线TCN（R²=0.746）。SHAP分析显示前期降水和短期降雨累积为主导因子，卫星特征占聚合SHAP重要性的约28.5%。

Conclusion: 双注意力时序卷积网络（FTA-TCN）能够在卫星信号与局地土壤-气象-管理背景耦合的条件下，有效捕捉湿年和干旱年间田间尺度的SSM动态变化，为精准农业水分管理提供了高精度的技术方案。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：90%。改进方案：（1）可引入更高分辨率雷达数据（如TerraSAR-X、COSMO-SkyMed）或极化分解特征增强SAR信息；（2）考虑加入植被含水量动态（如从微波植被光学深度VOD）以消除植被散射对SSM反演的影响；（3）将FTA-TCN扩展为时空图网络（ST-GCN）以利用相邻田块的空间相关性；（4）引入物理约束（如土壤水平衡方程）作为损失函数正则项，提升物理可解释性与极端条件下的鲁棒性；（5）探索迁移学习策略，将模型泛化到未观测区域或不同物候期。

Abstract (英文): Accurate field-scale surface soil moisture (SSM) measures are important for agricultural water management. Conventional satellite SSM products remain too coarse for within-field applications. Here, we developed sequence-aware deep learning models for growing-season SSM estimation by fusing data from Sentinel-1 C-band SAR, harmonized Landsat-8/Sentinel-2 (HLS), and local ancillary datasets. We assembled a multi-source dataset on Sentinel-1 overpass time for 2016–2024 (May–September), yielding 1469 samples and 65 features per sample, including SAR and optical features, meteorological data, soil texture and bulk density, topography, crop labels, irrigation-likelihood flag, and irregular-time-step encoding. We compared long short-term memory (LSTM) and temporal convolutional neural network (TCN) architectures together with attention-augmented variants, including feature attention (FA), temporal attention (TA), and the combined feature–temporal attention (FTA). Models were trained and tested on seven years of data and were validated based on a temporal generalization using combined data of a wet year (2016) and a dry year (2023). The best model, FTA-TCN, achieved R2 = 0.851, RMSE = 0.024 m3.m−3, and MAE = 0.020 m3.m−3 on the withheld validation years, outperforming the base LSTM (R2 = 0.422; RMSE = 0.053 m3.m−3; MAE = 0.043 m3.m−3) and the base TCN (R2 = 0.746; RMSE = 0.034 m3.m−3; MAE = 0.022 m3.m−3). Shapley additive explanations (SHAP) analysis indicated that antecedent precipitation and short-term rainfall accumulations were dominant forcings, while soil texture, elevation, incidence angle, and vegetation indices modulated SSM variability. Satellite-derived features accounted for ~28.5% of aggregated SHAP importance. Overall, the results show that dual-attention temporal convolution can capture field-scale SSM dynamics across wet and dry seasons when satellite signals are coupled with local soil-meteorological-management context.

*Yue Wang,Ningxin Yong,Siyu Zhu,Yang Hong*

Abstract (英文): With global warming and rapid urbanization, short-duration summer rainstorms are becoming more intense and localized, posing growing challenges to urban flood resilience. However, their spatiotemporal characteristics, vertical structures, and environmental drivers remain poorly understood. Here, we combine multi-source remote sensing datasets and China’s new-generation satellite-borne dual-frequency precipitation radar observations to investigate summer rainstorms in Nanjing, China, during 2017–2024. Results reveal pronounced spatiotemporal heterogeneity, with higher rainfall intensities concentrated over urban and adjacent areas. During the study period, rainstorm intensity and duration increased by 7.44% and 38.63%, respectively, while the affected area decreased by 8.18%, indicating a transition toward more localized yet more intense rainfall events. Environmental analyses suggest that large-scale thermodynamic conditions and regional topographic forcing provide a favorable background for convection development, while local urban thermal effects may further modulate rainfall enhancement. Three-dimensional radar detection of an illustrative rainstorm event indicates an inverted-cone vertical structure, suggesting a mixed convective-stratiform precipitation structure involving both warm-rain and ice-phase processes. An Explainable Bayesian-Optimized XGBoost (EBOX) model further identifies near-surface air temperature and specific humidity as the primary environmental factors associated with rainstorm occurrence and development. Overall, this study highlights the value of integrating satellite remote sensing with explainable artificial intelligence to improve understanding of urban extreme rainfall and provide new insights into how climate change, topography, and urbanization jointly shape precipitation extremes in rapidly urbanizing monsoon regions.

### [126] [Multi-Modal Data Fusion for Dynamic Target Depth Retrieval in Aquatic Environments](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132230)
*Xiangyong Liu,Zhiqiang Xu,Tianhong Ding*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于多源数据融合的动态目标深度估计方法，联合光学RGB图像与神经形态视觉(NeuroIV)数据，构建三通道特征提取融合网络。通过超图结构建立动态与静态节点的关联权重，以逐元素乘法替代点积注意力降低计算复杂度，并引入轻量化可变形注意力金字塔与扩散模型优化深度图像边缘，在MAE指标上提升超过20%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1) 以RGB图像与神经形态视觉数据为联合输入，构建三通道特征提取融合网络；2) 利用超图结构建立动态(时间)与静态(空间)节点间的关联权重，捕获时空相关性；3) 以逐元素乘法替代传统点积注意力，降低高维多模态数据的计算复杂度；4) 引入轻量化可变形注意力金字塔和扩散模型，细化深度图像边缘，抑制估计结果的断续与突变。

Abstract (英文): To address the challenges of severe optical attenuation and dynamic feature extraction for moving target depth retrieval in complex underwater remote sensing environments, this paper proposes a dynamic target depth estimation method based on multi-source data fusion. Taking optical RGB imagery and neuromorphic vision (NeuroIV) data as joint inputs, the proposed method constructs a three-channel feature extraction and fusion network. By leveraging a hypergraph structure, it establishes association weights between dynamic (temporal) and static (spatial) nodes to capture spatiotemporal correlations. To efficiently process the high-dimensional multi-modal data, the traditional dot-product attention is replaced with element-wise multiplication, significantly reducing computational complexity. Furthermore, a lightweight deformable attention pyramid (DAP) and diffusion model is introduced to refine depth image edges, effectively suppressing discontinuities and abruptness in the estimation results. Compared to single-modality optical imagery, the fused multi-modal data yields a superior signal-to-noise ratio and foreground contrast, achieving an improvement of over 20% in the MAE index. These results validate the effectiveness and superiority of the proposed multi-modal fusion strategy for dynamic target observation and depth retrieval in aquatic environments.

### [127] [High-Resolution Inversion, Driving Mechanisms, and Source Apportionment of Near-Surface Ozone in Arid Urban Clusters: A Case Study of the Tianshan North Slope Urban Agglomeration](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132191)
*Guangrui Pan,Yunyun Xi,Tuodi Wang,Liqiang SHEN,Yi Luo,Z Y Li,L Wang,徐律 Lü XU,Linlin Cui,Xicheng Zhang,Xiangjun Lu,Yongpeng Tong*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本研究构建多模型比较框架，基于XGBoost实现天山北坡城市群2023年高精度每日O₃空间反演（R²=0.93），并利用SHAP、后向轨迹模型及潜在源贡献分析方法，从高精度反演、驱动机理分析和跨区域传输识别三个维度系统阐明了干旱区城市群O₃污染的形成机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 臭氧作为关键二次污染物具有显著时空异质性，对区域协同空气污染控制构成挑战，但目前对于干旱区城市群高分辨率O₃空间反演及其驱动机制的系统性理解仍然有限。

Method: 以天山北坡城市群为研究区，构建包含XGBoost、RF、ET、GBDT等16种机器学习和深度学习模型的多模型比较框架；利用SHAP量化驱动因子贡献和非线性响应关系；结合后向轨迹模型、WPSCF和WCWT方法识别潜在源区和传输路径。

Result: (1) XGBoost性能最优（R²=0.93, RPD>3），高O₃浓度主要分布于乌鲁木齐南部、昌吉南部和塔城南部；(2) 下行短波辐射和气温是主要空间驱动因子，两者对O₃生成呈现显著非线性响应和阈值效应；(3) 西风传输是主要外源贡献路径，潜在源区位于北天山周边及中亚地区（哈萨克斯坦东部、吉尔吉斯斯坦北部）。

Conclusion: 本研究从高精度反演、驱动机理分析和跨区域传输识别三个维度系统阐明了干旱区城市群O₃污染形成机制，为精准大气污染防控策略提供了科学依据。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。该文已涉及遥感空间反演核心技术。改进方案：(1) 引入卫星遥感O₃柱浓度数据（如TROPOMI、OMI）作为辅助变量，弥补地面站点稀疏导致的插值偏差；(2) 将MODIS或Landsat地表参数（地表温度、植被指数、不透水面比例）纳入模型特征，增强对下垫面异质性的刻画；(3) 利用GOCI或Himawari-8等高时间分辨率遥感数据捕捉O₃日间演化过程，提升反演时间分辨率；(4) 结合卫星气溶胶光学厚度（AOD）数据，解析气溶胶-O₃耦合机制对反演精度的影响。

Abstract (英文): Ozone (O3), as a key secondary pollutant, exhibits pronounced spatiotemporal heterogeneity, posing significant challenges to coordinated regional air pollution control. However, systematic understanding of high-resolution O3 spatial inversion and its driving mechanisms in arid urban agglomerations remains limited. In this study, the Tianshan North Slope Urban Agglomeration (TNSUA) was selected as the study area, and a multi-model comparative framework was established to comprehensively evaluate the O3 inversion performance of 16 machine learning and deep learning models, including Extreme Gradient Boosting (XGBoost), Random Forest (RF), Extremely Randomized Trees (ET), and Gradient Boosting Decision Tree (GBDT). Based on the optimal model performance, high-precision daily O3 spatial reconstruction for the year 2023 was achieved across the study region. The contributions of individual driving factors and their nonlinear response relationships were quantitatively interpreted using Shapley Additive Explanations (SHAP). Furthermore, a backward trajectory model combined with the Weighted Potential Source Contribution Function (WPSCF) and Weighted Concentration Weighted Trajectory (WCWT) methods was employed to identify potential source regions and transport pathways of O3. The results indicate that: (1) The XGBoost model exhibited the best performance (R2 = 0.93, RPD &gt; 3). The reconstructed results reveal that high O3 concentrations in 2023 were primarily distributed in southern Urumqi, southern Changji, and southern Tacheng, with southern Urumqi identified as the most prominent hotspot. (2) The spatial variability of O3 was predominantly driven by downward shortwave radiation (DSR) and air temperature (TEM), both of which showed significant nonlinear responses and threshold effects on O3 formation. (3) Source apportionment analysis indicates that westerly transport serves as a major exogenous contribution pathway, with potential source regions mainly located in the surrounding areas of the northern Tianshan slope as well as Central Asia, particularly eastern Kazakhstan and northern Kyrgyzstan. This study systematically elucidates the formation mechanisms of O3 pollution in arid urban agglomerations from three aspects—high-precision inversion, driving mechanism analysis, and cross-regional transport identification—thereby providing a scientific basis for precise air pollution control strategies.

### [128] [A Multi-Frequency SAR Framework for Methane Emission Estimation in Thai Rice Paddies](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132194)
*Nuntikorn Kitratporn,Kanjana Koedkurang,Panu Nueangjamnong,Kittiphop Simachokchai,Chompunut Chayawat,Shinichi Sobue,Thuy Le Toan*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出一个自动化框架，融合多频段SAR（Sentinel-1 C-band时间序列 + ALOS-2 PALSAR-2 L-band全极化）与IPCC方法，对泰国平原灌溉稻田的甲烷排放进行估算。物候检测MAE约6-8天，水情分类平衡准确率0.59-0.89，全流程MAE为18.5 kgCH4/ha（21.4%），偏差3.5 kgCH4/ha，并指出水层分类是主要算法误差源，而IPCC Tier 1排放因子结构不确定性远大于算法误差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 水稻种植是农业部门甲烷排放的主要来源，其全球变暖潜能远高于二氧化碳。目前缺乏可规模化、准确的稻田甲烷排放量化方法，亟需结合遥感与碳核算方法的自动化框架以满足碳会计需求。

Method: (1) 利用Sentinel-1 C-band SAR时间序列进行水稻物候检测，识别种植与收获日期；(2) 利用ALOS-2 PALSAR-2 L-band全极化SAR进行水情分类（连续淹水、单次排水、多次排水），采用基于水稻生长阶段的SVM-RBF分类器；(3) 结合IPCC水情缩放因子估算甲烷排放，并通过四轨道反事实分解进行端到端集成。

Result: 物候检测种植和收获日期MAE分别为6.1±1.4天和8.3±1.7天，检测率97.0%±2.7%；水情分类各阶段平衡准确率0.59-0.89；全流程MAE为18.5±4.5 kgCH4/ha（21.4%），偏差3.5±5.8 kgCH4/ha。水层分类是主要算法误差源，IPCC Tier 1排放因子结构范围（-32%至+48%）超过所有算法误差总和。

Conclusion: 该框架提供了将多频SAR数据集成到IPCC合规甲烷估算的空间显式方法，可支持监测、报告与核查应用。水层分类是后续改进重点，而IPCC排放因子不确定性是更大的系统误差来源。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。本文本身就是遥感与农业碳核算交叉的典范。改进方向：(1) 引入Sentinel-2光学数据辅助水层分类，提升多云条件下的分类稳健性；(2) 将SVM-RBF替换为深度学习模型（如时序Transformer或CNN-LSTM）以提升水情分类精度；(3) 扩展至不同气候区与水稻品种，验证框架普适性；(4) 结合TROPOMI或GOSAT等大气CH4柱浓度观测进行排放估算的独立验证；(5) 引入土壤有机碳和温度数据作为额外特征，实现从Tier 1到Tier 3的升级。

Abstract (英文): Rice cultivation is a major source of methane (CH4) emission in the agricultural sector, with a significantly higher global warming potential than carbon dioxide. Accurate and scalable quantification of CH4 from rice paddies is essential for carbon accounting. This study presents an automated framework for estimating rice CH4 emissions from irrigated paddies in the central plain of Thailand, integrating multi-sensor Synthetic Aperture Radar (SAR) observations with the IPCC methodology. The framework combines Sentinel-1 C-band SAR time series for phenological detection, ALOS-2 PALSAR-2 L-band full-polarimetric SAR for water regime classification, and IPCC water-scaling factors corresponding to Continuous Flooding, Single Drainage, or Multiple Drainage regimes. Evaluated across five stratified holdout sets, the phenology detection algorithm achieved planting and harvesting date Mean Absolute Errors of 6.1 ± 1.4 and 8.3 ± 1.7 days, with a 97.0% ± 2.7% operational detection rate. Water regime classification employed rice growth stage-specific Support Vector Machine classifiers with Radial Basis Function kernels (SVM-RBF), achieving per-stage test Balanced Accuracy ranging from 0.59 to 0.89. End-to-end integration using a four-track counterfactual decomposition yielded a full-pipeline mean absolute error of 18.5 ± 4.5 kgCH4ha−1 (21.4% of the mean ground-based CH4 calculation) and a mean bias of 3.5 ± 5.8 kgCH4ha−1. Water level classification was confirmed as the dominant algorithmic uncertainty source, while the IPCC Tier 1 emission factor structural range (−32% to +48% of the default) exceeded all algorithmic errors combined. The proposed framework provides a spatially explicit approach for integrating multi-frequency SAR data into IPCC-compliant methane estimation, supporting Monitoring, Reporting, and Verification applications.

</details>


### [129] [Inundation Monitoring in Rice Fields Using ALOS-2 PALSAR-2: A Case Study of An Giang, the Mekong Delta in Vietnam](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132190)
*Phung Hoang-Phi,Nguyen Lam-Dao,Nghi Dang-Pham-Bao,Thuy Le-Toan,Thi Truong-Nhat-Kieu,Shinichi Sobue*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本研究通过融合ALOS-2 PALSAR-2（L波段）和Sentinel-1（C波段）多时相SAR数据，在越南安江省2025年冬春水稻季实现了对水稻冠层下淹水状况的可靠分类，总体精度达81%，Kappa系数0.77，证明了L波段VV极化穿透稠密植被监测淹水的潜力，为温室气体清单和间歇灌溉（AWD）等低碳水管理提供关键数据支撑。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 准确监测水稻田淹水状态对优化水分利用效率和减少甲烷排放至关重要，但密集水稻冠层下淹水探测是当前遥感领域的主要挑战。现有方法难以穿透稠密冠层实现水下淹水状况的可靠识别。

Method: 集成多时相ALOS-2 PALSAR-2（L波段）和Sentinel-1（C波段）SAR数据，结合实地调查。利用Sentinel-1时间序列估算水稻物候（稻龄），分析ALOS-2 PALSAR-2多极化后向散射在不同生长阶段区分淹水与非淹水条件。

Result: L波段信号（尤其是VV极化）能有效穿透稠密植被，淹水分类总体精度81%，Kappa系数0.77。生成的多时相遇涝图与实地观测一致。

Conclusion: L波段VV极化SAR数据可用于水稻冠层下淹水状况表征，多频SAR集成方法为温室气体清单和间歇灌溉（AWD）等低碳水管理实践验证提供了关键数据支持，推动了气候智慧型农业监测。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。该研究是典型的遥感应用论文，改进方向包括：（1）引入更高时间分辨率的L波段数据（如NISAR任务）提升动态监测能力；（2）结合深度学习（如时序Transformer或CNN-LSTM）自动提取SAR时序特征，减少人工阈值设定；（3）融合光学数据（如Sentinel-2）解决阴雨天云覆盖问题，补充植被指数约束冠层结构信息；（4）扩展到双极化或紧凑极化模式（如RCM）探索极化分解参数（如表面散射占比）对淹水识别的增强效果；（5）增加多尺度特征融合或迁移学习策略，将方法推广到不同水稻种植区（如中国、印度、东南亚）以提高泛化能力。

Abstract (英文): Accurate monitoring of inundation in rice paddies is essential for optimizing water use efficiency and mitigating methane emissions; yet, detecting water beneath dense rice canopies remains a major challenge. This study proposed a reliable classification approach applied to the Winter–Spring 2025 season in An Giang province, Vietnam, by integrating multi-temporal ALOS-2 PALSAR-2 (L-band) and Sentinel-1 (C-band) SAR data with in situ field surveys. Time-series Sentinel-1 observations were used to estimate rice phenology (rice age), while multi-polarization backscatter from ALOS-2 PALSAR-2 was analyzed to discriminate inundated from non-inundated conditions across different growth stages. Results demonstrated that L-band signals, particularly in VV polarization, penetrated dense vegetation effectively, enabling classification of inundated vs. non-inundated fields with an overall accuracy of 81% and a Kappa coefficient of 0.77. The resulting multi-date inundation maps revealed distinct flooding regimes consistent with local field survey observations. These findings demonstrated the potential of L-band VV SAR data for characterizing sub-canopy inundation conditions under rice canopies. Crucially, the approach provides essential data for greenhouse gas inventories and supports the verification of low-emission water management practices, such as Alternate Wetting and Drying (AWD). Overall, the study demonstrated the value of multi-frequency SAR integration for advancing agricultural monitoring and climate-smart management in rice-growing regions.

### [130] [Village-Scale Winter Wheat Yield Prediction in Coastal Saline–Alkali Farmland Using a Three-Stage Fusion XGBoost Framework and SHAP](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132233)
*Wenxi Jia,Jingzhao Lu,杨其展,Yuhang Xie,Xing Cao,Yuqing Pan,Qi Xu,Yapeng Zhou,Jun Zhao,Li Wang,Xiaofei Liu,Fujun Zhao,Y ZHANG*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种物候引导的特征集成方法，结合Sentinel-2影像、气候因子和地形变量，用于预测滨海盐碱农田的村庄级冬小麦产量。研究以河北省黄骅市为例，采用XGBoost模型（R²=0.6382）及三阶段融合XGBoost模型（R²=0.6439），并通过SHAP分析识别关键驱动因子，实现产量空间预测，内陆地区产量（5145 kg/ha）显著高于沿海地区（4198 kg/ha）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 滨海盐碱农田存在强烈的空间异质性和多重环境胁迫，准确估计村庄级冬小麦产量极具挑战性，现有方法难以有效整合物候信息与环境约束因子，因此需要构建针对性的预测框架。

Method: （1）构建物候引导的特征集，融合Sentinel-2影像、气候因子和地形变量（高程、地形湿度指数、距海岸线距离、距水系距离）；（2）采用XGBoost进行基线预测，并与Gradient Boosting、Random Forest、SVR、Ridge回归和Decision Tree对比；（3）设计三阶段分支模型（Three-Stage Fusion XGBoost），分阶段识别盐度指数（SI）、NDVI和产量的主要驱动因子；（4）使用SHAP分析解释各特征对产量预测的贡献。

Result: 物候引导特征集成XGBoost的R²=0.6382，RMSE=450.15 kg/ha；三阶段融合XGBoost的R²=0.6439，RMSE=446.24 kg/ha，MAE=363.38 kg/ha；SHAP分析显示SI、距离因子、高程、TWI和NDVI是关键驱动因子；空间预测显示内陆产量（5145 kg/ha）高于沿海（4198 kg/ha）。

Conclusion: 该框架有效支持滨海盐碱农田村庄级冬小麦产量预测，并通过分阶段建模和SHAP分析提升了模型可解释性，揭示了环境约束与植被响应对产量的联合影响机制。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。（1）可将该物候引导特征集成框架迁移至其他盐碱或边际农田区域（如东北苏打盐碱地、滨海盐沼）的作物产量估算；（2）三阶段分支建模思路可应用于遥感时序数据分析中，如分阶段识别不同生长期植被指数与环境胁迫因子的交互作用；（3）引入更多雷达遥感数据（如Sentinel-1）表征土壤盐分和水分状况，进一步提升模型精度；（4）SHAP解释性分析框架可用于遥感反演模型的因子归因和可解释性增强。

Abstract (英文): Accurately estimating village-level winter wheat yield in coastal saline–alkali farmland is challenging because this region has strong spatial differences and multiple environmental stresses. In this study, Huanghua City, Hebei Province, was selected as a typical coastal saline–alkali area. Sentinel-2 images, climate factors, and topographic variables, including elevation, topographic wetness index, distance to the coastline, and distance to water systems, were combined to build a phenology-guided feature set for winter wheat yield prediction in coastal areas. The results showed that Phenology-Guided Feature Integration XGBoost achieved an R2 of 0.6382 and an RMSE of 450.15 kg/ha, which was slightly better than Gradient Boosting (R2 = 0.6256) and Random Forest (R2 = 0.6098), and clearly better than SVR (R2 = 0.4792), Ridge regression (R2 = 0.4582), and a single Decision Tree (R2 = 0.3088). Then, a three-stage branch was designed to identify the main drivers of SI, NDVI, and winter wheat yield at different stages, helping explain how environmental constraints and vegetation responses jointly affect final yield. The Three-Stage Fusion XGBoost Model achieved an R2 of 0.6439, an RMSE of 446.24 kg/ha, and an MAE of 363.38 kg/ha, showing a slight improvement in prediction accuracy. SHAP analysis showed that SI, distance-related factors, elevation, TWI, and NDVI were important drivers of winter wheat yield variation. Spatial prediction results showed higher winter wheat yield in inland areas (5145 kg/ha) and lower yield in coastal areas (4198 kg/ha). This framework supports village-scale winter wheat yield prediction in coastal saline–alkali farmland and improves model interpretability.

### [131] [Scale Effects on Dominant Drivers of Commercial Plantation Productivity: Novel Insights from High-Resolution Multi-Sensor UAV Remote Sensing and Interpretable AI](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132235)
*Zhansheng Mao,Bo Zheng,Y F LIU,D G Liu*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本研究通过整合10米高密度土壤采样、无人机激光雷达和多光谱遥感数据，利用XGBoost-SHAP可解释机器学习框架，系统解析了亚热带山核桃人工林中叶片叶绿素指数（LCI）在3-50米尺度上的驱动因素。研究发现：细尺度（3-10米）主要由树冠结构（树高）控制；中尺度（10-20米）出现冠层-土壤交互耦合窗口，而20米处交互减弱；大尺度（>30米）交互重新增强，主导因素转向地形和土壤质地。基于此提出了尺度分层的精准林业管理框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 亚热带山地经济林种植园受资源可用性空间异质性制约，但土壤属性、地形和冠层结构调控植被活力的空间尺度尚未明确，缺乏对多尺度驱动机制的定量理解。

Method: 构建空间一致的多尺度数据集（3-50米），包括10米高密度土壤采样、UAV-LiDAR和多光谱遥感数据；采用可解释机器学习框架XGBoost-SHAP分解冠层、土壤和地形对LCI的相对贡献及其跨尺度变化。

Result: 细尺度(3-10米)由树高主导；中尺度(10-20米)出现冠层-土壤耦合窗口，20米交互减弱；大尺度(>30米)交互增强，主导因素转为地形和土壤质地；土壤-冠层关系随空间尺度重组而非静态不变。

Conclusion: 提出了尺度分层的精准林业框架，将管理干预措施与主导因子所操作的生态尺度对齐，为山地经济林种植园的多尺度精准管理提供了科学依据。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。该研究本身即为遥感与生态学的交叉典范。改进方向：(1) 可引入Sentinel-2或Planet等高时间分辨率卫星数据，将分析扩展至时间尺度（如季节动态），探讨植被活力驱动因素的时间尺度依赖性；(2) 将XGBoost-SHAP框架推广至其他经济林（如油茶、橡胶林）或多树种混交林，验证尺度耦合窗口的普适性；(3) 结合GEDI或ICESat-2星载LiDAR数据，将空间分析尺度扩展至区域级（>100米），探索更大尺度下的驱动机制转变；(4) 引入因果推断方法（如结构方程模型或因果森林）补充SHAP的相关性分析，揭示驱动因素间的因果链条。

Abstract (英文): Subtropical mountain economic tree plantations are constrained by pronounced spatial heterogeneity in resource availability, yet the spatial scales at which soil properties, topography, and canopy structure regulate vegetation vigor remain poorly resolved. To address this gap, a spatially consistent multi-scale dataset combining 10 m high-density soil sampling, UAV-LiDAR, and multispectral remote sensing was used to quantify the scale-dependent drivers of the Leaf Chlorophyll Index (LCI) across 3–50 m within a Chinese hickory (Carya cathayensis Sarg.) plantation. The relative contributions of canopy, soil, and topography to LCI were decomposed across scales using an interpretable machine-learning framework (XGBoost–SHAP). At fine scales (3–10 m), vegetation vigor was primarily controlled by tree-level canopy structure, particularly tree height, reflecting localized resource acquisition. At intermediate scales (10–20 m), a distinct coupling window emerged, characterized by increased interaction complexity: LCI was predominantly driven by interactions between canopy structure and soil nutrient availability, whereas single-factor effects weakened. Notably, at 20 m this interaction pattern largely weakened and reverted to single-metric dominance. At broader scales (&gt;30 m), complex interactions re-emerged, and dominant SHAP contributions shifted from nutrients and canopy structure toward topography and soil texture. These findings reconcile strong fine-scale drivers with weaker predictability at intermediate extents and demonstrate that soil–canopy relationships reorganize across spatial scales rather than remaining static. On the basis of these findings, a scale-hierarchical framework for precision forestry is proposed that aligns management interventions with the ecological scales at which dominant correlates operate across spatial supports.

</details>


### [132] [Diffusion-Model-Based Data Augmentation for Target Detection in Side-Scan Sonar Images](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132193)
*Yuanxu Yang,Tao Zhang*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出基于FLUX.1扩散模型和LoRA微调的侧扫声纳图像数据增强方法，在有限数据条件下显著提升了YOLOv8n目标检测性能，mAP@0.5从0.740提升至0.858，并优于传统增强方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 侧扫声纳图像数据集规模小、采集成本高、类别不平衡，限制了深度学习检测器的性能，亟需有效的数据增强方法。

Method: 采用FLUX.1扩散模型作为基础生成框架，通过LoRA低秩适配在有限数据下微调预训练模型，生成样本经筛选后仅加入训练集，使用固定YOLOv8n检测器在相同超参数和随机种子下进行公平评估。

Result: FLUX+LoRA增强将mAP@0.5从0.7400±0.0132提升至0.8582±0.0328，mAP@0.5:0.95从0.3994±0.0187提升至0.5115±0.0164，优于传统增强方法；600样本人工标注的FLUX+LoRA子集在图像质量和检测性能上均优于FLUX-base和SD1.5+LoRA。
