与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。该数据增强方法可直接迁移至遥感目标检测领域，尤其适用于合成孔径雷达（SAR）图像、高光谱图像等小样本场景。遥感领域同样面临标注数据稀缺、类别不平衡问题，FLUX+LoRA的扩散模型微调策略可应用于遥感影像生成，弥补稀有目标（如特定舰船类型、小型地物）的样本不足。需注意遥感图像与侧扫声纳的成像机理差异，建议在预训练模型选择和LoRA适配参数上针对遥感域进行调优。

Abstract (英文): Side-scan sonar images play an important role in underwater target detection, seabed mapping, and marine environment monitoring. However, the performance of deep learning-based detectors is often limited by the small scale of available sonar datasets, the high cost of data acquisition, and class imbalance among target categories. To address these issues, this paper proposes a diffusion-model-based data augmentation method for side-scan sonar target detection. A FLUX.1 diffusion model is adopted as the base generative framework and is fine-tuned using low-rank adaptation (LoRA) to adapt the pretrained model to the side-scan sonar image domain under limited training data conditions. The generated samples are further filtered and added only to the training set, while the validation and test sets are kept unchanged and contain only real sonar images. To ensure a fair evaluation of the augmentation strategy, all detection experiments are conducted using a fixed YOLOv8n (You Only Look Once version 8 nano) detector under the same training hyperparameters and three random seeds. Compared with training on the original dataset, the proposed FLUX+LoRA augmentation improves mean average precision (mAP)@0.5 from 0.7400 ± 0.0132 to 0.8582 ± 0.0328 and mAP@0.5:0.95 from 0.3994 ± 0.0187 to 0.5115 ± 0.0164. It also outperforms conventional augmentation methods under the same real-only validation/test protocol. In addition, Fréchet Inception Distance (FID)/Kernel Inception Distance (KID)-based image quality evaluation, generated-sample amount ablation, screening-strategy ablation, LoRA-rank sensitivity analysis, and a controlled 600-sample diffusion-backbone comparison are conducted. The results show that the 600-sample manually annotated FLUX+LoRA subset selected from generated samples achieves better image quality and detection performance than FLUX-base and SD1.5+LoRA under the same annotation budget. These findings demonstrate that FLUX+LoRA-generated sonar images can provide useful structural diversity for detector training and improve target detection performance under limited-data conditions.

### [133] [Land-Cover-Stratified Validation and Uncertainty Prioritization for SSP-Based NDVI Projection at 1 km Resolution in Northeast China](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132203)
*Eslam Rashad,Yujie Liu,J S Liu,Tao Pan,Ahmed Refaee*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文针对1km分辨率NDVI投影在异质景观中掩盖类别级预测弱点的问题，以中国东北为研究区，构建了四组件评估工作流。通过多阶段模型选择（LightGBM表现最优），进行2040年三种SSP情景下的NDVI投影。结果表明，尽管区域平均NDVI有所增加，但类别分层验证揭示了显著的类别异质性（R²从0.576到-0.886），水体、未利用地和建设用地被识别为最高优先级验证目标。研究强调，土地覆盖分层误差分解和不确定性排序能揭示聚合精度指标所掩盖的类别特定投影局限性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 1km分辨率NDVI投影在异质景观中虽整体空间一致，但隐藏了显著的类别级预测缺陷，这一问题在NDVI投影文献中缺乏系统研究。

Method: 采用四组件评估工作流：（1）多阶段模型选择（空间块交叉验证、时间留出验证、长距离外推、气候扰动测试）；（2）土地覆盖分层验证；（3）基于分位数回归的不确定性表征；（4）验证优先级排序。评估了三种基于树的模型，最终选择LightGBM进行2040年SSP1-2.6、SSP2-4.5和SSP5-8.5情景下的投影。

Result: LightGBM表现最优（空间CV R²=0.654±0.123，时间留出R²=0.710，长距离外推R²=0.671）。区域平均NDVI从2020年0.393增至2040年0.414-0.417。类别验证显示R²范围为0.576（建设用地）到-0.886（未利用地），水体和未利用地R²为负。不确定性风险指数（URI）在建设用地最高、农田最低。历史残差与未来URI共同确定水体、未利用地和建设用地为最高优先级验证目标。

Conclusion: 土地覆盖分层误差分解和不确定性优先级排序能够揭示聚合精度指标所掩盖的类别特定投影局限性，不同类别需要针对性的模型改进策略。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。作为遥感领域NDVI投影研究的直接成果，本研究的改进方向包括：（1）将四组件评估工作流扩展应用到其他遥感参数（如LAI、Albedo、地表温度）的时空投影中；（2）引入深度学习模型（如CNN-LSTM、ConvLSTM）替代LightGBM，以更好捕捉空间上下文和时序依赖；（3）在类别不平衡处理上可引入合成过采样或代价敏感学习策略，改善建设用地和未利用地的预测表现；（4）不确定性量化可进一步采用贝叶斯神经网络或蒙特卡洛dropout等概率深度学习方法；（5）未来可融合多源遥感数据和更细空间分辨率（如30m Landsat）进行降尺度投影验证。

Abstract (英文): At 1 km resolution, NDVI projections for heterogeneous landscapes can appear spatially coherent in aggregate while concealing substantial class-level prediction weaknesses, a limitation that has received limited systematic attention in the NDVI projection literature. This study applies a four-component assessment workflow to Northeast China (NEC) for 2040 under SSP1-2.6, SSP2-4.5, and SSP5-8.5, integrating multi-stage model selection, land-cover-stratified validation, quantile-regression-based uncertainty characterization, and validation-priority ranking. Among three candidate tree-based models evaluated using spatial block cross-validation, temporal holdout validation, long-jump extrapolation, and climatic perturbation tests, LightGBM showed the most balanced and consistent performance, with spatial CV R2 = 0.654 ± 0.123, temporal holdout R2 = 0.710, and long-jump R2 = 0.671, and was therefore selected for the 2040 projection. Projected regional mean NDVI increased modestly from 0.393 in 2020 to 0.414–0.417 across scenarios, with limited divergence among SSP pathways at this near-term horizon. Class-stratified validation of the 2020 holdout prediction revealed that global model performance masked strong class-level heterogeneity, with R2 values ranging from 0.576 for Construction land to −0.886 for Unused land. Water bodies and Unused land exhibited negative R2 values, indicating weak class-level predictive support relative to a simple class-mean benchmark. Residual decomposition showed that Water bodies combined high random error with elevated systematic deviation, whereas Unused land was mainly characterized by systematic bias, suggesting different needs for class-specific model improvement. The Uncertainty Risk Index (URI), derived from 95% prediction intervals, was highest in Construction land and lowest in Cropland across all scenarios. Integrating historical residuals with future URI-identified Water bodies, Unused land, and Construction land as the highest-priority classes for future targeted validation. These priorities arise from both limited class representation and intrinsic NDVI-related complexity, including low vegetation signal, mixed-pixel effects, and heterogeneous land-surface composition. These results demonstrate that land-cover-stratified error decomposition and uncertainty-informed priority ranking reveal class-specific projection limitations that aggregate accuracy metrics can conceal.

### [134] [Future Climate-Driven Changes in Carbon Stocks in the Yellow River Basin of China](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132205)
*Xia Fang,Liangzhong Cao,Ziwei Pei,Shihua Zhu,Yuhong He*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本研究利用干旱生态系统模型（AEM）模拟了黄河流域1981–2060年四种主要碳库（总碳、植被碳、土壤有机碳、凋落物碳）的时空演变。结果显示，1981–2020年总碳增加0.09 Pg C（+3.54%），主要由CO2施肥效应驱动；2021–2060年在SSP5高排放情景下总碳预计增加0.114 Pg C（+4.81%）。凋落物碳变异性最高（−18%至+22%），是碳汇稳定性的敏感指标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 干旱与半干旱生态系统的碳储量动态是全球碳循环评估中的主要不确定性来源，尤其是在黄河流域这一关键区域，有必要系统量化其碳库的时空演变规律及未来趋势。

Method: 采用干旱生态系统模型（Arid Ecosystem Model, AEM），在因子化气候情景下模拟黄河流域1981–2060年总碳（TOTC）、植被碳（VEGC）、土壤有机碳（SOC）和凋落物碳（LTRC）四种碳库的时空演变。

Result: 1981–2020年TOTC增加0.09 Pg C（+3.54%），VEGC（+21.43%）和SOC（+2.78%）均有贡献；2021–2060年SSP5情景下TOTC预计增加0.114 Pg C（+4.81%），VEGC贡献最大（+23.87%）。CO2施肥效应主导碳汇变化，仅增温或仅降水变化的效应较弱。LTRC变异性最高（−18%至+22%）。

Conclusion: 黄河流域碳汇受CO2施肥效应主导，但存在显著的空间异质性和非线性气候-碳相互作用；需要制定因地制宜的适应性策略，结合生态修复与气候适应，以增强碳汇并支撑中国碳中和目标。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。该论文采用模型模拟方法，遥感可提供关键支撑：（1）利用MODIS NDVI/EVI、GPP等遥感产品校验和优化AEM模型中的植被碳参数；（2）利用SMAP土壤水分遥感数据改进模型对半干旱区土壤湿度的模拟精度；（3）利用遥感反演的LAI、fPAR等数据作为模型输入或验证，提升凋落物碳模拟精度；（4）可利用遥感土地覆盖分类数据细化黄河流域不同生态分区碳库模拟；（5）结合InSAR或GRACE等遥感手段监测生态系统水分变化，改进模型对气候-碳非线性相互作用的表现。

Abstract (英文): Carbon storage dynamics in dryland and semi-arid ecosystems remain a major uncertainty in global carbon cycle assessments, particularly in regions like the Yellow River Basin (YRB). Using the Arid Ecosystem Model (AEM), we simulated the spatiotemporal evolution of four major carbon pools—total carbon (TOTC), vegetation carbon (VEGC), soil organic carbon (SOC), and litter carbon (LTRC)—from 1981 to 2060 under factorial climate scenarios. During 1981–2020, TOTC increased by 0.09 Pg C (+3.54%), driven by gains in VEGC (+0.03 Pg C, +21.43%) and SOC (+0.06 Pg C, +2.78%). LTRC showed minimal net change but was highly sensitive to interannual variability. From 2021 to 2060, under the high-emission SSP5 scenario, TOTC is projected to increase by 0.114 Pg C (+4.81%), with VEGC contributing most of the gain (+23.87%). CO2_only simulations showed similar increases, underscoring the dominant role of CO2 fertilization. In contrast, warming and precipitation alone produced weaker and more variable effects. Spatially, upper YRB regions are expected to maintain strong sink capacity, while the Loess Plateau and central-western subregions remain vulnerable to warming and moisture decline. LTRC exhibited the highest variability across scenarios (−18% to +22%), highlighting its role as a sensitive indicator of sink stability. These findings emphasize the need to account for nonlinear climate–carbon interactions and regional heterogeneity. Region-specific, adaptive strategies that integrate ecological restoration and climate adaptation will be critical to enhancing carbon sinks and supporting China’s carbon neutrality targets in the Yellow River Basin.

### [135] [Less Is More: Online Spatio-Temporal Selective Learning for Multi-Variable Meteorological Forecasting](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132202)
*Pu Zhang,Deping Xiang,Chunlei Huo,Kun Ding,Shiming Xiang*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为ST-SL（时空选择性学习）的在线训练框架和VASTFormer骨干网络，通过选择性监督高收益的时空预测单元来提升高维气象场的预测精度，在ERA5数据集上SOTA相对提升8.84% MSE。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高维气象场预测中不同时空单元的训练难度存在异质性，现有深度模型对所有预测单元进行统一优化，导致过度强调低收益或弱泛化能力的监督信号，限制了模型泛化性能。

Method: 1) ST-SL：利用冻结参考模型比较每个预测单元的可学习性，仅对高收益时空单元计算损失；2) VASTFormer：包含变量感知跨变量依赖建模、物理增强的太阳位置编码、以及高效时空转换器来捕捉大气轨迹。

Result: 在ERA5再分析数据集上，VASTFormer+ST-SL相比最强基线在MSE、MAE、RMSE上分别降低8.84%、6.70%、4.54%；ACC平均0.9801，RMSESS平均0.8104；极端条件评估下也保持一致性改进。

Conclusion: 选择性监督能够有效提升稠密气象场预测的泛化能力，ST-SL框架在推理时不引入额外参数或计算成本即可显著提升精度。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：90%。该工作与遥感时空预测（如遥感影像序列预测、数值模式降尺度、地球系统变量预测）高度契合。具体交叉方案：1) 将ST-SL选择性子监督机制引入遥感影像预测任务，针对不同区域（如云覆盖区/无云区）或不同预报时效动态选择高收益像素进行损失计算；2) VASTFormer的变量感知注意力机制可直接用于多光谱/高光谱遥感数据的跨波段依赖建模；3) 太阳位置编码可适配遥感中光照角度变化敏感的观测场景（如光学卫星影像）；4) 将VASTFormer应用于遥感参数反演任务（如海表面温度、植被指数等物理量的时空序列预测）。

Abstract (英文): Accurate forecasting of high-dimensional meteorological fields remains challenging due to the complex spatio-temporal dynamics of atmospheric systems and the presence of heterogeneous training difficulty across space and lead time. Existing deep forecasting approaches usually optimize all prediction units uniformly, which may overemphasize low-benefit or weakly generalizable supervision signals. To address this issue, we propose Spatio-Temporal Selective Learning (ST-SL), an online training framework that estimates the learnability of each prediction unit by comparing the main model with a frozen reference model and computes the loss only over selected high-benefit spatio-temporal units. To provide an effective forecasting backbone, we further introduce VASTFormer, a variable-aware spatio-temporal Transformer that models cross-variable dependencies, incorporates physics-enhanced Solar Positional Encoding, and captures atmospheric trajectories with an efficient temporal translator. Experiments on the ERA5 reanalysis dataset show that VASTFormer outperforms representative spatio-temporal baselines, while ST-SL further improves accuracy without adding inference-time parameters or computational cost. Compared with the strongest baseline, VASTFormer+ST-SL reduces MSE, MAE, and RMSE by 8.84%, 6.70%, and 4.54%, respectively. Meteorological skill evaluation further shows an average ACC of 0.9801 and RMSESS of 0.8104, and percentile-based extreme-condition evaluations confirm consistent improvements across standard and high-impact forecasting scenarios. These results indicate that selective supervision can improve generalization in dense meteorological forecasting.

### [137] [Experiences of the Scan of Existing Bridge Structures with Multiple Real-World Case Studies in Germany](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132185)
*Monika Lederer,Christoph Stahl,Jan‐Iwo Jäkel,Peter Gölzhäuser,Annette Schmitt,Katharina Klemt-Albert,Alexander Reiterer*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文通过十座德国真实桥梁的多案例研究，系统评估了TLS、MLS和UAS三种扫描技术在桥梁数字化中的性能差异，并提出了一个符合BPMN标准的通用流程模型，以指导结构工程中的数据采集工作流优化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 桥梁扫描工作流常依赖从业者的隐含经验而非标准化协议，缺乏系统性的性能对比和可复用的流程指南，导致数据质量和效率难以保障。

Method: 采用多案例研究方法，对德国十座异构真实桥梁进行TLS、MLS和UAS摄影测量扫描，对比分析各技术在精度、遮挡、灵活性、几何噪声和轨迹漂移等方面的表现，并基于BPMN标准构建通用流程模型。

Result: TLS精度高但存在阴影遮挡问题；UAS操作灵活但在细部结构上存在摄影测量重建噪声，且在振动跨段存在SLAM轨迹漂移；MLS介于两者之间。各技术存在明显的性能权衡。

Conclusion: 研究提供了一个包含法律和空间约束的、可操作的BPMN兼容流程模型，为结构工程中的数据质量和效率优化提供了实用指南。

Abstract (英文): Efficient bridge scanning and documentation are crucial for creating reliable digital 3D models. However, scanning workflows often rely on implicit practitioner experience rather than standardized protocols. This paper presents practical insights derived from a Multiple Case Study (MCS) of ten heterogeneous, real-world bridges in Germany. The study evaluates Terrestrial Laser Scanning (TLS), Mobile Laser Scanning (MLS) and Unmanned Aerial Systems (UAS) photogrammetry. The findings isolate distinct performance trade-offs. TLS offers high accuracy but suffers from shadowing occlusions. Conversely, UAS provides operational flexibility but introduces geometric vulnerabilities, including photogrammetric reconstruction noise on fine structures and SLAM trajectory drift on vibrating spans. To unify these insights, a generalized, BPMN-compliant process model mapping the complete data acquisition lifecycle under legal and spatial constraints is defined. This research provides an actionable, practical guide to optimize data quality and efficiency in structural engineering workflows.

</details>


### [138] [A Comparative Evaluation of UAV-Based Remote Sensing and Geophysical Techniques for Landmine Detection on a Seeded Minefield](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132182)

TL;DR: 本文基于34个多模态数据集，在标准化试验场对9种探测模态（RGB、热红外、多光谱、高光谱、LiDAR、SAR等）进行地雷与未爆弹药检测性能评估。RGB在表面检测中表现最佳（94.8%），手持电磁感应和磁力仪对铁质埋设目标>95%但塑料目标<10%，探地雷达是唯一能检测埋设塑料目标（55.6%）的模态。所有数据已公开并附带交互式网络地图。

Abstract (英文): Reliable and scalable landmine detection technologies are essential for humanitarian mine action (HMA), yet standardized benchmarks for Unmanned Aerial Vehicle (UAV)-based sensing in operationally relevant environments remain limited. This study presents a comprehensive evaluation of 34 multimodal datasets acquired over a standardized seeded test site for landmine and unexploded ordnance detection. Nine sensing modalities, including RGB, thermal, multispectral, hyperspectral, LiDAR, and Synthetic Aperture Radar (SAR), are evaluated using the Anomaly, Identifiable Anomaly, Unique Identifiable Anomaly (AIU) index to establish a unified framework for quantifying detection fidelity. Results indicate that RGB imagery achieves the highest surface detection rate (94.8%), with 45.4% of targets classified as uniquely identifiable, reducing false-positive risk. For sub-surface detection, handheld electromagnetic induction (EMI) and magnetometry exceed 95% detection for ferrous items but fall below 10% for plastic ordnance. Ground-penetrating radar (GPR) is the only modality capable of detecting buried plastic targets (55.6% for cart-based systems), whereas UAV-mounted GPR remains limited (18.2%) at current operational flight heights. Based on the comparative analysis, we discuss the gaps in current detection capabilities, compare false-positive rates across modalities, and perform a cost–benefit analysis fitting contamination scenarios with the most cost-effective detection method. All datasets are publicly released, along with an interactive web-map, to support reproducible benchmarking and cross-modality comparison in UAV-enabled explosive hazard detection.

### [139] [A Two-Stage Reference-Guided Workflow for Improving VIIRS Leaf Area Index Retrieval over Mixed Pixels](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132214)
*Tengqi Yue,Haiyong Ding,Yuanfei Zhang*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种参考引导的两阶段工作流，通过亚像素组分校正标签（第一阶段）和随机森林模型（第二阶段），显著提升了VIIRS LAI产品在异质景观上的反演精度，在LOSO验证中R²达0.901，RMSE为0.703，优于官方VNP产品。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 中分辨率LAI产品在异质景观上受两个问题影响：一是粗分辨率预测变量中未解决的亚像素组成，二是由高分辨率产品聚合而来的监督标签存在结构偏差。现有方法未能同时解决这两个问题，导致LAI反演精度受限。

Method: 两阶段工作流：(1) 标签校准阶段，利用亚像素PFT分数和森林敏感铰链项对聚合的Sentinel-2 LAI进行校正，生成500m校正标签；(2) 模型训练阶段，以VIIRS光谱反射率、观测几何、植被指数、纹理和亚像素组成变量为输入，训练随机森林模型。使用2020-2021年美国11个GBOV站点数据训练，通过同站点时间迁移（2019/2022）和留一站点交叉验证评估。

Result: 标签校准使与GBOV的一致性从R²=0.752/RMSE=1.110提升至R²=0.908/RMSE=0.676；LOSO验证下最终模型R²=0.901/RMSE=0.703；在与官方VNP产品的2019/2022重叠子集对比中，本方法R²=0.905/RMSE=0.609，远优于VNP的R²=0.755/RMSE=0.978。

Conclusion: 参考引导的标签校正结合显式亚像素组分信息能够有效改善异质混合像元上的VIIRS LAI反演精度，证明了在训练标签层面消除聚合偏差对提升中分辨率LAI产品的重要性。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。该工作流可直接迁移至其他中分辨率传感器（如MODIS、FY-3 MERSI）的LAI反演；其标签校正策略可应用于GEOV2、MCD15等同类产品的再训练；随机森林模型可替换为深度学习模型（如CNN、Transformer）以进一步提取空间-光谱特征；铰链项设计可拓展至其他生物群系（如农田、湿地）以增强普适性。

Abstract (英文): Moderate-resolution leaf area index (LAI) retrieval over heterogeneous landscapes is affected not only by unresolved subpixel composition in coarse-resolution predictors, but also by structural bias in supervisory labels aggregated from higher-resolution products. To address this issue, we developed a reference-guided two-stage workflow to improve LAI retrieval from the Visible Infrared Imaging Radiometer Suite (VIIRS). In the first stage, aggregated Sentinel-2 LAI was calibrated against Ground-Based Observations for Validation (GBOV) LP3 reference LAI using subpixel plant functional type (PFT) fractions and forest-sensitive hinge terms to generate corrected 500 m labels. In the second stage, a random-forest model was trained using VIIRS spectral reflectance, viewing geometry, vegetation indices, texture, and subpixel compositional variables. Model development was based on 2020–2021 data from 11 U.S. GBOV sites. Performance was evaluated by same-site temporal transfer to 2019 and 2022 and by strict leave-one-site-out (LOSO) validation. Label calibration improved agreement with GBOV from a coefficient of determination (R2) of 0.752 and a root mean square error (RMSE) of 1.110 to an R2 of 0.908 and an RMSE of 0.676. Under LOSO validation, the final model achieved an R2 of 0.901 with an RMSE of 0.703. On the 2019/2022 overlap subset shared by the final VIIRS retrieval, the official VNP product, and the GBOV reference, the final model achieved an R2 of 0.905 and an RMSE of 0.609, compared with 0.755 and 0.978 for the official VNP product. These results show that reference-guided label correction, combined with explicit subpixel compositional information, can substantially improve VIIRS LAI retrieval over mixed pixels within the evaluated study domain.

### [140] [DST-SARNet: A Dual-Stage Texture-Aware SAR Prior Network for Cloud Removal in Optical Remote Sensing Images](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132199)
*Z Wang,Mingzhi Zhang,Yue Wang,Xudong Qiu,Jingqi Yan,Na Niu*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出DST-SARNet，一种双阶段SAR结构引导网络，用于光学遥感图像去云。该网络在输入端提供早期结构骨架引导，在输出端附近进行晚期高频调制，中间插入纹理感知非对称检索模块作为瓶颈记忆检索，避免了密集SAR注入带来的噪声传播问题。实验表明该方法能有效恢复云污染图像且模型紧凑。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有云去除方法存在以下问题：(1) CNN方法恢复局部纹理好但难以建模大范围云覆盖区域的全局结构和颜色一致性；(2) Transformer方法能捕获长距离依赖但标准自注意力对高分辨率遥感图像计算和内存成本高，高效注意力又削弱边缘和纹理判别性；(3) SAR图像能穿透云层提供地表结构信息，但重复的SAR注入会传播散斑噪声、跨模态未对齐和成像差异。因此需要一种既能有效利用SAR结构信息又避免噪声传播的去云方法。

Method: 提出DST-SARNet双阶段SAR结构引导网络：(1) 双阶段SAR引导：早期在输入端提供结构骨架引导，晚期在输出端附近进行高频调制；(2) 在两个阶段之间放置纹理感知非对称检索模块，作为瓶颈记忆检索操作，而非第三个密集SAR注入阶段；(3) SAR分支负责结构骨架、可读纹理记忆和终端细节补偿，光学分支负责颜色、语义和光谱外观恢复。

Result: 在SMILE-CR和SEN12MS-CR数据集上的实验表明，DST-SARNet能有效恢复云污染图像，且模型规模紧凑。

Conclusion: DST-SARNet通过双阶段SAR结构引导和纹理感知非对称检索的设计，实现了高效且紧凑的SAR辅助光学云去除，验证了该框架在SAR辅助光学遥感去云中的潜力。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。该论文本身就是遥感领域的云去除研究。可能的改进方向：(1) 可引入多时相光学图像作为补充信息，与SAR结构引导形成多模态融合，提升在时序变化区域的去云鲁棒性；(2) 纹理感知非对称检索模块可进一步结合可变形卷积或动态滤波器，提升对不同形状和尺度云图的适应性；(3) 可探索无监督或自监督训练策略，减少对配对SAR-光学数据的依赖；(4) 引入频域分解（如小波变换）分别处理低频结构和高频纹理，与双阶段设计协同增强细节恢复能力。

Abstract (英文): Cloud contamination obscures ground objects, interferes with surface reflectance, and disrupts spatial continuity. In thick-cloud regions, surface structures and spectral information are often extensively missing. CNN-based cloud removal methods can recover local textures, but they are less effective at modeling global structures and color consistency over large cloud-covered areas. Transformer-based methods capture long-range dependencies; however, standard self-attention introduces high computational and memory costs for high-resolution remote sensing images. Efficient attention reduces this cost but may weaken edge and texture discriminability. SAR imagery can penetrate clouds and provide surface structural information, yet repeated SAR injections may propagate speckle noise, cross-modal misalignment, and imaging discrepancies through deep restoration layers. To address these issues, this paper proposes DST-SARNet, a dual-stage SAR structural guidance network for optical remote sensing image cloud removal. In this framework, dual-stage refers to two explicit SAR-guidance positions: early structural skeleton guidance at the input side and late high-frequency modulation near the output. The Texture-Aware Asymmetric Retrieval module is placed between these two stages as a bottleneck memory retrieval operation rather than as a third dense SAR injection stage. With this design, SAR provides structural skeletons, readable texture memory, and terminal detail compensation, while the optical branch remains responsible for color, semantics, and spectral appearance recovery. Experiments on the SMILE-CR and SEN12MS-CR datasets show that DST-SARNet effectively restores cloud-contaminated imagery with a compact model scale, demonstrating its potential for efficient SAR-assisted optical cloud removal.

### [141] [Physics-Guided Physical-Coordinate Center Detection for Measured Radar Point Targets Under Ground Clutter](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132204)
*Z H Zhang,Xiaoxiong Li,Jiachen Yang,Weiwei Li,Xi Zhang*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出波形与物理引导的中心检测器（WPG-Center），将雷达点目标检测重新定义为连续物理坐标中心定位，通过四通道杂波感知距离-多普勒表示、各向异性主干网络、波形分辨率感知高斯标签监督和条件物理先验解码，在实测LSS-Ku-1.0数据集上实现了0.850的检测概率和18.16米的距离RMSE，优于现有方法和CFAR基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实测雷达点目标检测中，弱目标回波常被地杂波峰值掩盖，且图像空间检测无法直接表达物理距离-多普勒坐标，现有方法难以兼顾检测精度与物理坐标定位准确性。

Method: 1) 将检测重构为连续物理坐标中心定位；2) 构建四通道杂波感知RD表示；3) 使用各向异性主干网络与距离-杂波响应调制；4) 波形分辨率感知高斯标签监督中心热图；5) 条件物理先验解码用于低带宽、近零多普勒情况下的候选重排序。

Result: 在实测LSS-Ku-1.0数据集上，采用严格分块5折LFM协议，WPG-Center达到Pd=0.850±0.101，距离RMSE=18.16±12.19 m，解码中心检测概率和距离精度均优于Radar-FPN热图检测器和CFAR基线；消融实验证实分辨率感知监督的必要性。

Conclusion: 波形与物理引导的中心检测方法在实测雷达数据上优于传统CFAR和现有学习基线，固定高斯消融效果显著下降，验证了分辨率感知监督的关键作用，步进频波形分析进一步界定了LFM结论的适用范围。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感领域（如SAR目标检测）可借鉴本方法：1) 将检测头从像素级分类改为物理坐标中心定位，提升亚像素精度；2) 引入杂波感知多通道表示适应复杂地表散射环境；3) 各向异性骨干可适配SAR图像中目标的长条状散射特征；4) 波形分辨率感知标签适用于不同SAR成像模式（条带/聚束）下的分辨率差异校准。

Abstract (英文): Measured radar point-target detection under ground clutter is difficult because weak target echoes often compete with clutter peaks, and image-space detections do not directly represent physical range-Doppler coordinates. This paper proposes a waveform- and physics-guided center detector (WPG-Center) for measured radar maps. The method reformulates detection as continuous physical-coordinate center localization, constructs a four-channel clutter-aware range-Doppler (RD) representation, uses an anisotropic backbone with range-clutter response modulation, and supervises the center heatmap with waveform-resolution-aware Gaussian targets. Conditional physical-prior decoding is used as a targeted candidate reranking step for low-bandwidth, near-zero-Doppler cases. Experiments are conducted on the measured LSS-Ku-1.0 dataset using a strict blocked 5-fold linear frequency-modulated (LFM) protocol with physical localization tolerances and decoded-center detection metrics. WPG-Center achieves a probability of detection (Pd) of 0.850±0.101 and a range root-mean-square error (RMSE) of 18.16±12.19 m, giving the best average decoded-center detection probability and range accuracy among the compared learned and constant false-alarm rate (CFAR)-style baselines, including an independent radar feature pyramid network (Radar-FPN) heatmap detector. The fixed-sigma ablation is substantially weaker, supporting the need for resolution-aware supervision. Fold-wise, qualitative, and stepped-frequency waveform (SFW) analyses are reported as auxiliary evidence to define the scope of the measured LFM conclusion.

### [142] [Replacing Yield Detrending with Direct Spatiotemporal Inputs Improves LSTM-Based Rice Yield Estimation](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132200)
*Nuo Chen,Fumin Wang,Xi Zhang,Zhen Zhao,Wenkai Wan,Junwei Liu,Zhou Shi,Songchao Chen*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本研究以美国六个州112个水稻种植县为研究对象，对比了传统统计去趋势方法与直接将时空变量输入深度学习模型的水稻产量估算效果。结果表明，直接输入年份比去趋势方法显著优越，LSTM模型R²从0.54提升至0.61；时空变量（年、经度、纬度）在SHAP分析中重要性高于大多数气象和遥感变量；空间信息可改善极端产量区域的系统偏差；综合配置在灌浆期（收获前1.5-2个月）即可达到近收获期精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有产量估算研究主要依赖统计去趋势方法（如移动平均、线性回归）分离时间趋势，但这类方法依赖于对时间-产量关系的事先假设，假设被违反时会引入系统偏差。同时，时间和空间信息各自的贡献及其交互效应尚未在统一框架下被系统评估。

Method: 选取美国六个州112个水稻种植县（2000-2021年），使用植被指数（NDVI）、气象指标（生长度日、致死度日、累积降水）和时空变量（年、经度、纬度），设计六种输入配置，比较传统去趋势与直接输入时间变量，在四种模型架构（LSTM、Random Forest、XGBoost、Transformer）上进行验证。

Result: (1) 直接输入年份在所有模型中均显著优于去趋势方法，时空组合配置表现最佳（LSTM R²=0.61 vs 去趋势0.54）；(2) SHAP分析中年份是最重要的预测因子，时空变量重要性高于大多数气象和遥感变量；(3) 空间信息持续提升精度并减轻极端产量区域的系统偏差；(4) 组合配置在不同州、年份和产量水平上均表现最佳，在灌浆期（收获前1.5-2个月）即可达到近收获期精度。

Conclusion: 将原始时空数据直接集成到深度学习模型中比统计去趋势方法更有效，为大尺度作物产量估算提供了一种更简单、更稳健的方法。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：90%。遥感水稻产量估算可借鉴以下方案：(1) 将时间（年份）作为直接特征输入到CNN、LSTM等深度学习模型中，替代传统的遥感时间序列去趋势预处理；(2) 引入空间坐标（经纬度）作为显式特征，结合遥感影像中的空间纹理信息，处理区域异质性；(3) 在遥感时空融合模型中（如STARFM、ESTARFM）中直接嵌入时间和空间变量作为协变量，减少预处理偏差；(4) 利用SHAP等可解释性分析评估遥感特征与时空特征的相对重要性，优化特征选择策略。

Abstract (英文): Accurate rice yield estimation is essential for food security. Two key factors affecting estimation accuracy are the long-term upward trend in yield over time and regional heterogeneity across space. Current studies predominantly employ statistical detrending methods (e.g., moving averages, linear regression) to isolate temporal trends. However, such methods rely on prior assumptions about the time–yield relationship and may introduce systematic bias when these assumptions break down. Meanwhile, the individual contributions of temporal and spatial information, and their interactive effects, have not been systematically evaluated within a unified framework. We selected 112 rice-growing counties across six U.S. states (2000–2021), using vegetation index (Normalized Difference Vegetation Index), meteorological indicators (growing degree days, killing degree days, and cumulative precipitation), and spatiotemporal variables (year, longitude, and latitude). We designed six input configurations to compare conventional detrending against direct temporal variable inclusion, testing across four model architectures (Long Short-Term Memory, Random Forest, XGBoost, and Transformer). Results showed that: (1) directly inputting year significantly outperformed detrending across all models, with the combined spatiotemporal configuration achieving the best performance (LSTM R2 = 0.61 vs. 0.54 for detrending); (2) year was the most important predictor in SHAP analysis, with spatiotemporal variables ranking higher than most meteorological and remote sensing variables; (3) spatial information consistently improved accuracy and mitigated systematic bias for extreme yield regions; (4) the combined configuration performed best across different states, years (including extreme climate events), and yield levels, achieving near-end-of-season accuracy at the grain-filling stage (1.5–2 months before harvest). This study demonstrates that integrating raw spatiotemporal data directly into deep learning models is more effective than statistical detrending, offering a simpler and more robust approach for large-scale crop yield estimation.

</details>


### [143] [UAV-Based Soil Salinity Estimation Using Stagewise Feature Optimization and Dual-Backbone Deep Learning Fusion](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132237)
*Chao Zhang,Yujie Hu,Min Tang,Shaoyuan Feng,Zhen Zheng,Ziang Xie,Zhijun Jia,Huailiang Wang,Lei Xie*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种结合轻量级多骨干网络与分阶段特征优化的无人机土壤盐分估测框架，在少量农业样本条件下有效提升了表层和次表层土壤盐分估测的精度、鲁棒性和可解释性，其中ResVGGNet在表层盐分估测中取得最佳表现（R²=0.820）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 小样本农业条件下土壤盐分精确估测面临三大挑战：标记数据稀缺、单骨干神经网络表征能力有限以及次表层盐分反演复杂度高。现有方法难以同时应对这些问题，亟需开发一种在少量样本约束下仍能保持高精度和鲁棒性的盐分估测框架。

Method: 首先利用RF-RFE、One-SE准则和VIF分析将129个候选变量优化为统一的16通道特征集；然后构建三种轻量级单骨干网络（VGGNet、ResNet、DenseNet）和三种双骨干特征级融合网络（DenseResNet、DenseVGGNet、ResVGGNet）进行表层与次表层盐分估测；最后采用SHAP分析进行可解释性评估。

Result: 单骨干网络中ResNet统计精度最高，DenseNet趋势保持最优；表层盐分估测中ResVGGNet表现最佳（R²=0.820, RMSE=0.626 g/kg, MAE=0.409 g/kg, RPD=2.31）；SHAP分析揭示植被和盐分敏感指数及光谱均值特征的主导作用，各主要输入通道呈现空间互补响应模式。

Conclusion: 轻量级多骨干特征级融合与精简特征优化策略的集成，能有效提升无人机土壤盐分估测在少量农业样本条件下的精度、鲁棒性和可解释性。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。改进方案：（1）可将该双骨干融合策略迁移到高光谱或SAR遥感数据中，替代原RGB+多光谱输入，提升对复杂地物类型的表征能力；（2）特征优化流程（RF-RFE+One-SE+VIF）可直接应用于遥感大数据特征降维，尤其在处理高维遥感指数时具有通用性；（3）SHAP可解释性分析可用于遥感反演模型的物理一致性验证，辅助识别关键波段与植被指数的物理意义；（4）未来可引入Transformer或Mamba等时序建模模块替代CNN骨干，进一步提升对遥感时间序列信息的捕捉能力。

Abstract (英文): Accurate soil salinity estimation under small-sample agricultural conditions continues to pose a formidable challenge, attributed to the scarcity of labeled data, inherent representational limitations of single-backbone neural networks, and the heightened complexity of subsurface salinity inversion. To mitigate these intertwined challenges, this study developed a UAV-enabled soil salinity estimation framework that integrated lightweight convolutional neural networks and staged feature optimization, leveraging both RGB and multispectral imagery. A feature selection framework integrating random forest recursive feature elimination (RF-RFE), the one-standard-error (One-SE) criterion, and variance inflation factor (VIF) analysis was employed to reduce 129 candidate variables to a unified 16-channel feature set, which served as the common input for estimating both surface and subsurface soil salinity. Three lightweight single-backbone (VGGNet, ResNet, and DenseNet) and dual-backbone feature-level fusion networks (DenseResNet, DenseVGGNet, and ResVGGNet) were constructed and systematically evaluated for their performance in estimating both surface and subsurface soil salinity. Among the single-backbone networks, ResNet yielded the highest overall statistical accuracy, while DenseNet exhibited superior performance in preserving estimation trends. For surface soil salinity estimation, ResVGGNet achieved the best performance among all evaluated models, with an R2 of 0.820, RMSE of 0.626 g/kg, MAE of 0.409 g/kg, and RPD of 2.31 on the test dataset. SHAP analysis further highlighted the dominant role of vegetation and salinity-sensitive indices, together with selected spectral mean features, and revealed spatially complementary response patterns among major input channels. Collectively, the integration of lightweight multi-backbone feature-level fusion with streamlined feature optimization strategies effectively enhances the accuracy, robustness, and interpretability of UAV-enabled soil salinity estimation, particularly under the constraint of small agricultural sample sizes.

### [144] [Memory-Guided Adaptive Spectral–Spatial Perception Model for Hyperspectral Image Classification](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132225)
*Xinhui Wang,Bin Yan,Pengyu Guo,Xiaolong Yang,Hongyu Liu,LZ Cao,Yong Liu,Zhi Yang,Yuhang Liu*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 提出一种记忆引导的自适应光谱-空间感知模型（MGASP），通过单样本级自适应感知Transformer、批次内度量学习和跨批次记忆引导策略，在极少标注样本（0.5%-1%）下实现高光谱图像高精度分类。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高光谱图像分类在样本稀缺条件下性能显著下降，现有方法难以在极小样本下充分捕获全局光谱-空间特征，亟需一种能够跨样本、跨批次聚合特征的高效分类模型。

Method: 1）单样本级：自适应感知Transformer结合可变形/扩张卷积与Transformer编码器提取单个样本的全局上下文；2）批次内级：度量学习策略显式捕获批次内样本间结构依赖与特征关系；3）跨批次级：记忆引导策略构建动态记忆库，存储并检索同类样本特征，弥合过去与当前分布。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。改进方案：1）可将动态记忆库扩展为类别平衡重放机制，缓解长尾类别遗忘；2）自适应感知Transformer中的可变形卷积可迁移至遥感目标检测任务，增强几何形变鲁棒性；3）三级全球化策略可直接应用于遥感语义分割中的半监督/弱监督场景，例如结合伪标签筛选实现跨批次特征一致性约束。

Abstract (英文): Accurate hyperspectral image classification is fundamental to geospatial applications but is often constrained by annotation scarcity. To achieve high classification performance under small-sample conditions, we propose the Memory-Guided Adaptive Spectral–Spatial Perception model, which incorporates a three-level globalization strategy. At the single-sample level, an adaptive perception Transformer combines deformable and dilated convolutions with a Transformer encoder to capture global context from individual samples. At the intra-batch level, we introduce a metric learning strategy that explicitly captures structural dependencies and feature relationships among samples within each mini-batch, enabling comprehensive feature aggregation in a localized context. At the cross-batch level, a memory-guided strategy constructs a dynamic memory bank to store and retrieve features from same-class samples across training iterations, bridging past and present distributions to enhance generalization. Using only 1% of the SaliLMSS, Pavia University and Kennedy Space Center datasets and 0.5% of the WHU-LongKou dataset as training samples, our method achieves outstanding overall accuracy of 96.15%, 97.81%, 89.22% and 99.32%, respectively, outperforming existing methods.

### [145] [UAV Remote Sensing for Drought-Adaptive Sesame Breeding: Flight-Altitude Benchmarking, Predictive Modelling, and Composite Stress Tolerance Indexing](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132181)
*Christos Petsoulas,Alexandros Tsitouras,Eleftherios Evangelou,Anastasia Kargiotidou,Chrysanthi Pankou,Dimitrios Ν. Vlachostergios*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文利用大疆Phantom 4多光谱无人机在40、80、120米三个高度对588个芝麻基因型进行高通量表型采集，对比灌溉和终端干旱两种环境。研究发现40米高度精度最高，光谱指数在干旱胁迫下重复性更好，基于结构-光谱数据的复合胁迫耐受指数（STI）能有效富集优良基因型，富集倍数达4.1倍（超几何检验p=4.5×10⁻⁵）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 芝麻早期育种需要在大面积未重复群体中对不同环境进行高通量表型鉴定，传统方法效率低，无人机遥感提供了一种快速、非破坏性的解决方案。

Method: 使用大疆Phantom 4多光谱无人机在40、80、120米高度飞行采集数据；通过运动恢复结构（SfM）生成冠层高度模型并与地面测量对比；从40米影像提取NDVI、NDRE、GNDVI、LCI四种光谱指数；采用普通最小二乘法、随机森林和梯度提升三种回归模型，在留一基因型、留一环境和留一日期的交叉验证框架下评估；用组内相关系数量化基因型重复性；构建复合胁迫耐受指数排序干旱胁迫表现。

Result: 40米高度冠层高度精度最高（充分灌溉R²=0.812，干旱R²=0.663）；留一基因型交叉验证R²≈0.83，但留一日期间交叉验证降至R²≈0.55；全结构-光谱OLS模型在留一日期间交叉验证下崩溃（R²=-0.203），而树集成模型保持稳定；干旱胁迫下光谱指数重复性提高约2倍（ICC(3,4)>0.84）；复合STI识别出38个优良基因型（占7.6%），其前30名中有10个进入育种者从全部588行选出的48个最优品种中，富集倍数4.1倍（超几何检验p=4.5×10⁻⁵）。

Conclusion: 无人机多光谱表型平台在芝麻育种中可行，40米是最佳飞行高度；树集成模型比线性模型更具鲁棒性；复合STI能有效筛选耐旱基因型，显著富集育种目标品种。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。该论文本身就是遥感与作物育种的交叉应用，可直接迁移至其他作物（如小麦、玉米、大豆）的耐旱育种。改进方向：(1)引入深度学习模型（如3D-CNN、时序Transformer）替代传统树集成模型以提升时序泛化能力；(2)结合高光谱或热红外传感器增加水分胁迫相关指标；(3)将STI与基因组选择结合，实现"遥感表型+基因组预测"的整合育种框架。

Abstract (英文): Early-generation sesame (Sesamum indicum L.) breeding requires high-throughput phenotyping of large unreplicated populations across contrasting environments. A DJI Phantom 4 Multispectral UAV was flown at 40, 80, and 120 m above ground level (AGL) over 588 M2 genotypes under full irrigation (ENV1) and terminal drought (ENV2; irrigation withheld from reproductive onset) on four dates (July–September 2025). Structure-from-motion canopy height models were compared with ground measurements, and four spectral reflectance indices—Normalised Difference Vegetation Index (NDVI), Normalised Difference Red Edge (NDRE), Green Normalised Difference Vegetation Index (GNDVI), and Leaf Chlorophyll Index (LCI)—were derived from 40 m imagery. Ordinary least squares (OLS), Random Forest, and Gradient Boosting were evaluated under leave-one-genotype-out (LOGO), leave-one-environment-out (LOEO), and leave-one-date-out (LODO) cross-validation; genotypic repeatability was quantified by intraclass correlation (ICC), and drought performance was ranked by a composite Stress Tolerance Index (STI) validated against an independent breeder assessment. The 40 m altitude gave the highest height accuracy (R2 = 0.812 in ENV1; 0.663 in ENV2). LOGO accuracy (R2 ≈ 0.83) fell to R2 ≈ 0.55 under LODO—the operationally relevant figure for a new phenological stage—and the full structural–spectral OLS model collapsed (R2 = −0.203) where tree ensembles remained stable. Spectral-index repeatability was up to ~2-fold higher under stress (ICC(3,4) &gt; 0.84). The composite STI flagged 38 elite genotypes (7.6% of 498); 10 of its top 30 were confirmed in the breeder’s 48-best selection from all 588 rows—a 4.1-fold enrichment over chance (hypergeometric p = 4.5 × 10−5).

### [146] [Assessing Urban Ventilation Resistance and Surface Warming Using Multi-Source Data: A Case Study of Kaifeng City](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132227)
*Huiqi Sun,Hao Zheng,Lu Yu,Jingyuan Cheng*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 该研究整合XGBoost、SHAP和多尺度地理加权回归（MGWR）方法，分析了1986-2024年开封市六种形态、生态和人类活动因子对地表温度（LST）的影响，发现夜间灯光（NTL）始终是主导指标，建筑足迹（BF）和NTL共同反映了城市扩张和人类活动加剧，且迎风面积密度（FAD）在城郊区域表现出更强的空间异质性，为城市热风险管理提供了长期证据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 综合集成XGBoost（机器学习模型）、SHAP（模型解释方法）和多尺度地理加权回归MGWR（空间异质性分析方法），对开封市1986-2024年五期（代表性年份）的六种因子（形态、生态、人类活动）与LST的关系进行建模与分析。

Result: (1) LST在1986-2024年间显著上升，但年际变率下降，热波动减弱；(2) NTL始终是主导指标，BF与NTL共同表征城市扩张与人类活动加剧；(3) FAD系数在城郊区域的空间异质性显著强于城市核心区（2020年城郊FAD系数离散度是核心区的2.74倍），FAD虽总体贡献较小但提供了密度指标无法捕捉的补充诊断信息，且表现出非线性、方向性和空间异质性响应。

Conclusion: 相比以往侧重短期或单一维度关系的研究，本研究将建筑致密化、通风形态阻力、生态条件和人类活动强度整合到长期LST驱动力框架中，为城市更新和向外扩张过程中的热风险管理提供了实证依据。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。该研究本身就是一篇典型的遥感城市热环境分析论文，应用了Landsat或类似遥感数据反演LST，并结合多源遥感（如NTL夜间灯光遥感）进行分析。改进方向：(1) 引入更高空间分辨率的遥感数据（如Landsat 8/9 TIRS波段或ECOSTRESS热红外数据），提升LST反演精度与时空连续性；(2) 增加三维建筑形态遥感因子（如从高分辨率立体影像或LiDAR提取的建筑高度、体积），细化FAD（迎风面积密度）的估算；(3) 扩展至多城市对比分析（如结合城市群尺度的遥感数据），检验结论的泛化性；(4) 引入遥感-derived的生态参数（如改进的NDVI、植被覆盖度、地表反照率等），增强生态因子的解释力。

Abstract (英文): Changes in urban form strongly affect surface thermal conditions, yet long-term quantitative assessments of this relationship, particularly the role of ventilation resistance, remain limited. To address this gap, this study integrates XGBoost, SHapley Additive explanations (SHAP), and multi-scale geographically weighted regression (MGWR) to examine how six morphological, ecological, and human-activity factors influence land surface temperature (LST) in Kaifeng City. The results indicate three main findings. First, LST increased significantly from 1986 to 2024, while interannual variability declined, indicating a gradual reduction in regional thermal fluctuations. Second, NTL was consistently the dominant indicator across the five representative years, while BF and NTL together captured the effects of urban expansion and intensified human activity. Third, FAD coefficients were more spatially heterogeneous in urban fringe areas than in the urban core. In 2020, the dispersion of FAD coefficients in fringe areas was 2.74 times greater than that in the central area, indicating stronger spatial differentiation in ventilation-related morphological constraints during urban expansion. Although FAD made only a modest contribution to overall predictive accuracy, it provided supplementary diagnostic information not captured by conventional density indicators and showed nonlinear, directional, and spatially heterogeneous responses. Compared with previous studies that mainly examined short-term or single-dimensional relationships between urban morphology and LST, this study integrates building densification, ventilation-related morphological resistance, ecological conditions, and human activity intensity into a long-term LST-driver framework, providing evidence to support heat-risk management during urban regeneration and outward expansion.

### [147] [Lagged Response of Groundwater Storage to Extreme Precipitation Using Machine-Learning-Downscaled GRACE Data at the Watershed Scale](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132217)
*Xiaoling Zheng,Yilei Yu,Jiyi Jiang,Lihu Yang,Shiqin Wang*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本研究利用LightGBM模型降尺度GRACE数据，生成了2002-2024年白洋淀流域1km分辨率的地下水位异常（GWSA）数据集，分析了地下水的长期变化及其对极端降水事件的响应，发现地下水经历了快速消耗、缓慢下降和显著恢复三个阶段，且极端降水事件对地下水补给存在约两个月的滞后效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 评估含水层对气候变异的恢复力需要理解地下水储量如何响应极端降水，但目前缺乏高分辨率的地下水储量异常数据及其与极端降水事件关系的定量认识。

Method: 利用LightGBM模型将GRACE观测数据的空间分辨率降尺度至1km，生成白洋淀流域2002-2024年GWSA数据集；基于该产品分析长期地下水变化，并通过复合分析量化11次极端降水事件前后GWSA的响应特征。

Result: 降尺度GWSA与独立水文数据集（GLDAS、地下水位异常）一致性良好；地下水呈现三阶段变化：2014年前快速消耗（-1.35 cm/yr）、2014-2019年缓慢下降（-1.04 cm/yr）、2020年后显著恢复（+3.45 cm/yr）；空间上自西南向东北递增；极端降水事件后地下水响应存在约2个月滞后；月有效降水量比短期日极端降水与GWSA恢复更相关，平原地区响应强于山区。

Conclusion: 极端降水事件提供脉冲式补给，但持续的地下水恢复依赖于累积气候输入和人为水资源管理的影响。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：90%。该研究为遥感水文学经典范式，可从以下方面改进：(1) 引入多源遥感数据（如SMAP土壤水分、SWOT地表水体变化）作为LightGBM的辅助特征，提高降尺度精度；(2) 将方法迁移至其他水资源敏感区域（如华北平原、印度西北部），评估不同气候区地下水对极端降水的响应差异；(3) 结合InSAR地表形变数据交叉验证地下水储量变化，减少GRACE信号中地表水与土壤水分离的不确定性；(4) 利用深度学习替代LightGBM捕捉更复杂的非线性时空映射关系。

Abstract (英文): Understanding how groundwater storage responds to extreme precipitation is essential for assessing aquifer resilience under climate variability. In this study, we developed a 1 km groundwater storage anomaly (GWSA) dataset for the Baiyangdian Watershed from 2002 to 2024 by downscaling GRACE observations with a Light Gradient Boosting Machine (LightGBM) model. The downscaled GWSA showed good consistency with independent hydrological datasets, including GLDAS and groundwater-level anomalies. Based on the downscaled product, we characterized long-term groundwater changes and quantified GWSA responses to extreme precipitation events (EPEs). Groundwater storage exhibited three distinct phases: rapid depletion before 2014 (−1.35 cm/yr), a slower decline during 2014–2019 (−1.04 cm/yr), and marked recovery after 2020 (+3.45 cm/yr). Spatially, GWSA generally increased from the southwest to the northeast of the watershed. Composite analysis of 11 EPEs revealed a delayed groundwater response, with the strongest signal occurring approximately two months after precipitation. Monthly effective precipitation was more closely associated with GWSA recovery than short-duration daily precipitation extremes, and the response was stronger in plains than in mountainous areas. These findings indicate that EPEs provide episodic recharge pulses, while sustained groundwater recovery depends on cumulative climatic inputs and human water-management influences.

### [148] [SAGE: Saliency and Geometry Enhanced Transferable Attacks for LiDAR Point Cloud Perception in Remote Sensing](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132209)
*Yuheng Wu,Shiwei Lin,Shibo Ping,Xingchao Zhai,Zhiyuan Fang,Meijuan Chen,Weiquan Liu*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 提出SAGE框架，通过显著性图与几何约束增强LiDAR点云对抗攻击的可迁移性，在保持几何质量的同时提升攻击成功率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LiDAR点云可迁移攻击方法仅关注对代理模型具有区分性的区域，但不同架构间稳定性差，导致可迁移性有限且产生明显几何畸变。

Method: SAGE统一了点坐标先验与源模型梯度信号生成显著性图，作为脆弱局部结构的可迁移指示器；基于显著性图指导扰动分配，并施加显式几何约束，在增强可迁移性的同时保持点云几何质量。

Abstract (英文): LiDAR point clouds are widely used in remote sensing perception scenarios, such as autonomous driving. However, LiDAR-based perception models remain vulnerable to adversarial perturbations, which may compromise the reliability of safety-critical 3D perception systems. Among different attack paradigms, transfer-based attacks are particularly practical because they generate adversarial examples on accessible surrogate models and apply the generated examples directly to unknown target models. Nevertheless, existing transferable attacks on point clouds often perturb regions that are discriminative for the surrogate model but insufficiently stable across different architectures, leading to limited transferability and noticeable geometric distortion. To address this problem, we propose SAGE, a Saliency And Geometry Enhanced transferable attack framework for LiDAR point cloud perception in remote sensing. Specifically, SAGE unifies point-coordinate priors with source-model gradient signals to generate a saliency map, which serves as a transferable indicator of vulnerable local structures. SAGE further leverages this map through saliency-guided perturbation allocation and explicit geometric constraints to enhance transferability while preserving point-cloud geometry. To demonstrate the effectiveness of SAGE, we evaluate SAGE on point-cloud classification benchmarks and further validate it on LiDAR-based 3D object detection using KITTI and nuScenes. Experimental results show that SAGE consistently outperforms existing transferable attack methods in attack success rate while preserving favorable geometric quality of adversarial point clouds. These findings demonstrate that SAGE offers an effective and practical framework for assessing the transfer robustness of LiDAR-based remote sensing perception systems.

</details>


### [149] [Finding the Features with LiDAR and SAR: Automated Detection of Archaeological Earthworks at Cahokia](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132229)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1) 使用三种LiDAR数据集（两种无人机搭载传感器和一种载人飞机调查）生成数字地形模型(DTM)并转化为局部地形模型(LRM)；2) 应用K-means聚类分割LRM为特征类别；3) 利用OpenCV库进行等高线边界检测以勾勒土墩和取土坑；4) 处理PALSAR-3和Sentinel-1的SAR局部入射角(LIA)栅格，通过角度偏差映射识别与考古特征相关的坡度异常。

Conclusion: 尽管仍需人工审查以过滤现代干扰和自然误报，该集成工作流能显著加速考古勘探并减少解释主观性。方法具有可扩展性、站点无关性，且使用开放获取数据，适用于全球考古景观。

Abstract (英文): Archaeological feature detection at complex, mixed-environment sites requires accurate, efficient methods for identifying subtle morphological signatures. This study presents a semi-automated remote sensing pipeline for the detection and delineation of archaeological earthworks at Cahokia Mounds (Illinois, USA), a major Mississippian urban center and UNESCO World Heritage Site. Three LiDAR datasets, two collected via UAV-mounted sensors and one from a piloted aircraft survey, were processed into Digital Terrain Models and transformed into Local Relief Models (LRM). K-means clustering was applied to segment the LRMs into feature classes, followed by contour bounding using the OpenCV library to outline mounds and borrow pits. Additionally, SAR-derived Local Incidence Angle (LIA) rasters from PALSAR-3 and Sentinel-1 were processed through angular deviation mapping to identify slope anomalies associated with archaeological features. Results across all five datasets demonstrate the complementary strengths of LiDAR and SAR: LiDAR excels at resolving elevation-defined features such as mound footprints, while LIA captures directional slope behavior that highlights mound edges, borrow pit rims, and linear features such as causeways. Comparative analysis of LiDAR acquisition frequencies reveals minimal differences in archaeological feature recovery between pulse settings, suggesting that sensor platform choice matters more than power-density tradeoffs for this application. Despite the need for human review to filter modern disturbances and natural false positives, the integrated workflow meaningfully accelerates prospection and reduces interpretive subjectivity. The methods are scalable, site-invariant, and work with open-access data, making them applicable to archaeological landscapes worldwide.

### [150] [YOLO-DC: A Crop Detection and Counting Network for UAV-Based Agricultural Scenes](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132187)
*Haotian Bai,Lei Liu,Haocheng Kong,X Li,Du Y*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 针对无人机航拍作物图像中小尺度、密集分布、严重遮挡和复杂背景导致的检测精度低和计数误差大问题，本文提出基于改进YOLOv12的作物检测与计数模型YOLO-DC，通过引入LGCB-AM注意力机制和MS-DH多尺度检测头，在小麦和水稻数据集上实现了检测精度、计数误差和模型效率的优越平衡，并验证了跨作物迁移潜力。

Method: 基于YOLOv12进行改进，提出YOLO-DC模型：1）引入LGCB-AM（局部-全局上下文桥接注意力机制），增强局部纹理提取、全局建模和前景-背景对比度；2）设计MS-DH（多尺度检测头），提升密集小目标的边界感知能力；3）在边界分支和排斥分支上进行针对性设计以增强密集目标判别能力。

Abstract (英文): Crop targets in UAV aerial images are typically characterized by small scale, dense distribution, severe mutual occlusion, and complex backgrounds, which often lead to low detection accuracy and large counting errors for existing deep learning models. To address these issues, this study proposes an improved YOLOv12-based crop detection and counting model, named YOLO-DC. By introducing an attention mechanism (LGCB-AM) and a multi-scale detection head (MS-DH), the proposed model effectively enhances local texture extraction, global modeling, foreground–background contrast, and boundary perception for dense small objects. Subsequently, a series of comparative experiments, ablation studies, and transfer experiments were conducted on the wheat and rice datasets. The results show that YOLO-DC achieves a favorable balance among detection accuracy, counting error, and model efficiency and overall outperforms the other comparison models. Ablation studies further verify the effectiveness of the proposed design, showing that LGCB-AM is the key contributor to the performance improvement, while the boundary branch and repulsion branch play critical roles in dense-target discrimination. In addition, an appropriate module insertion strategy can effectively balance high-level semantic enhancement and feature fusion stability. Transfer experiments demonstrate that pretraining on the wheat dataset and fine-tuning on the rice dataset significantly outperform training from scratch, indicating strong cross-crop transfer potential. Overall, the proposed YOLO-DC provides an effective solution for high-precision crop detection and counting in agricultural scenarios.

### [152] [A Hybrid VRT-S-BR Method for Composite Electromagnetic Scattering from Targets Above Vegetated Rough Surfaces](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132183)
*Yu-Feng Zou,Shui‐Rong Chai,Xiao-Jie Qu,Jiajun Li,Kun Chao,Lixin Guo,Wei Liu*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出一种混合VRT-S-BR方法，用于预测植被覆盖粗糙表面上目标的复合电磁散射。通过将植被层建模为分层随机介质，利用VRT-S模型生成植被诱导的复反射系数数据库，替代BR射线追踪中传统的菲涅尔反射项，并引入面元依赖的相位补偿方案。在天然草地实测数据上验证，HH和VV极化的RMSE分别为1.82 dB和3.10 dB。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的混合电磁散射模型在描述植被覆盖地表上目标的复合散射时，通常采用经验性的随机相位扰动来近似植被效应，导致物理精度不足。本文旨在提出一种更精确、更具物理基础的混合方法，将植被层的辐射传输物理特性（衰减和相干散射）系统地纳入弹跳射线法框架中。

Method: (1) 将植被层建模为分层随机介质；(2) 利用矢量辐射传输射击法（VRT-S）在不同入射角下预计算植被诱导的复反射系数，构建离线数据库；(3) 在BR射线追踪过程中，用该系数逐次替代传统菲涅尔反射项；(4) 引入面元依赖的确定性相位补偿方案，替代经验性随机相位扰动。

Result: 在天然草地实测后向散射数据上验证，HH极化RMSE为1.82 dB，VV极化RMSE为3.10 dB。数值实验表明该方法能有效表征不同植被覆盖率、植被高度、地形背景及双站观测几何下的目标-植被耦合散射特性。

Conclusion: 所提出的VRT-S-BR混合方法能够更准确地预测植被覆盖地表上目标的复合电磁散射，相比基于经验随机相位扰动的传统混合模型具有更高的物理保真度和预测精度。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。改进方案：(1) 将该方法应用于星载/机载SAR森林区域隐蔽目标检测，利用极化分解技术增强目标-背景区分度；(2) 扩展VRT-S模型以支持多层植被结构（如林冠-灌木-草地分层），提升对复杂森林场景的建模能力；(3) 引入机器学习方法加速离线复反射系数数据库的构建与插值，实现实时或近实时的散射预测；(4) 结合全极化SAR数据，利用该模型反演植被参数（高度、含水量、覆盖度等），实现散射建模与参数反演的闭环优化。

Abstract (英文): This paper proposes a hybrid Vector Radiative Transfer Shooting (VRT-S)-Bouncing Ray (BR) method, referred to as the VRT-S-BR method, for predicting composite electromagnetic scattering from targets above vegetation-covered rough surfaces. In this proposed framework, the vegetation layer is modeled as a stratified random medium and incorporated into the BR solver through VRT-S-derived amplitude modulation and deterministic phase compensation. Specifically, an offline database of vegetation-induced complex reflection coefficients is first generated using the VRT-S model over a set of incidence angles. During the BR ray-tracing process, these coefficients are used to replace the conventional Fresnel reflection terms on a per-interaction basis, thereby accounting for vegetation-induced attenuation and coherent scattering effects. In addition, a facet-dependent phase compensation scheme is introduced to describe propagation-path variations of individual rays through the vegetation canopy, avoiding the empirical random phase perturbation used in previous hybrid models. The proposed method is validated against field-measured backscattering data over natural grassland, achieving root mean square height (RMSE) values of 1.82 dB and 3.10 dB for horizontal-horizontal (HH) and vertical-vertical (VV) polarizations, respectively. Numerical results further demonstrate the capability of the method to characterize target–vegetation coupled scattering under different percentages of vegetation cover, vegetation heights, terrain backgrounds, and bistatic observation geometries.

### [153] [Locally Adaptive Mamba and Multi-Scale Feature Enhancement for Optical Remote Sensing Image Change Detection](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132226)
*Mingxuan Ding,Qirong Zhou,Qiaolin Ye,Le Sun*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 提出LADENet框架，融合CNN、Transformer和Mamba范式，通过局部自适应Mamba模块、多尺度特征增强和双分支差异增强模块，解决遥感双时相变化检测中局部与全局特征协同建模不足、差异表示单一、跨尺度特征通信不畅等问题。在四个基准数据集上取得领先性能（LEVIR-CD: F1 91.06%, IoU 85.28%）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有遥感变化检测方法面临三大挑战：局部细节与全局特征难以协同建模、双时相差异构表征单一、跨尺度特征缺乏有效通信，导致模型在复杂环境下的精度和鲁棒性受限。

Method: 1) 权重共享的多层Transformer编码器+序列缩减机制生成多尺度全局特征；2) 基于状态空间扫描(SSS)的双时空自适应局部特征标记模块，含自适应扫描策略、跨时相状态空间扫描和滑动窗口边界校准；3) 双分支差异增强模块（注意力增强差异分支+多尺度卷积拼接分支）；4) 全局跨尺度空间特征融合解码器（空间注意力+二维选择性扫描）。

Result: LEVIR-CD: F1 91.06%, IoU 85.28%；WHU-CD: F1 90.51%, IoU 82.45%；CLCD-CD: F1 82.15%, IoU 72.83%；GVLM-CD: F1 89.12%, IoU 77.78%。

Conclusion: LADENet在多个复杂双时相观测环境中展现出优异的检测精度、边界描绘能力和泛化性能，显著优于现有前沿方法。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。该论文本身就是为遥感双时相变化检测设计的，以下为改进方向：1) 可引入多模态遥感数据（如SAR+光学）扩展输入通道，利用Mamba处理长序列优势融合异源特征；2) 滑动窗口边界校准机制可进一步结合条件随机场(CRF)进行边界后处理优化；3) 序列缩减机制可适配高光谱遥感数据的波段选择与降维；4) 状态空间扫描策略可扩展至三维遥感（如时序遥感影像）实现时序-空间联合建模。

Abstract (英文): Within the domain of Earth observation, tracking terrestrial transitions via high-resolution optical data plays a fundamental role. Nevertheless, current methods face critical challenges, including the difficulty in collaborative modeling of local details and global features and the singularity of bi-temporal difference representation, along with insufficient cross-scale feature communication, thereby constraining both the precision and resilience of models when applied to complicated environments. To solve these problems, we propose LADENet (Locally Adaptive Mamba and Multi-scale Feature Enhancement Network), an innovative framework that synergizes CNN, Transformer, and Mamba paradigms. By leveraging customized local contextual refinement alongside sophisticated hierarchical fusion, this integration delivers highly precise and resilient detection performance. LADENet adopts a weight-sharing multi-level Transformer encoder combined with a sequence reduction mechanism to generate multi-scale global features, achieving precise alignment of bi-temporal features and global context modeling while reducing computational complexity. To realize accurate localization and local enhancement of changed regions, we design a dual spatiotemporal adaptive local feature marking module based on State-Space Scanning (SSS). This module screens high-saliency changed regions through an adaptive scanning strategy, realizes pixel-aligned spatiotemporal feature fusion via cross-temporal state-space scanning, and introduces a sliding window boundary calibration mechanism to alleviate boundary information loss caused by window segmentation. To strengthen the feature representation of changed regions, a dual-branch difference enhancement module is constructed, which collaboratively captures global change trends and fine-grained local features through an attention-enhanced difference branch and a multi-scale convolution concatenation branch, effectively suppressing background interference. To address the semantic gap between cross-scale features, a global cross-scale spatial feature fusion decoder is proposed, which balances local detail preservation and global context perception through the synergy of spatial attention and two-dimensional selective scanning, completing refined multi-scale feature fusion and spatial resolution recovery. To rigorously validate the proposed LADENet, comprehensive experiments were conducted across four widely adopted bi-temporal benchmarks: LEVIR-CD, WHU-CD, CLCD-CD, and GVLM-CD. The presented architecture establishes substantial superiority over existing cutting-edge methodologies across primary evaluation criteria. Specifically, it yields an F1-measure of 91.06% alongside an IoU of 85.28% in the LEVIR-CD tests, while registering 90.51% (F1) and 82.45% (IoU) for WHU-CD. Similarly, robust outcomes are delivered on CLCD-CD (82.15% F1, 72.83% IoU) as well as GVLM-CD (89.12% F1, 77.78% IoU). These results demonstrate that LADENet possesses excellent detection accuracy, boundary delineation capability and generalization performance in diverse and intricate bi-temporal observation environments.

### [154] [Efficient Sea Clutter Suppression Algorithm Based on BCD-Accelerated Dictionary Learning and TQWT Denoising](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132201)
*Jin Wang,Yubing Han,Yancun Lyu*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出一种结合块坐标下降（BCD）加速字典学习与可调Q因子小波变换（TQWT）去噪的海杂波抑制方法，通过BCD替代全局SVD、自适应软阈值算子和批量自适应OMP算法，在IPIX等实测雷达数据上取得平均SCNR提升17.48 dB，执行时间仅7.99秒，显著优于传统K-SVD方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 复杂海况下弱目标检测面临非平稳海杂波和尖峰干扰，而传统字典学习杂波抑制算法计算复杂度高，难以兼顾抑制性能与实时性。

Method: 1) 使用块坐标下降（BCD）替代全局SVD进行字典学习，结合自适应软阈值算子实现字典原子和稀疏系数的低复杂度联合优化；2) 采用批量自适应OMP算法，预计算Gram矩阵并引入双停止机制，实现高效重构与杂波初步消除；3) 通过TQWT利用其窄带特征表示和平移不变性，滤除残差非平稳杂波和噪声。

Result: 在IPIX数据库和《雷达学报》公开数据集上，平均SCNR提升17.48 dB，总执行时间仅7.99秒，在抑制性能与计算效率之间取得了优异平衡。

Conclusion: 所提方法有效克服了传统K-SVD算法计算开销大的瓶颈，在复杂海况下实现了高效且稳定的海杂波抑制，为雷达弱目标检测提供了可行方案。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。该文方法可直接迁移至遥感海洋目标检测（如SAR图像中的舰船检测），将BCD加速字典学习与TQWT去噪用于SAR海面杂波抑制与弱目标增强。改进方向：1) 将TQWT替换为更适合遥感图像的多尺度变换（如Curvelet/Contourlet）以增强空间结构保持能力；2) 结合深度学习特征进行字典初始化，进一步提升字典表达能力；3) 针对SAR多极化数据扩展批处理自适应OMP支持多通道联合稀疏重构。

Abstract (英文): Detecting weak radar targets in complex sea conditions is inherently challenging due to non-stationary sea clutter and sea spikes. Furthermore, traditional dictionary learning algorithms for clutter suppression suffer from high computational complexity. To address these issues, this paper proposes an efficient sea clutter suppression method cascading Block Coordinate Descent (BCD)-accelerated dictionary learning with Tunable Q-factor Wavelet Transform (TQWT) denoising. During dictionary learning, a BCD strategy replaces global Singular Value Decomposition (SVD) with analytical optimization. Combined with an adaptive soft-thresholding operator, this enables low-complexity joint optimization of dictionary atoms and sparse coefficients, drastically reducing training time. Subsequently, a batch-adaptive Orthogonal Matching Pursuit (OMP) algorithm featuring Gram matrix precomputation and a dual-stop mechanism achieves efficient reconstruction and preliminary cancellation of clutter components. Finally, TQWT is applied to filter out residual non-stationary clutter and noise by leveraging its narrowband feature representation and shift invariance. Experiments on measured radar data from the IPIX database and datasets published by the Journal of Radars demonstrate that the proposed method significantly outperforms traditional K-SVD-based algorithms. Specifically, it improves the average signal-to-clutter-plus-noise ratio (SCNR) by 17.48 dB and requires a total execution time of only 7.99 s, achieving a highly favorable trade-off between suppression performance and computational efficiency.

### [155] [MCPF-Net: Multi-Stage LiDAR-Image Collaborative Perception Fusion Network for Point Cloud Semantic Segmentation of Urban Scenes](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132218)

Abstract (英文): Multimodal fusion unlocks the potential of point cloud semantic segmentation, thereby driving advancements in surface observation and visual perception tasks. Although light detection and ranging (LiDAR) systems capture precise 3D structural geometry and optical images provide rich semantic and textural information, existing fusion methods struggle with limited cross-modal perception and insufficient information complementarity. To address these limitations, we propose a multi-stage LiDAR-image collaborative perception fusion network (MCPFNet) for point cloud semantic segmentation of urban scenes. At the middle fusion stage, the network incorporates an elevation-guided geometric-aware fusion module and a semantic-aware cross-attention fusion module to enable bidirectional feature injection between LiDAR and image modalities. In the late fusion stage, a bidirectional adaptive fusion module further refines semantic representations through gated weighting and bidirectional cross-attention mechanisms. Extensive experiments on three multimodal datasets with different resolutions, i.e., ISPRS Vaihingen, N3C-California, and UAVScenes, demonstrate that MCPFNet outperforms existing fusion methods, achieving mIoUs of 74.51%, 95.15%, and 62.76%, respectively. Hence, our multi-stage fusion and bidirectional interaction strategy is more reliable and accurate than existing methods in performing segmentation across diverse and complex urban scenes.

### [156] [Total Ozone Column Changes over Northeast China: Trends and Variability Analysis](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132189)
*Yu Shi,O. Evtushevsky,Gennadi Milinevsky*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 基于MSR-2和ERA5数据集，分析了2015-2024年中国东北地区(40-53°N, 115-135°E)月平均臭氧总量(TOC)的变化，并结合龙凤山站地基观测数据，研究了TOC的季节性特征及其与臭氧浓度和温度的关联，发现东北地区TOC年均值比纬向均值高25 DU(7.4%)，且与地表臭氧浓度呈强正相关(|r|=0.8-0.9)，与地表温度呈强负相关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索中国东北地区TOC的区域季节性变化规律，以及TOC与平流层和对流层臭氧浓度、空气温度之间的关系，填补该区域TOC长期变化研究的空白。

Method: 使用MSR-2和ERA5再分析数据集分析2015-2024年月平均TOC时空变化；利用龙凤山站WMO/GAW地基观测数据进行验证；通过相关性分析研究TOC与臭氧浓度和温度的关系；结合Brewer-Dobson环流、准定常波和东北冷涡进行机制讨论。

Result: TOC无显著线性趋势；年均TOC超纬向均值25 DU(7.4%)；年最大值在2月、最小值在8月，分别比北半球中纬度早1-2个月；TOC从东北(~415 DU)向西南(~330 DU)递减；TOC与地表臭氧浓度强正相关、与地表温度强负相关(|r|=0.8-0.9)；龙凤山站与MSR-2数据吻合良好(偏差±15 DU)。

Conclusion: 中国东北地区TOC呈现独特的季节性和空间分布特征，与纬向均值存在显著差异；地面观测数据能可靠代表区域TOC变化；Brewer-Dobson环流、准定常波和东北冷涡是影响TOC模式的重要因素；研究成果可用于东亚臭氧观测、TOC变率和平流层-对流层耦合分析。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。改进方案：1) 可引入国产风云系列卫星(FY-3/4)的臭氧总量反演数据与MSR-2进行多源遥感融合，提高区域TOC反演精度；2) 利用高分五号(GF-5)大气环境监测卫星的痕量气体传感器数据，获取更高空间分辨率的O3廓线信息，提升对东北地区TOC空间异质性的刻画能力；3) 结合CALIPSO或国产激光雷达卫星的平流层气溶胶数据，研究气溶胶-臭氧相互作用对TOC的间接影响；4) 利用静止轨道卫星(如FY-4A)的高时间分辨率数据，研究TOC日变化与东北冷涡等天气系统的短时耦合机制。

Abstract (英文): Based on the Multi-Sensor Reanalysis Version 2 (MSR-2) and ERA5 datasets, variations in monthly mean total ozone column (TOC) over Northeast China (40–53°N, 115–135°E) from 2015 to 2024 are analyzed. Local ground-based observations at the regional WMO/GAW Longfengshan Station are also used. The aim is to investigate regional seasonality in TOC pattern and the relationship between TOC and ozone concentration and air temperature in the stratosphere and at the surface. No statistically significant linear trend was found for TOC; however, the annual mean TOC in the study region exceeds the zonal mean TOC by 25 DU (7.4%), and the annual maximum in February and minimum in August are observed one and two months earlier, respectively, than in the Northern Hemisphere mid-latitudes. A climatological decrease in TOC from the northeastern (~415 DU) to southwestern (~330 DU) parts of Northeast China was found. We also found a strong correlation, approaching |r| = 0.8–0.9, between TOC and ozone concentration (positive) and temperature (negative) at the surface. The time series from Longfengshan Station for 2015–2022 closely match the MSR-2 data averaged over Northeast China: the monthly mean difference varies within ±15 DU (±4.2%), validating the reliability of the station data as a representative proxy for regional TOC variability. The role of the Brewer–Dobson circulation, quasi-stationary waves, and the Northeast China cold vortex in the detected patterns and quantitative associations of TOC is discussed. The findings of this work can be applied to analyze the ozone observations, TOC variability, and stratosphere–troposphere coupling in East Asia.

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文分析了1985-2024年中国三大城市群（京津冀、长三角、粤港澳大湾区）的不透水面面积时空动态，并利用位置中心性指数（LCI）研究了五个特大城市（北京、上海、广州、深圳、天津）的扩张结构和模式。结果显示三大城市群ISA从22,544.10 km²增至69,348.59 km²，扩张速率和强度呈减速趋势，但各城市群达峰阶段不同；城市尺度上，邻接扩张已成为主导增长类型（超过50%）。

Method: 采用不透水面扩张指标揭示ISA时空动态，并应用位置中心性指数（LCI）研究五个特大城市的扩张结构和模式。

Abstract (英文): Analyzing the impervious surface area (ISA) of China’s three major urban agglomerations and expansion pattern of representative cities is of great significance for formulating context-specific urban planning policies and enhancing the resilience of urban development. This research employs impervious surface expansion indicators to reveal the spatiotemporal dynamics of impervious surface area, and further applies the location centrality index (LCI) to investigate the expansion structures and patterns of five megacities. The results indicate that the ISA of China’s three major urban agglomerations expanded from 22,544.10 km2 to 69,348.59 km2 from 1985 to 2024; both the expansion rate and intensity have exhibited a distinct decelerating trend. However, significant regional variation exists in the peak expansion phases: the Guangdong–Hong Kong–Macao Greater Bay Area Urban Agglomeration (GBA) peaked during the Initial Exploratory Phase (1985–1995), whereas the Yangtze River Delta Urban Agglomeration (YRD) and Beijing–Tianjin–Hebei Urban Agglomeration (BTH) reached their peaks during the High-speed Development Phase (2005–2015). At the urban scale, LCI-based analysis of urban expansion across five megacities reveals that adjacency expansion type has become the predominant form of growth, exceeding 50% in most cities. These findings enhance our understanding of evolutionary trajectories of ISA within urban agglomerations and the expansion patterns of five megacities, providing a scientific basis for sustainable urban planning and urban resilience.

### [158] [MSIA-YOLO: A Multi-Scale Semantic Interaction and Alignment Network for Small Object Detection in Low-Altitude UAV Remote Sensing Images](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132210)
*Wen Zhang,Xiaorong Xue,Bingyan Lu,Yishuo Tian,Jingtong Yang,Xin Zhao,W X Wang*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: MSIA-YOLO是一种基于YOLOv11的小目标检测器，通过多尺度语义交互与对齐（特征建模、高分辨率语义补偿、任务协同对齐）来增强小目标检测能力。在VisDrone、TinyPerson和RSOD数据集上，mAP50分别提升7.7%、10.3%和1.0%，优于多种先进检测器。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1) 在骨干网络中集成感受野注意力卷积(RFAConv)增强边缘和纹理等局部细节；2) 构建CHSP-P2小目标检测框架，增加P2分支并通过尺度序列融合机制实现跨尺度混合输入的高分辨率语义补偿；3) 设计DTIA-Head（动态任务交互与对齐头），通过动态任务交互和空间对齐促进分类与定位的联合优化。

Abstract (英文): Small object detection is fundamentally constrained by the lack of discriminative fine-grained features. Although introducing higher resolution detection scales can improve performance, it also amplifies background noise. In addition, the independently decoupled design of conventional detection heads is insufficient to address the persistent challenges of missed detections and false positives for small objects. To this end, we propose MSIA-YOLO, a YOLOv11-based detector with multi-scale semantic interaction and alignment, optimized from three complementary perspectives: feature modeling, high resolution semantic compensation, and task coordinated alignment. First, Receptive Field Attention Convolution (RFAConv) is integrated into the backbone to enhance critical local details, such as edge and texture cues, via receptive field aware attention. Second, to alleviate fine detail attenuation caused by repeated downsampling, we construct a CHSP-P2 small object detection framework with an additional P2 branch. A scale sequence fusion mechanism is further introduced to perform high resolution semantic compensation through cross scale hybrid inputs. Finally, we design a DTIA-Head (Dynamic Task Interaction and Alignment Head), which promotes joint optimization of classification and localization through dynamic task interaction and spatial alignment. Extensive experiments on the public datasets VisDrone, TinyPerson, and RSOD show that, compared with the YOLOv11n baseline, MSIA-YOLO improves mAP50 by 7.7%, 10.3%, and 1.0%, respectively, while also outperforming several advanced detectors. These results demonstrate the effectiveness and generalization capability of the proposed method in small object, dense object, and complex scene object detection scenarios.

Abstract (英文): The BepiColombo spacecraft, designed by ESA and JAXA, is currently in its cruise phase toward Mercury. Leveraging precise measurements from this state-of-the-art radio tracking system, MORE is expected to provide new insights into Mercury’s interior, refining and expanding upon the findings of the MESSENGER mission. This work evaluates the performance of MORE’s gravity and rotation experiment, specifically assessing how BepiColombo’s improved radio tracking data can reduce uncertainties in the determination of Mercury’s gravity field, Love number k2, and rotational state. Differently from previous covariance analyses, this work includes errors in the dynamical model to assess the experiment’s performance under controlled mismodeling conditions. ### [160] [Realistic Error Budget and Cross-Validation of Sentinel-1 3D Displacement for the 2025 Dingri Earthquake](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132252)
*Zhangdi Xie*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本研究系统量化了2025年定日地震（Mw 7.1）双轨道InSAR三维形变场的不确定性，基于Sentinel-1升降轨数据通过最小二乘反演构建三维同震位移场。结果表明该地震为南北走向正断层破裂，垂直分量最大沉降-403.3 mm、最大抬升+621.1 mm，东西分量最大向西-592.3 mm、向东+332.1 mm。不确定性分析显示形式误差（1σ: 垂直1.09 mm, 东西1.38 mm）严重低估真实精度，蒙特卡洛模拟给出的实际误差约13.8 mm（垂直）和17.2 mm（东西），系统误差贡献远大于随机噪声。交叉验证进一步支持该评估（升降轨LOS位移R分别为0.88和0.62；三维分量中垂直R=0.88，东西R=0.59），差异主要源于东西分量对处理策略和观测几何更敏感。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 双轨道InSAR三维形变反演中，传统形式误差传播方法通常假设随机噪声主导，但实际应用中系统误差（如轨道误差、大气延迟、解缠误差等）影响显著，导致不确定性被严重低估。目前缺乏针对双轨道InSAR三维反演不确定性的系统性量化分析，特别是对比形式误差与真实误差差异的研究，这限制了InSAR结果的可靠性评估和科学解释的置信度。

Method: 利用Sentinel-1升轨和降轨数据，采用最小二乘反演构建三维同震位移场。不确定性分析分两步：(1) 形式误差传播，基于观测误差协方差矩阵通过误差传播定律计算理论1σ不确定度；(2) 蒙特卡洛模拟，对输入数据进行扰动以评估实际误差水平。此外，通过独立Sentinel-1处理链进行交叉验证（计算相关系数R），并对比形式误差与实际误差的差异，分析系统误差与随机噪声的相对贡献。

Result: 形式误差传播给出垂直和东西分量的1σ不确定性分别为1.09 mm和1.38 mm；蒙特卡洛模拟显示实际误差约为13.8 mm（垂直）和17.2 mm（东西），比形式误差高一个数量级。系统误差贡献远超过随机噪声。交叉验证中，升降轨LOS位移相关系数R分别为0.88和0.62；三维分量中垂直分量R=0.88，东西分量R=0.59，东西分量一致性较差。

Conclusion: 形式误差传播严重低估了双轨道InSAR三维反演的实际不确定性；系统误差是误差的主要来源，其贡献远大于随机噪声。东西分量因对处理策略和观测几何更敏感，其不确定性更大且交叉验证一致性更差。研究强调在InSAR应用中应重视系统误差的影响，采用更可靠的误差评估方法（如蒙特卡洛模拟）以提高结果的可信度。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：90%。改进方案：(1) 将蒙特卡洛误差评估框架引入其他InSAR应用（如形变时间序列分析、地壳应变监测），替代传统形式误差传播；(2) 针对东西分量敏感性高的问题，可融合更多轨道方向（如ALOS-2、SAOCOM等不同入射角数据）或联合GPS/GNSS观测来约束三维反演；(3) 在系统误差建模中引入深度学习或经验正交函数分解方法，分离大气、轨道等系统误差成分，提高不确定性估计的准确性；(4) 将该不确定性量化方法推广到多轨道InSAR（≥3轨道）三维形变反演，评估不同轨道配置下的误差特性。

Abstract (英文): This study presents a systematic uncertainty quantification of the two-track InSAR three-dimensional (3D) deformation field of the 2025 Dingri earthquake (Mw 7.1). Using Sentinel-1 ascending and descending track data, a 3D coseismic displacement field was constructed via least-squares inversion. The results revealed that the earthquake produced a north–south-striking normal fault rupture, with the vertical component reaching a maximum subsidence of −403.3 mm and a maximum uplift of +621.1 mm, and the east–west component reaching a maximum westward displacement of −592.3 mm and an eastward displacement of +332.1 mm. Uncertainty analysis reveals a divergence between formal errors and actual accuracy: formal error propagation yields 1σ uncertainties of 1.09 mm and 1.38 mm for the vertical and east–west components, respectively; a realistic error budget based on Monte Carlo simulations indicates that the actual errors are approximately 13.8 mm for the vertical component and 17.2 mm for the east–west component, with systematic error contributions far exceeding random noise. Cross-validation against an independent Sentinel-1 processing chain supports the above error assessment: the correlation coefficient R for ascending track line-of-sight (LOS) displacement is 0.88, whereas it is 0.62 for the descending track; for the three-dimensional components, R reaches 0.88 for the vertical component and 0.59 for the east–west component, with discrepancies arising primarily from the greater sensitivity of the east–west component to processing strategies and observation geometry. This study demonstrates that formal error propagation underestimates the actual uncertainty of two-track InSAR inversion and that systematic error sources contribute far more than random noise does.

</details>


### [161] [Physically Consistent SAR Image Generation for Unseen Aspect Angles via Attributed Scattering Center Evolution](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132247)
*Zihao Jiang,Chao Liu,Zhangzeyu Xing,Yamei Wang,Shuwen Xiao*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 针对SAR目标图像在未见方位角下的数据稀缺问题，本文提出了一种物理一致性框架，利用ASC启发的稀疏散射结构先验引导生成器合成结构合理的散射布局，并采用双一致性方案联合约束目标区域散射一致性和背景区域统计一致性，在未见角度插值与留出实验下显著优于基线方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: SAR目标图像对方位角高度敏感，实际数据采集通常仅提供有限视角下的稀疏观测，导致在未见方位角下数据严重匮乏。现有生成方法要么未充分利用散射结构线索，要么在角度条件化时无法同时保持目标散射响应变化和背景斑点统计的真实性。

Method: 提出ASC启发的稀疏散射结构先验作为可微分的角度感知结构代理，近似SAR图像平面中的主要散射响应；设计双一致性方案，联合约束目标区域散射一致性与背景区域统计一致性。

Result: 在严格的未见角度插值与留出协议下，所提方法在图像保真度、目标区域散射一致性、背景统计一致性及角度条件一致性上均优于代表性基线方法。

Conclusion: ASC启发的稀疏散射结构先验在物理一致的SAR视角补全中发挥关键作用，验证了引入物理先验引导生成的有效性。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。该文本身就是遥感（SAR）领域的论文。改进方向：(1) 将ASC稀疏散射先验扩展到极化SAR（PolSAR）多通道场景；(2) 结合时域或干涉信息（如InSAR）进一步提升角度外推的物理真实性；(3) 探索更高效的稀疏先验表示（如基于学习的散射中心参数化）以降低计算开销；(4) 将框架推广到SAR视频或时序图像中的多视角补全任务。

Abstract (英文): Synthetic aperture radar (SAR) target images are highly sensitive to aspect angle, while practical data acquisition usually provides only sparse observations over limited viewpoints. This leads to severe data scarcity at unseen aspect angles and makes cross-angle generation prone to scattering-structure distortion and background statistical mismatch. Existing SAR image generation methods either focus on distribution matching without sufficiently exploiting scattering-related structural cues, or emphasize angle conditioning while failing to jointly preserve physically plausible dominant scattering-response variations and realistic background speckle statistics at unseen aspect angles. To address this issue, we propose a physically consistent framework for SAR image generation at unseen aspect angles. The proposed method introduces an ASC-inspired sparse scattering-structure prior to approximate the dominant scattering responses in the SAR image plane. Rather than performing full parametric ASC inversion, this prior serves as a differentiable and angle-aware structural proxy that guides the generator toward synthesizing SAR images with structurally plausible scattering layouts. In addition, a dual-consistency scheme is introduced to jointly enforce target-region scattering consistency and background-region statistical consistency, thereby improving the physical realism of the generated results in both the target and background regions. Extensive experiments under strict unseen-angle interpolation and hold-out protocols demonstrate that the proposed method consistently outperforms representative baselines in image fidelity, target-region scattering consistency, background statistical consistency, and angle-conditioned consistency. Further visualization and ablation studies verify the critical role of the ASC-inspired sparse scattering-structure prior in physically consistent SAR view completion.

### [162] [Mapping Evapotranspiration Patterns in the Desert-Oasis Ecotone Using UAV-Based Thermal Infrared Imagery with a Three-Temperature Model](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132242)
*Siying Li,Yuhua Xing,Dapeng Zhang,Pei Wang*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本研究通过将无人机热红外遥感与三温度（3T）模型耦合，在河西走廊荒漠-绿洲过渡带实现了米级尺度的蒸散发（ET）高分辨率估算。结果表明该框架有效捕捉了从农田到沙漠的ET空间梯度，与SEBAL模型空间验证R²达0.90-0.95，与双源模型点尺度验证MAE为0.38 mm d⁻¹，为干旱区生态水文监测提供了可行技术方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 荒漠-绿洲交错带蒸散发估算面临气象观测稀疏与卫星遥感空间分辨率粗的两大瓶颈，难以解析高度异质性的地表过程，亟需发展高分辨率ET估算方法。

Method: 将无人机搭载的热红外传感器获取的米级地表温度（LST）数据，结合气象与植被数据，驱动三温度（3T）模型生成高分辨率ET图。空间尺度上以SEBAL模型为基准进行分层像素对比验证，点尺度上与双源模型对比验证。

Result: （1）3T模型成功捕捉从农田（3-10.69 mm d⁻¹）、防护林带（3-6 mm d⁻¹）到沙漠（<3 mm d⁻¹）的ET梯度；（2）与SEBAL模型空间验证R²=0.90-0.95，RMSE=0.22-0.43 mm d⁻¹，农田精度最高（R²=0.92，RMSE=0.24 mm d⁻¹）；（3）与双源模型点验证MAE=0.38 mm d⁻¹。

Conclusion: 无人机热红外数据与3T模型结合能有效模拟复杂生态过渡带的高分辨率ET，为干旱区生态水文监测与水资源评估提供了有前景的技术途径。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。该框架已是遥感与生态水文交叉的典型成功案例。改进方向：（1）将3T模型中的经验参数（如空气动力学阻抗）替换为物理模型或深度学习估计，减少对地面气象数据的依赖；（2）将无人机局部高分辨率结果与卫星（如Landsat/Sentinel-2）大范围数据融合，实现时空尺度扩展；（3）引入时序模型（如LSTM）处理多时相无人机数据，提升连续监测能力。

Abstract (英文): Evapotranspiration (ET) estimation in desert-oasis ecotones remains challenging due to sparse meteorological observations and the coarse spatial resolution of satellite remote sensing, which limit the ability to resolve highly heterogeneous surface conditions. To address this issue, this study develops a high-resolution ET estimation framework by integrating unmanned aerial vehicle (UAV)-based thermal infrared remote sensing with a three-temperature (3T) model in the Hexi Corridor. UAV-derived land surface temperature (LST) at meter-scale resolution, together with meteorological and vegetation data, was used to drive the model and generate high-resolution ET maps. The model’s performance was validated spatially against the Surface Energy Balance Algorithm for Land (SEBAL) model and at the point-scale against a two-source model. The results show that: (1) The 3T model effectively captured the spatial gradient of decreasing ET from cropland (3–10.69 mm d−1), through shelterbelts (3–6 mm d−1), to desert areas (&lt;3 mm d−1). (2) Spatial validation against the SEBAL model was conducted using stratified pixel-wise comparisons across four land-cover types over 14 UAV transects, showing strong agreement (R2 = 0.90–0.95; RMSE = 0.22–0.43 mm d−1). The model achieved highest accuracy in cropland (R2 = 0.92; RMSE = 0.24 mm d−1), with slight overestimation in shelterbelts. (3) Point-scale validation against the two-source model yielded an MAE of 0.38 mm d−1. This study demonstrates the effectiveness of combining UAV thermal infrared data with the 3T model for high-resolution ET simulation in complex ecological transition zones, offering a promising technical approach for ecohydrological monitoring and water resource assessment in arid regions.

### [163] [Multi-Scale Assessment of Nighttime Heat Health Risk and Dominant Factors Using MODIS and SDGSAT-1 Observations](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132243)
*Zhuang Tan,Qixia Man,Baolei Zhang,Pinliang Dong,Haiying Sun,Zhongchang Sun,Linlin Lu,Changyong Dou,Xiaomin Yang,Changyin Han,Cong Zhou,Xia Sun,Yi-Xiang Wang,Z G Li*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本研究构建了基于“危害-暴露-脆弱性”框架的多尺度夜间高温健康风险评估体系，以山东省为例，结合宏尺度（MODIS 1 km）和细尺度（SDGSAT-1 30 m）数据，识别了高风险集群及其主导因素，发现紧凑高层/中层建筑区（LCZ 1-2）多因素主导风险，而开放低层/稀疏建成区（LCZ 6/9）无主导因素。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
