Method: 采用“危害-暴露-脆弱性”框架，宏尺度使用MODIS夜间地表温度（1 km）和区级社会经济统计数据；细尺度使用SDGSAT-1热红外数据（30 m）和街区级社会经济与基础设施数据；通过热点分析识别高风险集群，并在LCZ框架下识别各空间单元的主导风险因素。

Result: （1）宏尺度上，高风险区集中在鲁南和主要城市核心区；（2）细尺度上，内陆城市整体风险高于沿海城市；（3）高风险等级伴随更复杂的主导因素配置；（4）LCZ 1-2以多主导因素为主，LCZ 6/9以无主导因素为主。

Conclusion: 本研究提供了高温风险治理的多层级视角，为宏尺度政策制定和细尺度干预提供了科学依据，有助于建设更具韧性和可持续性的城市。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。本文本身就是遥感在高温健康风险评估中的典型应用。改进方向：（1）可引入国产高分多光谱数据（如高分一号、资源三号）辅助LCZ分类，提升土地利用分类精度；（2）结合InSAR地表形变监测数据，评估热膨胀与地表沉降的耦合风险；（3）可融合GOCI静止轨道卫星数据实现逐小时热风险动态监测；（4）利用遥感反演的植被覆盖度（如NDVI/植被覆盖度）和地表反照率进一步优化暴露-脆弱性评估模型。

Abstract (英文): Climate change is amplifying heat-related health risks, making heat health risk assessment increasingly important for sustainable urban development. However, current studies still face three challenges: (1) macro-scale and fine-scale assessments remain weakly linked; (2) nighttime heat health risk has received limited attention; and (3) dominant factor identification remains insufficient, especially within the Local Climate Zone (LCZ) framework. To address these gaps, this study developed a hazard–exposure–vulnerability-based, multi-scale framework for assessing nighttime heat health risk in Shandong Province, China. At the macro scale, MODIS nighttime land surface temperature (1 km) was used to characterize heat hazard, and district-level risk was assessed by integrating socio-statistical data. Hotspot analysis was then applied to identify high-risk clusters and select cities for fine-scale assessment. At the fine scale, SDGSAT-1 thermal infrared data (30 m) were used to characterize intra-urban nighttime heat hazard, and block-level risk was assessed by integrating socioeconomic and urban infrastructure data. Dominant risk factors were further identified for each spatial unit. Results show that (1) at the macro scale, high nighttime heat health risk districts are concentrated mainly in southern Shandong and major urban cores; (2) at the fine scale, overall risk is higher in inland cities than in the coastal city, and the inland cities show similar spatial patterns; (3) at both district and block units, higher risk levels are associated with more complex dominant factor configurations; and (4) compact high- and mid-rise zones (LCZ 1–2) are mainly characterized by multiple dominant factors, whereas open low-rise/sparsely built zones (LCZ 6/9) are mainly characterized by no dominant factor. This study provides a multi-level perspective for heat-risk governance, offers a scientific basis for both macro-scale policy formulation and fine-scale intervention, and contributes to more sustainable and resilient cities.

### [164] [Estimation of High-Resolution Multi-Layer Soil Moisture Using Land Data Assimilation and the Three-Cornered Hat Method](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132248)
*Xinlei He,Wenbin Zhu,Shaomin Liu,Tongren Xu,Zhitao Wu,Sayed M. Bateni,Zhen Hao,Xiang Li,Dongxin Wu,Hanxue Liang*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本研究通过融合多源遥感数据（SMAP、HJ-2、Sentinel-2、Gaofen-6）和ESTARFM算法生成16米分辨率的高分辨率土壤湿度（HRSM）数据集，并采用集合卡尔曼滤波（EnKF）框架将HRSM同化到Noah-MP陆面模型中，利用三帽法（TCH）估计的相对不确定性优化观测误差和卡尔曼增益，最终实现16米分辨率的土壤湿度廓线估计。在云南中部春旱期验证表明，该方法相比同化SMAP数据能显著提升表层和根区土壤湿度估计精度，提供更高分辨率的空间特征和异质性，且与PDSI干旱指数吻合良好。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 土壤湿度在陆地能量-水交换和农业生产中至关重要，但现有遥感土壤湿度产品空间分辨率较低（如SMAP约9-36公里），难以满足精细农业和干旱监测需求，亟需发展高分辨率土壤湿度同化方法。

Method: 1) 利用ESTARFM融合SMAP、HJ-2、Sentinel-2和Gaofen-6数据生成16米HRSM；2) 采用三帽法（TCH）估算HRSM相对不确定性；3) 在EnKF框架内将HRSM及其不确定性同化到Noah-MP模型，更新观测误差和卡尔曼增益；4) 在云南中部春旱期用实测数据验证。

Result: 1) DA_HRSM显著改善Noah-MP模型的表层和根区土壤湿度估计；2) DA_HRSM模拟的土壤湿度相对不确定性更低；3) 相比同化SMAP数据，DA_HRSM提供更高分辨率的空间特征，增强20个灌区的空间异质性；4) DA_HRSM有效捕捉云南中部春旱，与PDSI指数吻合良好。

Conclusion: 将高分辨率土壤湿度数据（16米）同化到陆面模型中的方法在农业和干旱监测系统中具有显著优势，能提供更精细的土壤湿度空间分布信息，提升干旱监测能力。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。改进方向：1) 可引入国产高分系列（如GF-5高光谱）或雷达数据（如Sentinel-1）替代或补充光学数据，克服云雨天气对ESTARFM融合的影响；2) TCH方法可扩展为多源不确定性贝叶斯融合框架，进一步提升观测误差表征精度；3) EnKF同化可考虑结合深度学习方法（如LSTM）进行状态参数联合估计，提升非线性和非高斯条件下的同化性能；4) 可推广至中国主要农业区和干旱频发区，构建区域高分辨率土壤湿度业务化监测系统。

Abstract (英文): Soil moisture (SM) plays a pivotal role in regulating terrestrial energy-water exchanges and exerts substantial influence on agricultural productivity. In this study, a high-resolution soil moisture (HRSM) dataset (16 m) was generated by integrating multi-source remote sensing data from SMAP, HJ-2, Sentinel-2, and Gaofen-6, together with the Enhanced Spatial and Temporal Adaptive Reflectance Fusion Model. The data assimilation (DA) method was implemented for assimilating HRSM within the Ensemble Kalman Filter (EnKF) framework using the Noah-MP model at a spatial resolution of 1 km. To enhance the spatial detail of SM, HRSM and its relative uncertainties derived from the three-cornered hat (TCH) method were used to update the observation error and Kalman gain in the EnKF framework, thereby improving SM profile estimates at a 16 m resolution. The performance of the DA method was evaluated against in situ measurements during the spring drought period in central Yunnan Province, China. The results show that assimilating HRSM (DA_HRSM) significantly improves surface and root-zone SM estimates in the Noah-MP model. The simulated SM from the DA_HRSM method demonstrates lower relative uncertainty. Compared to the assimilation of SMAP SM, the DA_HRSM method provides higher-resolution spatial features of SM and enhances spatial heterogeneity across 20 irrigation districts. The DA_HRSM method effectively captured the spring drought in central Yunnan, demonstrating good agreement with the Palmer Drought Severity Index (PDSI). The result highlights the advantages of incorporating high-resolution SM data into agricultural and drought monitoring systems.

### [165] [Reconstruction of Land Surface Temperature Based on EATC Constraints and Spatially Adaptive Residual Correction: A Case Study of the Qinghai–Tibet Engineering Corridor](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132254)
*Minghan Xu,Qian Li,Shufang Tian,Shiqi Kuang,Tianqi Li*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 针对青藏高原等复杂地形中卫星LST数据因云覆盖导致缺失的问题，提出物理约束空间残差学习框架（PCSRL），结合增强年温度循环（EATC）模型捕捉时间基线，并利用地理XGBoost（G-XGBoost）建模空间非线性残差，在模拟云掩膜测试中达到R²=0.88、RMSE=1.92K的精度，优于传统物理模型和全局机器学习方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 卫星LST产品在青藏高原等复杂地形中受云和大气影响导致数据大量缺失，现有时空插值方法在大范围缺失下精度有限，物理模型因气象输入不足而受限，数据驱动方法又忽略局部空间变化导致热模式平滑和系统误差，亟需一种高精度、保留空间细节的LST重建方法。

Method: 提出物理约束空间残差学习框架（PCSRL）：1）利用增强年温度循环（EATC）模型捕获LST时间基线；2）将多源辅助数据集成到地理XGBoost（G-XGBoost）算法中建模空间非线性残差，通过自适应局部带宽和权重调整减少边界伪影并恢复复杂地形的热空间模式。

Result: 在青藏工程走廊2017年MODIS LST数据集模拟云掩膜上验证：R²=0.88，RMSE=1.92K，平均偏差0.07K；季节性评估冬季表现最佳（RMSE=1.19K），夏季表现稳健；有效减少边界伪影，准确再现复杂地形热空间模式。

Conclusion: 该框架为异质高寒地表上的高精度LST重建提供了可靠方法，通过物理模型与空间机器学习相结合的方式，在精度和空间细节恢复上均优于单一物理模型和全局机器学习模型。

Abstract (英文): Satellite-based land surface temperature (LST) products are frequently affected by cloud cover and atmospheric conditions, resulting in missing data that significantly limits the continuous monitoring of the thermal environment in complex terrains, such as the Tibetan Plateau. Existing spatiotemporal interpolation methods face clear accuracy limitations when addressing extensive data gaps, while physical models often struggle due to insufficient meteorological inputs in complex landscapes. Moreover, conventional data-driven approaches usually overlook local spatial variations, resulting in smoothed thermal patterns and systematic errors. To overcome these issues, we propose a Physically Constrained Spatial Residual Learning framework. In this framework, we use the Enhanced Annual Temperature Cycle (EATC) model to capture the temporal baseline of LST first. Then, we integrate multi-source auxiliary data into the Geographical-XGBoost (G-XGBoost) algorithm to model spatial nonlinear residuals. Using simulated cloud masks on the 2017 MODIS LST dataset from the Qinghai–Tibet Engineering Corridor, we show that the hybrid model outperforms both individual physical models and global machine learning models in accuracy and spatial detail recovery. Validation results yield an R2 of 0.88, an RMSE of 1.92 K, and a mean bias of 0.07 K. Seasonal evaluations indicate best performance in winter (RMSE = 1.19 K) with robust performance in summer. Furthermore, the framework reduces boundary artifacts and accurately reproduces thermal spatial patterns in complex terrain through adaptive local bandwidth and weight adjustments. This approach provides a reliable method for high-precision LST reconstruction over heterogeneous alpine surfaces.

### [166] [Filling Satellite Microwave Observation Gaps via Generative Synthesis](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132256)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 极轨微波辐射计虽能提供全天候大气状态测量，但重访间隔长达数小时，在快速演变的天气事件中存在关键观测缺口，亟需一种能从高时间分辨率红外观测中重建微波亮温场的方法。

Method: 基于扩散概率模型（Denoising Diffusion Probabilistic Model, DDPM）的MIDAS框架，以10分钟间隔的地球静止卫星红外观测为条件，生成对应时刻的微波亮温场；通过合并采样机制（merge-sampling）将实时极轨观测作为物理约束融入生成过程，实现观测约束下的概率推断。

Conclusion: 生成模型（扩散模型）能有效从高时间分辨率红外观测中重建物理合理的微波湿度场，弥合极轨微波观测的时空覆盖缺口，为数值天气预报提供可同化的高时间分辨率微波数据。

Abstract (英文): Polar-orbiting microwave radiometers provide indispensable all-weather measurements of the atmospheric state, yet revisit intervals of many hours leave critical gaps during rapidly evolving weather events. To address this limitation, we developed MIDAS (Microwave Inference via Diffusion Across Satellites), a probabilistic framework that estimates microwave brightness temperature (BT) fields across the geostationary full-disk domain from infrared observations at 10 min intervals. This study focuses on the five Microwave Humidity Sounder-2 (MWHS-2) humidity-sounding channels near 183 GHz, which provide vertically resolved water vapor information. MIDAS achieves relative errors below 0.5% for the majority of cases, with a channel-averaged mean absolute error of 1.15 K, outperforming a deterministic U-Net baseline (1.43 K). Beyond per-sample evaluation, MIDAS reproduces large-scale climatological patterns across the full-disk domain over a three-month summer period, consistent with Radiative Transfer for TOVS–Scattering (RTTOV-SCATT) simulations. In deep convective scenes where reconstruction is most difficult, the ensemble spread naturally tracks reconstruction difficulty, providing a built-in indicator of prediction confidence. Notably, MIDAS incorporates real-time polar-orbiting observations as physical constraints via a merge-sampling mechanism, reducing ensemble RMSE by over 20% and improving probabilistic calibration by more than 30%. Proof-of-concept assimilation experiments for two high-impact weather cases show that MIDAS-generated fields yield forecast improvements comparable to those from real satellite observations, reducing tropical cyclone track errors from approximately 110 km to 40 km and improving heavy precipitation forecasts at extreme rainfall thresholds where direct infrared assimilation shows no benefit. Overall, our framework demonstrates the potential of generative models to supplement sparse observational coverage and provide physically plausible microwave humidity fields for downstream applications.

### [168] [DEAF-Net: Dual-Domain Enhanced Adaptive Fusion Network for UAV Visible–Infrared Object Detection](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132241)
*Qian Weng,Yu Zhang,Xiansheng Huang,Liming Deng,Jiawen Lin*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出DEAF-Net，一种双域增强自适应融合网络，用于解决无人机多模态目标检测中红外与可见光模态可靠性的空间异质性问题。核心包括双域渐进细化模块（DDPR）进行频域-空间域联合特征提纯，以及一致性-差异性引导融合模块（CDGF）基于VMamba选择性扫描机制动态生成局部模态贡献图进行自适应融合。在DroneVehicle和VEDAI数据集上mAP@0.5达到81.9%和76.2%，在弱光、浓雾等场景下鲁棒性显著提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有无人机目标检测中，复杂光照和天气使得单一可见光模态难以实现全天候感知；红外模态虽可补充但单模态可靠性高度场景相关；现有多模态检测方法采用静态融合策略，忽略了模态可靠性的空间异质性，且未充分探索空间-频率协同表征，限制了动态环境下的检测鲁棒性。

Method: 提出DEAF-Net，包含两个核心模块：(1) 双域渐进细化模块（DDPR），通过频域可学习滤波和空间域尺度感知上下文细化联合设计，抑制噪声、增强纹理，获得纯净融合特征基；(2) 一致性-差异性引导融合模块（CDGF），利用VMamba选择性扫描机制建模模态间一致与差异模式，动态生成局部模态贡献图实现自适应融合，并通过熵权重校准引入全局场景先验。

Result: 在DroneVehicle数据集上mAP@0.5达到81.9%，在VEDAI数据集上达到76.2%，优于主流多模态检测方法。在弱光、浓雾、稀疏类别场景下展现出更强的鲁棒性。

Conclusion: DEAF-Net通过双域特征提纯和自适应融合策略，有效解决了多模态目标检测中模态可靠性的空间异质性问题，显著提升了无人机在复杂环境下的全天候感知鲁棒性。

Abstract (英文): In Unmanned Aerial Vehicle (UAV) object detection tasks, complex lighting conditions and variable weather render robust all-weather perception challenging when relying solely on the visible modality. Although infrared modalities can provide complementary information, the reliability of individual modalities is highly scene-dependent. Existing multimodal detection methods typically adopt static fusion strategies, which ignore spatial heterogeneity of modal reliability and under-explore spatial-frequency collaborative representation, thus limiting detection robustness in dynamic environments. To address these issues, this paper proposes a Dual-domain Enhanced Adaptive Fusion Network (DEAF-Net), with two core innovative modules to tackle the above challenges. First, the Dual Domain Progressive Refinement (DDPR) module mitigates feature degradation caused by poor imaging conditions via the joint design of frequency-domain learnable filtering and scale-aware contextual refinement in the spatial domain, effectively suppressing noise, enhancing textures, and yielding a purified feature basis for fusion. Second, the Consistency–Discrepancy Guided Fusion (CDGF) strategy leverages the selective scanning mechanism of VMamba to model consistent and differential patterns across modalities, dynamically generates local modal contribution maps for adaptive fusion, and integrates global scene prior via entropy weights for calibration. Extensive experiments on the DroneVehicle and VEDAI datasets show that DEAF-Net outperforms mainstream multimodal detection methods, achieving mAP@0.5 scores of 81.9% and 76.2%, respectively, while delivering improved robustness in low-light, dense fog, and sparse-category scenarios.

### [169] [Stereo Matching in Satellite Imagery: A Depth Estimation Foundation Model-Assisted Iterative Approach](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132245)
*Kunpeng Hu,Wei Zhao*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出IFMA-Stereo，一种结合单目深度基础模型的双目视差估计方法，通过多尺度空间信息金字塔、注意力交互机制和循环迭代精化模块，解决遥感立体匹配中的纹理缺失、重复模式、遮挡及时空异质性等问题，在US3D和高分七号数据集上达到SOTA精度。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract (英文): In optical remote sensing 3D reconstruction, high-resolution satellite stereo matching is a critical task, yet it is challenged by extreme imaging geometries, texture-less and repetitive patterns, occlusions, and scene variations caused by spatio-temporal heterogeneity. To address these issues, we propose IFMA-Stereo, an innovative binocular disparity estimation method that leverages a monocular depth foundation model. Our approach constructs a multi-scale spatial information pyramid to jointly integrate the foundation model with a disparity extraction network. At the feature level, an attention interaction mechanism captures multi-dimensional contextual dependencies and transforms general scene understanding priors into long-range associative features suitable for stereo cost volume construction. At the pixel level, a cyclic iterative refinement module embeds depth information from the foundation model throughout the iteration process and performs joint optimization, enhancing the model’s adaptability in geometrically complex regions. Experiments on the US3D and GaoFen-7 datasets demonstrate that IFMA-Stereo achieves superior performance in challenging areas (texture-less regions, disparity discontinuities, repetitive patterns) and effectively mitigates prediction errors caused by spatio-temporal heterogeneity, albeit at the cost of increased inference time compared to baseline methods. Quantitatively, the method achieves an end-point error (EPE) of 1.347 and a D1 error of 7.26% on the US3D dataset, and an EPE of 1.585 and a D1 error of 13.41% on the GaoFen-7 dataset. Notably, the method also yields precise predictions for unseen urban areas, indicating strong generalization. These results confirm that IFMA-Stereo achieves state-of-the-art accuracy in remote sensing disparity estimation.

TL;DR: 本文提出一种自适应湿路延迟校正(WTC)方法，通过重叠风况建模、多尺度样本平衡和模型软融合策略，解决现有方法在风速依赖的非线性海面微波辐射响应和稀疏观测分布下的系统偏差问题。基于HY-2C卫星CMR观测数据验证，该方法在不同风速条件下均能提高WTC反演精度和稳定性，尤其改善了稀疏观测区域的系统偏差。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1）建立了低、中、高风速区的重叠过渡带建模框架，分别训练子模型；2）设计结合全局和局部权重的多尺度样本平衡策略，增强对稀疏样本的学习；3）采用基于梯形隶属度函数的软融合策略，动态加权子模型输出，保证过渡带的连续性。

Result: 基于HY-2C CMR观测数据，与模型衍生WTC及Jason-3 AMR-2对比，所提方法整体提高了WTC反演精度和稳定性，有效减少了稀疏观测风速区间的系统偏差。

Conclusion: 所提出的自适应WTC方法在不同风速条件下均能实现高精度、鲁棒的WTC反演，为卫星测高和海洋动力环境监测提供了有效支撑。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。该论文本身就是遥感领域的WTC方法研究。改进方向：1）可将重叠风况建模思想推广至其他海况参数（如海面温度、盐度）的反演中，建立多参数联合的分区建模框架；2）多尺度样本平衡策略可引入主动学习或难例挖掘机制，进一步提升稀疏观测区域的样本利用效率；3）软融合策略可扩展为自适应隶属度函数学习，减少人工设定参数带来的偏差；4）可尝试引入深度学习模型（如Transformer）替代传统子模型，提升非线性拟合能力。

Abstract (英文): High-precision WTC is essential for satellite altimetry and ocean dynamic environment monitoring. Existing WTC approaches often rely on globally unified statistical frameworks, which inadequately represent wind-speed-dependent nonlinear sea-surface microwave radiative responses and are prone to systematic bias under uneven observation distributions. To address these limitations, this study proposes an adaptive WTC method integrating overlapping wind-regime modeling, multi-scale collaborative sample balancing, and a model soft-fusion strategy. Firstly, a modeling framework with overlapping transition zones for low-, moderate-, and high-wind-speed regimes is established according to wind-speed-driven variations in sea-surface radiative responses, and sub-models are trained independently. Subsequently, a multi-scale sample balancing, combining global and local weights, is designed to enhance learning from sparse samples. Finally, a soft-fusion strategy based on a trapezoidal membership function is applied to dynamically weight sub-model outputs, ensuring retrieval continuity across transition zones. Using HY-2C Calibration Microwave Radiometer (CMR) observations, the proposed method is developed, trained, and evaluated against model-derived WTC and collocated Jason-3 AMR-2 measurements. Results show that the proposed method improves overall WTC retrieval accuracy and stability while effectively reducing systematic biases under wind-speed regimes with sparse observations, providing an effective and robust approach for high-accuracy WTC retrieval under various wind-speed conditions.

</details>


### [171] [On the Spectral–Phenological Features for Crop Mapping Under Complex Planting Patterns: A Case Study in Jiangsu Province, China](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132244)
*Ziyin You,Jiajun Wu,X F Wang,Bo Wang,Xuan Xu,Pei Zhan,N LI,Chitfai Yan*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 针对碎片化农业景观中的作物制图问题，本研究利用Sentinel-1/2影像构建了275个季节特异性光谱-物候特征变量，提出了一种先验引导的遗传算法（GA）进行特征选择。在江苏省水稻、玉米、大豆、冬小麦和冬油菜的五类分类任务中，GA选择的紧凑子集（9-39个变量）在独立验证集上实现了91.77%的总体精度和93.95%的靶向作物F1分数，显著优于完整特征库（86.96%）和单一传感器方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 碎片化农业景观中，作物物候重叠以及多源时序变量间的冗余导致作物制图精度受限，亟需有效的特征选择方法以提升分类性能与可解释性。

Method: 1) 构建275个季节特异性光谱-物候特征变量（125个夏季作物+150个冬季作物）；2) 采用辅助二元随机森林（RF）计算OOB置换重要性，构建搜索先验；3) 先验引导的遗传算法（GA）筛选紧凑特征子集；4) 作物特异性五类RF模型评估子集并生成最终分类；5) 固定80/20分层划分进行开发-验证。

Result: GA选择子集（9-39变量）在独立验证集上：五类总体精度91.77%，靶向作物F1分数93.95%。相比之下，光学/植被指数方案F1为78.42%，SAR方案F1为83.74%，完整特征库F1为86.96%。合并背景类后季节性地图总体精度81.20-95.03%。8月和4月分别是夏/冬作物的主要判别期，VH后向散射和SWIR相关指数（STI、NDTI）贡献最突出。

Conclusion: 先验引导的GA特征选择能在RF工作流中实现作物特异性、可解释的降维，显著提升分类精度；但结论的泛化性需多年度、多区域验证。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。改进方案：1) 将先验引导GA特征选择框架扩展到高光谱或雷达（如PolSAR、InSAR）等多模态遥感数据，处理更高维特征空间；2) 结合深度学习（如1D-CNN或Transformer）替代RF分类器，验证子集效应在不同学习算法下的迁移性；3) 引入时空注意力机制或地理加权策略，提升模型在异质性景观中的空间泛化能力；4) 将方法迁移至其他复杂农业区（如东南亚热带轮作区）进行跨区域验证。

Abstract (英文): Accurate crop mapping in fragmented agricultural landscapes is challenged by overlapping crop calendars and redundancy among multi-source time-series variables. Using Sentinel-1/2 imagery from December 2022 to December 2023, we constructed 275 season-specific spectral–phenological feature–month variables (125 for summer crops and 150 for winter crops) for rice, maize, soybean, winter wheat, and winter rapeseed in Jiangsu Province, China. An auxiliary binary Random Forest (RF) was used to estimate out-of-bag (OOB) permutation-based predictive contributions and construct search priors. A prior-guided genetic algorithm (GA) then identified compact subsets, with crop-specific five-class RF models used both to evaluate candidate subsets and to produce the final classifications. A fixed stratified 80/20 development–validation split was maintained throughout the analysis, with the validation subset reserved for final assessment. August and April were the principal discriminative periods for summer and winter crops, respectively, while VH backscatter and SWIR-related indices, particularly STI and NDTI, showed recurrent predictive contributions across crops. On the independent validation subset, the optical/vegetation-index scheme, SAR-only scheme, and the complete feature library achieved mean target-crop F1-scores of 78.42%, 83.74%, and 86.96%, respectively. The GA-selected subsets retained 9–39 variables and achieved a mean five-class overall accuracy of 91.77% and a mean target-crop F1-score of 93.95%. After non-target classes were merged into a single background class, the integrated seasonal maps achieved overall accuracies of 81.20–95.03% on the same validation subset. Supplementary classifier comparisons indicated that subset effects depended on the crop and learning algorithm. The findings support crop-specific, interpretable dimensionality reduction within the RF workflow, while broader transferability requires multi-year and multi-region evaluation.

### [172] [Deep Learning Enables the Automatic Mapping of Tell Sites on Satellite Synthetic Aperture Radar Products](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132255)
*Elena Chiricallo,Giulio Poggi,Sara Ferro,Sebastiano Vascon,Arianna Traviglia*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种基于YOLOv8-Seg深度学习管道，利用Sentinel-1 SAR影像和DEM数据自动检测和分割伊拉克中部考古遗址土丘(tells)，在测试区域取得0.495的平均精度和0.361的IoU，并展示了向伊朗地区的迁移潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: SAR技术在考古景观研究中具有成熟应用，但由于缺乏鲁棒的自动化分析方法，难以在大规模考古探测中推广使用。现有方法无法高效处理海量SAR数据，亟需自动化解决方案。

Method: 采用YOLOv8-Seg实例分割模型，输入数据为Copernicus Sentinel-1 IW模式GRD SAR影像和30米DEM数据，对伊拉克中部地区考古土丘进行自动检测与语义分割。

Result: 在测试区域，模型平均精度(AP)为0.495±0.010，像素级交并比(IoU)为0.361±0.048。考古解读确认了模型定位和分割遗址的可靠性，并发现了此前未标记的潜在遗址。向伊朗迁移测试显示可行但需区域微调。

Conclusion: 本研究为基于SAR影像的深度学习考古探测建立了基线，验证了自动化考古遗址检测的可行性，但跨区域应用仍需针对地形和环境的区域差异进行微调。

Abstract (英文): Satellite Synthetic Aperture Radar (SAR) is an established technology for studying and monitoring archaeological landscapes, providing insights into surface morphology and the presence of near subsurface features. However, its application in large-scale archaeological prospection is limited by the lack of robust, automated methods for SAR data analysis. This study introduces a novel Deep Learning pipeline to automatically detect and segment archaeological settlement mounds, known as tells, in central Iraq on satellite SAR data. The pipeline leverages a state-of-the-art supervised method for instance segmentation, YOLOv8-Seg, and medium-resolution satellite SAR products, specifically the Copernicus Sentinel-1 Interferometric Wide Swath Mode Ground Range Detected and Copernicus Global 30-m Digital Elevation Model products. The model identifies tell sites with an Average Precision of 0.495±0.010 and a pixel-wise Intersection over Union of 0.361±0.048 over the test areas. Archaeological interpretation of the model’s inferences confirms its reliability in locating and segmenting archaeological sites, leading also to the identification of previously unmapped potential sites. After a main test in central Iraq, the proposed workflow demonstrates promising transferability to a nearby test area in Iran, although with a need for regional fine-tuning to account for inherent variations in feature morphology and environmental context. This research establishes a baseline for future Deep Learning applications in Synthetic Aperture Radar-based archaeological prospection.

### [173] [Mapping Acid Mine Drainage Areas with Sentinel-2 and WorldView-3 VNIR Satellite Images: An Example in the SE of Spain](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132240)
*Inés Pereira,Eduardo García‐Meléndez,Montserrat Ferrer‐Julià,H.M.A. van der Werff*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本研究评估并比较了Sentinel-2与WorldView-3的VNIR波段在西班牙Cartagena–La Unión矿区对次生铁矿物（赤铁矿、针铁矿、黄钾铁矾）的制图和区分能力。结果表明，Sentinel-2由于红边和近红外波段配置更优，尤其在抛物线拟合方法下能更好地区分这三种矿物，而WorldView-3主要只能区分赤铁矿与针铁矿-黄钾铁矾组合。基于X射线衍射验证，Sentinel-2可用于矿区氧化过程的系统监测和环境风险评估。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 硫化物矿床开采导致硫化物矿物氧化，产生富含硫酸盐和溶解金属的酸性矿山排水（AMD），并形成次生铁矿物（赤铁矿、针铁矿、黄钾铁矾）。这些矿物在可见光-近红外（VNIR）区域具有诊断性特征，因此多光谱卫星数据提供了一种经济有效的监测手段。本研究旨在评估和比较Sentinel-2与WorldView-3 VNIR波段在制图和区分次生铁矿物方面的性能。

Method: 以西班牙Sierra Minera de Cartagena–La Unión矿区为研究区，分别使用Sentinel-2和WorldView-3的VNIR波段数据。采用波段比值法和抛物线拟合技术（聚焦反射率最大值）分析数据，并对74个地表土壤样本进行X射线衍射分析以验证矿物制图结果。

Result: 两种传感器均能再现铁矿物分布的主要空间格局。Sentinel-2能更好地区分赤铁矿、针铁矿和黄钾铁矾，尤其是在采用抛物线拟合方法时；而WorldView-3 VNIR数据主要能区分赤铁矿与针铁矿-黄钾铁矾组合。Sentinel-2的优越性能归因于其红边和近红外波段配置。

Conclusion: 免费开放的Sentinel-2影像能够支持矿区氧化过程的系统监测，并有助于退化景观的环境风险评估。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。该论文本身就是遥感应用于矿山环境监测的典型研究。改进方案：（1）结合高光谱数据（如PRISMA、EnMAP）提升矿物种类识别精度；（2）引入机器学习方法（随机森林、支持向量机或深度学习）以替代传统波段比值和抛物线拟合，提高分类鲁棒性；（3）融合时序分析，监测氧化过程的动态变化；（4）结合DEM数据考虑地形阴影对反射率的影响；（5）扩展至其他矿山类型或区域以验证泛化能力。

Abstract (英文): Mining of sulfide-rich deposits enhances the oxidation of sulfide minerals, generating acid mine drainage (AMD) characterized by high sulphate and dissolved metal concentrations and the formation of secondary iron minerals (hematite, goethite, and jarosite). As these minerals display diagnostic features in the visible–near-infrared (VNIR) region, multispectral satellite data provide a cost-effective means of monitoring. Here, the performances of Sentinel-2 and the VNIR bands from WorldView-3 are assessed and compared for the mapping and discrimination of secondary iron minerals in Sierra Minera de Cartagena–La Unión (SE Spain). Both datasets were analyzed using a band ratio and a parabola fitting technique focused on reflectance maxima. Band ratio results were interpreted as broad spectral patterns rather than definitive mineral identifications. Mineral maps were validated by applying X-ray diffraction on 74 surface soil samples. Although both sensors were able to reproduce the main spatial patterns of iron mineral distribution, Sentinel-2 data better discriminated hematite, goethite, and jarosite, especially when using the parabola fitting approach, whereas WorldView-3 VNIR data distinguished mainly hematite from the combined goethite–jarosite group. The better performance of Sentinel-2 is attributed to its red-edge and near-infrared band configuration. These findings indicate that freely available Sentinel-2 imagery can support systematic monitoring of oxidation processes in mining environments and contribute to environmental risk assessment in degraded landscapes.

### [174] [A Sentinel-2-Based Framework for Methane Point-Source Detection and Quantification Using Low-Reflectance Artifact Detection](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132251)
*Kun Cai,T -Y Chen,Liang Zheng,Shenshen Li,Xinhui Zhou,Ying Liu,X Chen*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为MBMC（多波段多约束）的综合甲烷监测框架，利用Sentinel-2 MSI影像，通过结合低反射率伪影检测（LRAD）算法、多波段多通道（MBMP）差分吸收反演模型和集成质量增强（IME）排放量化方法，实现对甲烷点源的高分辨率、高频次卫星监测。在美国亚利桑那州的单盲控制甲烷释放实验中，该方法在0.5-3.0 t/h排放率范围内实现了21.6%的平均绝对百分比误差（MAPE），并在中国西北天然气田成功识别和量化了多个甲烷点源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 甲烷是仅次于CO₂的第二大温室气体，其短期全球变暖潜力高且减排可行性强，因此监测甲烷点源排放对减缓气候变化至关重要。现有卫星监测技术存在空间覆盖范围有限以及地表信号干扰等技术瓶颈，亟需开发新的监测框架以提高甲烷点源的识别和量化精度。

Method: 提出了MBMC综合甲烷监测框架，包含三个核心模块：(1) 低反射率伪影检测（LRAD）算法，有效抑制低反射率地表和异质背景造成的伪影，提高信噪比和甲烷柱增强反演精度；(2) 多波段多通道（MBMP）差分吸收反演模型；(3) 集成质量增强（IME）排放量化方法。此外，还开发了结合形态学操作与空间数据库的半自动羽流分割工作流，用于改进甲烷羽流提取和源定位。

Result: 在美国亚利桑那州的单盲控制甲烷释放实验中，该方法在0.5-3.0 t/h排放率范围内实现了21.6%的平均绝对百分比误差（MAPE）。在中国西北天然气田的Sentinel-2观测中，成功识别并量化了与集气站相关的多个甲烷点源。

Conclusion: 该框架为基于Sentinel-2的高分辨率、高频次卫星监测甲烷点源提供了实用方法，能够支持石油和天然气行业甲烷排放清单的完善和减排策略的制定。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。该论文本身即为遥感甲烷监测研究。(1) 可将MBMC框架扩展至其他多光谱卫星传感器（如Landsat 8/9 OLI、Planet SuperDove、GF-6 WFV等），验证跨传感器的适用性；(2) 引入深度学习（如U-Net、Transformer）替代半自动羽流分割工作流中的形态学操作，实现全自动、更鲁棒的甲烷羽流分割和源定位；(3) 结合大气化学传输模型（如GEOS-Chem、WRF-Chem）进行排放通量同化，进一步提升定量精度；(4) 针对阴云天气下Sentinel-2观测受限的问题，可考虑与TROPOMI、GOSAT等低分辨率但高重访率的传感器融合，实现多尺度时空互补监测。

Abstract (英文): Methane (CH4) is the second most significant greenhouse gas after carbon dioxide (CO2). Due to its high short-term global warming potential and the feasibility of emission abatement, monitoring methane point-source emissions has become a critical strategy for mitigating climate change. To address existing technical bottlenecks associated with spatial coverage limitations and surface-induced signal interference in satellite-based monitoring, this study proposes an integrated methane monitoring framework termed Multi-Band Multi-Constraint (MBMC) using Sentinel-2 MSI imagery. The MBMC framework combines a Low-Reflectance Artifact Detection (LRAD) algorithm, a Multi-Band Multi-Pass (MBMP) differential absorption retrieval model, and Integrated Mass Enhancement (IME)-based emission quantification. The LRAD module effectively suppresses artifacts caused by low-reflectance surfaces and heterogeneous backgrounds, thereby improving the signal-to-noise ratio (SNR) and retrieval accuracy of methane column enhancements. In addition, a semi-automatic plume segmentation workflow integrating morphological operations with a spatial database is developed to improve methane plume extraction and source localization. The framework was validated using data from single-blind controlled methane release experiments conducted in Arizona, USA. Results show that the proposed method achieved a mean absolute percentage error (MAPE) of 21.6% for emission rates ranging from 0.5 to 3.0 t/h, demonstrating promising performance for Sentinel-2-based screening and quantification of methane point sources, particularly for emissions above approximately 0.5 t/h under favorable observation conditions. The framework was further applied to Sentinel-2 observations over a natural gas field in Northwest China, where multiple methane point sources associated with gas gathering stations were successfully identified and quantified. The proposed framework provides a practical approach for high-resolution and high-frequency satellite monitoring of methane point sources and supports the refinement of methane emission inventories and mitigation strategies in the oil and gas sector.

</details>


### [175] [The Impact of Dynamic Observation Error and Hydrometeor Control Variables on GK-2A AMI All-Sky Radiance Assimilation](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132246)
*Seo-Youn Jo,Ki‐Hong Min*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 研究动态观测误差在全天空辐射率（ASR）同化中对水凝物控制变量（HCV）配置下的分析和降水预报的影响。结果表明，动态误差相比常数误差能改善云分析和热力场，尤其在包含固相水凝物时效果更显著。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: ASR同化中直接更新水凝物场存在较大不确定性，而观测误差的设定对同化效果至关重要。目前缺乏对动态观测误差在不同水凝物控制变量配置下影响的系统研究。

Method: 采用五次多项式模型将观测误差表示为云影响参数的函数，实现随空间和时间变化的场景依赖误差；在不同水凝物控制变量配置下进行ASR同化实验，对比动态误差与常数误差的效果。

Result: 动态观测误差改善了云分析和热力场；常数误差在强云区域过度加权ASR观测，降低分析质量；动态误差优势在包含固相水凝物时更明显；结合动态误差与固相水凝物直接更新的实验获得了最真实的亮温和反射率分析，并最大程度改善了降水预报。

Conclusion: 云依赖的观测误差建模在ASR同化中至关重要，特别是在使用固相水凝物控制变量时，动态误差能有效提升分析和预报质量。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：90%。该研究直接涉及遥感数据（全天空辐射率）的同化方法改进，与遥感领域高度相关。可进一步扩展到：（1）将动态观测误差建模方法应用于其他遥感数据（如微波成像仪、红外探测器）的同化；（2）探索更复杂的云影响参数化方案（如机器学习模型）来替代五次多项式；（3）将该方法推广到陆面遥感数据同化，考虑地表类型对误差的影响；（4）结合神经网络或深度学习构建更精细的场景依赖误差模型。

Abstract (英文): Assimilation of all-sky radiance (ASR) observations informs atmospheric states and cloud distributions; however, it does not always lead to improved analyses or forecasts. In particular, directly updating hydrometeor fields introduces substantial uncertainty into ASR assimilation. This study examines the impact of dynamic observation errors on analyses and precipitation forecasts under different hydrometeor control variable (HCV) configurations. Observation errors are prescribed using a fifth-order polynomial model as a function of a cloud impact parameter, allowing spatiotemporally varying (i.e., scene-dependent) errors that adapt to cloud conditions. Results indicate that dynamic observation errors generally improve cloud analyses and associated thermodynamic fields. By contrast, constant errors tend to overweight ASR observations in heavily cloud-affected regions, thereby degrading analysis quality. The advantages of dynamic errors are more pronounced when solid-phase hydrometeors are included in the HCV, as these strongly influence brightness temperature (BT) analysis and the representation of convective cloud tops. Among all experiments, those combining dynamic errors with direct updates of solid-phase hydrometeors produce the most realistic BT and reflectivity analyses, as well as the greatest improvements in precipitation forecasts. These results underscore the importance of cloud-dependent observation error modeling in ASR assimilation, particularly when solid-phase HCVs are employed.

### [176] [GHF-DETR: An Improved DETR Framework with a Multi-Path Backbone and Dual-Domain Downsampling for UAV Object Detection](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132239)
*Lei Hu,Qingming Huang,Zhixiang Liu,Hongwei Ye*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: GHF-DETR是一种基于Transformer的无人机小目标检测器，通过异构多路径卷积网络（HMC）骨干、动态多尺度聚焦（DMSF）模块和高频选择性保留（HSP）下采样模块，在VisDrone2019上以15.4 GFLOPs和7.59M参数达到33.1% mAP@0.5，比DFINE-n基线提升5.4%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无人机图像中的小目标检测面临像素覆盖少、背景复杂和下采样信息丢失三大挑战，现有检测器缺乏增强弱目标信号的显式机制。

Method: 提出GHF-DETR，包含三个协同模块：1) HMC骨干网络，采用部分卷积和门控线性单元减少计算冗余并保持小目标特征判别性；2) DMSF模块，结合学习偏移对齐和多核深度可分离卷积进行跨尺度特征融合；3) HSP下采样模块，结合空间到深度卷积与2D离散小波变换，在空间和频率域补偿信息损失。

Result: 在VisDrone2019上，GHF-DETR达到33.1% mAP@0.5和18.6% mAP@0.5:0.95，参数量7.59M，计算量15.4 GFLOPs；相比DFINE-n基线分别提升5.4%和3.1%，AP_S达10.1%。在NWPU VHR-10上验证了泛化性。

Conclusion: GHF-DETR在效率与精度之间取得了良好的平衡，适用于高效的无人机小目标检测任务。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。作为遥感小目标检测论文，改进方向：1) HMC骨干可引入通道注意力机制进一步抑制复杂背景干扰；2) DMSF模块可扩展至多尺度金字塔结构，适应遥感图像中目标尺度差异更大的场景；3) HSP下采样中的DWT可尝试与其他频域变换（如曲波变换）结合，提升对纹理信息的保留能力；4) 可引入旋转目标检测分支（如定向边界框），适应遥感图像中目标任意朝向的特性。

Abstract (英文): Detecting small targets in Unmanned Aerial Vehicle (UAV) imagery is challenging due to low pixel coverage, complex backgrounds, and information loss during downsampling. Existing detectors lack explicit mechanisms for enhancing weak target signals. We propose GHF-DETR, a Transformer-based detector featuring three collaboratively designed modules. First, a Heterogeneous Multi-Path Convolutional Network (HMC) backbone uses partial convolution and gated linear units to reduce computational redundancy while maintaining discrimination of small-object features. Second, a Dynamic Multi-Scale Focusing (DMSF) module integrates learned offset alignment with multi-kernel depthwise convolutions for cross-scale feature fusion. Third, a High-Frequency Selective Preservation (HSP) downsampling module combines space-to-depth convolution with 2D Discrete Wavelet Transform (DWT) to compensate for information loss in both spatial and frequency domains. On VisDrone2019, GHF-DETR achieves 33.1% mAP@0.5 and 18.6% mAP@0.5:0.95 with 15.4 GFLOPs and 7.59 M parameters, improving over the DFINE-n baseline by 5.4% and 3.1%, respectively, with AP_S reaching 10.1%. Generalization is validated on NWPU VHR-10. These results demonstrate that GHF-DETR achieves a favorable accuracy–efficiency balance for efficient UAV small-object detection.

### [177] [Development of PXB-BVC Framework for Multivariate Flood-Risk Assessment Under Climate Change](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18142275)
*Aili Yang,Wenjie Li,Pangpang Gao,Yurui Fan,Xiuquan Wang*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出PXB-BVC框架（融合SWAT、HBV、XGBoost、贝叶斯模型平均和双变量Copula），用于改进径流预测和多元洪水风险评估。在湘西河流域应用表明，该框架在日径流模拟中NSE达0.95（校准）和0.89（验证），未来径流总体增加，洪水特征间依赖结构呈现非平稳性，高排放情景下复合风险显著增强。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 气候变化加剧洪水风险，现有方法在径流预测精度和多变量洪水风险评估方面存在不足，亟需开发融合物理机制与机器学习、能够处理非平稳依赖结构的综合框架。

Method: 1) 利用ArcGIS处理30m土地利用遥感数据进行空间显式水文模拟；2) 集成SWAT和HBV两种物理水文模型与XGBoost机器学习；3) 采用贝叶斯模型平均(BMA)融合多模型输出；4) 引入双变量Copula分析洪水特征（洪峰、洪量、历时）的联合分布与非平稳依赖结构；5) 基于4种GCM和3种SSP情景进行未来预测。

Result: 日径流模拟NSE校准0.95/验证0.89；未来径流呈增长趋势，SSP585下Sen斜率达0.46 m³/s/年；洪峰-洪量Kendall's tau在0.6-0.8之间呈现非平稳性；高排放条件下，给定极端洪峰时伴随高洪量的概率从0.23升至0.56，伴随长历时的概率从0.18升至0.45。

Conclusion: PXB-BVC框架能够有效支持非平稳条件下的多元洪水风险评估，为气候适应性水资源管理和基础设施规划提供有价值的信息。

Abstract (英文): Flood risks are escalating under climate change, necessitating advanced methods to improve runoff prediction and multivariate flood-risk assessment. In this study, a physics–XGBoost-based Bayesian model averaging with bivariate copulas (PXB-BVC) framework was developed by integrating the Soil and Water Assessment Tool (SWAT), the Hydrologiska Byråns Vattenbalansavdelning (HBV) model, Extreme Gradient Boosting (XGBoost), Bayesian model averaging (BMA), and bivariate copulas. Spatially detailed underlying surface parameters including 30 m land-use data derived from the 2000 China land-use remote sensing monitoring data were pre-processed and reclassified using ArcGIS to support spatially explicit hydrological simulation. The framework was applied to the Xiangxi River Basin (XXRB), China, under four general circulation models and three shared socioeconomic pathways. PXB-BVC improved daily runoff simulation by combining process-based hydrological information with nonlinear machine learning correction, achieving Nash–Sutcliffe efficiency (NSE) values of 0.95 during calibration and 0.89 during validation. Future runoff generally increased from the near-term to the late-century period, with stronger changes under SSP585 and Sen slopes reaching up to 0.46 m3 s−1 yr−1, although the magnitude and significance of trends varied among GCMs. The dependence structures among flood peak, flood volume, and flood duration showed non-stationary behavior under future climate forcing, with Kendall’s tau for peak–volume pairs mostly ranging from 0.6 to 0.8. The revised bivariate return-period analysis further indicates that inferred flood-risk changes depend on the joint risk definition. Under SSP245 and ACCESS-ESM1–5, OR-type joint return periods show that representative near-future 50-year events may become more frequent in 2061–2100, whereas AND-type return periods show weaker and less uniform changes among flood-characteristic pairs. Conditional probability analysis also indicates enhanced compound risk under high-emission conditions: given an extreme peak flow, the probability of accompanying high flood volume increases from 0.23 to 0.56, while the probability of prolonged duration increases from 0.18 to 0.45. These results demonstrate that the PXB-BVC framework can support non-stationary multivariate flood-risk assessment and provide useful information for climate-resilient water-resource management and infrastructure planning.

### [178] [CAF-Net: A Unified Framework for Resolving Spatial–Frequency Representation Conflicts in Multimodal Remote Sensing Segmentation](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18142284)
*Ming Ma,S S Wu,X Li,Wei Hong*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出CAF-Net，通过跨模态结构引导、自适应跨频率模块和不确定性感知融合解决多模态遥感分割中空间域结构与频域语义的不一致问题，在ISPRS Vaihingen和Potsdam数据集上分别达到84.35%和86.86%的mIoU。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法忽视了多模态遥感分割中空间域结构细节与频域语义之间的不一致问题，导致复杂场景下特征对齐不良和性能下降。

Method: 提出CAF-Net，包含三个核心模块：(1) 跨模态结构引导(CMSG)提取DSM的高通结构线索并条件调制光学特征；(2) 自适应跨频率模块(ACFM)通过固定径向掩码分离DCT系数并自适应重加权低频/高频分量；(3) 不确定性感知融合(UAF)预测像素级相对可靠度分数并跨模态归一化以抑制低置信度响应。

Result: 在ISPRS Vaihingen和Potsdam数据集上分别达到84.35%和86.86%的mIoU。

Conclusion: 显式建模空间-频率不一致性可以有效提升多模态分割精度和表示一致性。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。作为遥感多模态分割论文，改进方向包括：(1) 当前方法仅适用于光学+DSM双模态，可扩展至SAR+光学、多光谱+高光谱等更多模态组合；(2) DCT径向掩码的频率划分方式可引入可学习的自适应频带划分机制；(3) 不确定性融合可结合不确定性估计的主动学习策略，用于自训练或半监督场景；(4) 可考虑引入频域增强数据增广策略进一步提升模型泛化能力。

Abstract (英文): Multimodal remote sensing segmentation commonly integrates optical imagery with Digital Surface Models (DSMs) to improve land-cover understanding. However, existing methods often overlook a critical issue, namely the inconsistency between spatial-domain structural details and frequency-domain semantics, which can lead to misaligned features and degraded performance in complex scenes. To address this problem, we formulate spatial–frequency representation conflict as a unified multimodal learning problem and propose the Conflict-Aware Fusion Network (CAF-Net). Specifically, Cross-Modal Structure Guidance (CMSG) extracts DSM-derived high-pass structural cues and conditionally modulates optical features to improve boundary consistency. The Adaptive Cross-Frequency Module (ACFM) separates DCT coefficients using a fixed radial mask, adaptively reweights low- and high-frequency components, and performs cross-modal alignment at the highest encoder stage. Uncertainty-Aware Fusion (UAF) predicts pixel-wise relative reliability scores and normalizes them across modalities to suppress low-confidence responses. This coordinated design links spatial refinement, frequency alignment, and reliability-guided fusion instead of treating them as independent feature-enhancement operations. Experiments on the ISPRS Vaihingen and Potsdam datasets yield mIoU scores of 84.35% and 86.86%, respectively. The results indicate that explicitly modeling spatial–frequency discrepancies can improve multimodal segmentation accuracy and representation consistency.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出结合行-列几何感知的回波区域预分类与频域直方图自适应抑制的轻量级预处理方法。具体包括：从归一化条纹图像中提取候选区域，按行-列形态学分类，基于局部幅度谱百分位数阈值滤波，并采用背景约束加权策略进行融合。

Abstract (英文): Long-range airborne streak tube imaging lidar (ASTIL) raw echo images are degraded by atmospheric speckle, detector noise, and weak-return fluctuations, which can bias centroid localization before range calculation. This study presents a lightweight preprocessing method combining row–column geometry-aware echo region pre-classification with frequency-domain histogram-based adaptive suppression. Candidate regions are extracted from normalized streak images, classified by row–column morphology, filtered using local magnitude-spectrum percentile thresholds, and fused with a background-constrained weighted strategy. The results show that preprocessing before centroid extraction can improve roof-level vertical consistency without neural-network training or complex point cloud post-processing.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract (英文): To advance crop type mapping in support of global food and water security, this study compared three spectral configurations: (A) the full 60-band DLR Earth Sensing Imaging Spectrometer (DESIS) hyperspectral narrowband (HNB) dataset, (B) a 14-band subset of DESIS-derived HNBs aligned with the planned Landsat 10 (formerly Landsat Next) spectral configuration (400–1000 nm), and (C) DESIS-based simulations of Landsat 10 superspectral broadbands. The analysis was conducted in California’s Central Valley, hereafter referred to as “the Central Valley”, during the peak growing month of August. DESIS imagery from August 2021, 2022, and 2023 was used sequentially for model development, testing, and independent validation. Over these three years, DESIS provided extensive hyperspectral coverage of much of the 4 million hectares in the Central Valley’s. Analyses were performed on Google Earth Engine using two pixel-based supervised classifiers, Random Forest (RF) and Support Vector Machine (SVM), to differentiate three major crop classes: row crops, grapes and tree crops, and winter wheat/fallow/other. The highest overall accuracy (86%) was achieved using SVM in combination with either the full DESIS hyperspectral dataset or the 14 DESIS narrowbands corresponding to Landsat 10. This finding aligns with earlier studies showing a small number of strategically positioned narrowbands can be optimal for crop type classification. Use of the narrowband datasets resulted in substantially higher accuracy (overall accuracy of 86%) compared to the simulated Landsat 10 broadbands (overall accuracy of 75%), supporting previous studies highlighting the utility of narrowbands. Despite the high accuracy using August imagery, the study indicates more granular crop type classification will require multi-temporal observations spanning the full phenological cycle (June–October), especially for a large number of crop classes. Acquiring task-based hyperspectral imagery over such large areas throughout the growing season remains operationally challenging. In contrast, Landsat 10 superspectral imagery could provide routine coverage across seasons and years that is practical and scalable for future large area crop type mapping and agricultural monitoring.

### [181] [Earth Observation Data and Indigenous Perspectives: Two-Eyed Seeing Approach to Understanding Long-Term Wildfire and Landscape Changes](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132259)

Motivation: 高纬度地区野火频发且气候变暖加速，而传统的单一科学方法难以全面理解野火与土地变化的复杂关系。作者希望融合西方科学与土著传统生态知识，以实现更精确的分析并为气候韧性和土著土地管理提供协作框架。

Method: 采用“双眼看”方法（Two-Eyed Seeing），整合地球观测数据（火烧迹地、地表温度、反照率、雪盖、土壤湿度、土地覆盖类型）与Tłı̨chǫ长老和官员的土著知识，并结合社区倾听与故事讲述环节获取深入的土著视角。

Result: 过去15年Tłı̨chǫ自有领地近一半森林转为其他地类，灌木林增加两倍、草地扩大十倍；春夏地表温度显著上升（p<0.05），降水和雪盖显著减少（p<0.05）；表土湿度下降与升温形成正反馈，加剧未来野火风险。

Conclusion: “双眼看”方法将本土土著知识与定量地球观测相结合，不仅提高了分析精度，还为制定减轻日益严重火灾制度和土地覆盖变化影响的针对性策略提供了协作框架。研究意义超越Tłı̨chǫ领地，对气候韧性和土著管理具有广泛启示。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：90%。该研究已成功将遥感地球观测数据与土著传统生态知识融合，未来可从以下方向进一步深化：（1）引入更高分辨率遥感数据（如Sentinel-2、Planet）以捕捉更精细的土地覆盖变化和火烧迹地边界；（2）结合SAR数据（如Sentinel-1）监测地表土壤湿度和植被结构变化，弥补光学数据受云覆盖的限制；（3）利用长时间序列的Landsat和MODIS数据建立更系统的野火风险评估模型；（4）将遥感衍生的地表参数（LST、反照率、NDVI等）与土著知识中的火灾历史口述记录进行时空交叉验证；（5）将该框架推广至其他高纬度土著社区，建立跨区域遥感-本土知识融合的野火监测与预警系统。

Abstract (英文): High-latitude regions are witnessing unprecedented wildfires and accelerated warming. This study explored wildfire patterns and land changes within the high-latitude Indigenous Tłı̨chǫ territory in the Northwest Territories, Canada. It used the Two-Eyed Seeing approach, which combines Western science, or Scientific Ecological Knowledge (SEK), with Indigenous knowledge, or Traditional Ecological Knowledge (TEK). This method integrated Earth observation data with insights from Tłı̨chǫ Elders and officials. We analyzed spatiotemporal variations in burned areas, land surface temperature (LST), albedo, snow cover, soil moisture, and land-cover types. A listening and storytelling session with community Elders provided an in-depth Indigenous perspective. Our findings indicate a concerning shift in wildfire activity on Tłı̨chǫ land, primarily driven by the interplay between climate change and land-cover changes. Land-cover estimates over the past fifteen years indicate that nearly half of the forested areas on Tłı̨chǫ-owned land have been converted to other land-cover types, with shrublands increasing twofold and grasslands expanding tenfold. We observed significant increases in spring and summer LSTs (p &lt; 0.05), alongside decreases in precipitation and snow cover (p &lt; 0.05), consistent with the Elders’ observations. The decline in topsoil moisture, coupled with rising temperatures, has triggered a positive feedback loop in forested areas, intensifying future wildfire risk. The study’s implications extend beyond the Tłı̨chǫ territory, suggesting a broader significance for climate resilience and Indigenous stewardship. It highlights the significance of place-based, integrated research for understanding complex wildfire behavior and land-cover transformations. The study indicates that the Two-Eyed Seeing approach, which weaves local Indigenous knowledge with quantitative Earth observations, not only improves analytical precision but also provides a collaborative framework for developing targeted strategies to mitigate the effects of increasingly severe fire regimes and land-cover changes.

### [182] [Intraspecific Drought Stress Responses Detected Using Remotely Sensed Vegetation Indices in Sitka Spruce (Picea sitchensis)](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18142280)
*Gerrard English,J. Rosette,Richard Whittet,Juan Carlos Pinilla Suárez*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本研究通过为期八周的受控干旱实验，评估高光谱植被指数是否能够检测锡特卡云杉种内干旱响应，以支持抗旱基因型筛选。结果表明，基于色素和红边的指数对干旱最敏感，克隆间存在显著的响应差异，高光谱方法可快速、非破坏性地检测抗旱表型。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 气候变化加剧英国林业干旱风险，锡特卡云杉作为主要商用针叶树的恢复力令人担忧，亟需一种能够快速、非破坏性检测种内干旱响应差异的方法，以支持抗旱基因型筛选。

Method: 对60株来自英国育种群体6个克隆组的嫁接锡特卡云杉进行为期8周的受控干旱实验，采集针叶级别高光谱反射率，推导与叶绿素状态、光保护色素和含水量相关的植被指数，同时测量叶绿素荧光（Fv/Fm）。

Abstract (英文): UK forestry faces increasing drought risk under climate change, raising concerns about the resilience of Sitka spruce, the UK’s dominant commercial conifer. This study assessed whether hyperspectral vegetation indices can detect intraspecific drought responses to support resilience screening. An eight-week controlled drought experiment was conducted on 60 grafted Sitka spruce trees representing six clonal groups from the UK breeding population. Needle-level hyperspectral reflectance was used to derive vegetation indices associated with chlorophyll status, photoprotective pigments, and water content, alongside chlorophyll fluorescence (Fv/Fm). Pigment-based and red-edge indices showed the strongest sensitivity to drought, with ARI1 increasing by up to 1.2 under drought relative to controls, while water-related indices captured later-stage hydraulic decline. Clonal variation was detected in the timing and magnitude of pigment regulation, water loss, and photosynthetic impairment, indicating contrasting drought-response trajectories among clones. These results demonstrate that hyperspectral approaches enable rapid, non-destructive detection of physiologically meaningful drought responses and can support the identification of drought-resilient genotypes for climate-adaptive forest management.

### [183] [Water Anomaly Type Identification Based on Deep Multisphere Decision Boundaries Using Remote Sensing Data](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18142273)
*Jinfeng Song,Kun Jia,Haishuo Wei,Biao Cao,Xing Yan,Jianbo Qi,Kai Yan,Jinlong Fan,Qiao Wang*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种深度多球决策边界（DMSDB）方法，用于从Sentinel-2影像中快速、高精度识别多种水体异常（如水华、藻类暴发等）。该方法构建5维物理可解释特征空间，利用改进的VM-UNet-v2网络提取水体异常响应特征，并通过多球对比损失函数优化类别决策边界，在10000 km²场景下33秒完成分类，平均F1分数0.8789，mIoU 0.7932。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有水体异常类型识别方法难以同时实现高精度和快速推理：依赖手工特征工程或计算密集的后分类流程，导致处理速度慢、光谱相似异常类别易混淆。

Method: 1) 从Sentinel-2影像中构建包含5个物理可解释指数的紧凑特征空间；2) 采用改进的VM-UNet-v2网络提取水体异常响应特征（WARFs），捕获空间-光谱特征；3) 设计多球对比损失函数，优化类别特定决策边界，压缩类内特征同时增大光谱相似类别的类间距离。

Result: 平均F1分数0.8789，mIoU 0.7932，10000 km²场景推理时间仅33秒，支持大规模高效推理。

Conclusion: DMSDB方法在高精度与快速推理之间取得了良好平衡，适用于地面或快速环境监测，能够支持对水体干扰的及时和类别特异性响应。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。该论文本身就是遥感应用论文，可直接用于遥感领域。改进方向：1) 可扩展到其他遥感数据源（如Landsat、高分系列、Sentinel-1 SAR等），增强时空连续性；2) 5维特征空间可引入更多时序特征（如NDVI时序变化率）以提升动态异常检测能力；3) 多球对比损失函数可结合弱监督或半监督学习框架，减少对标注样本的依赖；4) 可尝试轻量化骨干网络（如MobileNet系列）进一步压缩推理时间，适配星载边缘计算场景。

Abstract (英文): The increasing frequency of water anomalies poses severe threats to aquatic ecosystem stability, water resource security, and socioeconomic sustainability. Rapid and accurate identification of these events is critical for early warning and informed environmental decision-making. However, existing type identification methods often fail to balance high precision with rapid inference since many depend on hand-crafted feature engineering or computationally intensive post-classification procedures that slow processing and increase confusion among anomalies with similar spectral characteristics. Therefore, in this study, a deep multisphere decision boundaries (DMSDB) method for unified, fine-grained identification of diverse water anomalies is developed. The method first involves constructing a compact 5-dimensional feature space by deriving physically interpretable indices from Sentinel-2 imagery. Then, a modified VM-UNet-v2 network is employed to extract water anomaly response features (WARFs) that capture the spatial–spectral characteristics of each anomaly. Finally, a multi-sphere-contrast loss function optimizes class-specific decision boundaries, compacting intraclass features while increasing the separation between spectrally similar anomaly categories. The validation results demonstrate that DMSDB achieves an average F1 score of 0.8789 and an mIoU of 0.7932, enabling efficient large-scale inference, and completing classification over a 10,000 km2 scene within 33 s. These results highlight the method’s potential for effective or ground-based rapid environmental monitoring, supporting timely and category-specific responses to aquatic disturbances.

### [184] [Consistent-Innovation-Aided Distributed Cooperative Localization for Multi-UAV Navigation in GNSS-Denied Environments](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18142286)
*Zhikuan Hou,Chao Xue,S T Chen,Chuan Xu,Changhui Jiang,Jiabao Niu*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文针对GNSS拒止环境下多无人机协同导航的通信与计算负担问题，提出了一种基于一致性创新辅助的分布式协同定位方法。该方法以捷联惯导为参考，利用超宽带测距作为协同约束，通过构建保守的创新协方差近似实现分布式量测更新，避免了全局交叉协方差的显式传播。在联邦滤波框架下融合高度、地磁和场景匹配子滤波器。仿真结果表明，相比非协同方法，位置、速度和偏航角RMSE分别降低27.14%、21.90%和9.68%；相比精确交叉协方差基线，定位精度相当但通信量减少约91.44%；在20%丢包率下误差仍保持有界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有集中式协同定位和基于精确交叉协方差的分布式方法需要全局状态管理或显式传播节点间交叉协方差，导致通信和计算负担沉重，难以适用于通信受限的多无人机集群协同定位场景。

Method: 提出一致性创新辅助的分布式协同定位方法：各节点仅维护本地状态与协方差，通过构建保守的创新协方差近似进行分布式量测更新，避免全局交叉协方差传播；与高度、地磁和场景匹配子滤波器通过自适应矢量信息分配的联邦滤波框架融合；采用捷联惯导作为参考源，节点间超宽带测距作为协同约束。

Result: 相比非协同方法，位置、速度和偏航角RMSE分别降低27.14%、21.90%和9.68%；相比精确交叉协方差基线，定位精度相当，通信量减少约91.44%；在20%丢包率下误差保持有界。

Conclusion: 所提方法在保证定位精度的前提下显著降低了通信负担，且在丢包环境下具有鲁棒性，适用于通信受限的无人机集群协同定位工程应用。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。该文提出的分布式协同定位方法可直接应用于遥感无人机集群在GNSS拒止环境下的协同导航。具体交叉方案：(1) 将超宽带测距约束替换为遥感图像间的视觉特征匹配或SAR图像匹配作为协同观测量；(2) 利用遥感影像（如正射影像）作为场景匹配子滤波器的先验地图，提升绝对定位精度；(3) 在遥感无人机集群执行大范围测绘任务时，采用该分布式联邦滤波框架降低机间通信需求，提升集群续航与作业效率；(4) 可将地磁匹配扩展为多光谱/高光谱地物特征匹配，增强环境适应性。

Abstract (英文): Cooperative localization provides a promising solution for multi-UAV navigation in GNSS-denied environments. However, centralized cooperative localization and exact cross-covariance-based distributed methods usually require global state management or explicit propagation of inter-node cross-covariance, resulting in heavy communication and computational burdens. To address this problem, this paper proposes a consistent-innovation-aided distributed cooperative localization method for multi-glider UAV swarms. The method uses a strapdown inertial navigation system as the reference source and introduces inter-node ultra-wideband ranging as cooperative constraints. Each node maintains only its local state and covariance, while a conservative innovation covariance approximation is constructed to perform distributed measurement updates without explicitly propagating global cross-covariance. The cooperative localization sub-filter is further integrated with altitude, geomagnetic, and scene-matching sub-filters through a federated filtering framework with adaptive vector information allocation. A GNSS-denied multi-glider release simulation is established to compare the proposed method with non-cooperative localization, centralized cooperative localization, and an exact-cross-covariance distributed baseline. The results show that the proposed method reduces the position, velocity, and yaw RMSEs by 27.14%, 21.90%, and 9.68%, respectively, compared with the non-cooperative method. Compared with the exact-cross-covariance baseline, the proposed method achieves comparable localization accuracy while reducing communication traffic by approximately 91.44%. Packet-loss experiments further show that the proposed method maintains bounded errors under a 20% packet loss rate, demonstrating improved robustness and engineering feasibility for communication-constrained UAV swarm localization.

Abstract (英文): Since the late 1970s, during the period of reform and opening-up, China has emerged as one of the fastest-urbanizing countries in the world. It is therefore crucial to elucidate the pattern of urban 3D morphological change and to investigate the factors that influence these changes. This study proposed a novel method of filtering new buildings using the ALOS and GBH building height data, combined with statistical data and panel data, focusing on spatial-temporal variations and their driving factors of 3D building morphological changes between 2002 and 2020 for 11 prefecture-level cities and 2 municipalities in the Beijing–Tianjin–Hebei (BTH) region. Our findings indicate that the 3D morphological change mechanisms of the same types of cities in the BTH region are similar. ### [186] [DWFSeg: A Dynamic Multiscale Feature Fusion and Dual Attention-Enhanced Network for High-Precision Water Body Segmentation Based on Super-Resolution Remote Sensing Imagery](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18142271)
*Z Li,Bingjie Liang,Jianzhong Guo,N Li,Weiran Luo,Baowei Zhang,Jiali Guo,Weizhen Zhang,Yan Zhou,Y ouzhong Guo,YJ Li*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出DWFSeg网络，结合Real-ESRGAN超分辨率重建和动态权重融合SegFormer架构，实现高精度遥感水体分割，在自建SID和公开GID数据集上分别达到98.08%和96.14%的总体精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 遥感影像在水体监测中面临空间分辨率与时间覆盖的权衡，现有水体分割方法在复杂水文环境下存在水陆边界模糊、多尺度水体特征捕获困难等问题。

Method: 首先采用Real-ESRGAN将中分辨率影像超分辨率重建至2.5m；构建DWFSeg网络，包含MixVision Transformer编码器和多尺度解码架构，提出动态多尺度特征融合(DMFF)机制自适应分配融合权重，以及双注意力增强(DAE)模块强化判别特征并抑制背景噪声。

Result: 在自建SID和公开GID数据集上，总体精度分别达到98.08%和96.14%，在多项定量指标上优于代表性基准模型，同时保持有竞争力的推理效率和良好的分割稳定性。消融实验验证了各组件的有效性和必要性。

Conclusion: DWFSeg为精细化水资源评估和可持续流域管理提供了可靠的技术方案。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。该论文本身就是遥感水体分割的完整解决方案。改进方向：(1) DMFF机制可进一步引入时序信息，对多时相水体动态变化进行融合分析；(2) DAE模块可扩展为三维注意力以适配高光谱或多模态遥感数据；(3) Real-ESRGAN的预训练策略可针对水体边缘特征进行领域自适应微调；(4) 可结合SAR影像进行多云雨环境下的多源融合水体分割；(5) 解码器部分可引入边缘监督分支以进一步优化水陆边界。

Abstract (英文): Remote sensing imagery provides a primary data source for large-scale surface water body monitoring, which is crucial for quantifying climate-related hydrological impacts, supporting flood control, and sustaining integrated water resource management. However, remote sensing images generally face the trade-off between spatial resolution and temporal coverage. To address this issue, the Real-ESRGAN super-resolution algorithm is employed to reconstruct temporally continuous, wide-coverage medium-resolution imagery to a 2.5 m resolution, effectively improving its capability to identify sub-pixel river boundaries. Water body segmentation (WBS) is an effective method for fine-detail surface water extraction. Nonetheless, when applied in complex hydrological environments, it still faces several limitations, such as ambiguous delineation of land–water boundaries and the difficulty in capturing multiscale water body characteristics. To address these issues, a Dynamic Weight Fusion SegFormer (DWFSeg) network is constructed, integrating a MixVision Transformer (MVT) encoder with a multiscale decoding architecture. Specifically, a Dynamic Multiscale Feature Fusion (DMFF) mechanism is proposed, which adaptively assigns semantic-guided fusion weights to multiscale feature water bodies. Furthermore, the Dual Attention-Enhanced (DAE) module strengthens discriminative essential features and suppresses background noise in both channel and spatial dimensions. Evaluated on a self-constructed super-resolution imagery dataset (SID) and the public GID, DWFSeg achieves overall accuracies of 98.08% and 96.14%, respectively. It outperforms representative benchmark models across multiple quantitative metrics, while maintaining competitive inference efficiency and favorable segmentation stability. Ablation studies verify the effectiveness and necessity of each proposed component. The presented network provides a reliable technical solution and supports refined water resource evaluation and sustainable watershed management.

</details>


### [187] [A Multi-Stage Outlier Removal Method for Point Clouds with High Outlier Ratio](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18142289)
*Zihan Meng,Chengzhi Qu,Pengyu Chen,Yaji Tang*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种针对高异常点比例点云的多阶段异常点去除方法MORPH，通过局部可达密度与密度峰值聚类粗去除、结构自适应精化、以及结合尺度一致性与局部平面残差得分的补全策略，在合成与真实点云数据上实现了鲁棒的异常点去除并更好保留了有效几何结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LiDAR点云通常含有大量异常点，严重降低下游处理性能。现有方法在高异常点比例情况下性能显著下降，因此需要一种能有效处理高污染率点云的鲁棒异常点去除方法。

Method: 提出多阶段异常点去除方法MORPH：1）利用局部可达密度结合密度峰值聚类粗去除明显异常点，保留全局结构骨架；2）结构自适应精化阶段生成不完整点云和候选点；3）提出结合成对尺度一致性与局部平面残差得分的补全策略，从候选点中识别内点，并用内点填充不完整点云完成异常点去除。

Abstract (英文): Point clouds acquired by LiDAR typically contain a large number of outliers, which can substantially degrade downstream processing. Existing outlier removal methods suffer from significant performance degradation on point clouds with high outlier ratios. In this study, we propose a multi-stage outlier removal method called MORPH for point clouds with high outlier ratios. The proposed method first employs local reachability density combined with density-peak clustering to coarsely eliminate prominent outliers while preserving the global structural skeleton. Subsequently, a structure-adaptive refinement stage is introduced to generate incomplete point clouds and candidate points. Finally, a completion strategy that integrates pairwise scale consistency with local plane residual score is proposed to identify inlier points from the candidate points. Outlier removal is completed by using the obtained inlier points to fill the incomplete point clouds. Experimental results on synthetic high-contamination point clouds and real-world scanned point clouds demonstrate that MORPH achieves robust outlier removal performance while better preserving valid geometric structures.

### [188] [Synergistic SAR and Wide-Swath Interferometric Altimetry Observations for Estimating Flood Dynamics and Water Storage Variations in East Dongting Lake](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18142283)
*Yixuan Li,Yunhua Zhang,Dong Li,Jiayi Song*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一种结合SAR（Sentinel-1）和宽刈幅干涉测高（SWOT/KaRIn）的集成框架，用于重建2024年东洞庭湖洪水事件的时空演变与蓄水动态。通过提出的自适应空间约束模糊C均值（AS-FCM）算法提取高精度淹没范围（OA=93.6%，IoU=0.89），结合SWOT-derived水位与实测数据建立经验水位-面积关系（R²=0.937），估算峰值阶段累积蓄水变化约10.7 km³，揭示了湖泊洪泛区的缓冲作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大型河流-湖泊系统中洪水动态的精确表征仍具挑战，现有方法难以同时捕捉快速变化水文条件下淹没范围和水面高程（WSE）的时空变化。

Method: 1) 基于Sentinel-1 SAR影像，提出自适应空间约束模糊C均值（AS-FCM）算法提取高分辨率淹没范围；2) 利用SWOT/KaRIn宽刈幅干涉测高技术获取二维WSE观测；3) 通过SAR淹没范围与SWOT+实测水位数据建立经验水位-面积关系（R²=0.937），重建逐日洪水动态并估算累积蓄水量变化。

Result: AS-FCM算法性能最优（OA=93.6%, IoU=0.89, Kappa=0.87）；SWOT-derived WSE与实测数据相关系数达0.988；峰值阶段累积蓄水变化约10.7 km³。

Conclusion: 该集成框架在复杂河湖系统的洪水监测与水文蓄量评估中展现出强大潜力，揭示了东洞庭湖洪泛区在2024年洪水事件中的缓冲作用。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。作为遥感洪水监测论文，可改进方向：1) AS-FCM算法可进一步引入时序SAR信息（如Sentinel-1密集时序）增强动态变化区域的分类稳定性；2) 可尝试融合更高分辨率光学数据（如Landsat/Sentinel-2）对AS-FCM结果进行精细化校正；3) SWOT数据与SAR的时空匹配可推广至其他大型湖泊-河流系统（如鄱阳湖、洞庭湖全湖）；4) 可引入深度学习（如U-Net）替代AS-FCM以提升复杂下垫面下的泛化能力。

Abstract (英文): Accurate characterization of flood dynamics in large river–lake systems remains challenging due to the difficulty of simultaneously capturing inundation extent and water surface elevation (WSE) variations under rapidly changing hydrological conditions. This study develops an integrated Synthetic Aperture Radar (SAR) and wide-swath interferometric altimetry framework to reconstruct the spatiotemporal evolution and storage dynamics of the 2024 flood event in the East Dongting Lake system, China. Sentinel-1 SAR imagery is utilized to derive high-resolution inundation extent, while the Surface Water and Ocean Topography (SWOT) mission, equipped with the Ka-band Radar Interferometer (KaRIn), provides two-dimensional WSE observations. To improve SAR-based flood extraction in heterogeneous floodplain environments, an Adaptive Spatially-Constrained Fuzzy C-Means (AS-FCM) algorithm is proposed by incorporating adaptive spatial regularization and structure-aware neighborhood weighting. Quantitative evaluation demonstrates that the proposed method achieves the highest performance among the evaluated conventional approaches, with an Overall Accuracy of 93.6%, an Intersection over Union of 0.89, and a Kappa coefficient of 0.87. The multi-temporal inundation sequence reveals a distinct flood evolution pattern characterized by rapid expansion during the rising stage and gradual recession during the post-peak period. SWOT-derived WSE observations exhibit strong agreement with synchronous in situ measurements after bias adjustment, with a correlation coefficient of 0.988. By integrating SAR-derived inundation extent with temporally matched water-level observations constrained by bias-adjusted SWOT and in situ gauge data, an empirical WSE–area relationship (R2=0.937) is established to reconstruct daily flood dynamics and estimate cumulative water storage variation. The results indicate that the East Dongting Lake floodplain played an important buffering role during the 2024 flood event, with cumulative storage variation reaching approximately 10.7km3 during the peak stage. Overall, the proposed framework demonstrates strong potential for flood monitoring and hydrological storage assessment in complex river–lake systems.

### [189] [Spectral Variability and Prediction of Nitrogen, Phosphorus, and Potassium in Fresh Sugarcane (Saccharum officinarum) Leaves by VIS–NIR–SWIR Spectroscopy](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132260)
*Marta Laura de Souza Alexandre,Izabelle de Lima e Lima,Carlos Augusto Alves Cardoso Silva,Mateus Lima Silva,Rodnei Rizzo,Peterson Ricardo Fiorio*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本研究利用甘蔗叶片VIS-NIR-SWIR光谱（350-2500 nm），结合PLSR方法预测氮、磷、钾含量，发现氮（R²=0.83）和磷（R²=0.80）预测效果良好，而钾（最大R²=0.25）难以预测，且光谱变异性受季节和物候期主导而非品种。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 评估可见光-近红外-短波红外叶片光谱技术预测甘蔗氮、磷、钾含量的潜力，并探究不同生长季节、物候阶段和品种间光谱变异对预测性能的影响。

Method: 使用FieldSpec 3光谱辐射计获取350-2500 nm光谱数据，经MSC、平滑和一阶Savitzky-Golay导数预处理；通过Spearman相关识别诊断波段；采用偏最小二乘回归（PLSR）建立预测模型；利用PCA分析光谱变异来源。

Result: 2023/2024季光谱均质性高但预测性能较低；2024/2025季光谱异质性高，氮预测R²=0.83（RMSE=0.78 g kg⁻¹），磷预测R²=0.80（RMSE=0.10 g kg⁻¹），钾预测最大R²=0.25。光谱变异主要受季节和物候期影响，品种效应为次要因素。

Conclusion: 叶片光谱技术对甘蔗新鲜叶片氮和磷含量预测潜力显著，但模型鲁棒性依赖于数据集的光谱变异程度；钾因其离子特性及与光谱特征缺乏显著相关性而难以预测。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。该光谱分析方法可直接迁移至遥感领域：(1) 将地面FieldSpec光谱与卫星/无人机高光谱数据（如PRISMA、EnMAP、Sentinel-2）进行光谱重采样匹配，构建跨尺度预测模型；(2) 针对遥感影像中混合像元问题，引入光谱解混算法提升营养元素反演精度；(3) 钾预测瓶颈可通过结合雷达数据（如Sentinel-1）或热红外数据，利用水分与钾的生理关联间接建模；(4) 将PLSR与机器学习（如随机森林、CNN）结合，利用遥感影像的多时相信息增强模型时空泛化能力。

Abstract (英文): This study evaluated the potential of VIS–NIR–SWIR leaf spectroscopy to predict N, P, and K contents in sugarcane, considering spectral variability across two growing seasons (2023/2024 and 2024/2025), phenological stages, and five varieties. Spectral signatures (350–2500 nm) were acquired using a FieldSpec 3 spectroradiometer and processed with MSC, smoothing, and the first Savitzky–Golay derivative. Diagnostic bands were identified by Spearman correlation, and prediction was performed using partial least squares regression (PLSR). PCA showed that spectral variability was driven mainly by seasonal and phenological factors, whereas varietal effects were secondary. In 2023/2024, greater spectral homogeneity was associated with lower predictive performance. In 2024/2025, greater spectral heterogeneity was associated with improved prediction for N (R2 = 0.83; RMSE = 0.78 g kg−1) and P (R2 = 0.80; RMSE = 0.10 g kg−1). Potassium remained the most challenging nutrient to predict (maximum R2 = 0.25), mainly due to its ionic nature and the resulting lack of significant correlation with specific VIS, NIR, and SWIR spectral features. These results indicate strong potential for predicting N and P in fresh sugarcane leaves, although model robustness depends on the extent of spectral variability in the dataset.

Method: 提出PAST三阶段框架：1) K-Shape标签质量控制；2) 并行双分支分类——时序分支实现Sentinel-1/Sentinel-2无插值跨模态物候融合，图像分支提取0.8m高分辨率影像冠层纹理特征；3) 决策级融合。

Abstract (英文): High-accuracy parcel-level agricultural mapping is fundamental to precision agriculture. However, in fragmented agricultural regions of the Yangtze River Delta, identifying cropping patterns at the parcel level faces two compounding challenges: asynchronous multi-source observations and mixed-pixel effects in small parcels. When historical archive records are used as training labels, inter-annual cropping pattern changes further introduce label noise that undermines model reliability. To address these challenges and the label noise issue, we propose PAST (Parcel-level Asynchronous SpatioTemporal), a parcel-level cropping pattern classification framework comprising three stages: K-Shape-based label quality control, parallel dual-branch classification, and decision-level fusion. PAST employs a dual-branch architecture: the temporal branch achieves interpolation-free cross-modal phenological fusion of Sentinel-1 and Sentinel-2 data, while the image branch extracts canopy texture features from 0.8 m high-resolution imagery to partially address mixed-pixel interference. Experiments in a typical fragmented agricultural region of the Yangtze River Delta demonstrate that PAST achieves an overall F1 score of 0.926 and a small-parcel F1 score of 0.906, outperforming mainstream time-series baselines. These results confirm that combining K-Shape label quality control at the data level with a dual-branch interference-robust architecture at the model level provides a complete integrated three-stage pipeline for fine-grained crop mapping under weakly supervised historical archive label conditions.

Method: 提出WCMNet，包含两个核心模块：(1) MWA模块，在小波域中对齐低频风格信息同时保留高频方向边缘结构；(2) GLMB模块，CNN分支捕获细粒度局部细节，Mamba分支建模长距离上下文，通过自适应门控融合机制融合两类特征。

Abstract (英文): With the increasing diversity of remote sensing image acquisition conditions and imaging scenarios, building extraction models often experience significant performance degradation in cross-dataset applications due to variations in sensors and scene characteristics. Improving their cross-domain generalization ability has therefore become a critical research problem. To address the challenges of appearance style discrepancy and feature distribution shift in cross-domain building extraction, this paper proposes WCMNet, a wavelet-guided and CNN–Mamba hybrid network for unsupervised domain adaptation in building extraction. Specifically, a Mamba Wavelet Alignment (MWA) module is designed to align low-frequency style information in the wavelet domain while preserving directional high-frequency edge structures, thereby mitigating cross-domain appearance discrepancies and reducing structural degradation during domain translation. In addition, a Global–Local Mamba Block (GLMB) is developed to jointly model local textures and global semantic dependencies. In GLMB, the CNN branch captures fine-grained local details and boundary cues, while the Mamba branch models long-range contextual information; an adaptive gated fusion mechanism further integrates the two types of features. Experimental results on six cross-domain transfer tasks across the WHU, Massachusetts, and Potsdam datasets demonstrate that WCMNet consistently outperforms existing state-of-the-art domain adaptation methods. In particular, WCMNet achieves an average IoU of 65.13% and an average BIoU of 74.80% across all transfer settings, with improvements of up to 27.35 percentage points in IoU and 38.32 percentage points in BIoU compared with the strongest competing methods. These results demonstrate that the proposed MWA and GLMB effectively improve building completeness, boundary delineation accuracy, and cross-domain robustness.

### [192] [RadarEchoMamba: A Fast, High-Fidelity Pyramidal Bidirectional Mamba Model for Radar Echo Extrapolation](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18142287)
*耿焕同,Zhanpeng Shi,Jinzhong Min,Fangli Wu,Han Zhao*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 提出RadarEchoMamba，一种基于Mamba模型的雷达回波外推框架，采用金字塔架构、双向时空Mamba骨干和时空先验模块，解决传统模型误差累积、时序信息丢失和计算复杂度高的问题，在华南和上海-2020数据集上取得较好效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于RNN、CNN和Transformer的雷达回波外推模型存在误差累积、时序信息丢失和二次计算复杂度的问题，导致预测模糊和精细细节失真，亟需更高效的解决方案。

Method: 提出RadarEchoMamba框架：1）金字塔架构捕获多尺度特征；2）双向时空Mamba骨干建模历史观测窗口内的时空依赖关系；3）时空先验模块利用输入序列指导解码阶段的高分辨率特征重建，生成细节丰富的预测。

Result: 在华南和上海-2020数据集上验证有效性；与强Transformer基线相比，轻量级变体参数量更少、推理延迟更低；在华南数据集上SSIM提升、LPIPS降低，视觉保真度指标更优。

Conclusion: RadarEchoMamba在保持竞争性预测质量的同时，以更低的计算开销实现了更好的视觉保真度，有效缓解了传统外推模型的预测模糊问题。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。该论文本身就是遥感领域（天气雷达降水临近预报）的工作，可直接作为遥感应用。改进方向：1）引入多波段雷达数据（如双偏振参量）丰富输入特征；2）结合地形高程等地理先验信息增强时空先验模块；3）扩展到多雷达拼图场景，处理区域间的空间一致性；4）引入物理约束（如大气运动方程）与数据驱动方法结合，提升物理可解释性；5）探索将Mamba用于其他遥感时序预测任务（如海冰变化、植被物候监测）。

Abstract (英文): Radar echo extrapolation is a fundamental task in precipitation nowcasting. However, existing models based on RNNs, CNNs, and Transformers are often constrained by error accumulation, the loss of temporal information, and quadratic computational complexity. Consequently, these limitations can lead to prediction blurring and the distortion of fine-grained details in extrapolated radar images. To address these challenges, we propose RadarEchoMamba, a novel extrapolation framework built on the efficient Mamba model. RadarEchoMamba uses a pyramidal architecture to capture multi-scale features, and its core is a Bidirectional Spatiotemporal Mamba backbone that models dependencies within the observed historical input window. Furthermore, we introduce a spatiotemporal prior module driven by the input sequence to guide the reconstruction of high-resolution features during the decoding phase. This design enables the model to generate detail-rich predictions, improving upon the blurring issues prevalent in traditional extrapolation models. Experimental results on the South China and Shanghai-2020 datasets show the effectiveness of our method. Compared with strong Transformer-based baselines, the lightweight variant uses fewer parameters and achieves lower measured inference latency, while maintaining competitive prediction quality. Its main advantages are observed in visual-fidelity metrics, with improved SSIM and reduced LPIPS on the South China dataset.

</details>


### [193] [Cross-Platform Comparison of Marine Boundary Layer Cloud and Drizzle Properties over the Southern Ocean Using Airborne, Shipborne, and Satellite Observations](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132262)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 南大洋海洋边界层云对辐射和降水有强烈影响，但不同观测平台对其垂直结构和微物理特性的认知存在较大不确定性，缺乏系统性的跨平台对比研究。

Method: 基于SOCRATES飞机实测雨滴谱开发经验性反射率-微物理反演框架，将该框架应用于MARCUS船基M-WACR云雷达和CloudSat CPR雷达的反射率观测，反演云和毛毛雨的垂直廓线（数浓度、有效半径、液态水含量），并进行三平台交叉对比。

Result: 三个平台在云边界高度和反演微物理特性上总体一致；CloudSat因粗垂直分辨率和低反射率灵敏度存在较大偏差，尤其对500米以下低云探测能力有限；观测的垂直结构与凝结增长、夹卷和碰并过程一致。

Conclusion: 三个平台在云和毛毛雨特性上表现出广泛一致性，同时揭示了仪器灵敏度、垂直分辨率和采样差异对云边界检测和微物理反演的影响。

Abstract (英文): Marine boundary layer (MBL) clouds strongly influence radiation and precipitation over the Southern Ocean (SO), yet their vertical structures and microphysical properties remain poorly constrained across observational platforms. This study compares macrophysical and microphysical properties of single-layer, liquid-dominant MBL clouds below 3 km using aircraft observations from the SO Clouds, Radiation, Aerosol Transport Experimental Study (SOCRATES), ship-based observations from Measurements of Aerosols, Radiation, and Clouds over the SO (MARCUS), and satellite observations from CloudSat. An empirical reflectivity–microphysics retrieval framework developed from in situ droplet size distributions (DSDs) measured during SOCRATES was applied to MARCUS M-WACR and CloudSat CPR reflectivity observations to retrieve vertical profiles of number concentration (N), effective radius (re), and liquid water content (LWC) for cloud and drizzle particles. Cloud boundary heights and retrieved microphysical properties show broad agreement across the three platforms within the limitations imposed by instrumental sensitivity, sampling differences, and retrieval uncertainties. However, CloudSat CPR observations exhibit larger deviations because of their coarser vertical resolution and lower reflectivity sensitivity, including limited detection of low clouds below ~500 m. The observed vertical structures are consistent with condensational growth, entrainment, and collision–coalescence processes. Overall, the results demonstrate broad consistency in cloud and drizzle properties across the three platforms, while highlighting the impacts of instrumental sensitivity, vertical resolution, and sampling differences on cloud boundary detection and microphysical retrievals.

### [194] [Attention-Guided Generative Adversarial Network for False Alarm-Resistant Change Detection in Remote Sensing Orthophotos](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18142290)
*Y HU,Zheng Ji,Wei Liu,Yichao Li*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出Attention-GAN，一种基于注意力引导的条件对抗框架，用于正射影像变化检测中的虚假警报抑制。通过引入多尺度空间注意力、通道注意力和PatchGAN判别器，并结合受控几何与辐射扰动生成的负样本训练策略，在三个公开数据集上取得竞争性结果，并将误检率降低至4.9%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实际多时相正射影像即使经过标准预处理，仍存在几何与辐射不一致性（如微小配准误差、建筑物位移、阴影移动、光照差异），这些“伪变化”会产生类似边缘的响应，导致大量虚假警报，增加人工核查成本并降低变化检测结果的可靠性。

Method: 提出Attention-GAN，包含三个核心组件：1）多尺度空间注意力模块和通道注意力模块，用于增强真实变化特征并抑制虚假响应；2）PatchGAN判别器，用于区分真实变化和伪变化；3）扰动负样本训练策略，对未变化图像对施加受控几何和辐射扰动，并分配全零变化掩码作为训练数据。

Result: 在LEVIR-CD、WHU-CD和DSIFN-CD数据集上F1分数分别达91.2%、92.45%和93.18%，优于或接近代表性基线。消融实验中，扰动负样本验证对上的误检率降至4.9%。重复实验统计和消融结果表明，所提训练策略主要通过减少虚假警报来提升鲁棒性。

Conclusion: 受控扰动作为一种可复现的方式能够有效训练和评估变化检测模型对虚假警报的抵抗能力，但更广泛的多视角、季节性及跨传感器畸变下的验证仍是必要的。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。本文本身就是遥感变化检测论文。改进方向：1）引入更多类型的扰动（如大气条件变化、传感器MTF差异）以增强泛化能力；2）将注意力机制扩展为可变形注意力或跨尺度 Transformer结构以更好地处理大尺度建筑位移；3）结合多模态数据（如SAR与光学）的配准误差建模，将扰动负样本策略推广到异源变化检测场景。

Abstract (英文): Orthophoto change detection is used to find real land cover changes in urban monitoring, disaster assessment, and environmental management. In practice, however, multi-temporal orthophotos are rarely identical in geometry and radiometry even after standard preprocessing. Small residual misregistration, local building displacement, shadow movement, and illumination differences can produce edge-like responses that look like change but do not correspond to any land cover transition. These false alarms increase manual checking costs and reduce the reliability of change maps. This study addresses that practical problem by proposing an attention-guided conditional adversarial framework, named Attention-GAN, for false alarm-resistant orthophoto change detection. The aim is not to detect small perturbations as changes but to detect real land cover changes while suppressing responses to nuisance variations that should be treated as unchanged. The framework integrates a multi-scale spatial attention module, a channel attention module, and a PatchGAN discriminator. It also introduces perturbation-negative training pairs, where controlled geometric and radiometric perturbations are applied to unchanged image pairs and assigned all-zero change masks. Experiments on LEVIR-CD, WHU-CD, and DSIFN-CD show competitive or moderately higher accuracy than the selected representative baselines, with F1 scores of 91.2%, 92.45%, and 93.18%, respectively. In the ablation experiment, the false change rate on perturbation-negative validation pairs is reduced to 4.9%. Repeated-run statistics and ablation results indicate that the proposed training strategy mainly improves robustness by reducing false alarms under the evaluated perturbation range. The results support the use of controlled nuisance perturbations as a reproducible way to train and evaluate false alarm resistance, while broader validation under real multi-view, seasonal, and cross-sensor distortions remains necessary.
