<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无人机航拍人体检测在灾后救援中至关重要，但深度学习模型对标注数据的数量和多样性高度敏感，现有数据增强策略在视角变化上创新有限，无法充分丰富训练数据集的多样性。

Method: 通过摄影测量技术重建三维人体模型，将其置于可控渲染环境中，生成覆盖广泛仰角和相机角度的合成图像，扩充训练集（4000基线+3000合成图像），训练定制CNN深度卷积分类器进行人体/非人体二分类。

Result: 在五轮独立训练中，摄影测量增强使分类准确率从88.06±0.97%提升至91.08±1.03%（提升3.02个百分点）；结合标准增强（旋转、平移、缩放、翻转）后达到95.21±0.61%（提升7.15个百分点），且精确率、召回率、F1分数均有一致提升。

Conclusion: 基于摄影测量的数据增强方法是一种实用且有效的方案，能显著提升无人机人体检测管线的性能，尤其适用于需要快速可靠识别的灾后场景。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：92%。本文本身就是遥感应用论文（无人机航拍），改进方案：（1）可引入更多样化的背景纹理（废墟、植被、水体等）以增强模型在灾后复杂环境中的泛化能力；（2）可结合多光谱或热红外数据，利用3D模型生成多模态合成图像；（3）可扩展至时序视角，生成连续飞行轨迹下的动态数据增强；（4）可将该方法迁移至其他遥感目标检测任务（如车辆、船只检测）的合成数据生成。

Abstract (英文): Recently, deep learning has enabled unmanned aerial vehicles (UAVs) to detect human bodies in aerial imagery, which is of particular importance in post-disaster situations such as floods and storms. Yet progress in this domain remains constrained by a familiar obstacle: the shortage of annotated training data. Neural networks, while powerful, are highly sensitive to data volume and diversity. Existing augmentation strategies help reduce this gap but typically introduce only incremental novelty, especially with respect to viewpoint variation, thereby limiting dataset richness. In this work, we propose a complementary strategy that leverages three-dimensional human models reconstructed via photogrammetric techniques. By situating these models within a controlled rendering environment, we generate synthetic imagery across a broad range of elevations and camera angles—perspectives that are rarely captured in conventional UAV datasets. These additions are designed to increase both the variability and the resilience of the training corpus. To evaluate the contribution of this approach, a custom CNN deep convolutional neural classifier was trained and benchmarked on a UAV human vs. non-human patch dataset of 4000 baseline images (128 × 128 px; 2800 train, 600 validation, 600 test), expanded with 3000 photogrammetry-derived synthetic patches (balanced by class) to 7000 total images for the 3DG setting. The primary metric was classification accuracy on the held-out test set, consistent with patch-level evaluation practice; detection-style metrics such as AP/IoU were not applicable to this binary classification protocol. Averaged over five independent training runs, the proposed augmentation improved classification accuracy by 3.02 percentage points over the baseline (88.06 ± 0.97% → 91.08 ± 1.03%), with consistent gains in precision, recall, and F1-score. When combined with standard augmentations (rotation, translation, scaling, flipping), accuracy reached 95.21 ± 0.61%, a gain of 7.15 percentage points over the baseline. These results suggest that photogrammetry-based augmentation offers a practical and effective enhancement for UAV-based human detection pipelines where timely, reliable identification is critical.

Abstract (英文): Real-time monitoring of cotton above-ground biomass (AGB) is crucial for monitoring crop growth and optimizing management practices. Spectral features, vegetation indices (VIs), and Gray Level Co-occurrence Matrix (GLCM) texture metrics were extracted and organized into three scenarios: RGB + MS, RGB-only, and MS-only. Recursive feature elimination with cross-validation (RFECV) was applied for feature selection, and six machine learning models were evaluated using both baseline and selected feature sets. Results showed that model performance was strongly influenced by growth stage, sensor configuration, and feature composition. Accuracy was highest at the seedling and squaring stages and decreased at flowering due to canopy complexity and spectral saturation. MS-only and fused features generally performed best at the seedling stage, while RGB-only features were competitive or superior at the squaring stage, highlighting the importance of high-resolution structural information. At flowering, fused RGB–MS features provided the most stable performance, although improvements were limited. RFECV exhibited stage-dependent behavior, improving performance mainly at early growth stages but showing inconsistent benefits later. SHAP analysis revealed a shift from texture-dominated predictors at the seedling stage to balanced feature contributions at squaring and vegetation index (VIs) dominance at flowering. Overall, cotton AGB estimation is a stage-dependent process requiring adaptive sensor and feature selection strategies.

*Yulong Xue,Leping Chen,Daoxiang An*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出一种联合统计滤波框架，用于解决HoloSAR 3D重建中因角度相关散射响应导致的动态范围失衡问题。该方法融合变异系数、子孔径间相关性和谱熵，结合自适应判别权重、高斯混合模型贝叶斯阈值和百分位匹配能量均衡变换，有效压缩动态范围、抑制背景噪声并恢复弱目标结构。在Ku波段无人机圆迹SAR数据上，TBR提升至11.2 dB，背景抑制比达-5.2 dB，结构完整性指数提升156%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统HoloSAR通过非相干叠加子孔径断层图像实现360°三维重建，但由于角度相关散射响应，宽角强散射体被重复放大而窄角弱结构被噪声淹没，导致严重的动态范围失衡问题，亟需一种后处理方法来平衡动态范围并恢复弱目标。

Method: 提出联合统计滤波框架：1）融合变异系数(CV)、子孔径间相关性(ISC)和谱熵(SE)三种统计特征，结合自适应判别加权；2）基于高斯混合模型(GMM)的贝叶斯最优阈值进行目标筛选；3）对分类为弱目标的像素，采用百分位匹配能量均衡变换(PM-EBT)自适应缩放能量至主目标参考水平，同时保持相对幅度关系。

Result: 在Ku波段无人机圆迹SAR数据上：TBR提升0.7 dB达到11.2 dB，背景抑制比-5.2 dB，结构完整性指数提升156%至1428.1，动态范围从超过50 dB被有效压缩，场景物理真实性保持(ENL ≈ 7.4×10⁻³)。

Conclusion: 该方法能有效压缩动态范围、抑制背景噪声、恢复传统非相干叠加中丢失的窄角弱结构，生成更完整且可解释的HoloSAR 3D重建结果。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：90%。该方法是纯遥感SAR成像后处理技术。改进方向：1）可将统计特征融合框架推广至其他SAR成像模态（如双基SAR、多基线InSAR）的动态范围压缩；2）GMM贝叶斯阈值可结合深度学习语义分割进一步优化弱目标分类精度；3）百分位匹配变换可引入空间正则化先验（如全变分约束）以增强结构连续性；4）该方法可迁移至光学遥感3D重建（如多视角立体）中的动态范围均衡任务。

Abstract (英文): Holographic synthetic aperture radar (HoloSAR) enables 360° three-dimensional reconstruction by incoherently stacking tomographic subaperture images. However, after conventional subaperture-wise TomoSAR reconstruction and non-coherent integration, the resulting 3D imagery suffers from severe dynamic range imbalance due to angle-dependent scattering responses: wide-angle strong scatterers are repeatedly amplified, whereas narrow-angle weak structures are buried below the noise floor. To address this post-processing challenge, we propose a joint statistical filtering framework operating on the reconstructed subaperture-domain 3D images that fuses the coefficient of variation, inter-subaperture correlation, and spectral entropy with adaptive discriminative-power weighting; target screening is then performed via a Gaussian mixture model-based Bayesian optimal threshold. For pixels classified as weak targets, a percentile-matching energy-balancing transformation is applied to adaptively rescale their energy to the main-target reference level while preserving relative amplitude relationships. Experiments on real-world Ku-band UAV circular SAR data demonstrate that the proposed method effectively compresses the dynamic range, suppresses background noise, and recovers weak narrow-angle structures that are lost in traditional non-coherent superposition, yielding more complete and interpretable HoloSAR 3D reconstructions. Quantitative evaluation on Ku-band UAV circular SAR data demonstrates that the proposed method improves the Target-to-Background Ratio by 0.7 dB (to 11.2 dB), achieves a Background Suppression Ratio of −5.2 dB, increases the Structural Completeness Index by 156% (to 1428.1), and compresses the original dynamic range imbalance, which exceeds 50 dB, while preserving scene physical realism (ENL ≈ 7.4 × 10−3).

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 地震或滑坡后需要救援的人员存活概率随时间快速下降，夜间搜救受限于能见度。卫星遥感可实现夜间广域观测，但空间分辨率不足以识别个体人员。无人机搭载热红外相机可在夜间成像，但缺乏足够的无人机热红外训练数据，且地面与空中视角存在域差距，导致现有模型检测性能不足。

Conclusion: 本文提出的基于Grounding DINO和地面-空中域适配策略的无人机热红外人员检测方法，有效解决了训练数据匮乏和域差距问题，在低热对比和夜间场景下均表现出优异性能。语言引导的语义先验是模型在复杂热噪声环境下保持鲁棒性的关键因素。

Abstract (英文): The survival probability of persons requiring rescue after large-scale earthquakes or landslides decreases rapidly with time, and nighttime search operations are constrained by limited visibility. Satellite remote sensing enables wide-area observation at night, but its limited spatial resolution restricts the identification of individual persons. This study develops an automated method for detecting persons in thermal infrared imagery captured by Unmanned Aerial Vehicles (UAVs) using the deep learning model Grounding DINO. To address the limited availability of Unmanned Aerial Vehicle (UAV)-based training data, thermal infrared imagery captured by fixed-point ground cameras was used for training. Spatial resizing and padding were applied to emulate UAV viewpoints and mitigate the ground-aerial domain gap. The proposed model outperformed the baseline on real-world datasets, with substantial Recall improvements in environments with low thermal contrast. An ablation study confirmed that spatial resizing, padding, and position-based augmentation each contribute progressively to detection performance. A comparison with the lightweight YOLOv8n and DETR-based RT-DETR detectors indicated that the Transformer architecture alone does not account for reliable detection in scenes with complex thermal noise. This robustness instead derives from the language-grounded semantic priors of Grounding DINO. An extended evaluation on nighttime imagery indicated that the proposed approach generalizes to nighttime acquisition.

### [201] [CT-TreeFlow: Probabilistic Groundwater-Potential Mapping Using Remote Sensing-Derived Environmental Predictors in Karst Aquifers](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132258)
*Saeid Pourmorad,Mostafa Kabolizadeh,Rui Ferreira,Samira Abbasi,Luca António Dimuccio*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 提出CT-TreeFlow框架，通过概率建模（而非确定性预测）实现岩溶地下水潜力评估，在扎格罗斯喀斯特系统应用中取得良好性能，并提供不确定性量化和可解释性分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统机器学习方法只能提供确定性预测，缺乏对预测不确定性和水文地质可靠性的信息，难以应对岩溶含水层强烈的空间异质性。

Method: 构建CT-TreeFlow概率框架，集成稀疏概率环境路由、条件密度估计、水文地质约束伪缺失生成、地理结构化空间验证和可解释性驱动解释，使用遥感衍生预测变量、DEM地貌变量、地质构造数据和气候水文指标。

Result: 在GroupKFold空间交叉验证下，平均RMSE为2.737，平均R²为0.852，提供空间显式不确定性估计和概率预测区间；裂缝密度、岩性、排水组织和地形控制的补给条件是主要控制因素。

Conclusion: 概率建模比确定性方法在结构复杂的岩溶环境中能提供更可靠和物理解释性更强的地下水评估，CT-TreeFlow框架可迁移应用于不确定性感知的地下水资源勘探。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。该框架可直接迁移至遥感水文地质领域：1）将遥感衍生的地表参数（如土壤湿度、蒸散发、植被指数）作为概率模型的环境协变量；2）利用InSAR形变数据作为含水层储水变化的空间约束；3）将条件密度估计方法应用于遥感反演的不确定性传递；4）伪缺失生成策略可用于遥感样本不平衡问题的处理。

Abstract (英文): Groundwater-potential assessment in karst aquifers is complicated by pronounced spatial heterogeneity driven by structural permeability, lithological variability, recharge redistribution, and unresolved subsurface conduit connectivity. Although machine-learning approaches have improved regional groundwater mapping, most existing models provide only deterministic predictions and offer limited information on predictive uncertainty and hydrogeological reliability. To address this limitation, we propose CT-TreeFlow. This probabilistic groundwater assessment framework goes beyond conventional machine-learning models by explicitly learning the full conditional probability distribution of groundwater favourability rather than a single deterministic estimate. The framework integrates sparse probabilistic environmental routing, conditional density estimation, hydrogeologically constrained pseudo-absence generation, geographically structured spatial validation, and explainability-driven interpretation within a unified modelling architecture, enabling simultaneous groundwater prediction, uncertainty quantification, and hydrogeological interpretation. The framework was applied to the Zagros karst system in Khuzestan Province, Iran, using remote-sensing-derived environmental predictors, Copernicus DEM-based morphometric variables, geological–structural datasets, and hydroclimatic indicators. Performance was evaluated against LightGBM and XGBoost using GroupKFold spatial cross-validation. CT-TreeFlow achieved a mean RMSE of 2.737 and a mean R2 of 0.852, while also providing spatially explicit uncertainty estimates and probabilistic prediction intervals. Explainability analyses identified fracture density, lithology, drainage organisation, and terrain-controlled recharge conditions as the dominant controls on groundwater favourability. Predicted high-favourability zones showed strong spatial correspondence with major carbonate formations and independent spring–cave inventories, supporting the hydrogeological plausibility of the mapped patterns. These results demonstrate that probabilistic modelling can provide more reliable and physically interpretable groundwater assessments than deterministic approaches in structurally complex karst environments. CT-TreeFlow offers a transferable framework for uncertainty-aware groundwater exploration and regional hydrogeological decision support in heterogeneous aquifer systems.

Abstract (英文): Urban blue–green spaces (UBGSs) serve as irreplaceable ecological infrastructure that underpins ecosystem service provision and human well-being improvement in densely populated urban regions. Based on 10-year (2014–2023) Landsat 8 OLI remote sensing imagery, this paper systematically investigates the temporal–spatial evolutionary characteristics and potential socioeconomic and policy-related associations with UBGS changes in the Shandong Peninsula urban agglomeration (SPUA), a pivotal coastal urban agglomeration in eastern China. The results demonstrate that the total UBGSs in the SPUA exhibited a pronounced increasing trend throughout the study period: the area of urban green spaces (UGSs) expanded from 28,311.66 km2 to 30,194.39 km2, while urban blue spaces (UBSs) grew from 1108.02 km2 to 1699.04 km2. Concurrently, the ecological quality of UGSs has markedly improved, with NDVI showing a significant upward trend in over one-third of the built-up areas, and vegetation greenness in cities such as Binzhou, Jinan, and Zibo increasing by more than 35%. Landscape pattern analysis reveals that the spatial structure of UGSs has transformed from a fragmented and scattered distribution to a centralized and contiguous layout. Specifically, the aggregation index (AI) and largest patch index (LPI) increased overall, while the landscape shape index (LSI) decreased by approximately 18.3%, indicating that the connectivity and structural integrity of urban green spaces have been substantially enhanced. National strategic policies, particularly the outline of ecological protection and high-quality development planning for the Yellow River basin, have effectively alleviated the encroachment pressure of population agglomeration and economic expansion on UBGSs, and played a decisive regulatory role in promoting the structural optimization of blue–green spaces. These findings provide empirical evidence for cross-city collaborative planning and integrated ecological governance of blue–green spaces at the urban agglomeration level, and offer valuable reference for achieving sustainable urban development in other rapidly urbanizing areas.

### [203] [Few-Shot Remote Sensing Scene Classification via Fusion of Zigzag Scanning Feature Sequence and Riemannian Geometric Barycenter Network](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132264)
*Xiliang Chen,Longwei Li,Yufeng Chen,Lei Liu,Zhenyu Wang,M. Liu,X Y Liu,Guobin Zhu*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为ZSFS-RGBN的小样本遥感场景分类方法，通过Zigzag扫描保持特征空间结构，利用ARMA模型和SPD流形进行非欧几何表示，并设计黎曼几何重心网络优化类内紧凑性和类间分离性，在三个公开数据集上取得了优于现有方法的表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 遥感图像存在类内差异大、类间相似性高、背景干扰复杂等问题；传统小样本学习方法在欧氏空间进行特征度量学习，难以捕捉遥感特征的非欧几何分布特性，且忽略了特征图中的空间结构信息。

Method: 1) ResNet12提取深度特征图；2) Zigzag扫描将二维特征图重组为一维特征序列，保留空间局部性和结构连续性；3) ARMA模型建模特征序列的空间依赖关系，并将其状态参数映射到SPD矩阵流形上，获得非欧几何空间的深层语义表示；4) 黎曼几何重心网络在SPD流形上学习每个类别的黎曼重心，并引入联合损失函数同时优化类内紧凑性和类间分离性。

Result: 在NWPU-RESISC45、UC Merced Land-Use和WHU-RS19三个公开数据集上，5-way 1-shot和5-way 5-shot设置下均一致优于多种代表性最新方法；消融实验验证了各模块的有效性。

Conclusion: 所提出的ZSFS-RGBN方法通过非欧几何空间的特征表示和黎曼几何重心学习，有效解决了遥感图像小样本场景分类中的关键挑战，显著提升了分类性能。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：100%。该方法本身就是遥感小样本场景分类论文。可改进方向：1) 可尝试更先进的骨干网络（如Swin Transformer、ConvNeXt）替代ResNet12以提取更丰富的特征；2) Zigzag扫描策略可扩展为更多样的空间扫描路径（如螺旋扫描、希尔伯特曲线）以探索最优的空间结构保留方式；3) ARMA模型的阶数选择可引入自适应机制以适配不同复杂度的场景；4) 黎曼重心学习可结合对比学习等自监督策略进一步增强小样本下的特征判别性；5) 可扩展至遥感图像语义分割、目标检测等其他小样本任务。

Abstract (英文): Few-shot remote sensing scene classification aims to accurately recognize unseen scene categories using only a scarce number of labeled samples, which has emerged as a research hotspot in the field of remote sensing image interpretation. However, remote sensing images intrinsically suffer from large intra-class variations, high inter-class similarities, and complex background interferences. Traditional few-shot learning methods typically perform feature metric learning in Euclidean space, making it difficult to capture the non-Euclidean geometric distribution characteristics of remote sensing features, and they often neglect the spatial structural information embedded in feature maps. To address these issues, this paper proposes a novel few-shot remote sensing scene classification method, termed ZSFS-RGBN, which integrates a Zigzag Scanning Feature Sequence with a Riemannian Geometric Barycenter Network. Specifically, ResNet12 is first employed as the backbone to extract deep convolutional feature maps from both the support and query sets. Second, a Zigzag scanning strategy is introduced to reorganize the two-dimensional feature maps into one-dimensional feature sequences, thereby effectively preserving the spatial locality and structural continuity of the features. Third, an autoregressive moving average (ARMA) model is constructed to characterize the spatial dependencies of the feature sequences, and its state parameters are mapped onto a symmetric positive definite (SPD) matrix manifold, enabling the deep semantic representations of remote sensing scenes in a non-Euclidean geometric space. Finally, a Riemannian geometric barycenter network is designed to learn the Riemannian barycenter of each category on the SPD manifold, where a joint loss function is introduced to simultaneously optimize intra-class compactness and inter-class separability. Comprehensive experiments are conducted on three public remote sensing scene datasets: NWPU-RESISC45, UC Merced Land-Use, and WHU-RS19. Experimental results demonstrate that the proposed method consistently outperforms several representative state-of-the-art approaches under both 5-way 1-shot and 5-way 5-shot settings. Furthermore, ablation studies verify the effectiveness of each component within the proposed framework.

</details>

*XL Mao,Jianbin Dong,Xi Zhang,Ni Ren,Weiwei Li,Jing Wang,Peiyu Dai*

Main category: Remote Sensing

Motivation: 蟹塘水生植被的精细监测对水质调控、生态平衡维持及中华绒螯蟹养殖优化至关重要，但复杂水环境、破碎化植被形态以及缺乏专用标注数据集导致传统遥感技术难以实现高精度语义分割与分类。

Method: 构建首个蟹塘水生植被无人机多光谱数据集（含Alternanthera philoxeroides、Vallisneria natans、Hydrilla verticillata、Elodea nuttallii四种，像素级标注）；提出MFSCNet，以MedNeXt为骨干，集成通道缩减注意力、空间频率选择、空间-频率融合模块和移动图卷积等分布式模块，在编码器、跳跃连接、解码器和输出头协同运作。

Result: MFSCNet仅19.38M参数，mIoU达0.9044，优于各类主流CNN和Transformer架构。

Conclusion: 该研究为蟹塘水生植被的多类别高精度识别与定量评估提供了遥感技术框架，并为精细化养殖管理及水生生态保护建立了可靠的数据支撑。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。本文本身就是遥感论文（无人机多光谱+语义分割）。改进方向：（1）可引入时序多光谱数据（物候特征）进一步提升分类鲁棒性；（2）可探索自监督预训练策略以减少对大规模像素级标注的依赖；（3）可将MFSCNet扩展到其他水产养殖场景（如虾塘、鱼塘）或内陆水体植被监测任务；（4）可结合轻量化部署技术（如模型剪枝、量化）实现边缘端实时推理。

Abstract (英文): Fine-grained monitoring of aquatic vegetation in crab ponds is essential for regulating water quality, sustaining ecological balance, and optimizing Chinese mitten crab (Eriocheir sinensis) aquaculture. However, owing to the complex water environment, fragmented vegetation morphology, and the absence of dedicated annotated datasets, traditional remote sensing techniques struggle to achieve highly accurate semantic segmentation and classification. In this study, we construct the first unmanned aerial vehicle (UAV) multispectral dataset for crab pond aquatic vegetation, encompassing four species, Alternanthera philoxeroides, Vallisneria natans, Hydrilla verticillata, and Elodea nuttallii, with pixel-level annotations verified by field surveys across typical aquaculture sites in Jiangsu Province, China. Furthermore, we introduce the Multi-scale Frequency–Spatial Collaborative Network (MFSCNet), built upon a MedNeXt backbone and augmented with distributed modules, including Channel Reduction Attention, Spatial Frequency Selection, a spatial–frequency fusion module, and Mobile Graph Convolution that operate cooperatively across the encoder, skip connections, decoder, and output head. This design suppresses complex water-background interference, enhances vegetation texture representation, and preserves the spatial continuity of vegetation patches. Experimental results demonstrate that, with a lightweight parameter size of merely 19.38 M, MFSCNet achieves a remarkable mean Intersection over Union (mIoU) of 0.9044, outperforming various mainstream convolutional neural network (CNN) and Transformer-based architectures. This study not only provides a high-precision remote sensing technical framework for the accurate multi-class identification and quantitative assessment of aquatic vegetation in crab ponds but also establishes reliable data support for refined aquaculture management and aquatic ecological conservation.

### [205] [Landslide Susceptibility Mapping Using Multi-Source Geospatial Data and XGBoost](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18142270)
*Dezhi Yang,Gang Ai,Dongjin Han*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract (英文): Landslides are among the most destructive geological hazards, posing significant threats to human life, infrastructure, and ecological environments. Geological factors, including fault distance and seismic point distance, were introduced to characterize the influence of tectonic activities on slope instability. A landslide inventory and a non-landslide sample dataset were established for model training and validation. The Extreme Gradient Boosting (XGBoost) model was employed for landslide susceptibility mapping, and SHapley Additive exPlanations (SHAP) analysis was used to interpret the contribution of different conditioning factors. The high-susceptibility areas were primarily distributed in the mountainous and hilly regions of northern and eastern Guangdong Province. Vegetation-related variables, road proximity, land-cover type, slope, and distance to coal mines were identified as important contributors to landslide occurrence. This study provides useful references for geological hazard prevention, risk management, and sustainable regional planning.

### [206] [A Scale-Invariance-Based Algorithm Application for Land Surface Temperature Downscaling in Denmark](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132263)
*Élio Pereira,Manvel Khudinyan,Inês Girão,Bruno Marques,Vitor Miranda,Hjalte Jomo Danielsen Sørup,Quentin Paletta,Ana Oliveira*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文利用Sentinel-3的粗分辨率LST（1 km）和细分辨率SDR（300 m）数据，开发了单时间戳（STS）和多时间戳（MTS）两种尺度不变性架构进行LST降尺度。结果表明，虽然机器学习模型在训练尺度上表现良好，但存在尺度特异性问题；线性回归在单时间戳架构下经残差校正后表现最优，而基于树的模型因外推限制表现不佳。多时间戳架构并未优于单时间戳架构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 城市空间和动态研究需要精细时空尺度的地表温度（LST）数据，而Sentinel-3提供的LST空间分辨率较粗（1 km），无法满足城市尺度需求。因此，需要利用其较高分辨率的SDR数据（300 m）进行降尺度。

Method: 基于尺度不变性假设，构建了单时间戳（STS）和多时间戳（MTS）两种降尺度架构。使用SDR衍生指数、季节和地理空间预测因子，在四个丹麦功能城市区域（FUA）上训练模型（包括LR、GB、RF、NN等），并以Landsat数据为验证真值，最后进行残差校正。

Result: 梯度提升（GB）在粗尺度上表现最佳，但在细尺度上表现最差；树模型因外推限制表现不佳；神经网络（NN）和线性回归（LR）更稳健。经残差校正后，单时间戳线性回归取得了最佳的细尺度性能，且多时间戳架构并未优于单时间戳架构。

Conclusion: 机器学习模型在其训练尺度上预测能力较好，但难以泛化到其他尺度，存在尺度特异性。单时间戳线性回归加残差校正是最可靠的操作方案。多时间戳架构可能反而降低性能。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。改进方案：（1）可将该方法应用于国产卫星数据（如高分四号或FY-4A）进行LST降尺度；（2）引入更丰富的时空先验信息（如地表覆盖类型、地形因子）作为预测变量；（3）可尝试深度学习模型（如超分卷积网络或Transformer）替代线性回归以提升非线性的尺度不变性建模能力；（4）可扩展到热红外与可见光-近红外多传感器协同降尺度框架。

Abstract (英文): With an ever-growing recognition of Land Surface Temperature (LST) as a key Essential Climate Variable (ECV), it becomes utmost important to have such a variable at the fine spatial and temporal scales of urban spaces and dynamics. Sentinel-3 provides coarse LST (1 km, daily) based on thermal imagery acquired by its Sea and Land Surface Temperature Radiometer (SLSTR) as well as fine Spectral Directional Reflectances (SDRs, 300 m, every two days) synergically inferred from both SLSTR and the Ocean and Land Colour Instrument (OLCI), which gives the opportunity for using the latter as a predictor in the downscaling of the former. Herein, two scale-invariance-based architectures were developed: a single-timestamp (STS) model, trained with coarse data of the timestamp whose fine target it infers; and a multi-timestamp (MTS) one, trained with multiple timestamps. Note that while several Machine Learning (ML) models besides Linear Regression (LR) were considered for the MTS architecture, only LR was used for the STS one due to the limited amount of available data which the former require for hyperparameter tuning. The models were developed over four Danish Functional Urban Areas (FUAs) using SRD-derived indices and seasonal and geospatial predictors and validated against Landsat data. While Gradient Boosting (GB) achieved the best coarse-scale performance it corresponded to the worst fine-scale performer together with Random Forest (RF), indicating scale invariance breakdown. Tree-based models performed poorly due to extrapolation limitations, whereas Neural Net (NN) and LR proved more robust. After residual correction, single-timestamp LR achieved the best fine-scale performance, making it the most reliable and recommended architecture for operations. The overall results showed that, although ML models may better predict the target at their training scale, their performance may not significantly generalise at others, therefore revealing scale specificity. Furthermore, the results suggested that usage of the more general multi-timestamp architecture instead of the single one may deteriorate performance.

### [207] [Intensifying Drought Under a Warming–Wetting Climate: Multi-Scale Impacts on Vegetation Phenology and Productivity in Xinjiang, China](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18142285)
*Tingting Pan,Yue Wang,Yaning Chen,Xueqi Zhang,Yi-Xiang Wang,Meiqing Feng*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文利用新疆86个气象站1962-2021年数据和MODIS产品（2001-2021），分析干旱动态及其对植被物候和生产力影响。发现1997年后新疆干旱频率和强度显著增加（97%以上区域），植被春季物候提前（-1.9天/十年）、生长季延长（+3.8天/十年），短期干旱（SPEI-3/6）主导植被动态，长期干旱（SPEI-12）控制生态系统稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 新疆干旱区植被对水文气候变率高度敏感，但干旱演变及其生态影响尚未被充分量化，亟需系统评估干旱-植被相互作用机制。

Method: 采用86个气象站点数据（1962-2021）结合SPEI指数和游程理论表征干旱动态，利用MODIS遥感产品（2001-2021）量化植被物候和生产力，通过多尺度分析和极端事件分析研究干旱-植被相互作用。

Result: 1997年后新疆97%以上区域干旱频率和强度显著增加，空间异质性集中在南疆；植被春季物候提前（-1.9天/十年），生长季延长（+3.8天/十年）；GPP和NPP呈增加趋势，尤其是北疆；短期干旱（SPEI-3/6）对植被动态影响最强，长期干旱（SPEI-12）控制生态系统稳定性和恢复。

Conclusion: 新疆呈现增暖-增湿但干旱加剧的矛盾格局，季节性干旱在调节气候变暖背景下植被功能中起主导作用。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。本文已利用MODIS遥感产品量化植被物候和生产力，改进方向：（1）可引入更高时空分辨率遥感数据（如Sentinel-2、Landsat融合数据）提升物候监测精度；（2）结合微波遥感（如SMAP土壤水分数据）建立干旱-植被耦合模型；（3）利用遥感蒸散产品（如MOD16、ETMonitor）替代气象站点插值，改进SPEI计算中的潜在蒸散估算；（4）可引入遥感植被健康指数（VHI）综合评估干旱胁迫。

Abstract (英文): Drought poses a major threat to ecosystem stability in arid regions. In Xinjiang, China, vegetation dynamics are highly sensitive to hydroclimatic variability, yet the evolution of drought and its ecological impacts remain insufficiently quantified. Using meteorological observations from 86 stations (1962–2021), drought dynamics were characterized using the Standardized Precipitation Evapotranspiration Index (SPEI) combined with run theory, while MODIS products (2001–2021) were used to quantify vegetation phenology and productivity. Results indicate that despite a regional warming–wetting trend, more than 97% of Xinjiang exhibits a significant increase in drought frequency and intensity after 1997, with pronounced spatial heterogeneity concentrated in southern Xinjiang. Vegetation phenology shows a significant shift, with spring onset advancing at a rate of −1.9 days decade−1 and growing season length increasing by +3.8 days decade−1. Vegetation productivity derived from MODIS shows strong spatial variability, with GPP and NPP exhibiting consistent increasing trends, particularly in northern Xinjiang. Multi-scale analysis reveals strong scale dependence in drought–vegetation interactions, where short-term drought (SPEI-3 and SPEI-6) exerts the strongest influence on vegetation dynamics, while long-term drought (SPEI-12) primarily controls ecosystem stability and post-drought recovery. Correlation and extreme-event analyses further indicate that seasonal drought and phenological shifts jointly regulate ecosystem productivity by altering water availability and carbon uptake periods. These results highlight a warming–wetting but drought-intensifying regime in Xinjiang and emphasize the dominant role of seasonal drought in regulating vegetation functioning under climate change.

### [208] [Phenology-Adaptive Maize Mapping Using an Enhanced Red-Edge NDVI from Sentinel-2 Across Representative Global Agroecosystems](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132261)
*Han Zhang,Lingbo Yang,Ran Huang,Limin Wang,Jingcheng Zhang*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 提出基于ENDVIre（增强红边归一化植被指数）和物候自适应框架的玉米遥感制图方法，利用Sentinel-2时间序列影像和可解释决策树模型，在美国、巴西、中国、肯尼亚、乌克兰六个区域取得93.27%的平均总体精度，在有限样本条件下实现高精度且可迁移的玉米制图。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大尺度玉米制图在参考样本有限、作物物候日历异质、光学数据频繁缺失的区域仍存在困难，需要一种不依赖大量训练样本、可解释且可迁移的制图方法。

Method: 构建ENDVIre指数（利用Sentinel-2红边4和红边2波段），采用上包络约束的Whittaker平滑器重建NDVI时间序列以识别关键物候阶段，将NDVI、ENDVIre、LSWI集成到物候对齐时间窗口的可解释决策树模型中，区分玉米与大豆、水稻、小麦及其他背景。

Result: 六个区域平均总体精度93.27%，F1-score 93.14%，Kappa系数0.8652；跨年实验总体精度89.80–96.80%；空间迁移实验总体精度87.40–95.40%；在黄淮海平原优于现有高分辨率玉米产品，更好平衡了遗漏误差和误判误差。

Conclusion: ENDVIre基物候规则为有限样本条件下的玉米制图提供了可解释、可迁移的解决方案，但持续性云覆盖和碎片化小农景观仍是重要挑战。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。改进方案：（1）可引入SAR数据（如Sentinel-1）填补光学云覆盖间隙，构建光学-SAR融合时间序列；（2）将决策树规则扩展为轻量级可解释机器学习模型（如可解释随机森林或决策规则集）以增强复杂场景适应性；（3）针对小农碎片化景观，可引入超像素分割或多尺度特征增强空间一致性；（4）该物候自适应框架可直接迁移至其他作物（如水稻、大豆）的遥感制图任务。

Abstract (英文): Accurate maize distribution information is critical for crop-area statistics, food-security assessment, and agricultural monitoring, but large-scale maize-mapping remains difficult in regions with limited reference samples, heterogeneous crop calendars, and frequent optical data gaps. This study proposes a phenology-adaptive maize mapping framework based on Sentinel-2 time-series imagery and an Enhanced Red-edge NDVI (ENDVIre). ENDVIre was constructed from the Sentinel-2 red-edge 4 and red-edge 2 bands to enhance the spectral response of maize during the silking-to-grain-filling stage, when maize develops a dense canopy and high chlorophyll content but is often confused with soybean. The framework first reconstructed the NDVI time series using an upper-envelope-constrained Whittaker smoother to identify key phenological stages, including sowing–emergence, vigorous growth, and maturity–harvest. NDVI, ENDVIre, and LSWI were then integrated into an interpretable decision-tree model with phenology-aligned time windows to distinguish maize from soybean, rice, wheat, and other non-maize backgrounds. The method was evaluated in six representative maize-growing regions across the United States, Brazil, China, Kenya, and Ukraine, covering different crop calendars, field sizes, and agricultural systems. The mean overall accuracy, F1-score, and Kappa coefficient across the six regions reached 93.27%, 93.14%, and 0.8652, respectively. Cross-year experiments in a winter-wheat–summer-maize rotation region from 2020 to 2024 achieved overall accuracies of 89.80–96.80%, while spatial-transfer experiments in six independent regions achieved overall accuracies of 87.40–95.40%. A comparison with existing high-resolution maize products in the Huang-Huai-Hai Plain further showed that the proposed method better balanced omission and commission errors. These results indicate that ENDVIre-based phenology rules provide an interpretable and transferable solution for maize mapping under limited-sample conditions, although persistent cloud contamination and fragmented smallholder landscapes remain important challenges.

### [209] [Crop-Tool-Augmented Active Perception with Reinforcement Learning for High-Resolution Remote Sensing Visual Question Answering](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18142288)
*Qi Li,Kailiang Chen,Yi Han,Xiangyang Xu*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于强化学习的裁剪工具增强主动感知框架，通过结构化token将推理过程组织为问题理解、裁剪决策、局部证据获取和答案生成四个阶段，结合教师引导的冷启动微调和分组相对策略优化（GRPO），在高分辨率遥感VQA任务上实现了对细粒度局部信息的主动获取与推理，在多个基准上取得竞争性结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有视觉-语言模型在处理超高分辨率遥感图像时，通常依赖固定的全局图像输入，导致关键局部细节丢失，难以应对稀疏信息区域、大尺度目标变化和复杂空间布局等挑战。

Method: 1) 构建结构化token显式组织推理过程（问题理解→裁剪决策→局部证据获取→答案生成）；2) 从LRS-GRO数据集构建教师引导的裁剪推理轨迹，对Qwen2.5-VL-3B进行冷启动监督微调；3) 引入分组相对策略优化（GRPO）优化主动感知策略；4) 设计区域感知奖励函数，包含输出格式约束、参考区域覆盖度、答案语义一致性和裁剪惩罚。

Result: 在VRSBench、MME-RealWorld-RS、XLRS-Bench和LRS-VQA四个基准上，方法在整体性能上与闭源、开源及遥感专用视觉-语言模型相比具有竞争力，在大部分基准上取得最优或可比结果。

Conclusion: 结构化监督微调、强化学习优化以及区域感知奖励函数设计均被消融实验验证为有效，所提框架能够主动决定是否需要裁剪操作并选择任务相关区域进行细粒度观察。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。改进方案：1) 当前方法依赖LRS-GRO数据集的裁剪轨迹注释，可引入弱监督或自监督方式自动生成裁剪区域伪标签，降低对人工标注的依赖；2) 奖励函数中的参考区域覆盖度可结合遥感场景下的多尺度目标检测先验（如分割掩码或边界框）进行加权；3) 可扩展到遥感视频VQA或时序变化检测任务，将时间维度的裁剪决策纳入强化学习框架。

Abstract (英文): High-resolution remote sensing visual question answering (RS-VQA) requires models to identify question-relevant regions and reason over fine-grained visual evidence. However, existing vision–language models usually rely on fixed global image inputs, which may lose critical local details in ultra-high-resolution imagery and struggle with sparse informative regions, large object-scale variations, and complex spatial layouts. To address these challenges, this paper proposes a crop-tool-augmented active perception framework with reinforcement learning. The framework introduces structured tokens to explicitly organize the reasoning process into question understanding, cropping decision-making, local evidence acquisition and final answer generation. Based on this design, the model can actively determine whether a cropping operation is needed and select task-relevant regions for further inspection. To enable stable tool-use and multi-turn reasoning in a compact vision–language model, we construct teacher-guided cropping reasoning trajectories from high-resolution images, question–answer pairs, and annotated regions in the LRS-GRO dataset, and use them for cold-start supervised fine-tuning of Qwen2.5-VL-3B. Furthermore, we introduce Group Relative Policy Optimization to refine the model’s active perception policy. A region-aware reward function is designed by integrating output-format constraints, reference-region coverage, answer semantic consistency, and cropping penalties, which encourages compact and informative region selection while reducing redundant tool invocations. Experiments on VRSBench, MME-RealWorld-RS, XLRS-Bench, and LRS-VQA demonstrate that the proposed method achieves competitive overall performance compared with closed-source, open-source, and remote-sensing-specific vision–language models, and obtains the best or comparable results on most benchmarks. Ablation studies further verify the effectiveness of structured supervised fine-tuning, reinforcement learning optimization, and the proposed reward design.

</details>


### [210] [UAV-Based Photogrammetric Inspection in Deep Vertical Shafts: A Case Study from the KGHM GG-1 Mineshaft in Poland](https://doi.org/10.3390/rs18132257)
*Wojciech Rutkowski,Jędrzej Szczepaniak,Tomasz Lipecki,A. Rzonca*

Main category: Remote Sensing

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种专为深部矿井竖井检查设计的六旋翼无人机系统，在波兰最深的GG-1竖井中进行了测试。该系统克服了高通风气流、狭窄空间和无GNSS信号等挑战，配备高分辨率相机和摄影测量能力，能够精确识别结构异常、记录竖井基础设施并增强安全监测。结果表明，无人机检查可作为传统检查的补充工具，提高数据质量并降低人员风险。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统矿井竖井检查受限于人类可达性、环境危害和主观评估，存在安全性差、效率低等问题，亟需一种新型、安全、高效的检查方法。

Method: 开发了定制六旋翼无人机（hexacopter），配备高分辨率相机和摄影测量设备；系统在设计上克服了高通风气流、狭窄几何空间和无GNSS信号的环境限制；采用分阶段进化路径，从无定位系统到包含定位系统和六台相机的最终配置，并在波兰Kwielice最深竖井GG-1中进行了高海拔飞行测试。

Result: 无人机检查能够提供足够精度以识别结构异常、记录竖井基础设施并增强安全监测；展示了从概念到早期开发阶段再到最终方案（含定位系统和六台相机）的完整演化过程，高海拔飞行测试验证了系统可行性。

Conclusion: 无人机技术可作为传统竖井检查的补充工具，提供更优的数据质量、降低人员风险，并为竖井维护提供新方法。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。该无人机竖井检查系统与遥感领域高度交叉：1）**多源数据融合**：将无人机获取的高分辨率可见光影像与LiDAR点云数据结合，构建竖井全结构三维模型，提升结构异常检测精度；2）**地下摄影测量增强**：针对GNSS缺失环境，可引入视觉SLAM（同步定位与地图构建）与惯性测量单元（IMU）深度融合的定位方案，提高无外部参考时的三维重建精度；3）**多光谱/热红外拓展**：在现有高分辨率相机基础上增加热红外传感器，实现竖井壁温度异常检测（如裂隙渗水、支护结构老化），拓展遥感的无损检测能力；4）**AI辅助诊断**：结合深度学习的遥感影像解译方法，对采集的竖井壁图像进行自动化裂缝、形变和腐蚀识别，提升检查效率与客观性。

Abstract (英文): Underground mining operations depend heavily on vertical shafts for access, ventilation, and ore transport, making their structural integrity and safety critical to overall mine performance. Traditional shaft inspections, though rigorous, are limited by human accessibility, environmental hazards, and subjective evaluation. This study presents the development and initial testing of a novel unmanned aerial vehicle (UAV) system designed specifically for shaft inspections in deep mining environments. The research focuses on the GG-1 shaft in Kwielice, Poland—the country’s deepest operational shaft—where challenging conditions such as high ventilation airflow, confined geometry, and absence of GNSS signals necessitated innovative solutions. A custom-built hexacopter equipped with high-resolution cameras and photogrammetric capabilities was deployed to capture detailed visual and spatial data. This article presents complementary path of UAV evolution, from concept, early development stage and results without positioning system through to the description of final results including positioning system and all six cameras until results of high-altitude flights. Results demonstrate that UAV-based inspection can deliver sufficient precision for identifying structural irregularities, documenting shaft infrastructure, and enhancing safety monitoring. The findings highlight the potential of UAV technology as a complementary tool to conventional inspections, offering improved data quality, reduced risk to personnel, and a new approach to shaft maintenance.

### [211] [Multi-Criteria evaluation and ranking of 28 precipitation products over China](https://doi.org/10.1016/j.jag.2026.105446)
*Le Xinlong,Kang Ling,L Zhou,J Wei,Hao Chen*

Main category: JAG

TL;DR: 本研究基于多准则决策框架，对4大类28种降水产品在中国及其7个气候区的表现进行了综合评估与排名，发现多源融合产品整体最优，但区域间存在显著异质性：干旱区偏爱再分析产品，高原区对卫星产品更敏感。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 中国复杂季风气候与剧烈地形梯度导致多源降水产品存在强区域差异，单一指标评价不足以支撑产品选择，亟需一套综合、透明的评估与排名框架。

Method: 选取4大类（站点插值、卫星反演、再分析、多源融合）28种降水产品；在网格尺度和7个主要气候区尺度上，综合运用常规误差统计、一致性度量、ETCCDI极端降水指数、降水探测能力及SAL诊断（评估强降雨事件的结构、幅度和位置），并通过集成多准则决策框架合成各指标，生成全国及区域排名。

Result: 多数产品能较好捕捉日降水变率，但对强降雨事件普遍存在幅度低估、误差扩大、结构扭曲和位置偏差。全国尺度上多源融合产品整体稳健性最强；区域排名呈现强空间异质性：干旱区和部分湿润区倾向再分析产品，高原区对卫星产品更敏感且排名不确定性更高。

Conclusion: 该综合评估框架为降水产品选择、多源融合候选池构建以及水文气象风险分析提供了透明且面向应用的指导，并给出了全国及气候区级别的产品排名。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。该框架可直接迁移至遥感蒸散发、土壤水分、积雪覆盖等多源遥感产品的综合评估与区域优选。具体方案：(1) 将ETCCDI极端降水指数替换为对应变量的极端事件指标（如热浪指数、干旱指数）；(2) SAL诊断可推广至遥感反演的降水场或土壤水分场的结构-幅度-位置偏差分析；(3) 多准则决策框架可直接用于遥感产品融合前的候选产品排序与权重分配，提升多源遥感数据融合质量。

Abstract (英文): Multi-source precipitation products exhibit strong regional differences across China’s complex monsoon climates and pronounced topographic gradients, making single-metric evaluations insufficient for product selection. This study evaluates 28 widely used precipitation products over China from four categories: gauge-based, satellite-derived, reanalysis, and multi-source merged products. Product performance is assessed at both grid and seven major climate-zone scales using conventional error statistics, consistency metrics, ETCCDI (Expert Team on Climate Change Detection and Indices) extreme precipitation indices, precipitation detection skill, and SAL (Structure–Amplitude–Location) diagnostics for the intensity, structure, and location of heavy-rainfall events. These indicators are further synthesized within an ensemble multi-criteria decision-making framework to derive national and regional rankings. The results show that most products capture daily precipitation variability reasonably well, but intense rainfall events remain associated with widespread amplitude underestimation and enlarged errors, while extremes also exhibit notable structural distortion and location bias. At the national scale, multi-source merged generally show greater overall robustness. Regional rankings further reveal strong spatial heterogeneity: arid zones and some humid regions tend to favor reanalysis-type products, whereas plateau regions show higher sensitivity to satellite products and greater ranking uncertainty. Overall, this study provides a transparent and application-oriented framework for integrated precipitation product evaluation and ranking over China. The resulting national and climate-zone-specific rankings offer practical guidance for precipitation product selection, candidate-pool construction for multi-source merging, and hydrometeorological risk analyses.

### [212] [LiDAR-based assessment of treetop dieback to detect asian longhorned beetle damage in poplar forests](https://doi.org/10.1016/j.jag.2026.105459)
*Quan Zhou,Rui Tang,Linfeng Yu,Peiyun Bi,Lili Ren,Youqing Luo*

Main category: JAG

TL;DR: 本文提出基于树冠内部归一化的比值框架，利用LiDAR点云检测亚洲长角天牛（ALB）引起的树梢枯死表型。通过将树冠在50%和80%高度处分割，计算上/下部冠层体积、点密度和叶面积指数的比值，并定义组合比值指标（如SRV）。在幼龄和老龄杨树样地验证表明，SRV在随机分割和跨样地迁移测试中分别达到76.23%和70.58%的总体精度，优于传统LiDAR指标。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LiDAR在森林胁迫检测中存在两个问题：(1)非特异性结构响应难以识别特定损伤表型；(2)结构指标在异质年龄和大小林分间迁移性差。ALB导致的树梢枯死表型（自上而下死亡）需要特异性检测方法。

Method: 选取幼龄和老龄杨树样地，基于野外证据将树木标记为健康、轻度损伤和重度损伤。对每棵树的LiDAR点云在50%和80%总高度处垂直分割，计算各段冠层体积（V）、点密度（PD）和叶面积指数（LAI），然后推导上/下部比值指标（以树冠下部为内部归一化因子），并定义组合比值（如SRV）。采用线性判别分析（LDA）评估指标可分性，进行随机分割和跨样地迁移测试。

Result: 组合比值指标SRV（Summary Ratio of Volume）性能最优：随机分割总体精度76.23%，跨样地迁移测试总体精度70.58%，显著优于其他提出指标和现有LiDAR指数。

Conclusion: 通过耦合表型聚焦特征与内部归一化，该方法能够精确检测树梢枯死，并提高跨年龄和大小异质林分的迁移能力。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。该方法的内部归一化比值框架可直接应用于遥感领域其他树冠胁迫检测场景：(1)可移植至多光谱或高光谱遥感，将上层/下层光谱比值（如红边归一化差值）作为特征，检测自上而下的冠层衰退；(2)可用于其他虫害（如松材线虫、云杉八齿小蠹）导致的树梢枯死检测；(3)改进方向：可引入深度学习（如PointNet++）替代LDA进行特征分类，进一步提升精度；结合时序LiDAR数据可捕捉枯死动态过程；在多树种混交林中验证其迁移性。

Abstract (英文): Effective forest management depends on accurately monitoring changes in forest health. The Asian longhorned beetle (ALB) has caused extensive mortality in broadleaf trees worldwide. ALB typically manifests as a distinctive treetop-dieback phenotype that progresses downward in damaged trees. Although LiDAR is widely used for plant-stress detection, two challenges persist: (1) non-specific structural responses that hinder the identification of damage-specific phenotypes and (2) limited transferability of structural metrics across age- and size-heterogeneous stands. We address these challenges with a within-tree ratio-based framework that targets the treetop-dieback phenotype with internal normalization. Two poplar plots (young, old) were selected to represent age- and size-related heterogeneity. Based on field evidence (oviposition pits, frass holes, exit holes), each tree was labeled as healthy, lightly damaged, or severely damaged. For each tree, we vertically segmented the point cloud at 50% and 80% of total height and computed crown volume (V), point density (PD), and leaf area index (LAI) of each segment. We then derived upper-to-lower ratio metrics, using the lower crown as an internal normalizer, to capture top-down dieback while normalizing size- and age-related heterogeneity. We also defined a family of combination ratios that aggregate ratios at 50% and 80% heights. Using Linear Discriminant Analysis (LDA), we evaluated separability of each metric under two strategies: (1) a 70/30 random split by trees and (2) a plot-transfer test (train: Stand young ; test: Stand old ). The results indicated that the proposed metrics, Summary Ratio of Volume (SRV = V u p p e r 50 % V l o w e r 50 % + V u p p e r 20 % V l o w e r 80 % ), achieved the highest overall accuracy (OA): 76.23% in random split, and 70.58% in plot-transfer, significantly outperforming other proposed metrics and existing LiDAR indices. By coupling phenotype-focused features with internal normalization, the approach enables precise detection of treetop dieback and improves transferability across age and size heterogeneity.

</details>


### [213] [Stratified and adaptive regression for NDVI-based land surface temperature downscaling over agricultural fields](https://doi.org/10.1016/j.jag.2026.105456)
*Jamal Elfarkh,Nadia Ouaadi,said grich,Abderrahman Liblab,Abdelghani Chehbouni*

Main category: JAG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为STAR-LST的线性回归方法，将地表温度（LST）从1公里降尺度到10米空间分辨率。该方法利用LST与NDVI在均匀条件下的线性关系，在(LST, NDVI)特征空间中划分三角形区域，为每个子区域建立回归模型。在橄榄树、Kernza、小麦和大麦田地的实测验证中，RMSE为2.79-4.49°C，相比DisTrad和TsHARP方法平均提升了33%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 农业田间管理需要高空间分辨率的热红外影像，但在发展中国家，农田碎片化且异质性高，现有卫星热传感器分辨率不足。亟需一种能够将低分辨率LST数据降尺度到高分辨率的方法，以满足小规模农田的精细化管理需求。

Method: 提出STAR-LST方法：基于LST与NDVI在均匀地表条件下的线性关系，在粗分辨率下将(LST, NDVI)特征空间的三角形形态划分为若干子三角形（共享一个顶部顶点），每个子三角形对应不同的NDVI范围；对每个子区域分别建立多元线性回归模型，然后将各模型应用于对应NDVI范围的高分辨率数据，从而得到10米分辨率LST。

Result: 在橄榄树、Kernza、小麦和大麦的实地验证中，STAR-LST的RMSE范围为2.79-4.49°C，相比DisTrad和TsHARP（RMSE 4.18-6.83°C）平均提升了33%。该方法还能利用插值后的NDVI实现每日LST估算，生成高时空分辨率的LST产品。

Conclusion: STAR-LST方法能够有效将LST从1公里降尺度到10米，精度优于传统方法，且能够实现每日LST估算，特别适用于碎片化农田的热管理，为发展中国家小规模农田提供了可行的热红外遥感解决方案。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：90%。改进方案：（1）引入更多光谱指数（如EVI、NDWI、SAVI）作为回归变量，提高在植被覆盖度低或水陆混合区域的降尺度精度；（2）将三角形划分策略拓展到三维特征空间（如LST-NDVI-Albedo），以更好地处理地表异质性；（3）结合深度学习（如超分卷积网络）对回归残差进行修正，进一步降低RMSE；（4）引入时间自相关的滤波方法（如卡尔曼滤波）优化每日LST估算的时间连续性。

Abstract (英文): Improving the spatial resolution of thermal imagery is essential for agricultural field management, especially in developing countries where fields are fragmented and heterogeneous. The existing downscale land surface temperature (LST) products are a promising solution while awaiting for further advances in satellite-based thermal sensors. In this study, a linear regression-based approach was proposed to downscale LST from 1 km to 10 m spatial resolution. The proposed method is hereafter referred to as Stratified and Adaptive Regression for Land Surface Temperature Downscaling (STAR-LST). Taking advantage of the linearity between LST and NDVI under homogeneous conditions, multiple linear regression models were first derived for different regions in the (LST, NDVI) feature space at coarse resolution. These regions were defined by partitioning the triangular form of the (LST, NDVI) feature space into sub-triangles, sharing a common top vertex. Each model is then applied to the corresponding NDVI range, allowing thus to derive LST at finer resolution. LST estimates were validated against in-situ measurements collected over olive trees, Kernza, wheat, and barley. Good results were obtained with RMSE values ranging from 2.79 to 4.49 °C for STAR-LST. This presents an improvement of an average of 33 % compared to the two classical methods DisTrad and TsHARP (RMSE in the range 4.18–6.83 °C), which showed similar accuracy. In addition, STAR-LST enabled daily LST estimation whenever coarse-resolution data were available, using interpolated NDVI to generate a high spatio-temporal LST product suitable for managing agricultural fields, particularly the small size fields.

</details>


### [214] [A machine learning framework for predicting agricultural terrace suitability using positive and unlabelled datasets: an application for the Troodos Mountains, Cyprus](https://doi.org/10.1016/j.jag.2026.105454)
*Aman Kumar Meena,Christos Zoumides,Hakan Djuma,Ioannis Sofokleous,Corrado Camera,Adriana Bruggeman*

Main category: JAG

TL;DR: 本研究提出了一个结合GIS和机器学习（正无标签学习）的集成预测框架，用于地中海山区梯田适宜性分析。在塞浦路斯特罗多斯山脉的应用中，该PU分类器达到了84.6%的召回率和81.5%的精确率，揭示了2017至2024年间梯田减少29%但亦有12%的复苏，并提供了可通过Google Earth Engine访问的适宜性地图。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 梯田是地中海山区景观的关键特征，但传统土地适宜性分析需要完整标注的数据集。现实中常见的情况是只有部分正样本可用，其余样本未标注。因此，需要一种能从正样本和无标签数据中学习的预测建模框架，以指导梯田的可持续管理和扩展。

Method: 采用两步式机器学习方法：首先从无标签（梯田缺失）单元中识别可靠的负样本，然后将这些可靠负样本与正样本（梯田存在）结合进行适宜性预测。基于5米DEM提取海拔≥500米、坡度≥15%的山地研究区，利用欧盟共同农业政策下的作物地块数据划分梯田存在/缺失单元。在完全随机选择假设下评估PU分类器性能。

Result: PU分类器在SCAR假设下达到84.6%召回率、81.5%精确率和83%的F1分数。特征重要性分析表明土地覆盖、地形坡度和树木覆盖密度是最重要的参数。2017至2024年间梯田农业用地减少29%，同时有12%的复苏。

Conclusion: 所提出的PU学习框架有效解决了只有正样本和无标签数据时的梯田适宜性分析问题，生成的适宜性地图及数据层可通过Google Earth Engine应用访问，为可持续景观规划提供决策支持。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：90%。该框架可直接应用于遥感领域的土地利用分类、滑坡易发性评估、耕地退化监测等任务。具体改进方案：(1) 结合高分辨率遥感影像（如Sentinel-2、WorldView）提取更精细的地表特征替代传统土地覆盖数据；(2) 引入时序遥感数据（如NDVI时间序列）增强对梯田废弃和复苏的动态监测能力；(3) 将DEM衍生地形因子（如地形湿度指数、太阳辐射）作为额外输入特征；(4) 尝试PU学习与深度学习（如CNN）结合，直接从遥感影像中学习空间上下文特征，提升分类精度。

Abstract (英文): Terraces are a defining feature of Mediterranean mountain landscapes, enabling agriculture on steep slopes while providing multiple ecosystem services. Land suitability analysis (LSA) can guide authorities and land users to sustainably manage and expand these environments. It typically requires fully labelled datasets, but in many real-world applications only a fraction of positive examples is available, with the rest unlabelled. This study aims to present an integrated predictive modelling framework that combines GIS with data-driven Machine Learning (ML) techniques, capable of learning from Positive and Unlabelled (PU) datasets for LSA. The proposed framework was applied to develop a terrace suitability map for Cyprus’ Troodos Mountains. A 5-m DEM was processed to extract the mountain area, with elevation ≥ 500 m and slopes ≥ 15%, defining the study area. Crop plots registered under the Single Area Payment Scheme of the European Common Agricultural Policy were used to classify the study area into Terrace-Present (TP) and Terrace-Absent (TA) cells, with TP serving as labelled positive and TA as unlabelled samples. A two-step ML approach was applied, first identifying reliable negatives from TA cells, then using these with TP cells for suitability prediction. The developed PU-classifier was evaluated under the selected completely-at-random (SCAR) assumption, achieving a Recall of 84.6%, Precision of 81.5% and an F1 score of 83%. Feature importance analysis identified land cover, terrain slope and tree cover density as the most influential parameters for terrace suitability. Comparative analysis between 2017 and 2024 revealed abandonment of terraced agricultural land (29% decrease) as well as revitalisation (12% increase). The resulting suitability map and accompanying data layers are accessible through a Google Earth Engine application, aiming to support informed decision-making for sustainable landscape planning.

</details>


### [215] [Simulating potential landward migration pattern of mangrove wetlands under the ‘two-way squeeze’ from sea level rise and human activities](https://doi.org/10.1016/j.jag.2026.105461)
*Zhaoxuan Ding,Bin Ai,Jiali Zeng,Yuchao Sun,Xiaoping Liu,Zhuokai Jian,Zhenlin Lai,Poyuan Ou*

### [216] [Multi-source complementary feature self-integration network for geological lithology interpretation](https://doi.org/10.1016/j.jag.2026.105463)
*Ying Cao,Diming Wu,Y W Li,Qing Cheng*

Main category: JAG

TL;DR: 本文提出CFSI-Net，一种用于多源遥感影像地质岩性解译的统一框架。通过跨域特征提取融合模块(CDFEFM)缓解多源特征空间异质性，通过频域-空间特征融合模块(FSFIM)和分割模块(SegM)改善分割边界模糊问题。在CUG-LithXZ数据集上，OA达80.13%，mIoU达66.18%，优于现有方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多源遥感影像中的地质岩性解译面临两大挑战：多源特征的空间异质性（不同来源影像特征不一致）和地质要素的碎片化空间分布，导致传统方法难以有效融合多源信息并进行精确解译。

Method: 提出CFSI-Net统一框架，包含：1) CDFEFM——双分支结构自适应提取和融合跨通道互补特征，减少冗余岩性信息；2) FSFIM——从频域和空间域捕获边界结构细节和空间上下文依赖；3) SegM——进一步细化跨通道空间依赖，丰富纹理细节，增强相邻要素判别能力。

Result: 在CUG-LithXZ数据集上，Geo-GZ区域OA 80.13%、mIoU 66.18%；Geo-LZ区域OA 72.49%、mIoU 50.26%，一致优于现有最先进模型。

Conclusion: 频域与空间信息的协同利用能为复杂地形下的地质岩性精确解译提供更丰富的细节信息，验证了多源特征融合与频域-空间联合建模的有效性。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。该论文本身就是遥感领域（多源遥感岩性解译）的论文。改进方案：1) 可引入注意力机制（如交叉注意力）进一步优化CDFEFM中多源特征的跨模态对齐；2) FSFIM可扩展为多尺度频域分支，以适配不同尺度地质体的边界特征；3) 可引入自监督预训练策略缓解标注数据稀缺问题；4) 可结合图神经网络建模地质要素之间的拓扑关系，增强碎片化区域的上下文理解。

Abstract (英文): Geological lithology interpretation in multi-source remote sensing imagery still faces challenges due to the spatial heterogeneity of multi-source features and the fragmented spatial distribution of geological elements. To address these issues, we propose the complementary feature self-integration network (CFSI-Net), a unified framework for multi-source feature fusion and lithology interpretation. To mitigate spatial heterogeneity in multi-source features, we developed the cross-domain feature extraction and fusion module (CDFEFM), a dual-branch structure that adaptively extracts and fuses complementary features across channels while reducing redundant lithology information. Furthermore, we introduced the frequency-spatial feature integration module (FSFIM) and a segmentation module (SegM) to alleviate the problem of boundary ambiguity in segmentation. FSFIM captures boundary structural details and spatial contextual dependencies from the frequency and spatial domains, whereas SegM further refines spatial dependencies across channels, enriching textural details and enhancing the discrimination of adjacent elements. Experimental results on the CUG-LithXZ dataset demonstrate that CFSI-Net consistently outperforms state-of-the-art models, achieving an OA of 80.13% and mIoU of 66.18% in Geo-GZ, and an OA of 72.49% and mIoU of 50.26% in Geo-LZ. These results confirm that the synergistic utilization of frequency and spatial information provides richer details for accurate geological lithology interpretation in complex terrains.

</details>


### [217] [Feasibility of space-borne remote sensing to detect features related to CO2 and N2O exchange of boreal agricultural fields](https://doi.org/10.1016/j.jag.2026.105455)
*Miia Salminen,Liisa Kulmala,Tuomas Laurila,Olli Nevalainen,Stephanie Gerin,Laura Heimsch,Henriikka Vekuri,Juval Cohen,Matias Takala,Kimmo Rautiainen,Narasinha Shurpali,Maarit Liimatainen,Jari Liski,Jouni Pulliainen*

Main category: JAG

TL;DR: 本文探索了微波卫星观测在表征 boreal 农业区 CO₂ 交换过程中的适用性。研究了芬兰三个区域（两个矿质土壤草地、一个泥炭土壤草地）的冻融、积雪积累与融化等微波辐射计信息对碳氮交换的解释能力。结果表明，空间微波辐射计可有效评估 CO₂ 交换年平衡与 N₂O 爆发；SAR 数据可填补光学 LAI 时间序列的云覆盖间隙；C 波段 Sentinel-1 SAR 与 GPP 动态显著相关，并能检测收割事件，支持全年农业监测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 评估空间微波卫星观测在表征 boreal 农业区 CO₂ 交换过程中的适用性，特别是利用冻融、积雪等景观尺度信息解释场尺度碳氮交换过程，以弥补光学遥感受云覆盖限制的不足。

Method: 基于三个芬兰 boreal 农业区（两个矿质土壤草地、一个泥炭土壤草地），利用 SMOS 和 SSMI/S 微波辐射计获取冻融和积雪信息，结合 C 波段 Sentinel-1 SAR 数据，分析其与 CO₂ 交换动态、N₂O 排放率及 LAI 时序的相关性。

Result: 微波辐射计衍生的冻融和积雪信息可有效区分具有不同 CO₂ 交换特征的季节期；SAR 数据可显著填补光学 LAI 时间序列的云覆盖间隙；C 波段 Sentinel-1 SAR 后向散射与 GPP 动态显著相关，并能检测收割事件。

Conclusion: 空间微波观测在评估 boreal 农业区 CO₂ 交换和 N₂O 爆发方面具有潜力；粗分辨率微波辐射计数据可约束生长季外的碳交换模型，SAR 与辐射计联合时间序列可支持全年农业监测。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。作为遥感论文，改进方向包括：1) 引入更高分辨率（如 L 波段）SAR 数据以提升对田块尺度管理事件的检测精度；2) 结合机器学习方法融合多源微波与光学数据，构建无缝 LAI/GPP 时序；3) 将微波冻融信息同化为过程式碳循环模型（如 BEPS、DNDC），提升模型对非生长季碳通量的模拟能力。

Abstract (英文): We explored the applicability of microwave satellite observations to characterize the carbon dioxide (CO 2 ) exchange processes in boreal agricultural fields for three regions in Finland. The sites under investigation included two grassland fields on mineral soil and one on peat soil. We evaluated whether the space-borne microwave radiometer data-derived information on freeze–thaw, snow accumulation and snow melt obtained at a landscape scale is useful in explaining carbon and nitrogen exchange processes at daily temporal and field scale spatial resolutions. Specifically, we focused on the annual balance and seasonal behaviour of CO 2 exchange, and the feasibility of microwave observations in explaining the observed nitrous oxide (N 2 O) emission rates from a peatland field. Additionally, the feasibility of space-borne synthetic aperture radar (SAR) data to support observation time series of optical satellite data on a field block level was investigated for the growing season. The results indicate the potential of space-borne microwave observations to provide information useful in assessing CO 2 exchange and N 2 O bursts from boreal agricultural fields. The results show that seasonal changes due to climate and management, detectable on a landscape scale from space-borne microwave radiometry, significantly contribute to the annual balance of CO 2 exchange of boreal fields. The results also suggest that SAR data can potentially be used to fill cloud cover induced gaps in leaf area index (LAI) time series available from optical-range satellite imaging, improving the usefulness of satellite data in the monitoring of field management. Results show that landscape-scale freeze–thaw and snow cover information derived from space-borne SMOS and SSMI/S observations distinguishes seasonal periods with distinct CO 2 exchange characteristics, indicating the potential of coarse-resolution microwave radiometer data to constrain carbon exchange models of boreal agricultural fields outside the summertime growing season. Further, C-band Sentinel-1 SAR backscatter observations were found to correlate significantly with GPP dynamics and enable detection of harvesting events, suggesting that combined SAR and radiometer time series can support year-round agricultural monitoring.

### [219] [Spatiotemporal fusion of radar backscatter for enhanced monitoring of surface melt dynamics over Antarctic ice shelves](https://doi.org/10.1016/j.jag.2026.105448)
*Chengyu Pu,Lei Zheng,Jingan Wu,Qi Liang,Teng Li,Gang Li,Xiao Cheng*

Main category: JAG

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为SRBDF的时空融合方法，首次将雷达散射计（ASCAT）与合成孔径雷达（Sentinel-1）的C波段后向散射数据融合，生成高分辨率（来自Sentinel-1）且每日覆盖（来自ASCAT）的南极冰架表面融冰监测数据集，并在Larsen C和George VI冰架上验证了其有效性（总体一致性≥0.90），揭示了2019-2020年极端融化季节的时空细节。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有雷达散射计可实现每日融冰探测但分辨率粗糙，SAR分辨率高但时间覆盖有限，两者之间存在时空分辨率权衡；而现有的时空融合方法仅适用于光学遥感，尚未成功应用于雷达后向散射数据，亟需开发针对雷达数据的融合方法以获取高时空分辨率的南极冰架表面融化监测数据。

Method: 提出Spatiotemporal Radar Backscatter Data Fusion (SRBDF)方法，融合Sentinel-1（高空间分辨率、低时间频率）与ASCAT（低空间分辨率、每日覆盖）两类C波段主动微波数据，生成每日高分辨率后向散射数据集。该方法首次将时空融合技术从光学遥感拓展至雷达后向散射领域，在Larsen C和George VI冰架的2018-2021年融化季节进行了应用验证。

Result: SRBDF生成的融合数据集保留了Sentinel-1的空间细节和ASCAT的每日时间频率；在Larsen C和George VI冰架上，融冰/冻结检测总体一致性接近或超过0.90；成功揭示了2019-2020年极端融化季节（融冰发生率比上一季节高出50%以上），并识别出Larsen C冰架由焚风驱动、George VI冰架由持续暖平流伴随低速北风驱动的显著融化事件。

Conclusion: SRBDF方法能有效捕捉南极冰架表面融化变异性，为极地表过程研究提供了高时空分辨率的新数据源，具有更广泛的应用潜力。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。本文本身即为遥感论文，以下为改进方案：1）可引入更多极化模式（如VV+VH双极化）和更多频段（如L-band、X-band）的SAR数据以增强融合鲁棒性；2）可结合深度学习（如GAN或Transformer-based融合模型）替代现有的传统时空融合策略，进一步提升融合精度及对复杂冰盖地形的适应能力；3）可与被动微波数据（如AMSR-E/2）进行多源融合，弥补主动微波在湿雪探测上的不确定性。

Abstract (英文): Surface meltwater over the Antarctic Ice Sheet acts as a primary modulator of the polar energy budget, potentially triggering ice shelf collapse and exerting far-reaching impacts on the global climate system. Radar scatterometers enable daily melt detection but at coarse resolution, whereas Synthetic Aperture Radar (SAR) achieves fine spatial detail with limited temporal coverage. Spatiotemporal fusion methods present a viable solution to balance this trade-off, but these approaches are applied only to optical remote sensing and have not yet been successfully adapted to radar backscatter data. In this study, we propose the Spatiotemporal Radar Backscatter Data Fusion (SRBDF) method, a multi-source C-band active microwave data fusion technique that can integrate Sentinel-1 and Advanced Scatterometer (ASCAT) observations. SRBDF generates a high-resolution daily backscatter dataset for monitoring surface melt dynamics at the Larsen C and George VI Ice Shelves throughout 2018–2021 melt seasons. The fused dataset preserves spatial details from Sentinel-1, while maintaining the daily frequency of ASCAT. Across the Larsen C and George VI Ice Shelves, SRBDF melt/freeze detection shows overall consistency approaching or above 0.90 with Sentinel-1 and ASCAT. High-resolution daily observations reveal an extreme melt season during 2019–2020, when melt occurrence was more than 50 % above the previous season. Pronounced melt was observed on Larsen C and George VI ice shelves driven by foehn winds and sustained warm air advection from low-speed northerly winds, respectively. These results demonstrate the effectiveness of SRBDF in capturing Antarctic ice shelf surface melt variability and its potential for broader applications in polar surface process research.

</details>


### [220] [Mapping the extent, type and remnant areas of the coastal dunes of Australia and New Zealand by integrating multi-source data](https://doi.org/10.1016/j.jag.2026.105464)
*Zhijia Zheng,Guanli Li,Chenjun Wang,Xiuyuan Zhang,Noam Levin*

Main category: JAG

TL;DR: 本研究利用地质地图划定海岸沙丘范围，结合面向对象图像分析（OBIA）与随机森林分类器，对澳大利亚和新西兰的六类海岸沙丘进行10米分辨率精细制图，总体分类精度达90.68%，并分析了城市化与保护区对沙丘的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 由于海岸沙丘空间异质性高、沿海环境光谱复杂，实现大尺度高精度沙丘类型制图对于海岸管理至关重要但极具挑战。

Method: 首先利用地质地图划定海岸沙丘场空间范围以掩膜非沙丘区域；其次采用面向对象图像分析（OBIA）结合随机森林分类器，融合多源特征，将沙丘分为活动沙丘、前沙丘、沙滩、半稳定沙丘、稳定沙丘和湿地（沙丘洼地）六类，最终生成10米分辨率分类图。

Result: 覆盖澳大利亚和新西兰27,564 km²，总体分类精度90.68%，稳定沙丘精度最高（96.81%）。约498 km²沙丘转为城市用地，但15,781.80 km²（59.44%）位于保护区内。

Conclusion: 该研究提供了一套可复制的海岸沙丘类型大尺度精细分类方法，生成的沙丘类型图可为监测海岸沙丘系统状态与演化提供科学支持。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。该研究本身就是遥感分类在海岸沙丘制图中的典型应用。改进方向：（1）引入深度学习方法（如U-Net或Transformer）替代随机森林，进一步提升复杂沙丘类型的分类精度；（2）结合多时相遥感数据（如Sentinel-1/2时序）捕捉沙丘动态演化特征；（3）融合LiDAR或InSAR高程数据以提高对沙丘地形细微差异的区分能力；（4）将方法迁移至全球其他海岸线区域，并结合潮汐与植被指数等辅助数据进行区域适应性调整。

Abstract (英文): Accurate large-scale mapping of coastal dune types is critical for coastal management but remains challenging due to the dunes’ high spatial heterogeneity and the spectral complexity in coastal environments. Therefore, this study aims to develop a coastal dune mapping approach and demonstrate its applicability across Australia and New Zealand. Firstly, we leveraged geological maps to delineate the spatial extent of coastal dune fields, effectively masking out non-dune areas. Secondly, we applied an object-based image analysis (OBIA), followed by a random forest classifier that integrated multi-source features to classify six coastal dune types within the delineated coastal dune fields, including active dunes, foredunes, sandy beaches, semi-stabilized dunes, stabilized dunes, and wetlands (dune slacks). Based on this approach, we generated a 10 m fine classification map of coastal dune types across Australia and New Zealand, covering a total area of 27,564 km 2 . Accuracy assessment yielded an overall classification accuracy of 90.68 %. Most categories achieved satisfactory performance, with stabilized dunes showing the highest accuracy (96.81 %). We also found that approximately 498 km 2 of coastal dune area has been converted to urban development land. However, this development pressure was mitigated by conservation efforts, as 15,781.80 km 2 (59.44 %) of the total coastal dune area was situated within protected areas. This study provides a replicable methodology for large-scale fine classification of coastal dune types. The resulting map offers scientific support for monitoring coastal dune systems state and evolution under human intervention.

</details>

### [222] [An explainable optical flow network for arctic sea ice drift extraction from multi-frequency AMSR2 passive microwave data](https://doi.org/10.1080/15481603.2026.2697124)
*Peng Jiang,Tiantian Feng,Yushi Yang,Yuxuan Hu,Chen Zhao*

Main category: GIScience & RS

TL;DR: 本文提出MF-IceDrift，一种基于多频AMSR2数据的可解释深度学习框架，用于全年、空间完整的北极海冰漂移提取。通过多频特征融合、Transformer-based TransUpdate块和自监督策略，在保持100%空间覆盖率的同时实现了最佳精度，并在FY-3D MWRI和DMSP SSMIS数据上展示了泛化能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 北极海冰漂移监测对理解极地气候动态至关重要。被动微波辐射计虽能提供每日观测，但不同频率通道存在权衡：高频通道空间细节更丰富但受大气和融雪噪声影响大，低频通道更稳定但分辨率不足以解析小尺度漂移。现有方法难以兼顾多频优势，亟需一种能融合多频互补特征的方法。

Method: 提出MF-IceDrift框架，包含三个核心模块：(1) 多频特征提取与融合模块，用于提取和融合不同频率通道的互补特征；(2) Transformer-based TransUpdate块，用于细化流估计；(3) 基于增广一致性自监督策略，确保漂移场的空间连续性。使用多频AMSR2数据进行训练和验证。

Result: 与浮标观测对比，MF-IceDrift在保持100%空间覆盖率的同时取得了最佳精度，显著优于现有的多频决策级融合方法和单频基线。提取的漂移场与业务化海冰漂移产品高度相关，证实了大尺度漂移模式的可靠性。在FY-3D MWRI和DMSP SSMIS数据上也展现出良好的泛化能力。

Conclusion: 本研究开发的深度学习网络为利用多频被动微波数据进行大尺度、长时序海冰漂移提取提供了新途径。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。作为一篇遥感领域论文，其改进方向包括：(1) 将多频特征融合策略扩展到其他被动微波传感器（如SMOS、WindSat）以实现多传感器协同；(2) 引入物理约束（如海冰守恒方程）作为损失函数项以增强物理一致性；(3) 将框架迁移至SAR数据（如Sentinel-1）与被动微波数据的联合反演；(4) 在TransUpdate块中引入注意力机制的空间-时间-频率三维立方体处理能力；(5) 可进一步结合北极海冰厚度、海面温度等辅助数据提升漂移场精度。

Abstract (英文): Arctic sea ice drift monitoring is essential for understanding polar climate dynamics. Passive microwave radiometers provide valuable daily observations of the Arctic region. However, their use for sea ice drift extraction involves a trade-off among frequency channels: high-frequency channels offer finer spatial details but are strongly affected by atmospheric factors and melt-related radiometric noise, whereas low-frequency channels are more stable but too coarse to resolve small-scale drift. To address these challenges, this study proposes MF-IceDrift, a novel explainable deep learning framework for year-round, spatially complete Arctic sea ice drift extraction using multi-frequency AMSR2 data. Specifically, a Multi-frequency feature extraction and fusion module is designed to extract and fuse complementary features from different frequency channels. Moreover, a Transformer-based TransUpdate block and an augmentation consistency-based self-supervised strategy are incorporated to refine the flow estimation and ensure the spatial coherence of the drift fields. Validation against buoy observations demonstrates that MF-IceDrift achieves the best accuracy while maintaining 100% spatial coverage, consistently outperforming existing multi-frequency decision-level fusion methods as well as single-frequency baselines. The extracted drift fields exhibit a high degree of correlation with operational sea ice drift products, confirming the reliability of the large-scale drift patterns. Furthermore, the MF-IceDrift demonstrates generalization capabilities on the Microwave Radiation Imager onboard the Feng-Yun 3D (FY-3D MWRI) and Defense Meteorological Satellite Program Special Sensor Microwave Imager/Sounder (DMSP SSMIS) data. The deep learning network developed in this study provided a new approach for large-scale and long-term sea ice drift extraction using multi-frequency passive microwave data.

</details>


### [223] [Generating a 1 km nationwide long-term NDVI dataset for China (1982–2015) via an enhanced vegetation monitoring super-resolution network](https://doi.org/10.1080/15481603.2026.2694173)
*Mengmeng Sun,Song Ji,Dazhao Fan,Rongrong Zhang,Xin Liu,Zhen Yan*

Main category: GIScience & RS

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种高性能超分辨率（HPSR）方法，通过将5 km AVHRR NDVI数据降尺度为1 km，生成了中国1982-2015年间的1 km NDVI时间序列数据集。该方法包含多尺度特征提取、CBAM注意力精炼和超分辨率重建三个子模块，结合DEM地形因子和土地覆盖数据，有效解决了传统NDVI产品在时空分辨率上的权衡问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的1 km MODIS NDVI产品起始于2000年，导致1982-2000年间缺乏高分辨率观测数据，限制了中国植被变化的系统性研究。为填补这一时空空白，需要构建一个长时序、高分辨率的NDVI数据集。

Method: 提出HPSR网络架构，包含三个子模块：(i)多尺度特征提取网络，通过不同尺度并行卷积提取纹理信息并融合；(ii)CBAM注意力精炼网络，结合通道和空间注意力机制对融合特征加权；(iii)超分辨率重建网络，利用上采样模块和残差块将特征图重建为高分辨率。以1 km MODIS NDVI为参考，辅以DEM和CLCD数据，将AVHRR NDVI从5 km降尺度到1 km。

Result: HPSR框架有效缓解了标准卷积模型中的数值集中问题，MAE降至0.050，RMSE降至0.061，PSNR保持在27 dB以上，成功保持了原始信号熵和统计分布特征。

Conclusion: 该研究解决了空间分辨率与时间覆盖范围之间的传统权衡问题，生成了中国1982-2015年1 km NDVI数据集，为十年尺度的生态监测和生物物理分析提供了一致、高质量的基础数据。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。该方法本身就是遥感降尺度研究，改进方案包括：(1)引入更多辅助数据如气象数据（降水、温度）和土壤水分数据，进一步提升降尺度精度；(2)探索时序注意力机制或3D卷积，更好地捕捉NDVI的时间动态特征；(3)将HPSR框架推广到其他遥感指数（如EVI、LAI、NPP）的降尺度重建；(4)结合生成对抗网络（GAN）进一步提升超分辨率重建的纹理细节；(5)考虑在模型中引入物理约束（如植被生长物候规律），增强降尺度结果的生态可解释性。

Abstract (英文): The Normalized Difference Vegetation Index (NDVI) serves as a crucial indicator for assessing extended vegetation trends. Existing 1 km MODIS NDVI products start from 2000, leaving a gap in high‑resolution observations for 1982–2000 and limiting systematic studies of vegetation change across China. To fill this spatio-temporal void, we built a 1 km nationwide NDVI time series dataset covering 1982–2015 by downscaling the 5 km AVHRR NDVI with a High‑Performance Super‑Resolution (HPSR) method. The proposed network architecture is composed of three key submodules that work sequentially and synergistically: (i) A multi-scale feature extraction network first extracts texture information across different receptive fields through parallel convolutions at varying scales, achieving multi-scale fusion via feature splicing. (ii) The resulting fused features are then passed to an attention refinement network that utilizes the Convolutional Block Attention Module (CBAM), incorporating channel and spatial attention mechanisms, to adaptively weight the fusedu features, thereby emphasizing significant vegetation regions while reducing irrelevant noise. (iii) Finally, the refined features are fed into a super-resolution network that utilizes up-sampling modules and residual blocks to reconstruct the feature maps to a high resolution. The model spatially downscales AVHRR NDVI data from an approximately 5 km resolution to 1 km, utilizing high-quality 1 km MODIS NDVI as a reference dataset, and integrating DEM terrain factors and the China Land Cover Database (CLCD) as ancillary data. The experimental findings indicate that the HPSR framework effectively mitigates the numerical centralization common in standard convolutional models through an integrated attention mechanism, achieving a significant reduction in MAE (0.050) and RMSE (0.061) while maintaining a PSNR above 27 dB. By ensuring a holistic enhancement of NDVI sequences from high spatial fidelity to long-term physical and logical consistency, the model successfully preserves the original signal entropy and statistical distribution characteristics across complex landscapes. Consequently, by resolving the traditional trade-off between spatial resolution and temporal coverage, this study produced a 1 km nationwide NDVI dataset for China (1982–2015), furnishing a consistent, high-quality baseline for decadal-scale ecological monitoring and biophysical analysis.

</details>


### [224] [A coherence time-series framework for earthquake-induced building damage detection using SAR](https://doi.org/10.1080/15481603.2026.2698138)
*Yeji Lee,Sang-Eun Park*

Main category: GIScience & RS

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于顺序相干时序框架的地震建筑损伤检测方法，通过显式建模震前、同震、震后各阶段的去相干分量，推导出两种互补损伤指标（ρ0和ρ1），并在日本两次地震的Sentinel-1数据上验证，相比传统方法显著降低虚警率，AUPRC提升至0.56-0.66。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有InSAR相干性建筑震害检测方法受多种非结构损伤去相干机制干扰，且仅依赖有限影像对提取相干性变化，难以将结构损伤信号与其他时变贡献分离，导致虚警率高。

Method: 构建顺序相干时序框架，根据时空特征显式区分震前、同震、震后各阶段去相干分量；通过候选像素选择和时域平均抑制非损伤相干性波动，放大与建筑损伤相关的阶跃变化；推导两种指标：ρ0（震前-同震平均相干比）用于快速初判，ρ1（震前-震后平均相干比，排除同震像对）用于高特异性持久损伤识别。

Result: 在益城町和轮岛市两个地震场景下，相比三种代表性相干性指标，该方法持续降低城市和非城市区域的虚警率；在不平衡类别条件下，ρ1的AUPRC分别达到0.56和0.66，而参考方法仅为0.22-0.39。

Conclusion: 相干去相干的显式时序建模为震后损伤制图提供了物理可解释且操作实用的方法基础。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：95%。本文本身就是InSAR遥感震害评估领域的论文。改进方案：①可引入多极化SAR（如双极化、全极化）相干性信息，增强对建筑结构损伤类型的区分能力；②结合光学遥感影像（如高分辨率卫星影像或无人机影像）进行多模态融合，利用光学影像的纹理特征辅助验证相干性检测结果；③引入深度学习时序模型（如LSTM、Transformer）替代手工设计的时域滤波规则，自动学习去相干分量的时空模式；④扩展至滑坡、火山等地质灾害的时序相干性分析，验证框架的泛化能力。

Abstract (英文): Earthquake-induced building damage detection using interferometric SAR coherence is complicated by multiple decorrelation mechanisms unrelated to structural damage. Most existing approaches rely on coherence changes extracted from a limited number of image pairs, which makes it difficult to isolate structural damage signals from other temporally varying contributions. This study proposes a sequential coherence time-series framework that explicitly models decorrelation components across pre-, co-, and post-seismic phases according to their distinct spatiotemporal characteristics, and derives two complementary damage indicators: the average pre-to-co-seismic coherence ratio (ρ0) and the average pre-to-post-seismic coherence ratio (ρ1). Both indicators combine candidate pixel selection and temporal averaging to suppress damage-irrelevant coherence variability while amplifying step-type transitions associated with building damage. ρ0 supports rapid initial assessment using the first post-event acquisition, whereas ρ1 provides higher specificity to persistent structural damage by excluding the co-seismic pair from the indicator computation. The framework is validated using Sentinel-1 time series over Mashiki Town and Wajima City, affected by the 2016 Kumamoto and 2024 Noto Peninsula earthquakes. Compared with three representative coherence-based damage indicators, the proposed approach consistently reduces false alarms in both urban and non-urban areas. ρ1 demonstrates substantially improved precision–recall performance under class imbalance conditions, with AUPRC values of 0.56 and 0.66 at the two sites, compared to 0.22–0.39 for the reference methods. These results indicate that explicit temporal modeling of coherence decorrelation provides a physically interpretable and operationally practical basis for post-earthquake damage mapping.

</details>

### [227] [Context Graphs for Proactive Enterprise Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07721)
*Avinash Kumar*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出基于上下文图的主动式智能体框架（Context Graph + Delta Detection Engine + Proactivity Scorer + Surfacing Layer），使企业AI系统从被动响应变为主动推送相关信息，在合同管理、事故响应和销售管线三个场景下达到Precision@5为0.83、误报率0.11、平均呈报时间从47分钟降至30秒以内。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RAG和智能体框架本质上是反应式的——必须等待用户查询才能行动，导致企业生产力提升受限。论文认为真正的企业效率提升需要系统能在用户提问前主动推送相关、可操作的信息。

Method: 构建上下文图（Context Graph）——一种实时关系型数据结构，建模企业实体、关系和状态变迁；在此基础上设计增量检测引擎（Delta Detection Engine）持续监控状态变化、主动评分器（Proactivity Scorer）按紧迫性、相关性和角色匹配度排序候选洞察、以及基于LLM的表层呈现层（Surfacing Layer）生成带可解释性依据的排名通知。形式化定义了统一主动评分函数，并用NetworkX和Anthropic Claude API提供了完整端到端Python实现。

Result: 在合同生命周期管理、工程事故响应和销售管线健康三个企业场景下，Precision@5达到0.83，误报率0.11，平均呈报时间从反应式基线的47分钟降至30秒以内。

Conclusion: 上下文图驱动的主动式框架能显著提升企业AI系统的主动性，在准确率和时效性上均优于传统反应式方法，为企业智能助手提供了从"等提问"到"主动推"的可行技术路线。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：75%。遥感领域同样存在大量"被动查询"模式（用户下载影像后才分析），可借鉴此框架实现主动监测：1）将遥感时序影像（如Sentinel-2时间序列）构建为"地理上下文图"，像素/对象为实体，空间邻接和时序依赖为关系；2）Delta Detection Engine对应变化检测（如土地利用变化、植被指数突变）；3）Proactivity Scorer按灾害紧迫性（如洪泛面积增速）、区域相关性和用户角色（应急部门vs科研）排序；4）Surfacing Layer用LLM生成变化报告及地理可解释性文本。需注意遥感数据量大、关系图稀疏性高，需优化图结构和增量更新策略。

Abstract (英文): Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) and agentic frameworks have advanced enterprise AI considerably, yet agents remain fundamentally reactive: they wait for a human query before acting. This paper argues that genuine enterprise productivity gains require proactive agents: systems that surface relevant, actionable information to workers before they ask. We propose the Context Graph, a live relational data structure that models enterprise entities, their relationships, and state transitions over time. Built on this graph, we define a Delta Detection Engine that continuously monitors state changes, a Proactivity Scorer that ranks candidate insights by urgency, relevance, and persona-fit, and a Surfacing Layer powered by an LLM that delivers ranked notifications with grounded explanations. We formalize each component, derive a unified Proactivity Score function, and provide a complete end-to-end Python implementation using NetworkX and the Anthropic Claude API. Evaluation across three generic enterprise case studies (contract lifecycle management, engineering incident response, and sales pipeline hygiene) demonstrates that context-graph-driven proactivity achieves Precision@5 of 0.83, a false positive rate of 0.11, and reduces mean time to surface from 47 minutes (reactive baseline) to under 30 second.

</details>

*Joshua R. Waite,Dana Golden,Brett Indelicato,Kevin Camp,Mojdeh Saadati,Shannon Regan,Patrick Schnable,Baskar Ganapathysubramanian,Carlos Messina,Suzanne Thornsbury,Soumik Sarkar*

Method: 将全球经济模型（GTAP）与作物生物物理模型（APSIM）进行集成，利用AI技术构建自然语言交互界面，使用户能够通过提问方式获取跨学科的分析结果。

Result: 成功开发了能够整合经济与生物物理模型的AI工具，实现了通过自然语言查询来分析和响应供应链冲击的跨学科影响。

Conclusion: 该AI工具能够有效整合经济和生物物理模型，为农业供应链冲击分析提供跨学科的自然语言交互平台，有助于提高决策效率。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。该工具框架可用于整合遥感数据（如卫星植被指数、土壤湿度、土地利用变化等）替代或补充APSIM的部分生物物理输入，从而实时监测作物生长状态和环境胁迫。同时，遥感数据可作为经济模型（如GTAP）中区域生产力冲击的空间显式输入，增强供应链冲击预测的时空精度。

Abstract (英文): Agricultural supply chains are vulnerable to disruptions through linked biophysical and economic systems. We develop an AI-powered tool that integrates economic models (GTAP) with biophysical models (APSIM) to analyze supply chain shocks, enabling policymakers and market participants to assess cross-disciplinary impacts through queries and responses written in natural language.
