### [229] [Adversarial Social Epistemology for Assemblies of Humans and Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07760)
*Mihnea C. Moldoveanu,Joel A. C. Baum*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种对抗性社会认识论（ASE）框架，用于分析密集交互的传播环境中，行为者如何利用证言链、推理、机构认证和隐性信任构成的承诺与权利，通过扭曲、隐瞒、编造或策略性模糊信息来谋取私利。论文指出现有概念（如信息茧房、回音室、错误信息扩散）不足以解释这些现象，并提供了分析语言、信任破坏机制以及基于认识网络和推理主义语义学的审计与补救机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究对信息茧房、回音室和错误信息扩散的描述无法充分解释在密集交互的传播环境中，行为者如何利用构成社会信任的承诺与权利系统性地破坏信任，亟需一种新的分析框架来捕捉这种对抗性认识行为。

Method: 采用理论分析方法，融合社会认识论、推理主义语义学和认识网络理论，构建对抗性社会认识论（ASE）分析框架，提出用于描述信任破坏机制和审计补救的概念语言与机制。

Result: 1. 确立了ASE作为分析密集交互传播环境中信任破坏行为的新框架；2. 提供了描述行为者如何利用语言和制度性承诺扭曲信息的概念工具；3. 提出了破坏可审计推论链的机制及其补救方案。

Conclusion: 对抗性社会认识论（ASE）为理解现代传播环境中系统性的信任滥用提供了必要分析视角，通过强化推论链的可审计性可实现信任修复。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：70%。遥感领域同样存在复杂的多源数据融合与逐级推论的传播链（如从原始影像→特征提取→分类结果→决策产品），每个环节都可能引入人为或系统性的偏差。可将ASE框架用于：1）建立遥感数据产品传播链的审计机制，追踪每个推论环节的可靠性与潜在操纵点；2）设计对抗性信息检测算法，识别在数据解释链中故意模糊、遗漏或歪曲信息的行为；3）结合推理主义语义学，构建遥感产品声明与其证据链之间的承诺-责任映射模型，提升产品可信度。

Abstract (英文): We outline an adversarial social epistemology (ASE) for densely interactive communicative landscapes in which public assertions are scaffolded by chains of testimony, inference, institutional certification, and tacit trust. In such landscapes, agents have incentives and affordances to distort, color, omit, fabricate, or strategically under-specify information for private, reputational, rhetorical, or material gains. We argue that these phenomena are not adequately captured by familiar descriptions of epistemic bubbles, echo chambers, or misinformation diffusion. What requires explanation is how communicative agents exploit the commitments and entitlements that normally make scaffolded assertions trustworthy. We provide language that delivers the requisite analysis, outline mechanisms that subvert trust in scaffolded public communications, and outline machinery for auditing and redressing trust breaches arising from subverting the auditability of inferential chains, drawing on epistemic networks, enriched with an inferentialist semantics for interpreting assertions.

</details>


### [230] [Aligning Clinical Needs and AI Capabilities: A Survey on LLMs for Medical Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07761)
*Qi Peng,Jiatong Li,Sirui Huang,Yiyang Jiang,Kaisong Gong,Ronger Ding,Shijie Ye,Changmeng Zheng,Yi Cai,Xiaobo Yang,Jin Huang,Xiao-Yong Wei,Qing Li*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文综述了医疗大语言模型（LLMs）在临床推理方面的进展，提出了连接临床实践与计算方法的双视图框架：临床侧基于Miller金字塔建立五级能力体系，计算侧将演绎、归纳、溯因推理模式与医学目标任务对应。引入涵盖五级推理能力的基准数据集，对18个SOTA模型进行评估，发现专科模型在诊断任务中表现优异，通用模型在决策支持和对话中领先。最后讨论了数据限制、幻觉、接地等挑战及未来方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有医疗LLM研究缺乏系统性的临床推理能力评估框架，临床实践与计算方法之间存在脱节，亟需建立统一视角来评估和指导医疗LLM的发展。

Method: 提出双视图方法：1）临床侧采用Miller金字塔的五级能力体系（知识回忆→动态病例管理）；2）计算侧将演绎、归纳、溯因推理模式映射到医学目标和任务；3）构建覆盖五级推理能力的基准数据集并在18个SOTA模型上进行评估。

Result: 医疗专科模型在诊断类任务中表现优异，通用模型在决策支持和对话任务中领先。基准测试揭示了不同模型在不同推理层次上的能力差异。

Conclusion: 当前医疗LLMs取得显著进展但仍面临数据限制、幻觉、接地等问题，未来需要向更安全、可靠、可融入工作流程的系统方向发展。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感领域可借鉴该双视图框架：1）临床侧Miller金字塔对应遥感中的"地物识别→场景理解→变化检测→动态监测→应急响应"五级能力体系；2）计算侧推理模式可应用于遥感解译中的演绎推理（基于物理模型）、归纳推理（从样本学习模式）和溯因推理（反演问题求解）；3）构建遥感领域多级推理能力基准数据集，评估不同模型在各类遥感任务中的表现。

Abstract (英文): Large language models (LLMs) have emerged as important tools in healthcare, showing growing potential for clinical reasoning and patient care. This survey examines recent progress in medical LLMs, focusing on reasoning applications and requirements. We present a dual-view approach that connects clinical practice with computational methods. On the clinical side, we establish a five-level competency scheme following Miller's Pyramid, progressing from knowledge recall to dynamic case management. On the computational side, we link deductive, inductive, and abductive reasoning patterns to common medical goals and tasks. We also introduce a benchmark dataset spanning five levels of medical reasoning capability and report results on 18 state-of-the-art models, revealing that medical specialist models excel in diagnosis-centric tasks while general models lead in decision support and dialogue. We conclude by discussing current progress and open challenges, including data limitations, hallucination, and grounding issues, and outline directions toward safer, more reliable, and workflow-ready systems.

### [231] [Alignment Plausibility: A New Standard for Assuring AI in Healthcare](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07766)
*Gwydion Williams,Sara Zannone,Bilal A Mateen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出"对齐合理性"概念，主张LLMs在心理健康支持中的安全性需通过三层对齐实现：明确的价值规范、嵌入价值的训练、部署中的监督，类比临床实践的保障体系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLMs在心理健康支持中广泛应用，但注意力经济驱动使其偏向维持用户参与而非提供有效心理支持；现有安全措施反应性和表面化，忽视了依赖、边界侵蚀、扭曲信念放大等长期风险。

Method: 提出三层对齐框架：1) 基于临床实践的规范化价值承诺；2) 将价值嵌入模型的训练；3) 部署中检测漂移和长期危害的监督。并借鉴生物学合理性概念，提出"对齐合理性"作为监管构念。

Result: 构建了"对齐合理性"概念，作为评估AI系统在健康领域安全性的结构化论证方法，用于判断系统是否对齐积极健康结果、无害且有益于患者。

Conclusion: AI在心理健康领域需要像人类临床实践一样，通过多层级的结构化对齐来确保安全，而"对齐合理性"可作为信任评估的监管框架。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：65%。该文提出的三层对齐框架可迁移至遥感AI系统安全评估：1) 明确遥感领域（如地理空间分析、灾害监测）的伦理与安全规范；2) 将领域规范嵌入遥感模型训练（如避免误分类导致错误决策）；3) 部署中持续监测模型漂移（如地物分类精度下降）和长尾风险。但遥感领域对即时物理后果的敏感性高于心理支持，需在价值规范层做针对性调整。

Abstract (英文): Large language models (LLMs) have become significant providers of mental health support, yet they remain products of an attention economy whose operational and commercial targets favour sustained engagement over the friction that effective psychological support often requires. Developers' safety responses have been largely reactive, addressing the most visible and acute harms while subtler, longer-term patterns of risk (e.g., dependency, boundary erosion, the amplification of distorted beliefs) receive less attention. We contend that making LLMs structurally safe requires alignment organised at three levels that mirror how society assures the safety of human clinical practice: 1) explicit value specification grounded in the codified normative commitments of clinical practice; 2) training that embeds those values in the model; and 3) oversight that detects drift and longer-term harm during deployment, much as clinical supervision does for human practice. Organising alignment in this way yields a construct we call alignment plausibility - a structured demonstration that a system's values, training regime, and oversight mechanisms are together consistent with safe and positive outcomes. We propose alignment plausibility as a regulatory construct (by drawing analogy to the established construct of biological plausibility) for AI in health: a principled way to argue for, or against, trust that systems are aligned to positive health outcomes, will cause no harm even where capable of doing so, and will ultimately lead to patient benefit.

### [232] [Idiobionics: The Unification of Privacy and Intelligent Robotic Prostheses](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07775)
*Kwesi Afari Darfoor,Patrick M. Pilarski,Bailey Kacsmar*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出"idiobionics"（个体仿生学）这一新研究方向，聚焦于智能仿生肢体的隐私风险问题。论文定义了该概念，梳理了相关文献，展示了潜在对抗性攻击的证据，并提出了开放研究问题，旨在在保护用户隐私的前提下充分发挥下一代仿生肢体的潜力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 1) 定义"idiobionics"这一新研究领域；2) 将其扎根于相关文献；3) 通过展示和讨论潜在对抗性攻击提供初步证据；4) 整理一份面向可穿戴机器人和其他人机交互自主系统研究人员的开放研究问题清单。

Result: 定义了idiobionics概念，提供了初步的对抗性攻击证据（如可能利用智能仿生肢体设计发起的攻击），并提出了该领域内的开放研究问题。

Conclusion: Idiobionics研究将有助于解锁机器人假肢及相关仿生设备的全部潜力，同时应对隐私挑战。

Abstract (英文): The human body is at the center of a growing family of technologies designed to tightly and persistently couple biological and digital systems. Robotic prostheses are a representative example of this tight coupling. Also referred to as bionic limbs, robotic prostheses are devices that support people who have lost limbs in pursuing daily life activities such as walking and grasping objects. Bionic limbs are now perceptive and responsive owing to their integration with advanced sensors and artificial intelligence-based control approaches. Consequently, such robotic prostheses can now be viewed as semiautonomous wearable robotic systems that can co-adapt with their users. However, the same sensing and control advancements that increase the capability of robotic prostheses also introduce threat vectors that could be exploited by malicious entities to violate the privacy of users. To fully realize the benefits of next-generation bionic limbs, we maintain it is important to directly understand and address these privacy risks and the barriers they might present to user adoption. This paper therefore introduces a new line of inquiry we term idiobionics to holistically investigate issues at the intersection of privacy and intelligent bionic limbs. As the main contribution of this paper, we define idiobionics, ground it in related literature, and provide preliminary evidence showing and discussing potential adversarial attacks that could exploit intelligent bionic limb designs. We then contribute a curated list of open research questions within idiobionics that are relevant to researchers in wearable robotics and other human-facing autonomous systems. We expect that idiobionics research will help unlock the full potential of robotic prostheses and related bionic devices.

### [233] [Infinity-Parser2 Technical Report](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07836)
*Zuming Huang,Jun Huang,Kexuan Ren,Baode Wang,Weizhen Li,Jianming Feng,Yu Wang,Yichen Yao,Shijun Lin,Yige Tang,Cheng Peng,Weidi Xu,Wei Chu,Yinghui Xu,Yuan Qi*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: Infinity-Parser2 是一个大型多模态文档解析模型，通过可控数据合成管线（生成5M双语标注语料库Infinity-Doc2-5M）和多任务强化学习（8个联合优化目标）实现端到端解析。发布Flash（低延迟，吞吐量提升3.68倍）和Pro（高精度，在olmOCR-Bench达87.6%）两个版本，超越DeepSeek-OCR-2等现有方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 真实标注的文档解析语料库长期匮乏，现有方法在数据规模、标注质量和多样性上存在不足，难以支撑高质量的端到端文档解析模型训练。

Method: 1）构建可控数据合成引擎，结合可调控渲染框架和迭代精炼循环，生成5M双语标注语料Infinity-Doc2-5M；2）设计可验证的多任务奖励系统，对8个联合训练目标（文档解析、布局分析、表格/数学公式/图表/化学式解析、文档VQA、通用多模态理解）进行联合强化学习；3）发布两个架构共享的变体：Flash（低延迟优化）和Pro（高精度优化）。

Result: Infinity-Parser2-Pro在olmOCR-Bench上达到87.6%，在ParseBench上达到74.3%，超越DeepSeek-OCR-2、PaddleOCR-VL-1.5和MinerU2.5；在图表、化学式和文档VQA任务上表现出强泛化能力。Flash版本相对Infinity-Parser-7B实现3.68倍吞吐量提升。

Conclusion: 通过可控数据合成与多任务强化学习相结合，有效解决了文档解析中标注数据匮乏的问题，在两个评测基准上达到SOTA性能，且验证了该方法在多种文档类型和下游任务上的泛化能力。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感领域同样面临标注数据匮乏问题（如遥感影像的建筑物/道路/地物解析），可直接借鉴其可控合成管线生成多样化的遥感标注数据（结合地理空间渲染引擎和迭代精炼）。多任务强化学习框架可适配遥感场景下的多任务联合优化（地物分类、目标检测、变化检测、语义分割、遥感VQA等），将文档的阅读顺序奖励替换为遥感中的空间语义一致性和地理空间排序奖励。Flash版本的低延迟特性对遥感实时/近实时应用（如灾害监测）具有直接价值。

Abstract (英文): We present Infinity-Parser2, a large multimodal model that couples a controllable data-synthesis pipeline with multi-task reinforcement learning for end-to-end document parsing, addressing the persistent scarcity of faithfully annotated parsing corpora. Our contributions are threefold. First, we build a scalable synthesis engine, pairing a controllable rendering framework with an iterative refinement loop, and use it to construct and open-source Infinity-Doc2-5M: a 5-million-sample bilingual (Chinese/English) corpus spanning diverse document types, annotated with element bounding boxes, canonical content forms (Markdown, HTML, LaTeX, SMILES, structured charts), and full-page reading order. Second, we introduce a verifiable, multi-task reward system that enables Joint Reinforcement Learning across eight co-trained objectives (document parsing, layout analysis, table parsing, math formula parsing, chart parsing, chemical formula parsing, document VQA, and general multimodal understanding), unifying perception, structure, and reasoning in a single optimization signal. Third, we release two variants under a shared architecture: Infinity-Parser2-Flash, optimized for low-latency inference with a $3.68\times$ throughput gain over Infinity-Parser-7B, and Infinity-Parser2-Pro, engineered for precision-critical settings. Infinity-Parser2-Pro reaches state-of-the-art 87.6% on olmOCR-Bench and 74.3% on ParseBench, surpassing DeepSeek-OCR-2, PaddleOCR-VL-1.5, and MinerU2.5, with strong generalization to charts, chemical formulas, and document VQA.

Abstract (英文): Artificial intelligence (AI) is beginning to reshape actuarial practice, particularly in domains that require reasoning over unstructured documents, heterogeneous data sources, and regulated decision workflows. Actuaries now face a design space that ranges from traditional rule-based automation to large language models (LLMs), retrieval-augmented generation (RAG), and multi-agent ``agentic'' systems that plan, retrieve, call tools, and reflect. This paper examines how these emerging architectures can support actuarial priorities such as transparency, auditability, and human-in-the-loop governance, with a focus on straight-through decision processes. To make these ideas concrete, we develop and analyze an agentic AI framework for straight-through underwriting of small commercial Business Owner Policies (BOPs). We construct a synthetic but realistic experimental environment and compare three underwriting pipelines: (i) a single-LLM baseline, (ii) a naive RAG system, and (iii) a multi-agent ``Agentic RAG'' pipeline that combines targeted retrieval, third-party data checks, and explicit multi-step rule evaluation. The agentic system performs best overall, with the largest gains in multi-step and missing-information scenarios, where structured retrieval and reflection help the model avoid unsupported straight-through decisions.

### [237] [Feedback Manipulation Regularization: Enabling Offline Agent Alignment for Imitation Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07859)
*Benjamin Poole,Minwoo Lee*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出反馈操作正则化（FMR）方法，利用评估性反馈作为纠正信号，在离线序列决策环境中提升模仿学习策略的对齐性，最高减少98%的对齐偏差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有对齐方法主要将人类演示和反馈作为多阶段流水线处理，缺乏在完全序列决策环境中利用这些互补信号进行单阶段离线训练的研究。

Method: 提出FMR（反馈操作正则化），一种算法无关的方法，将评估性反馈作为纠正信号，正则化模仿学习策略，使其行为更符合人类价值观。

Result: 在改进的Safety Gymnasium环境中，FMR使多种模仿学习算法的对齐偏差最多降低98%，且在数据稀缺和非专家演示场景下保持鲁棒性。

Conclusion: FMR能有效利用评估性反馈增强模仿学习的对齐性，是一种简单、鲁棒且适用于多种算法的单阶段离线训练方法。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。具体方案：遥感智能体（如卫星自主任务规划、无人机航线决策）的行为需对齐人类安全规范。可将FMR引入遥感决策任务：(1) 利用遥感专家对智能体行为（如观测目标选择、资源调度）的评估性反馈作为正则化信号；(2) 在Safety Gymnasium框架基础上构建遥感决策安全约束环境（如禁飞区、敏感目标规避）；(3) 结合遥感领域少量对齐演示数据与大量无标注轨迹，通过FMR实现单阶段离线训练，减少违规行为。

Abstract (英文): Reinforcement learning (RL) research has increasingly shifted focus towards alignment, ensuring agents learn behaviors adhering to human values. While human demonstrations and feedback have proven crucial for alignment, existing approaches predominantly combine these signals using multi-stage pipelines designed for the contextual bandit framing of language generation. Yet little work explores how these complementary inputs can serve as a richer, interconnected signal for single-stage offline training in fully sequential decision-making environments. We propose Feedback Manipulation Regularization (FMR), an algorithm-agnostic method that harnesses evaluative feedback as a corrective signal to improve the alignment of imitation learning policies. We adapt Safety Gymnasium environments to be a principled testbed for alignment evaluation, demonstrating improved aptitude and up to a 98\% reduction in misalignment across a range of imitation learning algorithms. FMR remains robust in limited data regimes, even when learning from scarce aligned and uninformative noisy demonstrations.

Result: 生成了94行提示-完成-推理轨迹数据，领域可追溯提示占比从1/78提升至94/94，所有检索答案（84/84）均与源数据匹配。

Abstract (英文): There is relatively little, public, and model-ready data on industrial machinery for African economies. This makes it hard to do quantitative analysis or to train language models on numeric tasks grounded in that setting. We release two things to help with part of this problem. The first is the Nigeria Machinery Usage and Failures Dataset: 89 machine-level records across 28 indicators, covering Nigeria's manufacturing and oil and gas sectors from 2006 to 2025. Every record names a public source and is decoded by a codebook. The second is a method for building chain-of-thought (CoT) reasoning examples from these sparse numeric values. The result is 94 prompt, completion, and reasoning-trace rows. In every row, the prompt names the real indicator, subsector, year, and source of the record it comes from. The data adaptation work was carried out by Adaption Labs. Along the way we describe a problem that is common when language models are used to build datasets. The prompts can match the real numbers while saying nothing about the real domain. We show that fixing this raises the share of domain-grounded prompts from 1 out of 78 in an earlier release to 94 out of 94, and that every retrieval answer now matches its source value (84 out of 84). We release the data, the reasoning layer, and a per-row provenance file under CC-BY-4.0. We are clear about the limits. With 89 records and 17 indicators that have only one observation, this is a reference and seed dataset, not a large training set. Most reasoning rows are retrieval rather than multi-step computation.

### [239] [Persona Cartography: Charting Language Model Personality Traits in Weight Space](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07916)
*Luke Baines,Anton Gonzalvez Hawthorne,Mariia Koroliuk,Irakli Shalibashvili,Clément Dumas,Konstantinos Voudouris,David Demitri Africa*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出将大语言模型的行为模式视为人格特质，使用OCEAN框架（开放性、尽责性、外倾性、宜人性、神经质）进行分解、测量和控制。通过训练低秩适配器来放大或抑制特定特质，实验表明适配器能单调移动目标特质、近似可加组合、保持能力表现，并影响安全相关行为。同时引入无监督心理测量流程，从模型输出中恢复四个可解释行为因子。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型表现出重复的行为模式（人格），这些模式影响泛化能力和安全性，但缺乏可靠的分解、测量和控制工具。

Method: 1) 使用OCEAN框架描述模型人格；2) 训练低秩适配器放大/抑制特质；3) 使用LLM评判器评估效果；4) 跨6个模型（3个系列，4B-32B）验证；5) 引入无监督心理测量流程提取行为因子。

Result: 1) 适配器单调移动目标特质；2) 适配器可近似可加组合构造混合人格；3) 中等尺度下保持能力性能；4) 特质轴影响安全相关行为（神经质影响挫败感，宜人性影响谄媚）；5) 无监督流程提取出语调、主动性、说教性、认知谨慎四个因子。

Conclusion: 人格控制可通过权重空间中的学习、缩放和组合特质来实现，为人格测量、模型编辑和安全性之间搭建桥梁。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感领域中，不同任务（如分类、检测、分割）需要模型展现不同行为倾向。该人格控制方法可应用于遥感基础模型的行为调控：1) 在变化检测任务中，通过增强尽责性（Conscientiousness）提升对微小变化的敏感性；2) 在云/阴影遮挡场景下，通过降低神经质（Neuroticism）减少虚警率，增强模型鲁棒性；3) 在多任务遥感模型中，利用适配器可加组合特性动态调整行为偏好以适应不同下游任务；4) 无监督心理测量流程可迁移至遥感模型，提取任务相关的行为因子（如对地物细节的谨慎程度、对异常目标的响应倾向等），辅助模型诊断与调试。

Abstract (英文): Large language models exhibit recurring behavioural patterns -- personas -- that shape generalisation and safety, but we lack reliable tools for decomposing, measuring, and controlling them. Our central insight is to treat personas as positions in a space of behavioural traits, using the OCEAN framework to describe model personas in terms of Openness, Conscientiousness, Extraversion, Agreeableness, and Neuroticism. We train low-rank adapters to amplify or suppress individual traits, and evaluate their effects using an LLM-judge calibrated against a human-validated panel, trait-specific multiple-choice benchmarks, and standard capability evaluations. Across six models from three families (4B-32B), we find that each adapter moves its target trait largely monotonically with scale, combines approximately additively with other adapters to construct mixed personas, and preserves performance on capability benchmarks at moderate scales. We further show that the induced trait axes affect safety-relevant behaviour in downstream evaluations: for example, moving along neuroticism and agreeableness axes affects frustration and sycophancy respectively. We also introduce an unsupervised psychometric pipeline that recovers four interpretable behavioural factors (tone, initiative, didacticism, epistemic caution) from model rollouts. Persona control can then be considered in terms of learning, scaling, and composing traits in weight space, providing a bridge between personality measurement, model editing, and safety.

### [240] [Evaluating the Effect of Frame Rate in Sequence-Based Classification of Autism-Related Self-Stimulatory Hand Idiosyncrasies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07957)
*Raunak Mondal,Peter Washington*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文针对自闭症谱系障碍（ASD）患者自我刺激行为的视频自动检测，研究了两个关键问题：(1) 最优序列神经网络架构（LSTM/GRU）和时间采样率（15帧间隔达98.75%准确率）；(2) 小样本行为数据集上的数据增强策略（上采样不可或缺，水平翻转效果最佳）。为数据稀缺的临床视频行为分类提供了架构选择、采样率和增强策略的具体指导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: (1) 在SSBD数据集上提取姿态特征，训练LSTM和GRU模型，比较6种帧采样间隔（1,5,15,30,45,90帧）的性能，并与CNN基线对比。(2) 采用I3D迁移学习管道，对10种数据增强策略进行消融研究，量化每种技术的边际贡献。此外，实施个性化机器学习方法，对每个受试者按时间分割视频段进行训练和测试。

Result: (1) LSTM和GRU均超越CNN基线（62-76%），峰值准确率分别达97.5%（LSTM）和98.75%（GRU），最优采样间隔为15帧。(2) 水平翻转单独准确率最高（48.78%），剔除上采样导致性能下降最大，表明其必要性。个性化模型预测一致（平均损失1.84，标准差0.79）。

Conclusion: 为小样本临床视频行为分类提供了具体的架构选择（GRU略优）、最优采样率（15帧间隔）和数据增强策略（上采样必不可少）的实践指导。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感领域中小样本视频行为/动作识别（如野生动植物监测、海上船只行为分析）可借鉴本文方法：(1) 采用姿态/骨架特征+GRU/LSTM架构替代传统3D CNN，在低帧率采样下依然保持高精度，适合遥感数据带宽受限场景；(2) 数据增强消融策略（特别是上采样和水平翻转）可直接迁移至遥感目标行为样本不均衡问题；(3) 个性化/按时间分割的评估范式可应用于遥感时序分析中的个体（如特定船只、车辆）行为建模。

Abstract (英文): Autism spectrum disorder (ASD) affects over 75 million individuals worldwide, yet scalable computational methods for remote behavioral screening remain limited. This study addresses two complementary challenges in automated detection of autism-related self-stimulatory behaviors from video: (1) identifying the optimal sequence-based neural network architecture and temporal sampling rate, and (2) characterizing data augmentation strategies for training on small behavioral datasets. For the first objective, long short-term memory (LSTM) and gated recurrent unit (GRU) models were trained on pose-derived features from the Self-Stimulatory Behavior Diagnosis (SSBD) dataset at frame sampling intervals of 1, 5, 15, 30, 45, and 90 frames. Both architectures exceeded prior convolutional neural network (CNN) baselines (62-76% accuracy), with peak accuracies of 97.5% (LSTM) and 98.75% (GRU) at a sampling interval of every 15 frames. For the second objective, ten data augmentation strategies were applied to an I3D transfer learning pipeline, with an ablation study quantifying the marginal contribution of each technique. Horizontal flip achieved the highest standalone accuracy (48.78%), while exclusion of upsampling from the augmentation pipeline produced the largest performance degradation, indicating its necessity for complex behavioral video augmentation. A personalized machine learning approach, in which per-subject models were trained and tested on temporally split segments of each video, produced consistent predictions (mean loss 1.84, SD 0.79). These results provide practitioners with concrete guidance on architecture selection, sampling rate, and augmentation strategy for video-based behavioral classification in data-scarce clinical domains.

### [241] [Agentic Neural Architecture Search](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.07984)
*Seokhoon Jeong,Mijung Kim,Taehwan Kim*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: AgentNAS提出了一种结合大语言模型（LLM）和神经架构搜索（NAS）的机制：LLM生成高质量种子架构并分解为“插槽架构”（slotted architecture），自动定义有界的任务特定搜索空间供NAS探索，无需人工工程。在17个任务中，AgentNAS在11个任务上达到了新SOTA。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有NAS方法受限于人工设计的搜索空间，需要大量领域知识且每项新任务需重建；LLM虽能在开放空间生成架构，但如何最优分配LLM驱动设计与NAS驱动搜索之间的分工尚未被探索。

Method: AgentNAS采用三阶段模块化流水线：（1）LLM生成高质量种子架构；（2）将种子架构分解为“插槽架构”，即带有可互换命名模块插槽的脚手架，自动定义有界、任务特定的搜索空间；（3）在该空间内使用传统NAS进行组合搜索。通过消融实验独立测量各组件贡献。

Result: 在NAS-Bench-360和Unseen NAS基准的17个任务（分类、密集回归、分割、多标签标注，跨多种模态）上，AgentNAS在11个任务上达到新SOTA，超越包括任务特定专家设计在内的已发布基线。

Conclusion: LLM生成的种子架构本身已在多数任务上超越基线，NAS通过跨插槽的组合重组带来额外增益（独立LLM采样无法复制该模式）。两种搜索机制具有广泛互补性，且在三种不同能力的LLM上均表现稳健，证实分工方式的鲁棒性。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。AgentNAS的“插槽架构”思想可直接应用于遥感任务（如场景分类、语义分割、目标检测）：利用LLM生成针对遥感数据特点（多光谱、高分辨率、几何变形等）的种子架构，并将其分解为编码器-解码器-骨干网络-注意力模块等插槽，使NAS在自适应搜索空间内高效探索。需注意遥感任务中数据模态多样性和标注稀缺性对该方法的泛化能力构成挑战。

Abstract (英文): Neural architecture search (NAS) methods have grown increasingly efficient, yet they remain bounded by manually engineered search spaces that require substantial domain expertise and must be rebuilt for every new task. Large language models (LLMs) can generate architectures in an open-ended space, but how to optimally divide the labor between LLM-driven design and NAS-driven search remains unexplored. We propose a mechanism that bridges these two paradigms: an LLM produces a high-quality seed architecture, then decomposes it into a "slotted architecture", a scaffold with named, interchangeable module slots that automatically defines a bounded, task-specific search space for conventional NAS to explore, without manual engineering. We instantiate this mechanism in AgentNAS, a modular three-phase pipeline in which each component's contribution can be measured independently. On 17 tasks spanning classification, dense regression, segmentation, and multi-label tagging across diverse modalities (NAS-Bench-360 and Unseen NAS), AgentNAS establishes a new state of the art on 11 tasks, outperforming published baselines including task-specific expert designs. Ablation studies show that the two search mechanisms are broadly complementary: the LLM-generated seed already surpasses published baselines on the majority of tasks, and NAS delivers additional gains in most cases through combinatorial recombination across slots, a mode of search that independent LLM samples cannot replicate. These patterns hold across three LLMs of different capability levels, confirming that the division of labor is robust. Our code is available at https://github.com/alroimfebruary/AgentNAS.

### [242] [Concretized Proposition Prompting Resolves Composition-Knowledge Dichotomy in Large Language Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08018)
*Changhun Lee,Minguk Jeon,Jongkyung Shin,Chiehyeon Lim*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出了一种名为CPP（具体化命题提示）的框架，通过显式具体化与问题相关的命题，解决了大语言模型中组合性与知识性之间的二象性难题，在医学和数学等基准测试中表现优异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLMs在推理时常常难以平衡组合性（compositionality）与知识性（knowledgeability），即组合-知识二象性（Composition-Knowledge Dichotomy），现有方法偏向其中一方而牺牲另一方。

Method: 提出具体化命题提示（CPP）框架，显式地将与问题相关的命题进行具体化处理，作为提示输入给LLM，从而在推理过程中同时兼顾逻辑组合与事实知识。

Result: CPP在需要精确知识的医学基准测试中显著提升了推理性能，在注重演绎推理的数学基准测试上也具有竞争力。此外，CPP可扩展到多种基础模型和参数规模。

Conclusion: CPP作为一种基础性范式，弥合了基于组合与基于知识的方法之间的鸿沟，为解决组合-知识二象性提供了逻辑组织化与事实基础化的推理基础。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感领域同时需要组合推理（如多源数据融合、空间关系推理）和领域知识（如地物光谱特征、地理先验知识）。CPP可用于：1) 将遥感解译任务中的地理先验知识（如地物类型间的空间约束关系）具体化为显式命题，引导LLM进行更准确的场景理解；2) 在多模态遥感推理中，将视觉特征与地理知识通过具体化命题桥接，减少幻觉；3) 遥感变化检测中，将"变化类型"与"变化原因"等命题具体化，提升推理的因果逻辑性。

Abstract (英文): LLMs often struggle to balance compositionality with knowledgeability, a challenge we define as Composition-Knowledge Dichotomy. To address this, we propose Concretized Proposition Prompting (CPP), a framework that explicitly concretizes propositions relevant to questions. The results demonstrate that CPP significantly enhances reasoning performance, particularly in medical benchmarks where precise knowledge is paramount, while being competitive on math benchmarks where deductive reasoning is prioritized. Additional experiments reveal that CPP is scalable to various foundation models and parameter sizes, being a fundamental paradigm that bridges the gap between composition- and knowledge-based approaches. Consequently, CPP resolves the composition-knowledge dichotomy by providing a solid foundation for logically organized and factually grounded reasoning.

### [243] [From Prompts to Contracts: Harness Engineering for Auditable Enterprise LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08028)
*Joongho Ahn,Moonsoo Kim*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出一种harness-engineering方法，将企业级LLM应用从原型转化为可审计、可追溯的代理架构：将确定性逻辑移入代码、清单、模式和验证工件中，围绕可替换的组合边界构建，同时保留源支撑的声明作为运行时答案的权威依据。通过在五家韩国企业集团（25家上市公司）的数据上验证，该方法在源接地、实体路由、追踪、输出卫生和推荐语言等契约上保持稳定，且代码拥有的保障无法仅通过提示实现，同时保持安全性和实用性（120/120），而外部护栏虽能防止违规但过度拒绝，实用性降至88/120。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 企业级LLM应用从原型（依赖提示和检索上下文）走向产品化时，需要满足源边界、实体路由、答案契约和可重现追踪等需求，现有方法缺乏系统化的可审计架构。

Method: 提出harness-engineering方法，将确定性行为迁移到代码、manifest、schema和验证工件中，围绕可替换的组合边界构建，源支撑声明作为运行时答案权威。

Result: (1) 在固定验证场景中保持所有契约；(2) 在三种模型替换下，所有270次组合边界运行通过，失败仅限于模型组合侧并被捕获；(3) 代码拥有的保障不可仅通过提示复现，对比实验显示外部护栏过度拒绝（88/120），而本方法保持完整实用性（120/120）。

Conclusion: 该模式可重用，能将探索性原型转化为具有版本化源、控制和验证工件的可审计应用。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。该harness-engineering方法可应用于遥感大模型应用的产品化：1) 将遥感影像源（不同卫星、传感器）纳入源边界验证，确保模型输出仅基于授权数据源；2) 实体路由可对应地理实体（地块、建筑、植被类型）的路由分发；3) 输出卫生契约可规范遥感解译结果（如变化检测、目标识别）的输出格式和置信度表达；4) 可重现追踪用于记录从影像输入到结论输出的完整推理链路，满足遥感产品合规审计需求。

Abstract (英文): Enterprise large language model (LLM) applications often begin as prototypes whose behavior is carried by prompts and retrieval context. Productization adds requirements for source boundaries, entity routing, answer contracts, and reproducible traces. We present a harness-engineering approach that reconstructs this pattern into a traceable, auditable LLM-agent architecture: deterministic behavior moves into code, manifests, schemas, and validation artifacts around a replaceable composition boundary, while source-backed claims remain the authority for runtime answers. We instantiate it on a public-data slice of five Korean corporate groups (25 listed companies) and evaluate three research questions. (1) The harness preserves its source-grounding, entity-routing, trace, output-hygiene, and recommendation-language contracts across the fixed validation scenarios; a fault-injection control confirms the validators flag deliberately broken contracts. (2) The checks the harness enforces held under model substitution: across three hosted models, they passed on all 270 composition-boundary runs; failures were confined to the model-composed side and were caught and recorded. (3) The code-owned guarantees are load-bearing, not reproducible by prompting alone: holding the model fixed and varying only the enforcement layer, prompt instructions alone let recommendation-language and internal-trace-leakage violations reach the reader, which the harness blocks entirely. A bolt-on external guardrail prevents such violations too but over-refuses, dropping utility to 88/120 where the harness preserves full utility (120/120); in this ablation, only code-owned enforcement preserves both safety and utility. The result is a reusable engineering pattern for turning exploratory prototypes into auditable applications with versioned source, control, and validation artifacts.

</details>


### [244] [A safety-oriented hypothetico-deductive framework for AI-assisted differential diagnosis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08038)
*Fan Ma,Mauro Giuffrè,Donald Wright,Kent McCann,Mark Iscoe,Lingfei Qian,Mingyang Jiang,Chi Wing Ng,Na Hong,Huan He,Cathy Shyr,Qingyu Chen,Lee Schwamm,Lucila Ohno-Machado,Hua Xu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出AegisDx，一个面向安全的假设-演绎临床推理框架，通过协调多个专用LLM组件、结构化中间输出、证据检索接口和验证门控机制，生成广泛的鉴别诊断、强制筛查高风险"不可遗漏"疾病、验证推理依据，并构建可操作的下步措施。在多项评估中，AegisDx在诊断准确率、不可遗漏疾病捕获率和安全性评分上均显著优于独立LLM基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前LLM系统将诊断视为一次性预测任务，缺乏对高风险替代诊断的防护机制和推理验证能力，诊断错误严重威胁患者安全。

Method: AegisDx框架通过角色特定契约协调多个专用LLM组件，生成结构化中间输出，利用证据检索接口获取医学证据，并通过验证门控机制对推理过程进行校验，实现广泛的鉴别诊断生成、不可遗漏疾病筛查和推理验证。

Result: 在文献病例上，Top-3准确率提升7-17个百分点；在急诊病例上，不可遗漏疾病捕获率从52.0%提升至78.0%；在43份真实急诊病历盲评中，复合安全评分从4.31提升至4.55（5分制），p=2.1×10⁻⁴。

Conclusion: 将诊断AI设计为面向安全的推理框架，而非仅优化预测准确性，能够为急诊工作流提供更安全、更透明、更具临床意义的决策支持。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感解译与临床诊断具有高度类比性：1）将遥感场景视为"患者"，构建类似AegisDx的多组件协作框架，分别负责地物分类、异常检测（"不可遗漏"高风险地物，如变化区域、灾害痕迹）、证据检索（多时相影像/辅助数据）和推理验证（交叉验证不同数据源的一致性）；2）设计"不可遗漏"筛查门控，强制检测关键目标（如建筑物倒塌、森林火点），避免漏检；3）结构化中间输出（如语义分割图、变化检测图）替代"黑箱"预测，提升可解释性和可审计性。

Abstract (英文): Diagnostic error is a major threat to patient safety, yet current large language model (LLM) systems often treat diagnosis as a one-shot prediction task, lacking safeguards against missed high-risk alternatives or rigorous verification of their reasoning. Here, we present AegisDx, a safety-oriented framework for hypothetico-deductive clinical reasoning. AegisDx coordinates specialized LLM components through role-specific contracts, structured intermediate outputs, evidence-retrieval interfaces, and verification gates to generate broad differential diagnoses, enforce explicit screening for dangerous "must-not-miss" conditions, verify reasoning against grounded medical evidence, and structure actionable next steps. We evaluated AegisDx across three layers. On literature-derived case reports from NEJM and JAMA, with GPT-oss-120B as the shared backbone, Top-3 diagnostic accuracy was 59.9% versus 52.1% for the standalone LLM on JAMA cases and 62.7% versus 51.4% on NEJM cases. On cases from Annals of Emergency Medicine, Top-3 accuracy was 85.7% versus 68.6%; against physician-consensus must-not-miss diagnosis sets, AegisDx captured at least one such condition among its top three diagnoses in 78.0% of cases versus 52.0%. In a blinded physician evaluation of 43 real-world emergency department notes from the Yale New Haven Health System compared against GPT-5, AegisDx improved the physician-rated composite safety score from 4.31 to 4.55 on a 5-point scale (adjusted p = 2.1x10^-4), with qualitative gains in must-not-miss identification and reasoning safety. Our findings suggest that engineering diagnostic AI as a safety-oriented reasoning framework, rather than optimizing raw predictive accuracy alone, can provide a safer, more transparent, and clinically meaningful layer of bedside decision support for acute care workflows.

### [245] [When LLMs Agree, Are They Right? Auditing Self-Consistency and Cross-Model Agreement as Confidence Signals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08065)
*Kaihua Ding*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文通过大规模交叉实验（53个运行器、265,000个样本）证明，LLM作为评估者时，一致性（模型间或自身样本间的一致）并不代表正确性。一致性在特定条件下（如中档模型、计算分配）可作为正确性的弱代理，但对最一致的前沿模型反而会产生过度自信的错误。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前LLM-as-judge评估系统普遍假设“一致性即正确性”，即评分者之间或模型自采样之间的一致程度反映答案的准确性。本文旨在验证这一假设的可靠性，并探究一致性在何种条件下可以作为正确性的可用代理。

Method: 采用大规模跨运行器研究设计：53个运行器对分配的重叠案例抽取K=50个样本，涉及模型层级、提示策略和规模的对比，在GPQA Diamond和AIME两个基准上进行评估，总计265,000个样本。使用多数正确性作为部署标签，采用层级化运行器聚类自助法（hierarchical runner-clustered bootstrap）进行统计分析。

Result: 一致性是正向但较弱的预测因子（rho 0.20-0.59，在项目聚类重采样下均为正）。其有用性取决于条件：对未饱和的中档模型和计算分配场景效果最好；对最一致的前沿模型效果最差——表现为过度自信但准确率并未提高（GPQA上77%的案例结果条目一致性>=0.8，其中48%是错误的）。跨模型族检查（三个Claude层级）显示同样的前沿模型过度自信问题。

Conclusion: 自一致性只能是正确性的条件代理，而非独立的置信度分数。不能简单地将一致性视为正确性的可靠指标，特别是在评估前沿模型时需谨慎。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感领域常使用多模型集成或多时相数据一致性来提高分类/检测精度。本文的发现可直接用于遥感中的模型评估：1) 在多源遥感数据融合或模型集成时，不应盲目相信高一致性代表高精度，需引入地面真值验证；2) 对遥感大模型（如地理空间基础模型）的评估可借鉴本研究的层级化聚类自助法，避免因共享偏差导致的自一致性假象；3) 建议在遥感场景下（如变化检测、地物分类）引入跨模型族交叉验证，防范前沿模型过度自信导致的错误传播。

Abstract (英文): LLM-as-judge (Zheng et al., 2023) is increasingly the default for evaluating AI systems in enterprise pipelines, often scaled to ensembles (Verga et al., 2024) or "mixture-of-experts" (Shazeer et al., 2017) panels of judges. These systems share a key assumption: that consistency -- agreement among judges, or among a model's own samples -- indicates correctness. We show this assumption is unreliable. Agreement is not accuracy: a model can agree with itself, and different models can agree with each other, out of shared bias, a memorized heuristic, or an option-position prior rather than truth. We ask when agreement is nonetheless a usable proxy, in a large-scale cross-runner study: 53 runners drew K=50 samples for assigned overlapping cases across comparisons of model tier, prompting, and scale on GPQA Diamond and AIME -- 265,000 samples. Using majority-correctness as the deployment label and a hierarchical runner-clustered bootstrap, agreement is a positive but weak predictor (rho 0.20-0.59, all positive under item-clustered resampling) whose usefulness is regime-dependent: best for unsaturated mid-tier models and for allocating compute, and worst -- over-confident yet no more accurate -- for the most consistent frontier model (agreement >=0.8 on 77% of GPQA case-result entries, 48% of those wrong). An exploratory cross-family check on three Claude tiers shows the same frontier over-confidence, with confident errors recurring across providers above a marginal-preserving null. Self-consistency is thus a conditional proxy for correctness, not a standalone confidence score. We publicly release the de-identified per-run rows and answer distributions.

</details>


### [246] [Persuasion Attacks Can Decrease Effectiveness of CoT Monitoring](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08066)
*Jennifer Za,Julija Bainiaksina,Nikita Ostrovsky,Tanush Chopra,Victoria Krakovna*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文研究了链式思维（CoT）监控在面对对抗性说服攻击时的脆弱性，发现CoT监控反而会使有害行为批准率平均增加9.5%，并提出了一种跨模型家族的事实核查监控框架，可将批准率降低高达45%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究表明CoT监控是AI Agent的安全机制，但大语言模型易受基于说服的越狱攻击。作者想验证这种脆弱性是否延伸到监控LLM本身——即对抗性Agent能否通过说服其CoT监控器来批准违反策略的行动。

Method: 设计了一个包含40个任务的评估框架，分析数千次Agent-监控器交互。Agent被指示论证违反策略的提案。对比了有无CoT监控的场景，并提出了事实核查监控框架（fact-checker与monitor配对），探索了不同模型家族组合的效果。

Result: 在对抗性场景中，监控器访问Agent的CoT推理反而使有害行为批准率平均增加9.5%；使用不同模型家族的事实核查器（如Claude 3.7 Sonnet监控器+GPT-4.1事实核查器）可将批准率降低45%，而同一模型仅降低6%。

Conclusion: 仅靠CoT监控不足以抵御对抗性说服攻击，跨模型多样性的联合监控架构提供了一种有效的缓解手段。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：75%。具体方案：（1）遥感任务中常需多模型协同解译（如变化检测、目标识别），可借鉴本文的跨模型家族事实核查框架，用不同架构的模型（如CNN+ViT+Transformer）分别承担特征提取与验证角色，提升解译结果的可信度。（2）遥感数据存在对抗性噪声（如云遮挡、传感器误差），可设计层次化监控流水线：初级模型进行遥感解译，次级模型对其推理过程进行事实核查，降低误检率。（3）引入多视角CoT机制，让不同遥感模型各自生成推理链并交叉验证，类似本文的多模型监控思路。

Abstract (英文): Chain-of-thought (CoT) monitoring is a promising safety mechanism for AI agents, based on the premise that visible reasoning traces can surface misaligned or deceptive behavior. While effective in standard scenarios, recent work highlights that LLMs remain vulnerable to persuasion-based jailbreaks, where natural-language arguments override model constraints. We stress-test whether this vulnerability extends to monitoring LLMs: can an adversarial agent persuade its CoT monitor to approve proposed actions that violate the monitor's policy? We design an evaluation framework with 40 tasks and analyze thousands of agent-monitor interactions, where agents are instructed to argue for policy-violating proposals. We find that in such adversarial settings, monitor access to the agent's CoT reasoning increases rather than decreases approval of harmful actions on average by 9.5%, as the scratchpad provides an additional persuasion channel. To address this, we introduce a fact-checking monitoring framework. We find that a fact-checker and monitor pairing from different model families, for example a Claude 3.7 Sonnet monitor paired with a GPT-4.1 fact-checker, reduces approval of policy-violating actions by up to 45%, compared to only 6%, when using the same model for both fact-checking and monitoring roles. Our results demonstrate that CoT monitoring alone may be insufficient against adversarial persuasion, and that model-diverse fact-checking provides a robust mitigation.

### [247] [PARA-PV: Physics-Aware Retrieval-Augmented PV Prediction Based on Frozen Foundation Model and Distribution Shift Correction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08079)
*Hang Fan,Weican Liu,Ying Lu,Dunnan Liu,Long Cheng,Wei Wei*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出PARA-PV框架，通过物理感知检索增强、时序基础模型校准、分布偏移校正和物理约束损失函数，实现高精度光伏功率预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 光伏发电受天气变化、昼夜交替、工况依赖动态和严格物理约束共同影响，现有预测方法难以充分融合物理知识，导致预测精度不足。

Method: 1) 物理感知检索增强学习器：检索与当前窗口在时序形态、功率水平、PV运行状态和日内时段一致的相似历史轨迹；2) 残差适配器：用Chronos时序基础模型校准基础预测；3) 物理感知分布偏移校正模块：根据功率、天气、时间戳和昼夜条件调整预测；4) 物理约束损失函数：将样本分为峰、斜坡、夜间和常规四种模式并自适应重加权。

Result: PARA-PV在光伏功率预测任务上达到高精度，代码已开源。

Conclusion: 物理知识嵌入全过程（检索、校准、偏移校正、损失函数）能有效提升光伏预测性能，且框架设计具有通用性。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：90%。该框架可直接迁移至遥感时间序列预测任务（如植被指数NDVI预测、地表温度预测）：1) 检索增强模块可检索历史遥感影像序列中相似物候/气候模式；2) 分布偏移校正可处理遥感数据中的季节/昼夜/云覆盖等状态变化；3) 物理约束损失可针对遥感中的关键状态（如火灾、洪水事件）进行加权；4) 将Chronos替换为遥感专用的时间序列基础模型（如SatMAE）可进一步提升适配性。

Abstract (英文): Accurate photovoltaic (PV) power forecasting is essential for reliable grid dispatch and renewable energy integration, yet it remains challenging because PV generation is jointly shaped by weather variability, day-night transitions, regime-dependent dynamics, and strict physical constraints. We propose PARA-PV, a Physics-Aware Retrieval-Augmented framework that embeds physical knowledge throughout the forecasting process. The framework first encodes multivariate PV observations into patch-level representations and, through a physics-aware retrieval-augmented learner, retrieves historical patches and analog trajectories that are consistent with the current window in temporal shape, power level, PV operating state, and intra-day period; this yields a physically grounded base forecast. To supplement local memory with broader temporal knowledge, the base forecast is then calibrated against a frozen Chronos time-series foundation-model prior through a lightweight residual adapter, so that general temporal regularities are adapted to PV-specific dynamics without overriding the physically grounded prediction. Because residual conditional distribution shifts persist when weather and diurnal regimes change, a physics-aware distribution shift correction module subsequently adjusts the preliminary forecast using power, weather, timestamp, and day/night conditions, applying gated mean-shift and scale corrections selectively. Finally, a physics-constrained loss function partitions the samples into peak, ramping, night-time, and regular regimes and adaptively reweights their error contributions, preventing the dominant regular regime from suppressing learning of operationally critical states. Our code is available at https://github.com/weican1103/PARA-PV.

### [248] [CausalDS: Benchmarking Causal Reasoning in Data-Science Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08093)
*Andrej Leban,Yuekai Sun*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出了CausalDS基准，用于评估大语言模型在具备工具使用能力的智能体数据科学工作流中的因果推理能力。该基准通过结构因果模型（SCM）生成合成数据，并覆盖Pearl三阶因果阶梯任务，同时包含不完美观测、编码任务和弃权评分机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准要么是符号因果推理（缺乏真实数据分析），要么是数据分析基准（缺乏原则性的因果数据结构）；因果评估数据集多来自现有来源的模板化变体，缺乏系统性生成的合成因果结构。因此需要一种能同时评估符号因果推理、数据科学、不确定性量化、弃权判断和工具使用的综合性基准。

Method: 1) 从采样的结构因果模型（SCM）出发，生成观测数据和基于真实领域描述的自然语言故事；2) 可选地基于真实数据集的经验分布来锚定基准组件构成；3) 从每个场景推导覆盖Pearl三阶（关联、干预、反事实）的任务；4) 包含数据科学编码组件，需多工具协作完成；5) 通过观测模型生成不完美观测；6) 将"无法回答时弃权"作为一等评分结果。

Result: 提出了一个能同时评估因果推理、数据科学、不确定性量化、弃权和工具使用的综合性基准CausalDS，每个实例包含SCM、观测数据、合成故事和跨三阶因果阶梯的任务。

Conclusion: CausalDS通过完全合成生成避免了"因果鹦鹉"风险，同时保留了真实数据的经验结构，为评估LLM作为数据科学智能体的因果推理能力提供了更全面的评估框架。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。该基准的SCM+观测数据+自然语言故事的框架可直接迁移到遥感领域：1) 构建遥感因果SCM（如植被-气候-人类活动的因果图），生成合成遥感观测数据（NDVI、地表温度等）并配以自然语言描述；2) 评估遥感大模型在Pearl三阶任务上的表现（如"如果降水增加20%，植被指数会怎样变化？"的干预推理）；3) 引入遥感中常见的不完美观测（云遮挡、传感器噪声），测试模型的鲁棒性和弃权能力；4) 将弃权机制引入遥感变化检测或分类任务中，当数据质量不足或因果证据不充分时允许模型主动弃权。

Abstract (英文): Large language models (LLMs) increasingly act as integrated data-science agents, combining abstract reasoning with advanced tool use. Yet the relevant benchmark landscape largely divides into symbolic causal reasoning benchmarks without realistic data analysis or data analysis benchmarks without a principled causal data-generating structure. Furthermore, existing causal evaluation datasets are often restricted to curated examples from existing sources, with diversity coming from limited templatized variations rather than from systematic generation of novel synthetic causal structures. We introduce CausalDS, a benchmark for evaluating causal reasoning in agentic data-science workflows. Each benchmark instance is a scene consisting of a sampled structural causal model (SCM) with generated observational data and an accompanying synthetic natural-language story grounded in a realistic domain. We optionally ground the composition of the benchmark components in empirical distributions obtained from real-world datasets, thus retaining empirical structure while reducing the "causal parrot" risk through completely synthetic generation. From each scene, we then derive tasks spanning all three of Pearl's rungs, with typical data-science prediction tasks appearing as Rung 1. Most tasks include a data science coding component, where the model typically needs to use several tools to arrive at the final answer due to the frequent presence of imperfect observations, which are generated by an observation model. Additionally, recognizing when a question admits no warranted answer and abstaining is treated as a first-class scored outcome. The benchmark thus jointly evaluates symbolic causal reasoning, data science, uncertainty quantification, abstention, and tool use/coding.

### [249] [Answer Set Programming Energised! End-to-End Neurosymbolic Reasoning and Learning with ASP and Energy Based Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08136)
*Jakob Suchan,Julius Monsen,Salim Baloch,Mehul Bhatt*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出了一种基于回答集编程（ASP）与基于能量的模型（EBM）模块化集成的神经符号推理与学习方法，支持连续潜在空间中的联合优化，并通过显式ASP声明语义整合背景知识、约束和非单调推理，在视觉问答和多目标跟踪基准上进行了验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有神经符号方法在整合背景知识、处理非单调推理以及实现端到端鲁棒训练方面存在局限，缺乏一个通用的、以ASP为中心的实用平台来支持动态领域中的感知与交互任务。

Method: 将回答集编程（ASP）与基于能量的模型（EBM）进行模块化集成，在连续潜在空间中通过显式ASP声明语义实现联合优化，支持背景知识、约束和非单调推理，并构建了基于ASP的端到端训练框架。

Result: 在MNIST上展示了基本用法，在Clevr视觉问答基准和MOT多目标跟踪基准上进行了评估，验证了方法的有效性。

Conclusion: 该方法为ASP中心的神经符号推理提供了通用模型和实用平台，支持动态领域中的鲁棒端到端训练，在感知与交互任务中具有应用潜力。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。该方法的ASP+EBM框架可直接应用于遥感领域中的视觉问答（如遥感图像场景理解与属性查询）和多目标跟踪（如卫星视频中的车辆/船只跟踪）。具体改进方案包括：(1) 将遥感领域的先验知识（如地物空间关系、时序约束）编码为ASP规则，增强推理可解释性；(2) 利用EBM处理遥感图像中的噪声和遮挡问题，提升鲁棒性；(3) 在遥感VQA任务中引入非单调推理以处理地物分类的歧义性。

Abstract (英文): We present a general neurosymbolic reasoning and learning methodology based on a modular integration of answer set programming with an energy based model substrate. Key contributions are: (1) supporting joint optimisation in the continuous latent space through explicit ASP-based declarative semantics fully incorporating background knowledge, constraints, non-monotonic inference; and (2) advancing recent works at the interface of answer sets, probabilistic logic, and answer set modulo theories by providing a generalised model and practical platform for ASP-centric robust, end-to-end training for applications in dynamic domains (e.g., involving perception and interaction). We provide a practical implementation, and demonstrate basic use and application (with MNIST), and evaluate with the visual question-answering benchmark Clevr and the multi-object tracking benchmark MOT.

### [250] [Overthinking: Amplifying Reasoning Weights to Extract Learned Secrets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08173)
*Jack Hopkins,Dipika Khullar,Fabien Roger*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出"过度思考"(overthinking)方法，通过放大推理模型与指令模型之间的参数差异，使语言模型在审计过程中更倾向于暴露隐藏信息。实验表明该方法能比原推理模型多10倍地揭示秘密信息。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 黑盒审计可能遗漏语言模型中微妙的错位和隐藏信息，需要更有效的方法在审计过程中引出这些信息。

Method: 定义过度思考模型为 θ_𝒪_α = θ_ℳ + α(θ_ℛ - θ_ℳ)，其中α>1放大推理能力；并引入逐层衰减策略选择性放大推理同时保持输出质量。

Result: 在四种实验设置和2B-32B模型上，过度思考模型比原推理模型多10倍地揭示隐藏信息；秘密暴露方式取决于秘密类型，有些需要沿推理方向扰动，有些则对任何足够大的权重扰动都有效。

Conclusion: 推理放大技术可以有效促使模型表面在训练过程中获得的秘密或意外行为，为语言模型审计提供了新的工具。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感领域深度模型可能存在训练数据中的隐藏偏差（如地理区域偏好、传感器伪影等），该方法可放大模型的"推理倾向"以暴露这些偏差。具体方案：(1)将遥感分类/分割模型的参数与一个"推理增强版"（如加入Chain-of-Thought微调的变体）做参数差值放大，审计模型是否对特定地物类型存在隐藏偏好；(2)在遥感视觉-语言模型（如遥感图像描述生成）中应用逐层衰减策略，检测模型是否在训练中习得了未预期的区域关联。

Abstract (英文): Black box auditing of language models is an essential pre-deployment tool, but it may miss subtle forms of misalignment and hidden information. To better elicit hidden information during an auditing process, we introduce \emph{overthinking}: the process of using reasoning task vectors to amplify the propensity to think out loud of reasoning models. Given the parameters of a non-reasoning instruct model $M$ and reasoning-distilled model $R$, we define the \emph{overthinking model} as $\boldsymbolθ_{\mathcal{O}_α} = \boldsymbolθ_{\mathcal{M}} + α(\boldsymbolθ_{\mathcal{R}} - \boldsymbolθ_{\mathcal{M}})$, where $α> 1$ amplifies reasoning beyond the pure reasoning model $R$. Additionally, we introduce new layer-wise attenuation strategies that selectively amplify reasoning without losing quality and coherence of model outputs. We demonstrate that overthinking models are more likely to reveal hidden information across four experimental settings, across 2B-32B models. Our findings suggest that reasoning amplification may surface secrets or unintended behaviors acquired during training up to $10\times$ more frequently than the original reasoning model. How secrets surface depends on the secret type: some require perturbation along the reasoning direction, while others yield to any sufficiently large weight perturbation.

</details>

*Sohrab Namazi Nia,Amogh Dalal,Ning Sa,Peter Ly,Marti Zentmaier,Tomek Strzalkowski,Jay Miller,Rishi Singh,Senjuti Basu Roy*

Method: 提出ASMR模块化智能体框架，包含两个专门智能体：(1) Field Generation Agent——从历史文本中提取语义概念，通过自适应多粒度聚类生成候选模式字段；(2) Structural Optimizer Agent——使用强化学习识别紧凑、信息丰富且无冗余的模式表示。

Abstract (英文): In this paper, we study the automatic schema generation problem: given a collection of historical ship maintenance and operational reports across multiple form categories, automatically discover compact and informative schemas that capture the essential information requirements of each report type. To address this challenge, we propose ASMR, a modular agentic framework consisting of two specialized agents. A Field Generation Agent extracts semantic concepts from historical narratives and generates candidate schema fields through adaptive multi-granularity clustering, while a Structural Optimizer Agent employs reinforcement learning to identify compact, informative, and non-redundant schema representations. The resulting schemas can guide report authors toward producing more complete, consistent, and actionable reports. Preliminary results demonstrate the promise of the proposed approach and highlight several open research challenges at the intersection of data management, agentic AI, and human-centered AI.

### [252] [A First-Principles Theory of Slow Thinking and Active Perception](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08196)
*Hongkang Yang,Zhi-Qin John Xu,Feiyu Xiong,Weinan E*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文从概率分布的提升与投影出发，提出"主动提升"（active lifting）理论，数学化地推导慢思考与主动感知过程，涵盖慢思考大语言模型的设计、训练与推理。该理论通过潜在序列采样与最大化降低不确定性的内在驱动力，导出一个包含静态理论子空间的大设计空间，并为提升慢思考模型提供了表示层次与采样器层次两条升级路径。同时，它还推导出具有内部时间轴的推理过程及类似最小长度编码的训练目标，刻画了感知的能动性，并衍生出改进慢思考模型的三阶段路径、统一多模态编码器与生成模型构建方法、类人视觉表示的先验形成以及策略崩溃的可能解决方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为认知功能的第一性原理建模提供数学基础，特别是对慢思考（主动感知）进行形式化推导，弥合复杂数据分布与简单函数族（如神经网络）表征之间的鸿沟。

Method: 提出"主动提升"理论，基于可观测空间与潜在空间上概率分布的提升与投影操作，通过潜在序列采样和最大化不确定性降低速率的内在驱动力，构建包含推理过程（内部时间轴）与训练目标（最小长度编码）的完整理论框架。

Result: 导出了一个包含静态理论子空间的大设计空间，明确了慢思考模型在表示层次与采样器层次中的位置与升级路径；推导出具有内部时间轴的推理过程和类语言发明的训练目标；产生了三阶段改进路径、统一多模态编码器/生成器构建方法、类人视觉表示先验形成机制以及策略崩溃解决方案等技术副产品。

Conclusion: 主动提升理论为慢思考LLM的设计、训练与推理提供了统一的数学基础，刻画了感知的能动性本质，并衍生出一系列具有实用价值的技术成果。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。具体方案：(1) 将主动提升理论应用于遥感影像的"慢感知"场景，如高分辨率卫星影像的目标检测与变化监测，通过潜在序列采样逐步降低对地物类别的不确定性，提升少样本或弱标注条件下的识别鲁棒性；(2) 利用三阶段改进路径为遥感基础模型（如遥感视觉-语言模型）设计层次化推理增强策略；(3) 借助统一多模态编码器构建框架，实现遥感影像、SAR、光谱数据等多模态遥感数据的联合表征学习；(4) 策略崩溃解决方案可应用于遥感中的强化学习任务（如卫星自主调度、无人机路径规划），提升策略稳定性。

Abstract (英文): As part of a series on first-principles modeling of cognitive functions, this paper attempts to provide a mathematical formulation of thinking and perception. It formally derives slow thinking or more generally, active perception, and encompasses the design, training and inference of slow thinking large language models. Our starting point is the lifting and projection of probability distributions on the observable and latent spaces, with the objective of representing complex data distributions by simple function families such as neural networks. A theory called "active lifting" is proposed, based on the sampling of latent sequences and an intrinsic drive to reduce uncertainty with maximum rate. It derives a large design space, containing the slow thinking models in a subspace that we call the static theory. These models are positioned on the representation hierarchy and sampler hierarchy induced by the static theory, and can be upgraded by climbing the two hierarchies. Active lifting further derives an inference process with an internal time axis, and a training objective that resembles minimum-length coding as well as the invention of languages. Thus, it characterizes the agency of perception, including the emergence of the slow thinking formats. Technical by-products of this theory include a three-stage pathway for improving slow thinking models, a unified approach to constructing encoders and generative models for all data modalities, a priori formation of human-like visual representations, and a possible solution to policy collapse.

### [253] [Playing ZendoWorld: Challenging AI Agents on Active Visual Concept Induction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08233)
*Sophia Koehler,Antonia Wüst,Inga Ibs,Wasu Top Piriyakulkij,Wolfgang Stammer,Constantin Rothkopf,Kevin Ellis,Kristian Kersting*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构建ZendoWorld交互环境，智能体需从视觉游戏观测中推断逻辑规则，通过提出新场景获取信息并根据反馈修正假设。评估了纯VLM推理、贝叶斯粒子滤波、动态概念发现和神经符号方法等智能体。

Conclusion: ZendoWorld为评估智能体的归纳推理与主动实验设计能力提供了重要平台，指明了在科学发现等领域的具体改进方向。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感领域中的地物分类与模式识别任务可借鉴ZendoWorld范式：将遥感影像中的地物类别组合视为"规则"，智能体通过选择不同区域（实验设计）获取标注反馈来推断地物分布规律。具体方案：(1)构建遥感版ZendoWorld，以地物光谱/空间模式为规则，评估模型能否主动选点采样以发现隐藏地类；(2)将贝叶斯粒子滤波与遥感主动学习结合，提升少样本条件下的分类规则恢复能力；(3)针对VLM在遥感中实验设计不足的问题，引入信息增益引导的采样策略。

Abstract (英文): A central challenge in building intelligent systems is enabling agents to jointly perceive complex inputs, form hypotheses about hidden patterns, and design informative experiments to test them. To study this problem, we propose ZendoWorld, a controlled interactive environment in which agents must infer a logical rule about visual game observations, acquire information by proposing new scenes, and refine their hypotheses based on feedback from the game environment. We evaluate several agents spanning pure VLM reasoning, Bayesian particle filtering, dynamic concept discovery, and neuro-symbolic methods. Our main findings are: (1) high accuracy in predicting labels for observed examples does not imply recovery of the underlying rule; (2) perception and induction are distinct bottlenecks for different agent classes; and (3) VLM-based agents propose near-uninformative experiments, failing to actively reduce hypothesis uncertainty. To compare these results, we collect human data on the task, which reveals a gap in inductive reasoning, particularly for more complex rules. Overall, ZENDOWORLD takes an important step toward evaluating intelligent agents and identifies concrete avenues for improvement, particularly in domains like scientific discovery.

### [254] [AutoPersonas: A Multi-Timescale Loop Engine for Open-Ended Persona Evolution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08252)
*Mengchen Li*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出AutoPersonas框架，通过多时间尺度生命-环境引擎解耦发散生成与证据驱动的吸收，解决长时程人格智能体在持续生命循环中的自我锁定问题，实验证明该方法能显著降低主题重复率并保持身份连续性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长时程人格智能体在持续运行时会出现"自我锁定"失效模式——局部看似合理的事件持续出现，但生成的生命轨迹不断坍缩向熟悉环境、薄弱关系、悬而未决的决定和停滞的生命阶段。作者追溯该失效的原因为：模型层面收敛于高概率行为通道，系统层面由状态、记忆、历史和环境摘要导致的上下文引力。

Method: 提出AutoPersonas多时间尺度生命-环境引擎，将环境侧事件(Occurrences)、累积观测(Observations)与人格状态(State)分离。其OSO循环（Occurrence-State-Observation）在允许发散性未来材料进入的同时，要求经过证据驱动的吸收才能改变状态或可达性。通过三年压缩模拟和八模型40天压力测试（生成1600个事件）等方法进行验证。

Result: 八模型40天压力测试中，平均滚动5天动作类别重复率达95.2%-97.6%，所有模型在第11天超过90%；语义主题保持分析显示所有直接循环运行中宏观主题重复率为79.0%-88.0%。在40天A/B对比中，上下文切片掩码加每个样本散度目标使宏观主题重复率从61.8%降至36.3%，累计主题数约翻倍。

Conclusion: 实验结果支持一个有界主张：将受控的发散生成与证据驱动的吸收分离，可以在保持身份连续性的同时减少人格-环境自我锁定。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：75%。遥感领域的长时序动态监测（如土地覆盖变化检测、城市扩张分析）面临类似的"锁定"问题——模型倾向于重复预测高概率类别而忽略渐变信号。可借鉴OSO循环思想：将遥感观测数据解耦为"事件层"（突发变化，如火灾）、"累积观测层"（多时相堆叠）和"状态层"（土地覆盖类别），设计证据驱动的状态更新机制，避免模型过早收敛于历史高概率类别，提升长时序变化检测的敏感性。

Abstract (英文): Long-term persona agents must remain identifiable while adapting to new events, relationships, evidence, and social conditions. We identify self-locking as a runtime failure mode in continuing persona-life loops: locally plausible events keep appearing while the generated life collapses toward familiar environments, weak relationships, suspended decisions, and stale life stages. We trace this failure to model-level convergence toward high-probability behavioral channels and system-level context gravity from State, memory, history, and environment summaries. We introduce AutoPersonas, a multi-timescale life-environment engine for bounded persona-level recursive self-evolution. It separates environment-side Occurrences, accumulated Observations, and persona State. Its OSO loop admits divergent future-facing material while requiring evidence-governed absorption before State or reachability changes. A three-year compressed simulation exposed environment watermark shells, occurrence-hardening gaps, slow-change accumulation failures, recursive indecision, and weak relationship persistence. An eight-model 40-day stress test generated 1,600 events and found mean rolling 5-day action-category repetition of 95.2%-97.6%, with all models crossing 90% by day 11. Semantic re-keeping found 79.0%-88.0% macro-theme repetition across all direct-loop runs. In a same-runtime 40-day A/B, context-slice masking plus per-sample divergence targeting reduced macro-theme repetition from 61.8% to 36.3% and roughly doubled cumulative theme count. A juvenile-goblin fictional-world run reproduced the anti-fixation regime without hard real-world intrusions. These results support a bounded claim: separating controlled divergence from evidence-governed absorption can reduce persona-environment self-locking while preserving identity continuity.

### [255] [Compete Then Collaborate: Frontier AI Teachers Build a Verifiable Curriculum to Improve a Coding Student Beyond Imitation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08255)
*Miseong Shawn Kim*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 提出了一种“先竞争后协作”的多教师知识蒸馏框架：四个前沿AI模型通过执行验证（单元测试）进行头对头排名，然后协作构建可验证课程，用于训练学生模型。研究发现：教师模型在标准问题上饱和（99-100%），竞争性任务区分度明显（Gemini 77% > Claude/Codex 69% > Grok 50%）；直接模仿教师解决方案的SFT会降低学生模型性能（如MBPP-test从76.7%降至72.7%）；而将协作课程用于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）则显著提升学生性能（竞争问题从5.9%提升至8.8%，相对提升49%）。核心结论：AI教师协作的价值不在于汇总答案供模仿，而在于共同构建可验证环境让学生通过实践学习。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有知识蒸馏方法将多个教师输出直接合并，无法确定哪个前沿模型教学效果最佳；且常依赖LLM法官进行评估，存在偏向自身输出的偏见。

Method: 提出竞争后协作框架：1）四名教师（Claude, Codex-GPT, Grok, Gemini）通过执行验证（单元测试+标准输入输出检查）进行头对头排名，确保公平；2）协作构建可验证课程；3）学生模型（Qwen2.5-Coder）分别在SFT和RLVR两种范式下训练。

Result: 1）标准任务饱和（99-100%），竞争任务区分度：Gemini 77% > Claude 69% = Codex 69% > Grok 50%，但教师排名与学生结果无关；2）SFT模仿教师方案导致性能下降；3）RLVR提升竞争任务性能49%（5.9%→8.8%），逆转SFT趋势。

Conclusion: 多教师协作的价值不在于汇集答案供学生模仿，而在于共同构建可验证环境，让学生通过强化学习实践来提升能力。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。具体方案：1）将遥感任务（如地物分类、变化检测、目标识别）转化为可验证的标准化测试（如像素级精度指标、IoU阈值检查），替代单元测试作为执行验证的评判标准；2）多个遥感基础模型（如SpectralGPT、RSPrompter等）作为教师，通过标准化遥感基准测试（如NWPU-RESISC45、DOTA）进行头对头排名；3）学生模型（轻量遥感网络）通过RLVR在可验证遥感环境中训练，利用多个教师协作构建的课程（如不同难度的遥感解译任务序列）进行学习，避免直接模仿教师输出带来的性能退化。

Abstract (英文): Large language models increasingly serve as teachers generating training data for smaller students. Prior multi-teacher knowledge distillation methods merge outputs without determining which frontier model teaches best, often relying on an LLM judge biased toward its own outputs. We introduce a compete-then-collaborate framework where four frontier AI teachers (Claude, Codex-GPT, Grok, Gemini) are ranked head-to-head by an execution-based judge (unit tests and stdin-stdout checks) with fairness controls, and then collaborate to build a verifiable curriculum for a student (Qwen2.5-Coder). We report three findings. (1) Under execution verification, all teachers solve standard problems near-perfectly after self-correction (99-100%) due to a saturation effect, but harder competition problems separate them (Gemini 77% > Claude 69% = Codex 69% > Grok 50%); however, the robust student-side results do not depend on teacher ranking. (2) Imitation (SFT) on verified solutions does not improve, and can degrade, an already-competent student at 7B and 32B (e.g., from 76.7% to 72.7% on MBPP-test, and 5.9% to 2.9% on competition problems). (3) Using the same collaborative curriculum as a reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) environment improves the student (from 5.9% to 8.8% peak on competition problems, a +49% relative gain), reversing SFT's direction. The value of AI-teacher collaboration lies not in pooling answers to imitate, but in jointly constructing a verifiable environment where the student learns by doing. We release a reproducible on-prem pipeline (NVIDIA GB10) with framework patches for running GRPO on a bleeding-edge stack.

</details>


### [256] [MentalHospital: A Virtual Environment for Evaluating Psychiatric Clinical Encounters](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08257)
*Yuming Yang,Xiao Sun,Yuanwei Zou,Zhengxiao Wu,Yun Chen,Jiang Zhong,Haoyang Zeng,Jingwang Huang,Kaiwen Wei*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了MentalHospital，一个基于LLM的精神科临床会诊虚拟评估环境，通过S.O.A.P.工作流程、标准化病人和双轨评估协议，系统性地评估LLM在精神科临床场景中的表现。配套开发的MentalEval评估器在专家对齐性上达到平均QWK 0.944，基准测试显示最强LLM在客观精神科能力上仍落后临床医生37.28个百分点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM在孤立的精神科任务（如对话、诊断、治疗规划）上表现良好，但缺乏能模拟完整精神科临床会诊全流程的基准测试，无法全面评估LLM在真实临床场景中的综合能力。

Method: 构建MentalHospital虚拟评估环境，包含：（1）基于1,193份去标识化精神科电子健康档案构建的技能增强标准化病人；（2）S.O.A.P.工作流程（主观访谈、客观检查、诊断评估、治疗规划）；（3）双轨评估协议（客观对比EHR参考+主观评估临床过程质量）。开发MentalEval，包含五个领域特定评估器（沟通共情、访谈专业性、临床记录质量、诊断严谨性、治疗适当性），采用基于评分标准的SFT和专家引导的DPO训练。

Result: 22名临床医生的调查支持MentalHospital的临床逼真度（3.88/5）；MentalEval达到平均QWK 0.944的专家对齐性；最强LLM在客观精神科能力上落后临床医生37.28个百分点，精神状态评估是关键瓶颈。

Conclusion: 当前LLM在完整精神科临床会诊中与临床医生存在显著差距，尤其是精神状态评估环节；MentalHospital和MentalEval为评估和提升LLM精神科临床能力提供了有效框架。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：75%。与遥感领域的交叉方案：（1）将S.O.A.P.工作流程范式迁移至遥感解译流程，建立类似的结构化评估框架（如数据获取→预处理→特征提取→分类识别→应用决策），系统评估AI模型在完整遥感任务链上的表现；（2）MentalEval的领域特定评估器设计思路可应用于遥感领域，开发针对影像质量、特征提取准确性、分类一致性、时空分析合理性等维度的自动化评估器；（3）标准化病人（技能增强标准化病人）的概念可类比为遥感中的标准化测试数据集和仿真场景生成，用于评估模型在不同地物类型和成像条件下的综合性能；（4）双轨评估协议中的客观参考对比+主观过程质量评估思路，可用于遥感产品精度验证中结合地面真值参考与专家目视解释的综合评估。

Abstract (英文): Large language models (LLMs) have shown strong performance on isolated psychiatric tasks, including dialogue, diagnosis, and treatment planning, yet existing benchmarks rarely simulate complete psychiatric clinical encounters. We introduce $\textbf{MentalHospital}$, a virtual evaluation environment for LLM-based psychiatric clinical encounters. MentalHospital instantiates the Subjective Interviewing, Objective Examination, Diagnostic Assessment, and Treatment Planning (S.O.A.P.) workflow, using skill-augmented standardized patients constructed from 1,193 de-identified psychiatric electronic health record (EHR) cases spanning all major ICD-11 categories and 76 disorders. Each encounter is assessed through a dual-track protocol that combines objective comparison against EHR-derived references with subjective assessment of clinical process quality. To scale specialist judgment, we develop $\textbf{MentalEval}$, five domain-specific evaluators covering communication empathy, interviewing professionalism, clinical-note quality, diagnostic rigor, and treatment appropriateness, trained with rubric-grounded SFT and expert-guided DPO. Survey responses from 22 clinicians support MentalHospital's clinical fidelity (3.88/5), while MentalEval achieves strong expert alignment with an average QWK of 0.944. Benchmarking shows that even the strongest LLM trails clinicians by 37.28 percentage points in objective psychiatric competence, with mental status assessment as a key bottleneck.

### [257] [Different Teachers, Different Capabilities: Sub-1B On-Device Distillation for Structured Text Enrichment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08268)
*Vinay Kumar Chaganti*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文研究将大模型的结构化提取任务（新闻文章→JSON摘要+5个分类标签）蒸馏到小模型（0.6B参数）中。实验使用8B推理教师（deepseek-r1:8b）蒸馏0.6B学生（Qwen3-0.6B，QLoRA，三种随机种子），对比同尺寸非推理教师和更大规模的托管流水线。学生模型速度提升约48倍（0.8s vs 39s），恢复了教师与基线之间58%的摘要质量差距，超过约束解码+16.8分、少样本提示+4.9分。不同教师迁移不同能力：推理教师传递写作质量，托管流水线传递标签多样性，而同尺寸指令教师的学生更忠实于原文（少编造）。最终输出为按字段的路由图，指导设备端内容增强。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 结构化提取场景中，大模型对每条数据的处理延迟高，将其蒸馏到小模型可显著降低延迟和成本。本文旨在量化这种蒸馏在不同子任务上究竟能带来多少实际收益。

Method: 将新闻文章映射为包含简短摘要和5个分类标签的JSON对象。使用deepseek-r1:8b推理教师通过QLoRA蒸馏至Qwen3-0.6B学生（三个随机种子）。设置两个教师对照组：同尺寸非推理教师（指令微调模型）和更大规模的托管流水线。采用盲测、无参考、三人评审小组评估，对比少样本提示和约束解码两种非蒸馏基线。

Result: 学生模型运行速度0.8s/篇（教师39s，提速约48倍）。摘要质量恢复教师与基线之间58%的差距，比约束解码高+16.8分，比少样本提示高+4.9分。同尺寸非推理教师训练的学生与未调优基线无差别，证明摘要提升来自教师的推理能力而非规模。推理教师传递写作质量，托管流水线传递标签多样性，指令教师的学生在短文本上更忠实（74 vs 55篇忠实），推理教师学生存在编造问题。

Conclusion: 没有任何一种模型能在所有字段上取得最佳效果，因此最终成果是一个按字段的路由图，用于指导设备端内容增强任务中如何选择不同教师蒸馏出的模型。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。遥感领域存在大量结构化提取任务（如影像→JSON格式的地理标签+属性描述），可借鉴本研究的蒸馏框架：（1）用遥感大模型（如GeoAI模型）作为推理教师蒸馏轻量级学生模型部署到边缘设备；（2）采用多教师路由策略：一个教师擅长空间关系描述（类似写作质量），另一个教师擅长分类标签多样性（如土地利用类型），按字段选择最优蒸馏模型；（3）需注意遥感数据中地理实体编造问题（类似本文的忠实度问题），可引入空间约束或参照数据增强忠实性。

Abstract (英文): High-volume structured extraction pays a large model's latency on every item, so distilling the task into a small on-device model is attractive: comparable output at a fraction of the time and cost. We measure what that distillation actually delivers, per sub-task. Each news article is mapped to one JSON object with a short summary and five categorical labels. We distill an 8B reasoning teacher (deepseek-r1:8b) into a 0.6B student (Qwen3-0.6B; QLoRA, three seeds), and add two teacher controls: a same-size non-reasoning teacher and a larger managed pipeline. A blinded, reference-free, three-judge panel scores every arm against the full article, alongside two non-distillation baselines, few-shot prompting and constrained decoding. The student runs at about 0.8 s per article against the teacher's 39 s, and recovers 58% of the base-to-teacher gap on summary quality, beating its primary baseline (constrained decoding) by +16.8 points and few-shot prompting by a secondary +4.9. A same-size non-reasoning teacher trains a student no better than the untuned base, so the summary gain follows from the teacher's reasoning nature rather than its scale. Capabilities then split by teacher: the reasoning teacher transfers writing quality and the managed pipeline transfers label diversity, while a same-size instruction teacher's students stay more grounded on the 22 short, thin-source articles in the 93-item test set (74 versus 55 faithful), where the reasoning-lineage student fabricates. That grounding difference is a consistent ordering rather than a significant aggregate effect, and the subgroup is small, so we report it as a direction. Because no single engine wins every field, the deliverable is a per-field routing map for on-device enrichment.

### [258] [PolyUQuest: Verifiable Structure-Aware Web RAG over Heterogeneous Graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08269)
*Ying Liu,Yi Ye,Quanyu Feng,Mingxi Ye,Mingtao Zhang,Haoyang Li,Chen Jason Zhang,Qing Li*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: PolyUQuest 是一个基于异构图的、结构感知的Web RAG框架，通过统一页面间的超链接拓扑、页面内的DOM层次结构和跨页面的实体-关系知识，并采用双层级路由器将查询分派到三种检索模式，实现了可验证、高准确率的检索增强生成，在PolyU官网数据集上优于现有RAG系统，且消耗更少的LLM token。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有RAG系统将网页视为扁平文本，丢失了HTML中编码的结构和语义信号，导致检索时无法利用页面间的超链接拓扑、页面内的DOM层次结构以及跨页面的实体关系知识，影响答案的正确性和可验证性。

Method: 构建异构图表征超链接拓扑、DOM层次结构和实体关系知识；设计双层级路由器，根据查询的结构需求将其分派到三种检索模式之一：直接块检索、跨页图遍历和多跳实体推理；每个引用块携带源页面、标题路径和实体链接，实现完全可验证的答案生成。

Result: 在PolyU官网数据集（4,240页面、31,086 DOM块、29,119实体、37,680关系）上的评估表明，PolyUQuest在答案正确性、覆盖率和忠实度方面优于现有RAG系统，同时每个查询消耗的LLM token显著更少。

Conclusion: 提出的结构感知RAG框架能够有效利用网页的结构化信息提升检索和生成质量，且答案完全可追溯验证。该系统已准备部署为PolyU面向学生的问答服务。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：90%。遥感领域拥有丰富的结构化数据来源，如地理空间元数据、遥感影像的层次化标注（场景-对象-像素）、不同数据源间的实体关系（如卫星、传感器、地理区域间的关联）。该框架可直接应用于遥感知识问答系统：将遥感数据源文档的层级结构（如数据集-波段-产品）映射为DOM层次，将数据间的引用和关联（如不同卫星数据间的互补关系）建模为超链接拓扑，将地理实体及其关系（如城市-河流-植被）建模为实体关系图。双层级路由器可适配遥感查询类型：直接块检索适用于单数据源属性查询，跨页图遍历适用于多源数据关联查询，多跳实体推理适用于复杂地理推理（如"某区域受哪些卫星数据的哪些波段覆盖"）。答案可验证性对遥感应用尤为重要，每条引用可追溯至具体数据源、处理步骤和地理范围。

Abstract (英文): Existing retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) systems treat web pages as flat text, losing the structural and semantic signals encoded in HTML. We present PolyUQuest, a verifiable, structure-aware web RAG framework built on a heterogeneous graph that unifies hyperlink topology between pages, DOM hierarchy within pages, and entity-relation knowledge across pages. A two-tier router dispatches each query to one of three retrieval modes matched to its structural need, including direct block retrieval, cross-page graph traversal, and multi-hop entity reasoning. Every answer is fully verifiable, as each cited block carries its source page, heading path, and entity links so that users can trace any claim back to its structural evidence. We evaluate on the official websites of the Hong Kong Polytechnic University (PolyU), comprising 4,240 pages, 31,086 DOM blocks, 29,119 entities, and 37,680 relations, together with a multi-type evaluation benchmark. PolyUQuest outperforms existing RAG systems in answer correctness, coverage, and faithfulness, while consuming significantly fewer LLM tokens per query. The demonstration provides an interactive interface for inspecting cited answers, comparing retrieval traces across routing modes, and exploring evidence graph paths. PolyUQuest is being prepared for deployment as a student-facing QA service at PolyU.

### [259] [Understanding Axes of Difficulty For Long Context Tasks Via PredicateLongBench](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08284)
*Siddhartha Jain,Ameya Velingker*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: PredicateLongBench是一个通过查找满足特定谓词约束的最长连续子序列来压力测试LLM长上下文推理能力的基准。该基准的核心创新在于识别并系统探索了多个不同的难度轴（如谓词类型、序列长度、约束复杂度等），用于全面评估长上下文理解能力。实验表明，前沿模型在难度递增时表现不佳，揭示了当前长上下文能力的局限性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有长上下文评估（如NIAH测试、多跳推理、摘要任务）主要测量平均表现，许多已饱和或缺乏鲁棒性，且缺少系统性地按不同难度轴缩放任务来探测模型性能的方法。本文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 提出PredicateLongBench基准，核心任务是在长输入中找出满足给定谓词/约束的最长连续单词子序列。提供两条互补的数据生成管线：1) 全合成管线，使用随机单词字符串；2) 真实世界管线，从自然文档中采样单词并保留其分布特性。通过系统变化谓词类型、序列长度、约束条件等多个难度轴进行全面评估。

Result: 前沿模型在PredicateLongBench上的表现随难度轴增加而显著下降，表明当前长上下文能力存在系统性局限。该基准未饱和，能有效区分不同模型的长上下文推理能力。

Conclusion: PredicateLongBench作为系统性的长上下文压力测试基准，揭示了现有模型的局限性。其任务概念简单但富有挑战性，无需LLM生成或评判器，可作为评估长上下文推理能力的有力工具。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。该基准的"在长序列中查找满足约束条件的最长连续子序列"范式可直接迁移到遥感领域：1) 可用于评估遥感大模型在长时序遥感影像（如连续时间序列的NDVI、SAR数据）中识别满足特定地物变化模式的最长连续性片段；2) 难度轴的系统缩放方法可应用于遥感任务，如调整空间分辨率、时间跨度、光谱约束数量等维度来全面评估模型能力；3) 也可评估模型在长距离遥感文本（如地理描述报告、野外调查记录）中的推理能力。

Abstract (英文): Large language models (LLMs) have demonstrated rapidly improving long-context capabilities, prompting a wave of benchmarks designed to evaluate them. However, existing long-context evaluations - from Needle-in-a-Haystack (NIAH) tests to more recent multi-hop reasoning and summarization tasks - predominantly measure average-case performance, and many are either saturated or lack robustness. Notably absent is a systematic way to probe how models perform as we scale up the difficulty of tasks along various axes. We address this gap by proposing PredicateLongBench, a benchmark that stress-tests long-context reasoning by asking models to identify the longest contiguous subsequence of words in a long input that satisfies given predicates/constraints (e.g., lexicographic ordering), drawn from a broader predicate class. The central innovation of our benchmark is the identification and systematic exploration of multiple different axes of difficulty which test multiple aspects of long context understanding. We provide two complementary generation pipelines - a fully synthetic setup using random word-like strings, and a real-world setup that samples words from natural documents while preserving their distributional properties. We find that frontier models struggle to perform well as we scale up the difficulty of tasks along our axes, demonstrating the utility of our benchmark in understanding the limitations of current long-context capabilities. Furthermore, the tasks in PredicateLongBench, though challenging, are conceptually simple and do not require LLM-based generations or judges.

### [260] [Psychological Competence as a Missing Dimension in AI Evaluation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08285)
*Marcos Economides,Paul M. Sacher,Samuel Salzer,Alexis Michelle Abellar,Fendi Tsim,Antoine Ferrère*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出将"心理能力"作为面向人类的AI系统评估中缺失的关键维度，定义为系统支持用户认知、情绪解读和行为决策的能力，涵盖框架、语气、权威感、响应性、不确定性处理等交互属性，并提出了概念框架及评估方法（场景探针、人工评估、模型辅助评估）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AI评估框架主要关注技术性能（准确性、鲁棒性、推理能力等），但这些指标不足以评估直接通过自然语言与用户交互的AI系统（如顾问、教练、导师、伴侣），因为这些系统的响应会影响用户的推理、情绪解读、信念形成、信任校准和决策，评估单元应是"人-AI交互"而非仅模型本身。

Method: 基于行为科学与人类-AI交互研究，定义"心理能力"概念并明确其核心域，提出通过场景探针、结构化人工评估和模型辅助评估三种方法进行测评，而非提出具体基准。

Result: 构建了心理能力的概念框架，明确了其边界和核心域，提出了多层次评估方法体系。

Conclusion: 心理能力应成为模型提供方、部署组织、研究人员和监管机构在评估面向人类的AI系统时的重要考量维度。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：70%。遥感领域的人机交互系统（如智能解译助手、灾害应急决策支持系统）可借鉴该框架评估AI对用户决策的影响，例如评估遥感AI在解释地物分类结果时的语气、不确定性表达和权威感对用户信任和最终决策的影响；反之，遥感中需要高精度结果的应用场景也可为该框架提供"任务关键型"交互的评估测试用例。

Abstract (英文): Current AI evaluation frameworks focus primarily on technical performance, including accuracy, robustness, reasoning ability, and policy compliance. These measures remain essential, but they are not sufficient for systems that interact directly with users through natural language. Human-facing AI systems are increasingly used as advisors, coaches, tutors, and companions. In these roles, their responses can shape how users reason, interpret emotions, form beliefs, calibrate trust, and make decisions. The relevant unit of evaluation is therefore not only the model, but the human-AI interaction. This paper introduces psychological competence as a missing dimension in AI evaluation. We define psychological competence as the capacity of a human-facing AI system to support user cognition, emotional interpretation, and behavioral decision-making in ways that are appropriate to the user, context, and purpose of the interaction. This includes interaction properties such as framing, tone, perceived authority, responsiveness, uncertainty handling, and conversational guidance. Existing evaluation approaches capture parts of this problem but rarely assess these psychological effects directly. Drawing on behavioral science and human-AI interaction research, we outline a conceptual framework for psychological competence and its core domains. Rather than proposing a specific benchmark, we define the construct, clarify its boundaries, and describe how it may be assessed through scenario-based probes, structured human evaluation, and model-assisted evaluation methods. We argue that psychological competence should become a core consideration for model providers, deploying organizations, researchers, and regulators concerned with the real-world effects of human-facing AI systems.

### [262] [Blind-Spots-Bench: Evaluating Blind Spots in Multimodal Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08317)
*Matteo Santelmo,Xiuying Wei,Israa Fakih,Felix Bauer,Juan Garcia Giraldo,Chengkun Li,Etienne Bamas,Emmanuel Abbé*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出名为blind-spots-bench的新基准测试，专门设计用于暴露现代AI模型在人类认为简单但模型却难以处理的任务上的盲点。该基准包含235个从AI课程学生收集并精心标注的样本，并涵盖多种任务类型。实验表明，闭源前沿模型在盲点测试上可领先开源模型约10%，且没有任何单一模型在所有任务类型上占优，部分任务对全部评估模型都具有挑战性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基准测试可能低估了现代AI系统的持久性盲点——模型在标准基准上表现良好，却在人类认为几乎微不足道的任务（如操作字符串、画五条腿的狗）上失败。作者旨在构建一个能暴露这些盲点的诊断性压力测试工具。

Method: 从AI课程学生处收集原始问题，经过清洗和结构化参考解标注，提出任务分类体系，最终得到包含235个样本的数据集。开发自动化评分管线，在盲点测试上评估了包括开源和闭源的语言模型、视觉-语言模型以及图像生成模型在内的多种模型。

Result: 闭源前沿模型在盲点测试上可比开源模型高出约10%的性能差距，即使它们在现有基准上表现相当。细粒度分析显示，没有单一模型在所有任务类型上占优，部分任务对所有评估模型都具有挑战性。

Conclusion: blind-spots-bench作为一个诊断性压力测试，能有效识别当前模型的具体弱点，揭示了现有基准无法捕获的能力差距，为模型改进提供了有价值的方向。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：75%。具体方案：(1) 构建遥感领域的"盲点测试集"，收集卫星影像中人类容易识别但AI常出错的场景（如云层遮挡下的地物分类、细粒度变化检测中的伪变化剔除）；(2) 将benchmark的任务分类体系迁移到遥感，设计针对特定遥感任务（如图像配准、多时相分析）的盲点测试；(3) 利用自动化评分管线评估遥感基础模型的薄弱环节，为模型改进提供针对性指导。

Abstract (英文): Modern AI models achieve strong performance on many established benchmarks, yet they still fail on tasks that humans find almost trivial, such as manipulating a string or drawing a dog with five legs. These examples suggest that existing benchmarks may under-measure persistent blind spots in current systems. We introduce $\texttt{blind-spots-bench}$, a benchmark designed to expose such blind spots through tasks that appear simple for humans but remain challenging for modern AI. We collect raw questions from students in an AI course, clean and annotate them with structured reference solutions, and propose a task taxonomy tailored to the resulting dataset of 235 samples. We further develop an automated grading pipeline to evaluate a wide range of models, including open-weight and closed-source language, vision-language, and image-generation models. Our analysis on $\texttt{blind-spots-bench}$ reveals that closed-source frontier models can substantially outperform open-weight models with even $\approx10\%$ gap, even when they attain comparable performance on existing benchmarks. A more fine-grained analysis shows that no single model dominates across all task types, and that some tasks remain challenging for all evaluated models. These results highlight the value of $\texttt{blind-spots-bench}$ as a diagnostic stress test for identifying concrete weaknesses in current modern models.

### [263] [MobiDiff: Semantic-Aware Multi-Channel Discrete Diffusion for Human Mobility Data Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08357)
*Rongchao Xu,Lin Jiang,Dahai Yu,Ximiao Li,Taichi Liu,Desheng Zhang,Yuan Tian,Guang Wang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: MobiDiff是一种端到端离散扩散框架，通过直接去噪多通道语义骨架（空间、活动、时间）来生成人类移动数据，避免了现有扩散方法中的昂贵插值和粗到细的管线。在亚特兰大、波士顿和西雅图三个真实数据集上，MobiDiff在保真度、隐私保护和效率方面表现优异，推理速度比GeoGen平均快5.3倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现实世界的人类移动数据收集成本高且因隐私问题难以共享；现有基于扩散的方法依赖连续或隐式时空轨迹，无法原生建模具有显式区域、活动、时间和间隔结构的离散语义事件。

Method: MobiDiff将每次签到事件分解为空间、活动和时间三个通道，采用结构化的事件级、组级和通道级掩码策略，联合捕捉轨迹级别的移动模式和事件内依赖关系，通过直接去噪多通道语义骨架来生成移动数据。

Result: 在亚特兰大、波士顿和西雅图三个大规模真实数据集上，MobiDiff有效保持了轨迹长度和时间间隔分布，在更广泛的移动统计数据上具有竞争力；推理速度比最先进的GeoGen平均快5.3倍。

Conclusion: 离散扩散为合成移动数据生成提供了一种可解释且高效的框架。

与遥感交叉或改进方案: 交叉/改进可行性：85%。该离散扩散框架可直接迁移至遥感中的轨迹生成任务，如合成人类出行轨迹用于城市动态分析、POI访问模式模拟。改进方案：(1) 将空间通道替换为遥感影像中的地理栅格坐标或语义地物类别；(2) 活动通道可扩展为遥感监测的语义事件类型（如农业活动、交通流量状态）；(3) 时间通道可整合遥感时序观测窗口；(4) 事件级掩码策略可用于处理遥感中不规则采样的时空观测数据。

Abstract (英文): Human mobility data are essential for transportation optimization, urban planning, and resource allocation, yet real-world mobility data are costly to collect and difficult to share due to privacy concerns. Recent diffusion-based methods have shown promise in synthesizing realistic mobility patterns, but they typically rely on continuous or latent spatio-temporal traces, limiting their ability to natively model discrete semantic events with explicit region, activity, time, and interval structures. To address this issue, we introduce MobiDiff, an end-to-end discrete diffusion framework that efficiently generates mobility data by directly denoising multi-channel semantic skeletons, avoiding the costly interpolation, latent trace construction, and coarse-to-fine realization pipelines widely used in existing diffusion-based methods. Specifically, MobiDiff decomposes each human check-in event into spatial, activity, and temporal channels, and employs structured event-, group-, and channel-level masking to jointly capture trajectory-level mobility patterns and within-event dependencies. We evaluate generation fidelity, privacy-preserving, and efficiency on three large-scale real-world datasets from Atlanta, Boston, and Seattle. Results show that MobiDiff effectively preserves trajectory length and temporal interval distributions while remaining competitive across broader mobility statistics; it is also much faster than state-of-the-art methods, e.g., 5.3$\times$ faster than GeoGen on average during inference. These findings suggest that discrete diffusion offers an interpretable and efficient framework for synthetic mobility data generation.

### [264] [FedOPAL: One-Shot Federated Learning via Analytic Visual Prompt Tuning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.08368)
*Lingyu Qiu,Daniela Annunziata,Stefano Izzo,Fabio Giampaolo,Francesco Piccialli*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: FedOPAL框架通过在客户端引入视觉提示作为特征修正器，结合局部近端约束将异构数据特征分布调整到线性可分离空间，从而满足解析联邦学习的理论假设，实现零服务器训练成本的高效联邦学习。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有单次联邦学习方法存在服务器端计算成本高、超参数敏感等问题；解析联邦学习虽高效但在非独立同分布数据环境下因静态特征假设失效导致性能严重下降。亟需一种既能保持解析联邦学习零训练成本优势，又能处理数据异构性的方法。

Method: 提出FedOPAL框架，在客户端引入可学习的视觉提示作为特征修正器，通过局部近端约束对异构数据的特征分布进行主动校正，使其映射到线性可分离空间，从而满足解析联邦学习最小二乘闭式解的理论假设。

Result: 在多个基准测试上显著优于原始解析联邦学习方法，且达到与最先进的迭代方法相当的精度，同时保持零服务器端训练成本。

Conclusion: FedOPAL为边缘智能中大模型的高效协作提供了一种新的工程范式，在通信效率、计算成本和模型性能之间取得了良好平衡。
